Abakwane̩
O̩jo̩ nyi e̩wñ
E̩gba abakwane̩ ejodudu O̩jo̩ nyi efojale kpai ane̩-ile̩.
Ane̩-ile̩-i la de̩ juguu te̩ ofofo, oñ e̩chubi bʼeju o̩lulu le̩ ma; Afu O̩jo̩ la tʼeju omi ale bebebe.
Oñ O̩jo̩ kakini, Ugane̩ ki do̩mo̩; tak ugane̩ do̩mo̩.
O̩jo̩ la fʼugane̩ le̩ li kʼi nyo̩; tak O̩jo̩ fʼugane̩ daru bʼe̩chubi te̩.
O̩jo̩ la do̩ ugane̩ le̩ ko̩ o̩ro̩ka, e̩chubi i la do̩ ko̩ odu. Oñ ane̩ do̩mo̩, odudu la do̩mo̩, o̩jo̩ ejodudu.
Tak O̩jo̩ kakini, Agbagba ki te̩ alumeji omi le̩, kʼi fʼomiofo daru bʼomiofo te̩.
Oñ O̩jo̩ fʼagbagba che te̩, i la fʼomiofo e-ki dʼo̩gane̩ agbagba le̩ daru bʼomiofo e-ki dʼate̩ agbagba le̩ te̩. Abe̩le̩ i la de̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ do̩ agbagba le̩ ko̩ efojale. Oñ ane̩ do̩mo̩, odudu la do̩mo̩, o̩jo̩ ekeji.
Tak O̩jo̩ kakini, Omiofo o̩gane̩ efojale ki najeju jʼugbo okate ke, ane̩ e̩gbe̩ ki kwotejugede. Abe̩le̩ i la de̩.
Oñ O̩jo̩ do̩ ane̩ e̩gbe̩ le̩ ko̩ ane̩-ile̩, ujeju omi i la do̩ ko̩ ohimini abadi. O̩jo̩ la li kʼi nyo̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ kakini, Ane̩-ile̩-i ki lu ije̩, kpai eñmi kʼi aro ulu-wñ, kpai oli ki aro e̩go̩ uche̩ o̩la-wñ, e-kʼe̩yo̩-wñ dʼef uwñ, ane̩-ile̩. Abe̩le̩ i la de̩.
Tak ane̩-ile̩ lu ije̩, owñ chʼeñmi ki aro ulu e̩go̩ uche̩ o̩la-wñ, kpai oli ki aro kʼe̩yo̩ dʼef e̩ro-wñ e̩go̩ uche̩ o̩la-wñ. O̩jo̩ la li kʼi nyo̩.
Oñ ane̩ do̩mo̩, odudu la do̩mo̩, o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta.
Tak O̩jo̩ kakini, E̩mu ki jʼagbagba efojale, ki fʼo̩ro̩ka daru bʼodu te̩, i ki la jʼo̩mo̩ todu ujiwe, kpai adiko o̩lo̩ji kpai uwo, kpai o̩jo̩ ki añwa kpai o̩do̩ o̩do̩,
i ki jʼo̩mo̩ kʼi chʼe̩mu agbagba efojale kʼi mʼane̩ ne̩ ile̩-i. Abe̩le̩ i la de̩.
Abe̩le̩ O̩jo̩ fʼe̩mu elile meji le̩ che, e̩mu e-ki tule ki nʼo̩da o̩ro̩ka, e̩mu e-ki nya ki nʼo̩da odu; kpai ilawo ge̩.
O̩jo̩ la mʼu kojo̩ agbagba efojale kʼi mʼane̩ ne̩ ile̩-i,
kʼi ño̩ nʼo̩da o̩ro̩ka kpai odu, kʼi la fʼugane̩ daru bʼe̩chubi te̩: O̩jo̩ la li kʼi nyo̩.
Oñ ane̩ do̩mo̩, odudu la do̩mo̩, o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩le̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ kakini, Ef omi ki ko̩ ñw amonugo e̩wñ iñmi ke, ame̩we̩ ki nawu ate̩ ane̩-ile̩ ef agbagba ki che̩chi te̩ efojale.
Abe̩le̩ O̩jo̩ nyi ame̩la lile ki jʼef omi, kpai onugo e̩wñ iñmi du ki achiche̩, e-ki che̩ko̩ ef omi, uche̩ uche̩-ma, kpai e̩we̩ du ki nʼika uche̩ uche̩-wñ: O̩jo̩ la li kʼi nyo̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ de̩nyo̩ ñw uma kakini, Ame̩ ki rabi ku me̩ wewe nyo̩gba ku me̩ che̩ko̩ ef omi ohimini abadi, ame̩we̩ ki nawewe nyo̩gba ane̩-ile̩.
Oñ ane̩ do̩mo̩, odudu la do̩mo̩, o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩lu.
Tak O̩jo̩ kakini, Ile̩ ki nakʼamonugo e̩wñ iñmi dufu uche̩ uche̩-ma, ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ kpai ame̩wñ ki afa kpai ame̩wñ iñmi ane̩-ile̩ uche̩ uche̩-ma. Abe̩le̩ i la de̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ che ame̩wñ iñmi ane̩-ile̩-i uche̩ uche̩-ma, kpai ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ uche̩ uche̩-ma, kpai ame̩wñ du ki afa ane̩pe̩te̩ uche̩ uche̩-ma: O̩jo̩ la li kʼi nyo̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ kakini, Awa ki che one̩ rʼojibo-wa, ku ma bi awa onugo: ama ki la nʼo̩da ame̩ja ki jʼef ohimini abadi, kpai ame̩we̩ ojale, kpai ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩, kpai ane̩-ile̩ du, kpai e̩wñ du ki afa, e-ki afa ane̩-ile̩-i.
Abe̩le̩ O̩jo̩ fʼone̩ nyi ojibo-wñ onugo, e̩go̩ ojibo O̩jo̩ oñ i nyʼi; e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩ oñ i nyi ma.
Tak O̩jo̩ de̩nyo̩ ñw uma, O̩jo̩ la ka ñw uma kakini, Ame̩ ki bi o̩ma, ku me̩ ki wewe nyo̩gba ku me̩ che̩ko̩ ane̩-ile̩-i ku me̩ fʼu dolo te̩; ame̩ ki la nʼo̩da ame̩ja ef ohimini kpai ame̩we̩ ojale kpai ame̩wñ iñmi du ki achiche̩ ane̩-ile̩-i.
Tak O̩jo̩ kakini, Go, omi mʼeñmi kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ du ki aro ulu-wñ ko ñw ume̩, e-du ki bʼane̩-ile̩ ma, kpai oli du kʼe̩ro-wñ nʼe̩yo̩ efu; e-le̩ achʼuje̩wñ ñw ame̩.
Kpai ame̩wñ iñmi ane̩-ile̩ okoke du, kpai ame̩we̩ ojale okoke du, kpai ame̩wñ du ki afa ane̩-ile̩-i; e-du kʼonugo e-iñmi dʼef uwñ, e̩wñ eñmi emimi kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ du chʼutodu uje̩wñ. Abe̩le̩ i la de̩.
O̩jo̩ la fʼe̩wñ du kʼi che li, me̩ la go, i nyo̩ tabale. Oñ ane̩ do̩mo̩, odudu la do̩mo̩, o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩fa.
Abe̩le̩ efojale kpai ane̩-ile̩ fʼoji ne̩ kpa, kpai uwewe ame̩wñ-ma du.
Oñ o̩jo̩ ekebie̩-wñ uko̩lo̩ kʼO̩jo̩ che le̩ takpa, tak o̩jo̩ ekebie le̩ i ñmi uko̩lo̩-wñ du kʼi che.
Tak O̩jo̩ de̩nyo̩ ñw o̩jo̩ ekebie le̩ i la chʼo kʼi fo̩, todabu ki chʼo̩jo̩ kʼi ñmi uko̩lo̩-wñ du e-kʼO̩jo̩ nyi kpai e-kʼi che.
Ade̩m kpai If ef uche̩ Ide̩n
Inabali efojale kpai ane̩-ile̩-i e̩gba ku ma nyi ma, o̩jo̩ ki Jihofa O̩jo̩ che ane̩-ile̩ kpai efojale le̩ de̩.
E̩gbale̩ e̩wñ emimi oko du dʼane̩-ile̩-i ta n, e̩wñ eñmi kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ oko du la tiga ta n— todabu ki Jihofa O̩jo̩ ma che kʼomi ki lo̩ bʼane̩-ile̩ ma ta n, e̩ne̩ du la do̩mo̩ kʼi aluche̩ ane̩ n;
chai eli chi kwane̩ ane̩-ile̩ oñ i chi omi bʼeju ane̩ du ma—
taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ nʼebutu fʼone̩ bo̩, oñ i ñmiñmi afu e-iñmi nyʼiñmo̩-wñ; oñ one̩ mud onugo one̩ kʼi nʼiñmi.
Taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ fʼe̩wñ gbe̩ ef uche̩ Ide̩n, o̩wo̩ olodudu-wñ; o̩mo̩ i la du one̩ kʼi bo̩ le̩ te̩.
Jihofa O̩jo̩ la che kʼoli du ki fe̩rʼeju kpai e-ki nyo̩ todu uje̩wñ kʼi tiga kwef ane̩, kpai oli e-iñmi alumeji uche̩ le̩ ge̩, kpai oli uma-e̩wñ-e̩nyo̩-kpai-e̩bie̩ne̩.
Ohiminiʼka la cha kwef Ide̩n ki chʼomi rʼuche̩ le̩, akwʼo̩mo̩ i la mukpe̩ akanaba me̩le̩.
Odu e-ejodudu ko̩ Piso̩n: owñ chʼe-ki le ane̩ Hafila du ugbo kʼo̩jamalia de̩ le̩ daka;
o̩jamalia ane̩ le̩ la chenyo̩: o̩mo̩ okuta de̩lium kpai o̩niks de̩.
Odu ohimini ekeji la ko̩ Giho̩n: e-le̩ chʼe-ki ale ane̩ Kush du daka.
Odu ohimini e̩ke̩ta la ko̩ Hide̩ke̩l: e-le̩ chʼe-kʼi a cha lʼo̩wo̩ olodudu Asiria le̩. Oñ ohimini e̩ke̩le̩ che Yufretis.
Oñ Jihofa O̩jo̩ mʼone̩ du, oñ i mʼu du tef uche̩ Ide̩n kʼi lʼo, kʼi la nade.
Taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ tuko̩ ñw one̩ kakini, E̩ro oli du ef uche̩-i e̩je̩ oñ e̩ je̩ hiaa:
ama e̩ro oli uma-e̩wñ-e̩nyo̩-kpai-e̩bie̩ne̩, uwe̩ ki je̩ e-le̩ n: todu o̩jo̩ kʼe̩ jʼe-le̩ eku oñ e̩ ku.
Taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ kakini, I nyo̩ kʼone̩ kate kʼi do̩mo̩ abe̩le̩ n; omi ache e̩ne̩ ki abʼo̩ che kʼi chʼoje̩go̩-wñ.
Jihofa O̩jo̩ la nʼike̩te̩ bo̩ ame̩wñ iñmi oko okoke du, kpai ame̩we̩ ojale okoke du; tak i mʼu ko wʼugbo one̩ kʼi go alu kʼi adʼodu ñw uma: oñ e̩wñ du kʼone̩ dʼodu onugo e̩wñ iñmi le̩ okoke du ko̩, mak e-le̩ chʼodu-wñ.
Oñ one̩ mʼodu du ñw ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ du, kpai ame̩we̩ ojale, kpai ame̩wñ iñmi oko okoke du; ma muda li e̩ne̩ kʼi chʼoje̩go̩ one̩ kʼi abʼo̩ che n.
Taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ je̩ ñw olu lile mʼone̩ du, oñ abu kʼi alolu i mʼikeli-wñ oka du, oñ i mʼo̩re̩la du dabi boma koji:
tak ikeli ki Jihofa O̩jo̩ du kwef one̩ i mudu che onobule̩, oñ i mʼowñ du wʼugbo one̩.
Tak one̩ kakini,
Ihii, fai tak e-kide̩ chʼachiku ki kwef achiku e-mi kpai o̩re̩la ki kwef o̩re̩la-mi;
ma adʼodu-wñ ko̩ Onobule̩,
todabu ku ma mʼu du kwef One̩.
Todule̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ atʼata-wñ kpai iye-wñ no̩ kʼi la amanyʼo̩ya-wñ, oñ ama amud o̩re̩la okate.
Ama meji la tago ofo, owñ chʼone̩ kpai o̩ya-wñ, ma la chanyo̩ n.
One̩ muñwa nane̩
Ejo le̩ la gbeju tʼame̩wñ iñmi oko du ki Jihofa O̩jo̩ che le. Oñ i ka ñw onobule̩ le̩ kakini, Ochochi, O̩jo̩ ka kʼame̩ ki jʼe̩ro oli du ef uche̩-i n?
Tak onobule̩ le̩ ka ñw ejo kakini, E̩ro oli uche̩-i a aje̩;
ama e̩ro oli e-kʼi dʼalumeji uche̩-i, O̩jo̩ kakini, Me̩ ki je̩ e-le̩ n, me̩ ki la do̩wo̩kadʼo n, tode̩gba ku me̩ aku.
Ama ejo le̩ ka ñw onobule̩ kakini, I chʼeku me̩ aku n.
Todu O̩jo̩ chema ka kʼo̩jo̩ ku me̩ je̩ e-le̩ e̩gbale̩ tak eju-me̩ ane̩, taku me̩ adab O̩jo̩, me̩ ama e̩nyo̩ kpai e̩bie̩ne̩.
Tak onobule̩ le̩ li ka kʼoli le̩ chenyo̩ todu uje̩wñ, kʼi laño̩ chʼuto̩ eju, kʼoli le̩ laño̩ chʼe̩wñ ki nyo̩ one̩ eju kʼi aje̩ ñw u nʼibe, i mʼe̩ro-wñ ka i la mudu je̩; i ño̩ mudu ñw o̩ko̩-wñ kpai owñ, i laño̩ je̩ ge̩.
Tak eju-ma meji mune̩, oñ ma ma ka ku ma tago ofo; taku ma fʼeñmi o̩gbaikolo ga mʼomune̩ oñ ma mʼu ko che e̩wñ ulago ñw o̩la-ma.
Taku ma gbo̩ abu ku Jihofa O̩jo̩ alule̩ ef uche̩ le̩ adiko e̩gba kʼafu afe̩rʼo̩la, tak one̩ kpai o̩ya-wñ mʼo̩la-ma ko maja bʼeju Jihofa O̩jo̩ te̩ ef ujʼoli uche̩ le̩.
Taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ nomudala do̩ one̩, i la ka ñw u kakini, Ugbo e̩ de̩?
Oñ i kakini, U gbʼiche̩-we̩ ef uche̩, oñ u railo, todabu kʼu tago ofo; tak u dʼo̩lami maja-i.
Tak i kakini, E̩ne̩ ka ñw e̩ ka kʼe̩ tago ofo? Uwe̩ je̩ e̩ro oli e-kʼomi tuko̩ ñw e̩ ka kʼe̩ we eje̩ le̩?
Tak one̩ kakini, Onobule̩ kʼe̩ duwa kʼi dʼugbo mi, owñ mʼe̩ro oli le̩ du ñw mi, oñ u mʼu du je̩.
Taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ ka ñw onobule̩ le̩ kakini, E̩wñ chʼe-kʼuwe̩ che-i? Tak onobule̩ le̩ kakini, Ejo le̩ gba mi ibe, tak u je̩.
Taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ ka ñw ejo kakini,
Todabu kʼuwe̩ che-i,
uwe̩ oñ ama amu tʼame̩wño̩re̩,
kpai ame̩la oko du le;
efu-we̩ oñ e̩ ne̩ alule̩,
ebutu e̩ ñʼaje̩
o̩jo̩ du kʼudeju-we̩ kade.
Nanyi o̩la tʼagbagba uwe̩ kpai onobule̩,
kpai agbagba ugbe̩-we̩ kpai ugbe̩-wñ;
i afʼuwe̩ oji gwenunu,
oñ uwe̩ afʼowñ agbe̩re̩ gwenunu.
Tak i ka ñw onobule̩ kakini,
Naje̩ ñw e̩do̩ e̩kpabie̩-we̩ ki nana nyo̩gba ololo kpai efu-we̩ kʼe̩ nyo̩;
o̩ma ebi-we̩ achʼe̩do̩dudu ñw e̩,
uwe̩ añeju o̩ko̩-we̩ kpo̩o̩,
owñ la anʼo̩da uwe̩.
Tak i ka ñw one̩ kakini,
Todabu kʼe̩ gba omu o̩ya-we̩ gbo̩,
kʼe̩ la mʼe̩ro oli
kʼomi tuko̩ ñw e̩ kakini,
E̩ ki je̩ n dʼu je̩ le̩,
ama fʼane̩pe̩te̩ mu tod uwe̩ me̩;
uwe̩ aje̩ e̩wñ kwefu-wñ kpai e̩do̩dudu o̩jo̩ du kʼudeju-we̩ kade;
ikeke kpai edudu egbe oñ i adufu ñw e̩ ge̩;
uwe̩ la aje̩ eñmi oko kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩.
Ugu atʼe̩ oji tak e̩ jʼuje̩wñ
gbogbo tak e̩ dabi tef ane̩,
todu efu-wñ oñ ma dʼuwe̩ kwo;
ebutu uwe̩ che,
e̩ ñʼadabi tef ebutu ge̩.
One̩ la dʼodu o̩ya-wñ ko̩ If todabu kʼowñ chʼugugu iye ñw e̩wñ du ki deju.
Taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ fʼafe̩ año̩ che tod one̩ kpai o̩ya-wñ, oñ i mʼu du tʼo̩la-ma.
Taku Jihofa O̩jo̩ kakini, Go, one̩ dab awa me̩, i chema e̩nyo̩ kpai e̩bie̩ne̩; fai, tode̩gba kʼi anʼo̩wo̩-wñ dala kʼi laño̩ mʼe̩ro oli e-iñmi ka, kʼi je̩, kʼi la adeju ogbegbele̩—
todule̩ Jihofa O̩jo̩ mʼowñ du kwef uche̩ Ide̩n dufu, kʼi naluche̩ ane̩ e-ku ma dʼowñ kwefu-wñ le̩.
Abe̩le̩ i fʼone̩ le̩ ne dufu; tak i kʼamiche̩rub, kpai o̩go̩ una kʼi dab o̩kwo̩chageli kʼi arida okokolo gugu o̩wo̩ olodudu uche̩ Ide̩n, ku ma de o̩na oli e-iñmi le̩.
Ken kpai Ebe̩l
Oñ one̩ fʼo̩ya-wñ If ma, oñ i fʼefu nyo̩ i la fu Ken bi, i kakini, U fʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ne̩ lʼugbo Jihofa me̩.
Tak i ño̩ bi o̩maye-wñ Ebe̩l ge̩. Ebe̩l la chʼadejute̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ egini, Ken muda chʼaluche̩.
Gbogbo taku Ken mʼe̩ro uche̩ ko wa kʼi du che Jihofa ele,
Ebe̩l ge̩, i ño̩ chi kwef amo̩mojo̩do̩ ame̩wño̩re̩-wñ egini wa, e-ki yoyo efu-ma. Jihofa la go Ebe̩l kpai e̩wñ ele kʼi kowa,
i muda go Ken kpai e̩wñ ele kʼi kowa le̩ n. Taku Ken we̩do̩ nana, eju-wñ la kpa.
Taki Jihofa ka ñwu Ken kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ we̩do̩, e̩wñ chi kʼeju-we̩ la chʼe̩kpa-i?
Iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ ache e̩nyo̩, eju-we̩ achʼeju anyi n? Iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ ma che e̩nyo̩ n, mak adure adade alugbo̩na le̩; i añeju we̩, uwe̩ ki muda nʼo̩da-wñ.
Taki Ken ko̩la ñw Ebe̩l o̩maye-wñ, oñ abu ku ma jʼoko, Ken kwane̩ tʼEbe̩l o̩maye-wñ o̩la, oñ i mʼu du kpa.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Ken kakini, Ugbo Ebe̩l o̩maye-we̩ de̩? Oñ i kakini, U ma no; omi chʼadejute̩ o̩maye-mi?
Tak i kakini, E̩wñ uwe̩ che-i? Omuko̩la e̩bie̩ o̩maye-we̩ dʼef ane̩ akwa do̩ mi.
Fai ama la fʼe̩ mu kwef ane̩, e-ki mʼalu-wñ chi te̩ kʼi gba e̩bie̩ o̩maye-we̩ kwef o̩wo̩-we̩ le̩.
E̩gba kʼe̩ luche̩ ane̩-i, akwe̩gba-i i ñʼadʼukpahiu-wñ ñw e̩ ge̩ n; e̩nara kpai e̩nujulu oñ uwe̩ ache ane̩-ile̩-i.
Taki Ken ka ñwu Jihofa kakini, Udu kʼe̩ bu mi-i i nana tʼumi le.
Go, e̩ fʼumi ne bʼeju ane̩ te̩ eñini-i me̩; u la ñʼamaja bʼeju-we̩ te̩ ge̩; tak u nachʼe̩nara kpai e̩nujulu ane̩-ile̩, i dʼabe̩le̩ mak e̩ne̩ du kʼi li mi adʼumi kpa.
Taku Jihofa ka ñw u kakini, I chʼabe̩le̩ n! E̩ne̩ du kʼi du Ken kpa, ma akpʼo̩chi-wñ onu mebie. Taki Jihofa mʼujiwe du gamu Ken o̩la, tode̩gba kʼe̩ne̩ kʼi liʼu adʼu kpa.
Taki Ken kwo bʼeju Jihofa te̩, oñ i kwo gugu ane̩ No̩d, o̩wo̩ olodudu Ide̩n.
Taki Ken fʼo̩ya-wñ ma, oñ i fʼefu nyo̩ i la fʼIno̩k bi; tak i le teke fʼodoʼka do, i la mʼodu ewo le̩ du rodu o̩ma-wñ, Ino̩k.
Ma la bi Irad ñw Ino̩k; Irad la bi Me̩hujae̩l, Me̩hujae̩l la bi Me̩tushae̩l, Me̩tushae̩l la bi Lame̩k.
Taki Lame̩k fʼo̩ya meji ne̩ ñw o̩la-wñ; odu oka ko̩ Ada, oñ odu ekeji-wñ ko̩ Zila.
Ada la bi Jabal; owñ chʼata abo ku ma gugu ef unyabo ku ma ne̩ ame̩wñ-ukpa.
Odu o̩maye-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ko̩ Jubal; owñ la chʼata abo du ku ma nʼumolo kpai o̩kpachine̩.
Taki Zila, onobule̩ le̩, bi Tubal-ken, owñ chʼe̩ne̩ kʼi anʼebijeikpa kpai ebije gwu e̩wñ eku ojoji du. O̩maye Tubal-ken onobule̩ che Naama.
Oñ Lame̩k ka ñw amo̩ya-wñ kakini:
Ada kpai Zila, me̩ nagbʼomu-mi;
ame̩ ku me̩ chʼamo̩ya Lame̩k, me̩ nanetirʼuko̩la-mi;
todu omi fʼone̩ kpa tod agbe kʼi che mi,
okolobiaʼka tod egwenunu kʼi fʼumi gwe̩nunu.
Iche̩wñ ku ma akpʼo̩chi Ken onu mebie,
mak e-Lame̩k achʼe̩te̩gwa nyoke mebie.
Ade̩m ño̩ fʼo̩ya-wñ ma ge̩, oñ i fʼo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi i la dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Se̩t, todu O̩jo̩ mʼugbe̩ omune̩ dute̩ ñwu mi koji Ebe̩l me̩, todu Ken fʼowñ kpa.
Se̩t ge̩, ma ño̩ fʼo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi ñw u, tak i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Ino̩sh. E̩gbale̩ tak amone̩ chane̩ e̩do̩ odu Jihofa.
Akwo Ade̩m wa Noa
O̩takada o̩lo̩pu Ade̩m o̩gba o̩gba de̩. Iko o̩jo̩ kʼO̩jo̩ nyi one̩ i chʼo kʼi biu O̩jo̩.
O̩ko̩ kpai o̩ya oñ i nyi ma, i laño̩ de̩nyo̩ ñwu ma oñ i dʼodu-ma ko̩ Ade̩m o̩jo̩ kʼi nyi ma.
Ade̩m la dʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩fa nyoke me̩gwa, tak i bi o̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ki chebiu owñ onugo, dab ojibo-wñ, i la dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Se̩t.
Oñ o̩jo̩ Ade̩m abu kʼi fu Se̩t bi ño̩ jo̩ o̩do̩ icham; i ño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
O̩jo̩ kʼAde̩m deju chaka du la chʼo̩do̩ icham nyʼo̩gbo̩ me̩fa nyoke me̩gwa; tak i leku.
Se̩t la dʼo̩do̩ ogume̩lu nyoke me̩lu, tak i bi Ino̩sh.
Abu kʼi fʼIno̩sh bi Se̩t ño̩ deju o̩do̩ icham nyoke mebie, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ Se̩t chaka du la chʼo̩do̩ icham nyʼogume̩lu nyoke me̩gweji; tak i leku.
Oñ Ino̩sh deju o̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩le̩ nyoke me̩gwa, tak i bi Kenan.
Abu kʼi fu Kenan bi Ino̩sh ño̩ deju o̩do̩ icham nyoke me̩gwe̩lu, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ Ino̩sh chaka du la chʼo̩do̩ icham nyʼogume̩lu nyoke me̩lu; tak i leku.
Oñ Kenan deju o̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩ta nyoke me̩gwa, tak i bi Mahalale̩l.
Abu kʼi fu Mahalale̩l bi Kenan ño̩ deju o̩do̩ icham nyʼo̩gbo̩ meji, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ Kenan chaka du la chʼo̩do̩ icham nyʼogume̩lu nyoke me̩gwa; tak i leku.
Oñ Mahalale̩l deju o̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩ta nyoke me̩lu, tak i bi Jare̩d.
Abu kʼi fu Jare̩d bi Mahalale̩l ño̩ deju o̩do̩ icham nyʼogue̩gwa, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ Mahalale̩l chaka du la chʼo̩do̩ icham nyʼo̩gbo̩ me̩le̩ nyoke me̩gwe̩lu; tak i leku.
Oñ Jare̩d deju o̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩jo̩ nyoke meji tak i bi Ino̩k.
Abu kʼi fu Ino̩k bi Jare̩d ño̩ deju o̩do̩ icham, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ Jare̩d chaka du la chʼo̩do̩ icham nyʼo̩gbo̩ me̩jo̩ nyoke meji; tak i leku.
Oñ Ino̩k deju o̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩ta nyoke me̩lu, tak i bi Matusala.
Abu kʼi fu Matusala bi Ino̩k tale kpai O̩jo̩ o̩do̩ oli me̩fa, i ño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ Ino̩k chaka du la che o̩do̩ oli mebie nyoke me̩gwe̩lu.
Ino̩k la tale kpai O̩jo̩; tak i ma ño̩ do̩mo̩ ge̩ n, todu O̩jo̩ mʼowñ du.
Oñ Matusala deju o̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩la nyoke mebie, tak i bi Lame̩k.
Abu kʼi fu Lame̩k bi Matusala ño̩ deju o̩do̩ ulo̩gwa nyʼo̩gbo̩ me̩la nyoke meji, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ Matusala chaka du la chʼo̩do̩ icham nyʼo̩gbo̩ me̩jo̩ nyoke me̩la; tak i leku.
Oñ Lame̩k deju o̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩la nyoke meji, tak i fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi,
oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Noa, i kakini, Owñ kide̩ anyʼuwa e̩do̩ ugbo uko̩lo̩-wa kpai ugbo akanya kʼa anʼo̩wo̩-wa che, todu ane̩ e-ki Jihofa nama ñw u.
Abu kʼi fu Noa bi Lame̩k ño̩ deju o̩do̩ oke me̩lu chi ulo̩gwa, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ Lame̩k chaka du la chʼo̩do̩ ulo̩gwa nyʼo̩gbo̩ me̩jo̩ nyoke me̩gwebie; tak i leku.
Oñ o̩do̩ Noa chʼoli me̩gwa: Noa la fu She̩m, kpai Ham, kpai Jefe̩t bi.
Inabali uwobi omi le̩
Abe̩le̩ e̩gba kʼamone̩ chane̩ ewewe bʼile̩-i ma, ku ma la bi amo̩ma onobule̩ ñwu ma,
amo̩ma O̩jo̩ fʼamo̩ma onobule̩ amone̩ li ku ma chefe̩rʼeju; taku ma fʼuma tu chaka oñ ma nʼo̩ya kwef abo e-le̩ ñw o̩la-ma.
Taku Jihofa kakini, Afu-mi achakanya nyʼone̩ gbogbo alo ef ila-ma ge̩ n, todabu kʼowñ chʼo̩re̩la, o̩jo̩-wñ achʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩fa ta.
Amakachi jʼane̩-ile̩ adiko le̩, kpai anubi-wñ ge̩, e̩gba kʼamo̩ma O̩jo̩ wʼejefu ugbo amo̩ma onobule̩ amone̩, ku ma bi amo̩ma ñwu ma. Abo kide̩ chʼamagbiti ku ma do̩mo̩ igbelegbele, ama chʼame̩nuwohi le̩.
Oñ Jihofa li kʼe̩bie̩ne̩ one̩ chʼololo ane̩-ile̩, kʼibe du ki dʼe̩do̩-wñ kʼi añwa chʼe̩bie̩ne̩ gbogbo dʼo̩jo̩.
Tak e̩do̩ Jihofa murida ugbo one̩ kʼi che ane̩-ile̩, i la kpʼowñ e̩do̩ bie̩.
Taki Jihofa kakini, Nakpʼone̩ kʼu nyi le̩ lu bʼeju ane̩ te̩, tʼone̩, tʼe̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩, tʼame̩wñ ki afa, tʼame̩we̩ ojale, todu e̩do̩-mi murida eche ma kʼu che ma le̩.
Jihofa muda li Noa eju.
Abo-i chʼo̩lo̩pu o̩gba o̩gba Noa. Noa chʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ o̩kpakpa, i mufu ef abo o̩gba-wñ; Noa tale kpai O̩jo̩.
Noa fʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ me̩ta bi, She̩m, kpai Ham, kpai Jefe̩t.
Ane̩-ile̩-i la mubie̩ te̩ eju O̩jo̩, oñ o̩lachi che̩ko̩ ane̩-ile̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ fʼane̩-ile̩-i go, go, i la mubie̩ te̩: todu o̩re̩la du fʼo̩na-wñ bie̩ ane̩-ile̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ ka ñwu Noa kakini, Eda o̩re̩la du lewa o̩gba-mi me̩; todu ane̩-ile̩ che̩ko̩ ñw o̩lachi lugbo ma; go, omi akpʼama bie̩ manyu ane̩-ile̩.
Uwe̩ ki nʼoli go̩fe̩r chʼo̩ko̩; e̩ fʼefu o̩ko̩ le̩ ko̩da unyi unyi, kʼe̩ dʼo̩bia kwo̩ ejefu-wñ kpai e̩j o̩do̩da-wñ.
Alu kʼuwe̩ ache de̩: ujiji o̩ko̩ le̩ ki chʼohiba oli me̩fa, unula-wñ ki chʼohiba ooje, o̩gba-wñ ki chʼohiba ogue̩gwa.
E̩ ki che ope̩ o̩ko̩ le̩, ki bo̩ ohibaʼka ate̩-wñ; e̩ fʼalugbo̩na o̩ko̩ che akolo-wñ o̩wo̩ʼka; uwe̩ ki che kʼi ne̩ unyi o̩gane̩, kʼi nʼekeji ate̩-wñ, e̩ke̩ta ki la de̩ otitala-wñ ate̩.
Tak omi, e̩ go, nadʼuwobi omi wa bʼane̩-ile̩ ma kʼu kpa o̩re̩la du kʼafu iñmi dʼefu-wñ bie̩ bʼo̩gane̩ efojale te̩; e̩wñ du ki jʼane̩-ile̩ aku.
Omi muda akpʼalo-mi kpai uwe̩; uwe̩ la awʼef o̩ko̩ le̩, uwe̩, kpai amo̩ma-we̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, kpai o̩ya-we̩, kpai amo̩ya amo̩ma-we̩ manyu uwe̩.
E̩wñ o̩re̩la du ki nʼiñmi, e̩ ki mʼuche̩uche̩-ma eji eji ko wʼef o̩ko̩, ku ma ki deju kpai uwe̩; ama ki chʼo̩ko̩ kpai ole.
Uche̩uche̩ e-ame̩we̩, kpai uche̩uche̩ ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩, kpai uche̩uche̩ e̩wñ ki afa ane̩ okoke du uche̩uche̩-wñ, e̩wñ ojoji ojoji du awʼugbo we̩ eji eji, ku ma deju.
Uje̩wñ du ku ma aje̩, e̩ naya jo̩ ugbo we̩; e-le̩ achʼuje̩wñ uwe̩ kpai ama.
Noa fʼabe̩le̩ che; alu du kʼO̩jo̩ ñwa ñw u, abe̩le̩ i la che.
Omi wobi te̩
Taki Jihofa ka ñwu Noa kakini, Uwe̩ kpai abo unyi-we̩ du ki nyʼef o̩ko̩, todu uwe̩ oñ omi li ka kʼe̩ chʼe̩no̩kpakpa o̩gba-mi ef abo o̩gba kide̩.
E̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ du ki de̩hio̩lo e̩ nako wʼugbo we̩ ebie ebie, o̩ko̩ kpai ole-wñ o̩ko̩ kpai ole-wñ; e-e̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ ku ma ma de̩hio̩lo n ki chʼeji eji, o̩ko̩ kpʼole-wñ;
kpai ame̩we̩ ojale ebie ebie̩ ge̩, o̩ko̩ kpai ole, kʼugbe̩-ma ki deju ane̩-ile̩-i.
Todu i bo̩ o̩jo̩ mebie tak u naje̩ ñw omi lo̩ bʼane̩-ile̩ ma o̩jo̩ o̩gbo̩ meji kpai odu o̩gbo̩ meji; oñ e̩wñ du kʼu che ki deju nakpalu bʼeju ane̩ te̩.
Noa la che alu du ki Jihofa ñwa ñw u.
O̩do̩ Noa la chʼulo̩gwa e̩gba kʼuwobi omi le̩ bʼane̩-ile̩ ma.
Oñ Noa kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai o̩ya-wñ kpai amo̩ya amo̩ma-wñ le tef o̩ko̩ le̩, todu uwobi omi.
Ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ hiolo, kpai ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ ki ma de̩hio̩lo n, kpai ame̩we̩, kpai e̩wñ du ki afa ane̩,
ma le tef o̩ko̩ ugbo Noa eji eji, o̩ko̩ kpai ole, alu kʼO̩jo̩ ñwa ñwu Noa.
Oñ i lewatu ab o̩jo̩ mebie jo̩ uwobi omi la bʼane̩-ile̩ ma.
Ef o̩do̩ udeju Noa e-ulo̩gwa le̩, ochu ekeji, o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩gwebie ochu le̩, o̩jo̩ le̩ gbage̩de̩ e̩bi omi o̩lulu mukpo̩fo̩, ope ojale la muchite̩.
Oñ omi ojale gulo̩ bʼane̩-ile̩ ma o̩jo̩ o̩gbo̩ meji kpai odu o̩gbo̩ meji.
O̩jo̩ le̩ gbage̩de̩ oñ Noa kpai She̩m kpai Ham kpai Jefe̩t, amo̩ma Noa le̩, kpai o̩ya Noa kpai amo̩ya amo̩ma-wñ me̩ta kpai ama, le̩ tef o̩ko̩,
ama kpai uche̩uche̩ ame̩-wñ iñmi okoke du, kpai ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ du uche̩uche̩-ma, kpai e̩wñ du ki afa, owñ chʼe-ki afa ane̩-ile̩-i uche̩uche̩-ma, kpai uche̩uche̩ ame̩we̩ du, e̩we̩ ojoji ojoji okoke du.
Oñ ma le tef o̩ko̩ ugbo Noa, owñ chʼejʼeji o̩re̩la du e-kʼafu iñmi dʼefu-ma.
Oñ abo ku ma tʼo̩, chʼo̩ko̩ kpai ole kwef o̩re̩la du alu kʼO̩jo̩ ñwa ñw u; taku Jihofa fʼo̩na re nyʼu.
Uwobi omi le̩ bʼane̩-ile̩ ma o̩jo̩ o̩gbo̩ meji; omi-wñ la nana nyo̩gba, oñ i dʼo̩ko̩ kwane̩, oñ i kwane̩ tʼate̩ ñw ane̩-ile̩.
Tak omi le̩ fʼukpahiu che i la nana nyo̩gba ololo bʼane̩-ile̩ ma; oñ o̩ko̩ le̩ nʼeju omi.
Omi le̩ laño̩ fʼukpahiu che ololo bʼane̩-ile̩ ma; tak omi lʼuwo du ki gbo̩gba ki dʼo̩gane̩ efojale chaka oji;
omi le̩ chʼukpahiu nyate̩ ohiba me̩gwe̩lu; oñ i lʼuwo du oji.
Tak ore̩la du ki achiche̩ ane̩-ile̩-i mʼiñmi da, tʼame̩we̩, tʼame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩, tʼame̩wñ iñmi oko, tʼe̩wñ du ki afa e-ki afa ane̩-ile̩-i, kpai one̩ okoke du;
e-du kʼafu iñmi dʼef iñmo̩-wñ, e-du ki de̩ ane̩ e̩gbe̩ leku.
Oñ i fʼe̩wñ du ki deju ane̩ kpalu, tʼone̩, tʼame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩, tʼame̩wñ ki afa, tʼame̩we̩ ojale; ma la fʼu kpalu bʼane̩-ile̩ te̩. Oñ i bo̩ Noa kate kpai abo ku ma jʼugbo-wñ ef o̩ko̩ le̩.
Oñ omi le̩ fʼukpahiu che bʼane̩-ile̩-i ma o̩jo̩ oli me̩ta.
Omi wobi te̩
Ibe O̩jo̩ la chʼekado Noa kpai ame̩wñ iñmi oko du kpai ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ du ku ma jʼef o̩ko̩ le̩ ugbo-wñ. Tak O̩jo̩ je̩ ñw afu ju bʼane̩-ile̩ ma, oñ omi le̩ chane̩ edu;
e̩bi omi o̩lulu le̩ kpai ope efojale ño̩ re ge̩, oñ ma fʼomi ojale ba;
tak omi mudabi bʼane̩-ile̩ te̩ alo waa. Ab o̩jo̩ oli me̩ta jo̩ omi le̩ ño̩ adabu waa;
oñ o̩ko̩ le̩ kwotane̩ oj uwo Ararat ochu ekebie, o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩gwebie ochu le̩.
Oñ omi le̩ dabu alo waa gbogbo wʼochu e̩ke̩gwa; ochu e̩ke̩gwa, o̩jo̩ ejodudu ochu le̩, ma li oj uwo oj uwo.
Oñ i lewatu ab o̩jo̩ o̩gbo̩ meji jo̩ Noa mʼope o̩ko̩ kʼi che le̩ bi,
tak i je̩ ñw o̩tagalama le dufu; oñ e-le̩ te̩ alelo lewa gbogbo tak omi gbe̩ bʼane̩-ile̩ te̩.
Oñ i je̩ ñw ikede kwʼugbo-wñ dufu tʼo̩do̩da, kʼi go abe̩k omi du bʼeju ane̩ te̩ abe̩k i du n;
ikede le̩ la lʼuña ki adu e̩re̩-wñ tane̩ n, tak i mudabi tʼugbo-wñ ef o̩ko̩, todu omi le̩ bʼeju o̩gbo̩ ane̩-ile̩ du ma ta. Tak i nʼo̩wo̩-wñ dala dufu oñ i mʼu du oñ i mʼowñ du wʼejefu ugbo-wñ ef o̩ko̩.
Oñ i ño̩ je̩ o̩jo̩ mebie omune̩, tak i dabi je̩ ñw ikede le̩ kwef o̩ko̩ dufu;
e̩gba ane̩ ikede le̩ la mudabi wʼejefu ugbo-wñ, me̩ la go, eñmi oli o̩lif kʼi chi jʼalu-wñ; abe̩le̩ Noa ma ka kʼomi du bʼane̩-ile̩ te̩ me̩.
Oñ i ño̩ je̩ o̩jo̩ mebie omune̩ ge̩, tak i je̩ ñw ikede le̩ le dufu; i laño̩ dabi wʼugbo-wñ ge̩ n.
Oñ i lewatu o̩do̩ ulo̩gwa nyokeʼka, ochu ejodudu, o̩jo̩ ejodudu ochu le̩, omi le̩ gbe̩ bʼane̩-ile̩ te̩; taki Noa mʼoji o̩ko̩ chi, oñ i go, me̩ la go, eju ane̩-ile̩ gbe̩ te̩.
Oñ ef ochu ekeji, o̩jo̩ ogu nyoke mebie ochu le̩, ane̩-ile̩ che̩ gbe̩ te̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ ka ñwu Noa kakini,
Kwef o̩ko̩ dufu, uwe̩ kpai o̩ya-we̩, kpai amo̩ma-we̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai amo̩ya amo̩ma-we̩ manyʼuwe̩.
Ame̩wñ iñmi du kʼi chʼo̩re̩la ki dʼugbo-we̩ tʼame̩we̩, tʼame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩, tʼame̩wñ ki afa e-ki afa ane̩-ile̩-i e̩ nako dufu kpai uwe̩, ku ma ki rabi ane̩-ile̩, ku ma la bi o̩ma, ku ma ño̩ wewe nyo̩gba ane̩-ile̩.
Taki Noa ledufu, kpai amo̩ma-wñ kpai o̩ya-wñ kpai amo̩ya amo̩ma-wñ manyʼowñ.
Ame̩wñ iñmi okoke du, e̩wñ ki afa okoke du, kpai e̩we̩ okoke du, e̩wñ du ki achiche̩ ane̩-ile̩, kwʼef o̩ko̩ dufu uche̩uche̩.
Taki Noa fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ne ñwu Jihofa, oñ i chi kwef ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ ki de̩hiolo okoke du kpai kwef ame̩we̩ hiolo okoke du, tak i mʼu ko wa chʼiche̩bo̩ e̩gujo oj ubo̩ le̩.
Jihofa la gbo̩ ekpo kʼi akpo, taki Jihofa ka ef e̩do̩-wñ kakini, U ñʼanama ñw ane̩ todu one̩ ge̩ n, todabu kʼaye e̩do̩ one̩ chʼe̩bie̩ne̩ kwo o̩jo̩ imo̩to̩-wñ; u ñʼadabi kpa ame̩wñ iñmi du alu kʼu che-i ge̩ n.
Gbogbo wʼiko kʼane̩-ile̩ kade, adiko e̩yo̩ e̩wñ egbe̩ kpai adiko e̩wñ eja wʼunyi, kpai afu kpai olu, kpai o̩lo̩ji kpai uwo, kpai o̩ro̩ka kpai odu, ñʼada ge̩ n.
O̩jo̩ kpʼalo kpai Noa
Tak O̩jo̩ de̩nyo̩ ñwu Noa kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ ki bi o̩ma ku me̩ wewe nyo̩gba, ku me̩ ko̩ ile̩-i.
E̩gahi-me̩ kpai ailo-me̩ amʼame̩wñ iñmi okoke du ile̩-i, kpai e̩we̩ ojale okoke, ama kpai e̩wñ du ki afa ane̩ kpai ame̩ja ef ohimini abadi du; ma mʼuma ko jʼef o̩wo̩-me̩.
E̩wñ du ki achiche̩ ki añmiñmi achʼuje̩wñ todu me̩; dabalu kʼe̩wñ oko emimi de̩, abe̩le̩ omi mʼo̩chaka e̩wñ du ko ñwu me̩ me̩.
Me̩ ki muda je̩ o̩re̩la manyu onugo iñmi-wñ n, owñ chʼe̩bie̩-wñ.
E̩bie̩-me̩ e-onugo iñmi-me̩ omi atene chuu; o̩wo̩ e̩la du natene owñ kpai o̩wo̩ one̩; ugbo o̩wo̩ o̩maye one̩ pitii natene onugo iñmi one̩.
E̩ne̩ du kʼi adʼe̩bie̩ one̩ dafo, lugbo one̩ ma adʼe̩bie̩ e̩ne̩ le̩ dafo; todu O̩jo̩ che one̩ ojibo owñ.
Ame̩, me̩ nabi o̩ma ku me̩ wewe nyo̩gba, me̩ ki fo̩ji ile̩-i ku me̩ wewe nyo̩gba efu-wñ.
Tak O̩jo̩ ko̩la ñwu Noa kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai owñ, i kakini,
Me̩ go, omi akpʼalo-mi kpai ame̩ kpai amugbe̩-me̩ ubi-me̩ ge̩,
kpai onugo e̩wñ du ki deju ki jʼugbo-me̩ le̩, ame̩we̩ kpai ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ kpai ame̩wñ iñmi ile̩-i okoke du manyʼame̩, e-du ki kwef o̩ko̩-i dufu, owñ chʼame̩wñ iñmi ane̩-ile̩-i okoke du.
Nakpʼalo-mi kpai ame̩, uwobi omi ñʼakpʼo̩re̩la du rinyo̩ ge̩ n, uwobi omi lañʼado̩mo̩ ki akpa ane̩-ile̩ bie̩ ge̩ n.
Oñ O̩jo̩ kakini, E-kide̩ chʼujiwe alo kʼu nakpe̩ ki dʼagbagba omi kpai ame̩ onugo kpai ame̩wñ iñmi du ki jʼugbo-me̩ le̩, tod abo o̩gba nʼo̩gba gbogbo alo:
omi adu o̩ba-mi tef akpa, i ado̩mo̩ todu ujiwe alo ekpe̩ agbagba omi kpai ane̩-ile̩.
Oñ i awatu e̩gba kʼu nadu akpa wa bʼoji ane̩-ile̩ ma, ma ali o̩ba ef akpa le̩,
oñ omi adibekado alo-mi kʼu kpe̩ e-ki dʼagbagba omi kpai ame̩ kpai onugo ame̩wñ iñmi du ki chʼo̩re̩la; omi ñʼawobi ki akpa o̩re̩la du bie̩ ge̩ n.
O̩ba le̩ adʼef akpa, tak omi onugo agʼo kʼu nadibekado alo-ekpe̩ e-ogbegbele̩ ki dʼagbagba O̩jo̩ kpai onugo ame̩wñ iñmi du ki chʼo̩re̩la, owñ chʼe-du ki dʼane̩-ile̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ ka ñwu Noa kakini, E-kide̩ chʼujiwe alo kʼomi kpe̩ agbagba omi kpai o̩re̩la du ki jʼane̩-ile̩.
Noa kpai omi achiwebe̩te̩ma le̩
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Noa ku ma kwef o̩ko̩ le̩ dufu la che She̩m, kpai Ham, kpai Jefe̩t. Ham la chʼata Kenan.
Ama me̩ta le̩ chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Noa; kwef ama me̩ta le̩ oñ amone̩ chʼe̩kpatuka bʼo̩gbo̩ ane̩-ile̩ ma chaka-i.
Taku Noa chane̩ eluche̩. I fʼuche̩ achiwebe̩te̩ma lo;
oñ ifʼomi-wñ ñmo̩, i la fʼu mu, oñ ukpo-wñ mutu jʼane̩ ef unyabo-wñ.
Taku Ham, ata Kenan, fʼago ofo ata-wñ li, oñ i mudu ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ meji o̩do̩da.
Taku She̩m kpai Jefe̩t mʼukpo ubo̩lama ko, ma la mʼu ko nʼika-ma meji, oñ ma le ubi ubi amʼu ko bʼago ofo ata-ma ma; ma fʼeju kparʼugbo omu-ne̩, ma ño̩ li ago ofo ata-ma n.
Oñ Noa mʼolu omi achiwebe̩te̩ma le̩ ji tak i ma e̩wñ kʼo̩ma-wñ kekele chʼo,
tak i kakini,
Ama ki fu Kenan mu;
adu amadu oñ i ache ñw amo̩maye-wñ.
I ño̩ kakini,
Jihofa, O̩jo̩ She̩m, ki nʼele;
Kenan ki chʼadu-wñ.
O̩jo̩ ki je̩ ñwu Jefe̩t ki nana,
kʼi gugu ef unyabo She̩m;
Kenan ki chʼadu-wñ.
Abu kʼuwobi omi le̩ le Noa ño̩ dʼo̩do̩ oli mebie.
O̩do̩ Noa du la chʼicham nyʼoli me̩ta; tak i leku.
Amo̩ma Noa
O̩lo̩pu amo̩ma Noa e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ o̩gba o̩gba de̩, She̩m, kpai Ham, kpai Jefe̩t; ma ño̩ fʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi ñwu ma abu kʼuwobi omi le̩ lale.
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Jefe̩t che: Gome̩r, kpai Mago̩g, kpai Madai, kpai Jafan, kpai Tubal, kpai Me̩she̩k, kpai Tiras.
Oñ amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Gome̩r che: Ashkenaz, kpai Rifat, kpai Togarma.
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Jafan la che: Elisha, kpai Tarshish, Kitim, kpai Dodanim.
Kwef abo-i abo o̩lomi kpe̩ jo̩ ojane̩ ojane̩-ma, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ne̩ alu kʼichi-wñ, alu kʼakwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi-ma de̩ ef abo uche̩ichi uche̩ichi-ma.
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Ham la che: Kush, kpai Mizraim, kpai Put, kpai Kenan.
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Kush la che; Seba, kpai Hafila, kpai Sabta, kpai Raama, kpai Sabte̩ka. Amo̩ma Raama la che: Shiba kpai Dedan.
Kush ño̩ bi Nimro̩d; owñ chʼuchane̩ agbiti ane̩-ile̩.
I chʼagbiti o̩de̩ eju Jihofa; todule̩ ma kakini, Dabu Nimro̩d kʼi chʼagbiti o̩de̩ ede̩ eju Jihofa.
Uchane̩ ojane̩-wñ la che Bebe̩l, kpai E̩re̩k, kpai Akad, kpai Kalne̩ ojane̩ Shainar.
I kwʼojane̩ le̩ nyi Asiria, tak i fʼunyi Nine̩fa ko̩, kpai Re̩hobo̩t-ir, kpai Kala,
kpai Re̩se̩n ki dʼagbagba Nine̩fa kpai Kala (e-le̩ chʼewo lile le̩).
Mizraim la bi abo Lud, kpai abo Anam, kpai abo Lehab, kpai abo Naftuh,
kpai abo Patrus, kpai abo Kaslu (ugbo kʼabo Filistia kwo wa le̩), kpai abo Kafto̩r.
Kenan la bi Saido̩n o̩mo̩gba-wñ, kpai He̩t,
kpai e̩ne̩ Je̩bius le̩, kpai e̩ne̩ Amo̩r, kpai e̩ne̩ Girgash,
kpai e̩ne̩ Hifai, kpai e̩ne̩ Arki, kpai e̩ne̩ Saini,
kpai e̩ne̩ Arfad, kpai e̩ne̩ Ze̩mar, kpai e̩ne̩ Hamat. Ubile̩ akwo̩ra unyi, akwo̩ra unyi abo Kenan le̩ kpʼo̩la-ma tuka rʼile̩.
Alo̩me̩ abo Kenan le̩ la kwo Saido̩n, abu kʼe̩ nyʼo̩wo̩ Gerar, gbogbo wa Gaza; abu kʼe̩ nyʼo̩wo̩ So̩do̩m kpai Go̩mo̩ra kpai Adma, kpai Ze̩boim, gbogbo wa Easha.
Abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Ham, akwo̩ra unyi, akwo̩ra unyi-ma, ichi ichi-ma, ojane̩ ojane̩-ma, ef abo uche̩ichi uche̩ichi-ma.
Taku ma ño̩ bi amo̩ma ñwu She̩m kʼi chʼata amo̩ma E̩be̩r chaka; She̩m le̩ chʼacho̩gba Jefe̩t.
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ She̩m che: Elam, kpai Ashur, kpai Arpaksad, kpai Lud, kpai Aram.
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Aram la che: Uz, kpai Hul, kpai Ge̩te̩r, kpai Mash.
Oñ Arpaksad bi Shela; Shela la bi E̩be̩r.
Oñ ma bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ meji ñw E̩be̩r: odu oka ko̩ Pe̩le̩g; todu ef adiko-wñ ma fʼile̩ kpe̩ru; odu o̩maye-wñ la ko̩ Jo̩ktan.
Jo̩ktan la bi Almodad, kpai Shele̩f, kpai Hazar-mafe̩t, kpai Je̩ra,
kpai Hado̩ram, kpai Uzal, kpai Dikla,
kpai Obal, kpai Abimae̩l, kpai Shiba,
kpai Ofir, kpai Hafila kpai Jo̩bab; abo-i chaka chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Jo̩ktan.
Odo-ma la te̩ kwo Me̩sha, abu kʼe̩ nyʼo̩wo̩ Sefar, ane̩ uwo olodudu le̩.
Abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-She̩m, akwo̩ra unyi, akwo̩ra unyi-ma, ichi ichi-ma, ojane̩ ojane̩-ma, abo uche̩ichi uche̩ichi-ma.
Abo-i chʼakwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Noa, o̩gba o̩gba-ma, ef abo uche̩ichi uche̩ichi-ma. Oñ kwef abo-i uche̩ichi uche̩ichi mukpe̩rʼojane̩ ile̩ abu kʼuwobi omi le̩ lale.
O̩do̩go̩ Bebe̩l
Oñ o̩gbo ile̩-i du chʼalu ichi okate uko̩la-ma la chʼoka.
Tak i lewatu abu ku ma mʼunyabo chi kwʼo̩wo̩ olodudu awa, kʼama fʼegbili li ane̩ Shainar taku ma kwojo̩ o̩mo̩.
Taku ma ka ñw o̩la-ma kakini, Me̩ lewa, kʼa nabo̩ otubeli, kʼa fʼu ro̩ nyo̩nyo̩. Taku ma ne̩ otubeli koji okuta, oñ ma ne̩ o̩bia bitume̩n chʼike̩te̩ ene.
Taku ma kakini, Me̩ lewa, kʼa kʼunyi ñw o̩la-wa, kʼa nʼewo, kpai o̩do̩go̩ kʼoji-wñ ki kad efojale, a che kʼa fʼodu ne̩, tode̩gba ku ma fʼuwa kpatuka rʼo̩do̩da bʼeju o̩gbo̩ ane̩-ile̩ du ma.
Taki Jihofa gwo̩ru wa kʼi li ewo kpai o̩do̩go̩, e-kʼamone̩ ne le̩.
Taki Jihofa kakini, Go, ma chʼaboʼka, ichi-ma la chʼoka ge̩; e̩wñ ku ma la chane̩ eche de̩ ta; fai e̩wñ du ku ma ñwa ef e̩do̩-ma ku ma che i nʼugbo ku ma akpo̩na nyʼuma ge̩ n.
Me̩ lewa, kʼa mugwo̩ru nyʼo̩mo kʼa fʼalu ichi-ma gwuji, todu kʼama ki we egbʼoji o̩la omune̩.
Abe̩le̩ Jihofa fʼuma kpatuka kwʼo̩mo̩ rʼo̩do̩da bʼeju ane̩-ile̩ du ma, taku ma tʼewo le̩ no̩ ene.
Todule̩ ma dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Bebe̩l, todabu ki Jihofa fʼichi abile̩ du gwuji o̩mo̩; tak akwo̩mo̩ Jihofa fʼuma kpatuka rʼo̩do̩da bʼeju ane̩-ile̩ du ma.
Akwo She̩m wa Ebraham
O̩lo̩pu She̩m o̩gba o̩gba le̩ de̩. O̩do̩ She̩m chʼogume̩lu tak i bi Arpaksad abu kʼuwobi omi le̩ takpa o̩do̩ meji;
abu kʼi bi Arpaksad She̩m ño̩ deju o̩do̩ oli me̩gwa, oñ i bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Arpaksad deju o̩do̩ ogue̩gwa nyoke me̩lu tak i bi Shela;
abu kʼi fu Shela bi Arpaksad ño̩ dʼo̩do̩ ulo̩ko̩ nyoke me̩ta, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Oñ Shela dʼo̩do̩ ogue̩gwa tak i bi E̩be̩r;
abu kʼi fʼE̩be̩r bi Shela ño̩ dʼo̩do̩ ulo̩ko̩ nyoke me̩ta, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Oñ E̩be̩r dʼo̩do̩ ogue̩gwa nyoke me̩le̩, tak i bi Pe̩le̩g;
abu kʼi fu Pe̩le̩g bi E̩be̩r ño̩ dʼo̩do̩ ulo̩ko̩ nyʼogue̩gwa, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Oñ Pe̩le̩g dʼo̩do̩ ogue̩gwa, tak i bi Reu;
abu kʼi fu Re̩u bi Pe̩le̩g ño̩ dʼo̩do̩ o̩gwo̩ko̩ nyoke me̩la, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Oñ Reu dʼo̩do̩ ogue̩gwa nyoke meji, tak i bi Se̩rug;
abu kʼi fu Se̩rug bi Reu ño̩ dʼo̩do̩ o̩gwo̩ko̩ nyoke mebie, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Oñ Se̩rug dʼo̩do̩ ogue̩gwa, tak i bi Neho̩r;
abu kʼi fu Neho̩r bi Se̩rug ño̩ dʼo̩do̩ o̩gwo̩ko̩, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Oñ Neho̩r dʼo̩do̩ ogu nyoke me̩la, tak i bi Te̩ra;
abu kʼi fu Te̩ra bi Neho̩r ño̩ dʼo̩do̩ ogume̩lu nyoke me̩gwe̩la, i laño̩ bi amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩.
Te̩ra dʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩ta nyoke me̩gwa, i la fʼEbram, kpai Neho̩r kpai Haran bi.
O̩lo̩pu Te̩ra o̩gba o̩gba la de̩. Te̩ra bi Ebram, kpai Neho̩r, kpai Haran; Haran la bi Lo̩t.
Oñ Haran leku dʼo̩gba ata-wñ Te̩ra ane̩ ugbo ku ma jʼubi-wñ, ane̩ Ur e-abo Kaldia le̩.
Ebram kpai Neho̩r la nʼo̩ya ñw o̩la-ma; odu o̩ya Ebram ko̩ Se̩rai, odu o̩ya Nehor la ko Milka, o̩ma Haran kʼi chʼata Milka kpai ata Iska.
Se̩rai la chʼagaji; i nʼo̩ma n.
Taku Te̩ra mʼo̩ma-wñ Ebram du kpai Lo̩t o̩ma Haran, aaju-wñ le̩, kpai Se̩rai o̩ya o̩ma-wñ Ebram, oñ ma kpe̩re̩ kwo Ur e-abo Kaldia dufu ku ma nyʼojane̩ Kenan; taku ma lewa Haran, oñ ma kwojo̩ o̩mo̩.
Oñ o̩do̩ Te̩ra chʼo̩do̩ o̩gwo̩ko̩ nyoke me̩lu; taku Te̩ra leku Haran o̩mo̩.
Inabali Ebraham; O̩jo̩ fʼu do̩; Ebraham nyi Kenan
Jihofa la ka ñwu Ebram me̩, kakini, Kwʼojane̩-we̩ dufu kpai kwugbo amefu-we̩ kpai kwugbo unyi ata-we̩ kʼe̩ lo tʼane̩ kʼu nadu ñʼuwe̩.
Tak u nadʼuwe̩ che abo uche̩ichi elile, oñ nade̩nyo̩ ñw e̩, nache odu-we̩ ki nana, uwe̩ ki la mud e̩nyo̩ ñw amone̩.
U ñʼade̩nyo̩ ñw abo ku ma kadua ñw e̩, oñ e̩ne̩ kʼi anama ñw e̩ na nama ñw u; oñ efu-we̩ ma ade̩nyo̩ ñw akwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi ane̩-ile̩-i du.
Oñ Ebram le, alu ku Jihofa ko̩la ñw u; Lo̩t ño̩ lebʼo̩. O̩do̩ Ebram la chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩ta nyoke me̩gwe̩lu e̩gba kʼi kwo Haran.
Taku Ebram mu Se̩rai o̩ya-wñ du, kpai Lo̩t o̩ma o̩maye-wñ le̩, kpai ane̩ ku ma fiye̩ jo̩ chaka, kpai amonugo one̩ ku ma ne̩ efu Haran; oñ ma le dufu ku ma nyʼane̩ Ke̩nan. Oñ ma lewa ane̩ Kenan,
taku Ebram lale gu efu ane̩ le̩ du tʼugbo ku ma do̩ ko̩ She̩ke̩m, ugbo oli te̩re̩bint e-More̩. Oñ e̩gbale̩ abo Ke̩nan jʼojane̩ le̩.
Taku Jihofa kwotejugede ñw Ebram, oñ i kakini, Ugbe̩-we̩ oñ omi adʼane̩ kide̩ ñw u. Tak o̩mo̩ i fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ne ñwu Jihofa, kʼi kwotejugede ñw u le̩.
I ño̩ kwʼo̩mo̩ nyʼugbo uwo ki dʼo̩wo̩ olodudu Be̩te̩l, oñ i fʼunyabo-wñ fa, Be̩te̩l de̩ olane̩-wñ, Ai la de̩ olodudu; o̩mo̩ i ño̩ fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ne ñwu Jihofa ge̩ tak i do̩ odu Jihofa.
Tak Ebram ño̩ kʼe̩re̩ nyʼule̩, tʼo̩wo̩ o̩pata o̩gane̩ alo waa.
Ebraham dʼIjipti
Ukpo̩ta la dʼojane̩ le̩ akpa. Oñ Ebram gwo̩ru nyʼIjipti kʼi ge̩ne̩ o̩mo̩, todu ukpo̩ta akpa tabale ojane̩ le̩.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba kʼi me̩ru egudu tʼIjipti, i ka ñwu Se̩rai o̩ya-wñ kakini, E̩ go mi ta, omi chema kʼuwe̩ chʼonobule̩ kʼi chefe̩ru one̩ eju ego;
abo Ijipti fʼuwe̩ li fai ma aka kʼo̩ya-wñ de̩; taku ma adʼumi kpa, ku ma la aje̩ ñw e̩ deju.
Narodubʼe̩ kʼuwe̩ ki ka kʼe̩ chʼo̩maye-mi, todu ki nyo̩ ñw omi lʼo̩la-we̩, todu kʼonugo-mi ki deju lʼugbo we̩.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba kʼEbram lewa Ijipti abo Ijipti go onobule̩ le̩ kʼi chefe̩rʼeju nana.
Tak amagboji Fero fʼowñ li, oñ ma ñwulo̩-wñ ñwu Fero. Taku ma mʼonobule̩ le̩ du le tef unyi Fero.
Tak i che e̩nyo̩ ñw Ebram todu owñ; oñ Ebram ne̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ egini kpai amokuno̩ kpai amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩ o̩ko̩ kpai amadu e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai amadu onobule̩ kpai amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩ ole kpai aminyakulumi.
Taku Jihofa je̩ ñw atulubo̩ elile ki lewa bu Fero kpai abunyi-wñ ma todu Se̩rai, o̩ya Ebram.
Taku Fero fʼEbram do̩, oñ i kakini, E̩wñ chʼe-kʼuwe̩ che mi-i? E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ ma ka ñwu mi kʼowñ chʼo̩ya-we̩ n?
E̩wñ chi kʼuwe̩ kakini, Owñ chʼo̩maye-mi, kʼomi la mʼu du chʼo̩ya-mi? Todule̩ e̩ la go, o̩ya-we̩ de̩, mʼowñ du, kʼe̩ lo we̩.
Taku Fero ñwa ñw abo-wñ ugbo o̩la-wñ; taku ma fʼahite̩-wñ che, kpai o̩ya-wñ kpai e̩wñ du kʼi ne̩.
Ebraham kpai Lo̩t mudaru
Abe̩le̩ Ebram mute̩gu kwʼIjipti alo, owñ kpai o̩ya-wñ, kpai e̩wñ du kʼi ne̩, Lo̩t la dʼugbo-wñ, ma le tʼo̩wo̩ o̩pata o̩gane̩.
Ame̩wñ ukpa kpai ajifa kpai o̩jamalia Ebram la gbe̩gbe̩.
Oñ i lʼule̩-wñ kwo o̩pata o̩gane̩ le̩ gbogbo wa Be̩te̩l, tʼugbo kʼunyabo-wñ de̩ ejodudu le̩, agbagba Be̩te̩l kpai Ai,
ugbo ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ kʼi ne o̩mo̩ e̩gba ejodudu le̩; o̩mo̩ Ebram la do̩ odu Jihofa.
Oñ Lo̩t ge̩, e-ki lebo̩ Ebram le̩, owñ ño̩ ne̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ egini kpai amokuno̩ kpai unyabo wewe,
ane̩ le̩ la bʼuma jo̩ ku ma bʼo̩la-ma gugu n; todu e̩wñ ku ma ne̩ chenana todu abe̩le̩ ma ma neke bʼo̩la-ma gugu n,
oñ uja chi ñw abo ku ma dejute̩ ame̩wñ ukpa Ebram kpai abo ku ma dejute̩ ame̩wñ ukpa e-Lo̩t. E̩gbale̩ abo Kenan kpai abo Pe̩re̩z gugu ane̩ le̩.
Tak Ebram ka ñwu Lo̩t kakini, Agba, uja ki dʼagbagba omi kpai uwe̩ n, kpai agbagba abo ku ma dejute̩ ame̩wño̩re̩-mi kpai abo ku ma dejute̩ ame̩wño̩re̩-we̩ n; todu awa chʼo̩maye.
I chʼo̩de̩de̩ ane̩ te̩ chaka eju-we̩-i n? Nagbo̩ko̩bʼe̩ kʼe̩ mudaru bʼumi te̩. Iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ mʼo̩wo̩ awohi du, mak u nale tʼo̩wo̩ awo̩to̩; i la che̩wñ kʼe̩ mʼo̩wo̩ awo̩to̩ du, e̩gbale̩ nalo tʼo̩wo̩ awohi.
Taku Lo̩t chi eju-wñ nyʼate̩, oñ i go egbili Jo̩rdan chaka kʼi chene̩ omiofo nyo̩nyo̩ ugbo du, i dab uche̩ Jihofa, i dab ane̩ Ijipti abu kʼone̩ alo tʼo̩wo̩ Zoar le̩; owñ chʼo̩gba taku Jihofa kpa So̩do̩m kpai Go̩mo̩ra bie̩.
Abe̩le̩ Lo̩t mʼegbili Jo̩rdan chaka du chʼe-wñ, taku Lo̩t lule̩ tʼo̩wo̩ olodudu; abe̩le̩ ma mudaru bʼo̩la-ma te̩.
Ebram la gugu ane̩ Kenan, oñ Lo̩t gugu ewo ewo egbili le̩ i la fʼunyabo-wñ fa afa ño̩ fa gbogbo wa So̩do̩m.
Oñ abo So̩do̩m le̩ chaʼabe̩bie̩ne̩, ma chʼamadu Jihofa re ololo.
Oñ abu ku Lo̩t mudaru bʼo̩ te̩, Jihofa ka ñw Ebram kakini, Fai uwe̩ ki namʼeju-we̩ chi nyʼate̩ ugbo kʼe̩ de̩ le̩ kʼe̩ go, o̩wo̩ o̩pata meji eji kpai o̩wo̩ olodudu kpai olane̩;
todu ane̩ du kʼe̩ li le̩ uwe̩ nadu ñw u, kpai ugbe̩-we̩ ogbegbele̩.
Omi ache kʼugbe̩-we̩ adabu ebutu ane̩-ile̩-i; todabe̩le̩ iche̩wñ kʼone̩ neke gbaluka ebutu ane̩-ile̩, maku ma neke gbaluka ugbe̩-we̩ ge̩.
Kwane̩, kʼe̩ lule̩ gu ane̩ le̩ du o̩wo̩ ujiji-wñ kpai o̩wo̩ unabe̩-wñ, todu uwe̩ nadu ñw u.
Tak Ebram mʼunyabo-wñ chi, oñ i lewa gugu me̩ru oli te̩re̩bint e-Mamre, kʼi jo̩ He̩bro̩n le̩; tak o̩mo̩ i fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ne ñwu Jihofa.
Ogu amonu le̩; ma fu Lo̩t mu; Lo̩t kwotane̩
Oñ i lewatu adiko Amrafe̩l onu Shainar, Ario̩k onu E̩laser, Chedo̩rlaome̩r onu Elam, kpai Taidal onu Goim,
kʼamonu le̩ kʼogu bo̩ Be̩ra onu So̩do̩m, kpai Birsha onu Go̩mo̩ra, Shainab onu Adma, kpai Sheme̩be̩r onu Ze̩boim, kpai onu Bila (owñ le̩ che, Zoar).
Abo-i chaka kʼo̩la-ma dama ef O̩go̩ Sidim (owñ chʼOhimini Omu).
O̩do̩ me̩gweji ma te̩tarire̩ ñwu Che̩do̩rlaome̩r, tak o̩do̩ e̩ke̩gwe̩ta ma ko̩.
Tak o̩do̩ e̩ke̩gwe̩le̩-wñ Chedo̩rlaome̩r lewa kpai amonu ku ma jʼugbo-wñ le̩ oñ ma fʼabo Re̩feim Ashte̩ro̩t-kamaim kpai abo Zuzim Ham, kpai abo Emin Shafe-Karia-taim,
kpai abo Ho̩r du oj uwo-ma ku ma do̩ ko̩ Se̩ir gbogbo wa E̩l-paran ki me̩rʼaje̩tachi le̩;
taku ma mudabi oñ ma lewa E̩runishpat (owñ che, Kede̩sh), taku ma fʼane̩ abo Amale̩k kpo̩fo̩, kpai e-abo Amo̩r ku ma dodo Hazazo̩n-temar.
Tak onu So̩do̩m, kpai onu Go̩mo̩ra, kpai onu Adma, kpai onu Ze̩boim, kpai onu Bila (owñ che, Zoar) le̩ dufu, oñ ma mʼo̩la-ma kodo jo̩ ku ma jogu kpai ama ef O̩go̩ Sidim
ma kobo̩ Chedo̩rlaome̩r onu Elam, kpai Taidal onu Goim, kpai Amiafe̩l nu Shainar, kpai Ario̩k onu E̩lase̩r, onu me̩le̩ kobo̩ onu me̩lu le̩.
O̩go̩ sidim le̩ la che̩ko̩ ñw o̩fe̩ o̩bia bitume̩n; tak amonu So̩do̩m kpai Go̩mo̩ra ra, oñ ma leane̩ o̩mo̩, tak abo ki bo̩ ra tʼoj uwo le̩.
Abe̩le̩ ma mʼane̩ So̩do̩m chaka ko kpai e-Go̩mo̩ra, kpai uje̩wñ-ma chaka, oñ ma le ma;
ma la mu Lo̩t, o̩mʼo̩maye Ebram kʼi gugu So̩do̩m le̩ kpai ane̩-wñ ko, taku ma le.
Tak e̩ne̩ʼka kʼi fʼuma o̩wo̩ lewa ka ñw Ebram, e̩ne̩ Hibru, kʼi la gugu ugbo te̩re̩bint e-Mamre e̩ne̩ Amo̩r, kʼi chʼo̩maye E̩shko̩l le̩, kpai o̩maye Ane̩r; abo le̩ chʼame̩ne̩-uma Ebram.
Tak e̩gba kʼEbram gbo̩ kʼogu fʼo̩maye-wñ je̩, i mʼabo-wñ ku ma ko̩che̩ ogu kodufu, owñ chʼabo ku ma bi ma ef unyi-wñ, one̩ oli me̩fa nyoke me̩gwe̩jo̩ ma che, oñ i ra no ma gbogbo wa Dan.
Tak i fʼabo-wñ kpe̩ru wa bʼuma ma odu, owñ kpai amadu-wñ, oñ i gwo ma i ño̩ ra no ma gbogbo wa Hoba, kʼi dʼo̩wo̩ awohi Damaskus.
Oñ i mʼane̩ chaka gba dabi wa i laño̩ mʼo̩maye-wñ Lo̩t du dabi wa kpai ane̩-wñ ge̩, kpai abobule̩ kpai amone̩ le̩ du.
Abu kʼi doji awa kwugbo ku ma kpa Chedo̩rlaome̩r kpai amonu ku ma jʼugbo-wñ, onu So̩do̩m ledufu kʼi ledʼowñ ugbo O̩go̩ Shafe̩ (owñ chʼO̩go̩ Onu).
Me̩lke̩side̩k kadua ñw Ebraham
Taku Me̩lke̩side̩k onu Se̩le̩m kʼakala kpai omi achiwebe̩te̩ma dufu wa; owñ la chʼatama O̩jo̩ Chamachala.
Tak i kadua ñw u, kakini,
O̩jo̩ Chamachala
e-kʼi ne̩ efojale kpai ane̩-ile̩ kʼi de̩nyo̩ ñw Ebram;
O̩jo̩ Chamachala kʼi nʼele,
Owñ ki mʼame̩nebi-we̩ ko jʼef o̩wo̩-we̩ le̩!
Tak i fʼe̩wñ le̩ du kpe̩ e̩gwa e̩gwa, oñ i mʼojiʼka ko ñw u.
Tak onu So̩do̩m ka ñw Ebram kakini, Mʼamonugo amone̩ le̩ ko ñwu mi kʼuwe̩ ki gwo̩nyu ane̩ le̩.
Tak Ebram ka ñw onu So̩do̩m kakini, Omi mʼo̩wo̩-mi du dago ñwu Jihofa O̩jo̩ Chamachala, e-kʼi ne̩ efojale kpai ane̩-ile̩,
ka kʼomi agba owuʼka abe̩k iku e̩daʼka abe̩k e̩wñ okate ki chʼe-we̩ n, tode̩gba kʼuwe̩ akakini, Omi chʼe̩wñ kʼEbram chʼanana.
Chai e-kʼabo okolobia je̩ kate, kpai ukpe̩ aboke̩le̩ ku ma lebʼumi; Ane̩r kpai E̩shko̩l, kpai Mamre le̩ ki gba ukpe̩ e-ma.
O̩jo̩ ka kʼi adʼo̩ma ñw Ebraham, kpai ane̩ Kenan ge̩
Ubi e̩wñ-i ge̩ o̩la Jihofa wʼugbo Ebram ef ane̩ ego, kakini, E̩ ki railo n, Ebram, omi chʼugbe̩yo̩-we̩; kpai uro̩me̩-we̩ ki nana ololo.
Tak Ebram kakini, Ondu Jihofa, e̩wñ e̩ du ñwu mi, abu kʼu nache kʼu tʼile̩ no̩ kʼu ma nʼo̩ma n, e̩ne̩ ki ane̩ unyi-mi la che E̩lieza e-Damaskus le̩?
Oñ Ebram kakini, Go, uwe̩ du ugbe̩ do̩ ñwu mi n; e̩ go, e̩ne̩ ku ma bi ef unyi-mi ofofo mud e̩ne̩ kʼi aje̩ e̩wñ ogu-mi.
Tak o̩la Jihofa wʼugbo owñ kakini, E̩ne̩ kʼe̩ ka-i chʼe̩ne̩ kʼi aje̩ e̩wñ ogu-we̩ n; chai e̩ne̩ kʼi akwef ifi-we̩ onugo aje̩ e̩wñ ogu-we̩.
Tak i mʼowñ du dufu wʼo̩do̩da oñ i kakini, Chi eju-we̩ nyʼojale kʼe̩ go, kʼe̩ kaluka awo ki jo̩ le̩, iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ aneke kaluka-wñ. Tak i ka ñw u kakini, Abe̩le̩ ugbe̩-we̩ ade̩.
Tak i dʼo̩la Jihofa rʼochochi; oñ i fʼe-le̩ lorʼo̩kpakpa ñw u.
Alo ekpe̩ manyʼe̩wñ kʼi ka tane̩ le̩
Tak i ka ñw u kakini, Omi che Jihofa kʼi dʼuwe̩ kwo Ur e-abo Kaldia wa, kʼu dʼane̩ kide̩ ñw e̩ kʼe̩ ne̩.
Tak i kakini, Ondu Jihofa, lugbo e̩wñ oñ nama ka kʼu nane̩-i?
Tak i ka ñw u kakini, Mʼagbadufu ole okuno̩, kpai ole ewo, kpai okolo kʼo̩do̩-ma chʼe̩ta e̩ta, kpai ikede, kpai o̩ma o̩ke̩te̩be̩ kowa ñwu mi.
Tak i mʼe̩wñ-i kowa ñw u chaka, oñ i fʼuma kpana nyigba, tak i mʼe̩kpana ojiʼka du tʼo̩wo̩ʼka oñ i mʼe̩kpana ekeji du tʼo̩wo̩ ekeji, chai ame̩we̩ kate oñ i ma kpana n.
Tak ame̩we̩ ku ma kpʼe̩la je̩ gwo̩ru bʼoku le̩ ma, oñ Ebram fʼuma ne.
Tak e̩gba kʼolu che kʼi tunyane̩, olu elile lewa bʼEbram ma; me̩ go, e̩wñ okpo e̩chubi lile bʼowñ ma.
Tak i ka ñw Ebram kakini, Uwe̩ ki ma ogbolo ka kʼugbe̩-we̩ achʼilowa ojane̩ ki ma che e-ma n, amugbe̩-we̩ le̩ achʼadu-ma, abo le̩ la afʼuma dema o̩do̩ ulo̩ko̩;
omi muda akajo̩ abo uche̩ichi ku ma chʼadu ñwu ma le̩, ubile̩ taku ma anʼane̩ nana kwʼo̩mo̩ wa.
Ama uwe̩ anyʼugbo amata-we̩ ef ure̩do̩; e̩gba kʼe̩ chʼogijo nyo̩nyo̩ taku ma adʼuwe̩ ji.
Oñ ef o̩gba e̩ke̩le̩ ma adabi wa emi ge̩; todu e̩wñ ugbite̩re̩ abo Amo̩r jo̩ kpa ta n.
Tak i lewatʼe̩gba kʼolu tunyane̩ kʼane̩ la chubi, me̩ go, aido ki akpʼodudu kpai e̩mu ki ajo mala mala lale gu alumeji e̩la ki chʼe̩ko̩da jo̩ le̩ du.
O̩jo̩ le̩ Jihofa fʼalo-wñ kpe̩ kpai Ebram, i kakini, Ugbe̩-we̩ oñ omi adu ane̩ kide̩ ñw u, akwo ohimini Ijipti le̩ gbogbo wa ohimini lile, owñ chʼohimini Yufretis,
ane̩ abo Ken, kpai abo Keniz, kpai abo Kadmo̩n,
kpai abo Ele̩t, kpai abo Pe̩re̩z, kpai abo Re̩feim,
kpai abo Amo̩r, kpai abo Kenan, kpai abo Girgash, kpai abo Je̩bius le̩.
Hega ra; i fʼIshmae̩l bi
Se̩rai, o̩ya Ebram, la bi o̩ma ñw u n. Oñ i ne̩ imo̩to̩ onobule̩ kʼi ache e̩wñ ñw u, e̩ne̩ Ijipti i che, odu-wñ ko̩ Hega;
oñ Se̩rai ka ñw Ebram kakini, Go ta, Jihofa fʼo̩na o̩ma ebi re nyu mi; narodubʼe̩ kʼe̩ nyʼejefu ugbo imo̩to̩-mi onobule̩ le̩; ikani nafʼunyi ne̩ lugbo-wñ. Tak Ebram netirʼomu Se̩rai.
Abu kʼEbram fʼo̩do̩ me̩gwa da ojane̩ Kenan, taku Se̩rai, o̩ya Ebram mu Hega, e̩ne̩ Ijipti, imo̩to̩-wñ onobule̩ le̩ du, oñ i m u du ñw Ebram o̩ko̩-wñ, kʼi chʼo̩ya-wñ.
Tak i nyʼejefu ugbo Hega, oñ i fʼefunyo̩; tak e̩gba kʼi li ka kʼi fʼefunyo̩, odu-wñ ño̩ wʼo̩ eju ge̩ n.
Taku Se̩rai ka ñw Ebram kakini, O̩lachi-mi ki dʼoji-we̩! Omi mʼimo̩to-mi onobule̩ da mʼuwe̩ e̩do̩, tak e̩gba kʼi li kʼi fʼefunyo̩, u mud e̩nibe̩te̩ eju-wñ. Jihofa ki kajo̩ omi kpai uwe̩!
Ama Ebram ka ñwu Se̩rai kakini, Go, imo̩-to̩-we̩ dʼef o̩wo̩-we̩ le̩; e̩ chʼo e̩wñ ki rʼuwe̩ eju. Taku Se̩rai kwo chʼo o̩lachi, oñ i ra bʼo̩ eju te̩.
Tak onuche̩ Jihofa fʼowñ li ugbo e̩bi omi ef aje̩tachi, owñ chʼe̩bi omi ki dʼo̩na Shur le̩.
Tak i kakini, Hega, imo̩to̩ Se̩rai, ugbo e̩ kwo wa ugbo e̩ ño̩ nyi? Oñ i kakini, Nara bʼeju odu-mi Se̩rai, te̩.
Tak onuche̩ Jihofa le̩ ka ñw u kakini, Mudabi tʼugbo odu-we̩, kʼe̩ fʼo̩la-we̩ kamuhite̩ ñw u.
Onuche̩ Jihofa le̩ ño̩ ka ñw u kakini, Nache kʼugbe̩-we̩ ki wewe nyo̩gba nana gbogbo taku ma ño̩ akaluka ma todu uwewe-ma ge̩ n.
Tak onuche̩ Jihofa le̩ ka ñw u kakini, Go, uwe̩ defu me̩, uwe̩ abi o̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩; uwe̩ adʼodu-wñ ko̩ Ishmae̩l, todabu ku Jihofa li o̩bata-we̩ kʼe̩ che.
Owñ la adʼef amone̩ dab o̩ke̩ke̩te̩ efoko; o̩wo̩-wñ achʼagwunyu e̩ne̩ du, o̩wo̩ e̩ne̩ du achʼagwunyu owñ; owñ la agugu akpejuru amo̩maye-wñ chaka.
Tak i dʼodu Jihofa e-kʼi ko̩la ñw u ko̩, Uwe̩ chʼO̩jo̩ kʼi agane̩, todu i kakini, U ño̩ dʼemi agʼo abu kʼi fʼumi go?
Todule̩ ma do̩ obuga le̩ ko Bir-lehairo̩i; go, i dʼagbagba Kede̩sh kpai Be̩re̩d.
Oñ Hega fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi ñw Ebram; Ebram la dʼodu o̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ku Hega bi ñw u le̩ ko̩ Ishmae̩l.
O̩do̩ Ebram la chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩le̩ nyoke me̩fa e̩gba ku Hega bi Ishmae̩l ñw Ebram.
Alo ekpe̩ e-e̩pi eda le̩
E̩gba kʼo̩do̩ Ebram jo̩ o̩gbo me̩le̩ nyoke me̩gwe̩la Jihofa kwotejugede ñw Ebram, i la ka ñw u kakini, Omi chʼO̩jo̩ Odobogagu; e̩ ki lule̩ eju-mi, o̩la-we̩ ki mufu.
Tak omi akpʼalo-mi agbagba omi kpai uwe̩, naño̩ che kʼuwe̩ ki wewe nyo̩gba ololo.
Ebram la fʼeju bʼane̩ ma; oñ O̩jo̩ ko̩la ñw u kakini,
I chʼomi, go, alo-mi kʼu kpe̩ i chʼomi kpai uwe̩, uwe̩ la achʼata abo uche̩ichi ojoji ojoji wewe.
Ma ñʼadʼodu-we̩ ko̩ Ebram ge̩ n, ama odu-we̩ ako̩ Ebraham; todu ata amone̩ uche̩ichi ojoji wewe omi dʼuwe̩ che.
U ñʼaje̩ ñw e̩ nʼugbe̩ ololo, nache kʼuwe̩ mud uche̩ichi amone̩ ojoji ojoji, amonu la akwʼef uwe̩ dufu ge̩.
Nadu alo-mi dago agbagba omi kpai uwe̩ kpai ugbe̩-we̩ ubi-we̩ ge̩ gbogbo tʼo̩gba o̩gba-ma du kʼi chʼalo e-ogbegbele̩, kʼu nachʼO̩jo̩ ñw e̩ kpai ugbe̩-we̩ ubi-we̩ ge̩.
Nadʼane̩ ugbo kʼe̩ ge̩ne̩ le̩, owñ chʼane̩ Kenan du, ñw e̩, kpai ugbe̩-we̩ ubi-we̩ kʼi mud e̩wñ-me̩ ogbegbele̩; u ñʼachʼO̩jo̩-ma.
Tak O̩jo̩ ka ñw Ebraham kakini, I la chʼuwe̩, uwe̩ ade alo-mi, uwe̩ kpai ugbe̩-we̩ ubi-we̩ tʼo̩gba o̩gba-ma.
Alo-mi ku me̩ la ade la de̩, i tʼagbagba mi kpai uwe̩ kpai ugbe̩-we̩ ubi-we̩ ge̩: kakini, E̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du efu-me̩ adʼe̩pi.
Me̩ la ada o̩re̩la e-año̩ ki bʼo̩gba-me̩ ma le̩, oñ e-le̩ achʼujiwe alo ki tʼagbagba omi kpai ame̩.
Me̩ la adʼe̩pi o̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du o̩gba o̩gba me̩ o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩jo̩ ku ma bi, tʼe̩ne̩ ku me̩ bi unyi, tʼe̩ne̩ ku me̩ dʼo̩ko̩ la ugbo ononojo du ki ma chʼugbe̩ e-we̩ n.
E̩ne̩ ku ma bi ef unyi-we̩ kpai e̩ne̩ kʼuwe̩ nʼo̩ko̩-we̩ la, ma adʼe̩pi-ma chuu. Abe̩le̩ alo-mi adʼef o̩re̩la-me̩ ki chʼalo ogbegbele̩.
Oñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du ki ma dʼe̩pi n kʼi ma la da o̩re̩la e-año̩ ki bʼo̩gba-wñ ma le̩ n, ma amʼonugo e̩ne̩ le̩ daru bʼabo-wñ te̩; i fʼalo-mi bie̩ me̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ ka ñw Ebraham kakini, I chʼe-Se̩rai, o̩ya-we̩, uwe̩ ki dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Se̩rai ge̩ n, chai Sara chʼodu-wñ.
Oñ nade̩nyo̩ ñw u, omi la adʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ñw e̩ lugbo owñ ge̩; ochochi nade̩nyo̩ ñw u, i la amud iye uche̩ichi amone̩ ojoji ojoji; amonu e-amone̩ ojoji ojoji akwʼefu-wñ dufu.
Tak Ebraham fʼeju-wñ bʼane̩ ma, anyanyi, oñ i ka ef e̩do̩-wñ kakini, Ma ñʼabi o̩ma ñw e̩ne̩ kʼo̩do̩-wñ chʼogu me̩lu ge̩? Sara, kʼo̩do̩-wñ la chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩le̩ nyoke me̩gwa, ñʼabi o̩ma ge̩?
Tak Ebraham ka ñw O̩jo̩ kakini, Ayaa, Ishmae̩l ki deju o̩gba-we̩ ke n!
Tak O̩jo̩ kakini, O̩da, chai Sara o̩ya-we̩ abi o̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ñw e̩, uwe̩ la adʼodu-wñ ko̩ Aise̩k. Oñ nadʼalo-mi kʼu kpe̩ le̩ dago kpai owñ kʼi chʼalo ogbegbele̩ tod ugbe̩-wñ ubi-wñ ge̩.
I chʼe-Ishmae̩l, u gbo̩ ab e̩ ka me̩; go, omi ade̩nyo̩ ñw u oñ naje̩ ñw u bi o̩ma, u ñʼaje̩ ñw u wewe nyo̩gba ololo; i abi amidachi me̩gweji, oñ naje̩ ñw u chʼuche̩ichi amone̩ ki wewe.
U muda adʼalo-mi dago kpai Aise̩k, e-ki Sara abi ñw e̩ iko-i o̩do̩ omune̩.
Tak i tʼo̩la no̩ eka kpai owñ, oñ O̩jo̩ kwugbo Ebraham le tʼojale.
Tak Ebraham mʼIshmae̩l o̩ma-wñ le̩ du kpai e̩ne̩ du ku ma bi unyi-wñ kpai e̩ne̩ du ku ma dʼo̩ko̩-wñ la, owñ chʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du kʼi dʼef abo unyi Ebraham, oñ i fʼe̩pi-ma da ef o̩re̩la e-año̩ ki bʼo̩gba-ma ma o̩jo̩ le̩ gbage̩de̩, alu kʼO̩jo̩ ka ñw u.
O̩do̩ Ebraham la chʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩le̩ nyoke me̩gwe̩la e̩gba ku ma fʼe̩pi-wñ da ef o̩re̩la ki bʼo̩gba-wñ ma;
oñ o̩do̩ Ishmae̩l, o̩ma-wñ, la chʼe̩gwe̩ta e̩gba ku ma fʼe̩pi-wñ da ef o̩re̩la ki bʼo̩gba-wñ ma.
O̩jo̩ʼkate ma fʼe̩pi Ebraham kpai Ishmae̩l, o̩ma-wñ, da;
kpai aboke̩le̩ unyi-wñ du, tʼabo ku ma bi unyi-wñ tʼabo ku ma dʼo̩ko̩ la kwʼo̩wo̩ ononojo, ma fʼabo le̩ e̩pi da kpai owñ.
Ebraham chʼamonuche̩ O̩jo̩ ojo
Taku Jihofa kwotejugede ñw u ugbo oli te̩re̩bint e-Mamre abu kʼi gugu alugbo̩na unyabo-wñ e̩gba kʼolu ada o̩ro̩ka.
Oñ i chi eju-wñ nyʼate̩ ago, me̩ go, aboke̩le̩ me̩ta dago jʼo̩gba-wñ. Tak e̩gba kʼi fʼuma li i fule kwʼalugbo̩na unyabo le̩ ledo ma, oñ i te̩kpe̩ wʼane̩ ñwu ma,
i kakini, Odu-mi, iche̩wñ kʼe̩ lʼumi eju, nagbo̩ko̩bʼuwe̩, e̩ ki lale gu adu-we̩-i du n.
E̩ je̩ ñwu ma che omiofo wa pe̩, ku me̩ gwe̩ e̩re̩-me̩, ku me̩ ñmi ofʼoli-i.
Oñ nadʼuje̩wñ wa pe̩, kʼo̩la-me̩ ki ruko, ubi le̩ tak ame̩ ale gudu—todabu ku me̩ wʼugbo adu-me̩-i. Oñ ma kakini, Mak e̩ che alu kʼe̩ ka ke.
Tak Ebraham hiane̩ tef unyabo ugbo Sara, oñ i kakini, E fʼe̩ñwa omu me̩ta fo̩ piopio, kʼe̩ fʼu nu, kʼe̩ mʼu du che akala.
Tak Ebraham fule nyʼugbo ujo̩ amokuno̩-wñ, oñ i mʼo̩ma okuno̩ o̩ko̩ ʼka kʼe̩la-wñ chʼemele kʼi la chenyo̩ du, tak i mʼu du ñw imo̩to̩-wñ, oñ e̩le̩ hika chʼuko̩lo̩-wñ.
Tak i mʼokume̩ agwe kpai omi e̩nyʼokuno̩ kpai o̩ma okuno̩ e-o̩ko̩ kʼi chʼuko̩lo̩-wñ le̩ ko, oñ i mʼu ko gugu o̩gba-ma; tak i kwo dago ugbo ma of oli le̩, ma la je̩.
Taku ma ka ñw u kakini, Ugbo Sara, o̩ya-we̩ de̩? Oñ i kakini. Go, i dʼef unyabo le̩.
Tak i kakini, Nadabi wa ugbo-we̩ iko-i o̩do̩ omune̩ chuu, e̩ la go, Sara, o̩ya-we̩ abi o̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩. Sara la dʼalugbo̩na unyabo e-kʼi dubigbo̩ le̩ agbo̩.
Ebraham kpai Sara la chʼogijo, ma wa kpo̩kpe̩ me̩; alu kʼabobule̩ ache le̩, e-Sara la muda.
Taku Sara kwonyanyi nye-kuma, i kakini, Abu kʼu chʼogijo-i, nali ejile-i? Odu-mi laño̩ chʼogijo?
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Ebraham kakini, E̩wñ chi ki Sara nyanyi, kʼi kakini, u ñʼabi o̩ma ab u chʼogijo-i ochochi?
E̩wñʼka do̩mo̩ ki firu Jihofa? Iko kʼu da le̩ nadabi wʼugbo we̩, owñ chʼiko-i o̩do̩ omune̩ oñ Sara ane̩ o̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩.
Taku Sara re̩ kakini, Omi nyanyi no; todu i chokpo. Tak e̩ne̩ le̩ kakini, O̩da, uwe̩ nyanyi gbo.
Ebraham fʼologu So̩do̩m che
Tak aboke̩le̩ le̩ kwane̩ o̩mo̩, oñ ma mʼeju korʼo̩wo̩ So̩do̩m; tak Ebraham fʼahite̩-ma che.
Oñ Jihofa kakini, E̩wñ kʼu nache nadu maja ñw Ebraham?
Abu kʼEbraham achʼuche̩ichi amone̩ ki nana ki nʼukpahiu, kʼuche̩ichi amone̩ du ane̩-ile̩-i ali e̩nyo̩ lefu-wñ?
Todu u chema owñ, ka kʼowñ chʼe̩ne̩ ki añwa ñw abimo̩to̩-wñ kpai abo unyi-wñ ubi owñ, kʼama ki de o̩na Jihofa, ku ma che e̩wñ o̩kpakpa kpai oj ajo̩ kʼi dute̩; todu ki Jihofa ki dʼe̩wñ kʼi kʼo̩la-wñ le̩ wa ñw Ebraham.
Taku Jihofa kakini, Ochochi, ukwa So̩do̩m kpai Go̩mo̩ra chenana, adure-ma la gbe̩gbe̩;
fai nanyʼo̩mo̩ kʼu li abe̩k e̩wñ ku ma che-i likpa alu kʼukwa-wñ ki wʼugbo mi le̩ de̩; i ma dʼabe̩le̩ n, u ma.
Tak aboke̩le̩ le̩ murida kwʼo̩mo̩ oñ ma le rʼo̩wo̩ So̩do̩m; Ebraham muda dago o̩gba Jihofa waa.
Tak Ebraham te̩ me̩ru oñ i kakini, E̩ ñʼafʼabo̩kpakpa lie̩ manyu ame̩ne̩bibi?
Ikani abo̩kpakpa ooje jʼef ewo le̩ fa; uwe̩ afʼu lie̩ kʼe̩ ma la do̩wo̩mo̩ ugbo kide̩ todu abo̩kpakpa ooje ku ma jʼefu-wñ n?
O̩la abe̩i eche ki jiji rʼuwe̩, kʼe̩ kpa ame̩no̩kpakpa manyu ame̩ne̩bibi, kʼame̩no̩kpakpa ki dabalu kʼame̩ne̩bibi de̩! e le̩ ki jiji rʼuwe̩ Akajo̩ ane̩-ile̩ du achʼe̩wñ tʼoji ajo̩ kʼi dute̩ n?
Taku Jihofa kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼu li ame̩no̩kpakpa ooje ef ewo So̩do̩m le̩, e̩gba le̩ natʼugbo kide̩ no̩ chaka todu ma.
Tak Ebraham dohi kakini. Go ta, ibenu naje̩ kʼu ko̩la ñw Ondu-i, omi kʼu chʼebutu kpai elulu.
Ikani e̩lu chi kwef ame̩no̩kpakpa ooje le̩ fa? E̩ kpʼewo le̩ bie̩ chaka tod e̩lu ki chi le̩? Tak i kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼu fʼone̩ o̩gbo̩ meji nyoke me̩lu li o̩mo̩ nakpʼo̩ bie̩ n.
Oñ i nako̩la ñw u waa kakini, Ikani ma fʼone̩ o̩gbo̩ meji li o̩mo̩ fa? I kakini, Nache n, todu one̩ o̩gbo̩ meji le̩.
Tak i kakini, O̩la kʼu naka-i i ki bi Ondu eju n. Ikani ma fʼone̩ ogue̩gwa li o̩mo̩ fa? Oñ i kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼu fʼone̩ ogue̩gwa li o̩mo̩ nache n.
Tak i kakini, E̩ go, ibenu naje̩ kʼu ko̩la ñw Ondu-i. Ikani ma fʼone̩ ogu li o̩mo̩ fa? Oñ i kakini, Nakpʼo̩ bie̩ n todu one̩ ogu le̩.
Tak i kakini, I ki bi Ondu eju n, kʼu nako̩la onukate ta. Ikani ma fʼone̩ me̩gwa li o̩mo̩ fa? Oñ i kakini, Nakpʼo̩ bie̩ n todu one̩ me̩gwa le̩.
Taku Jihofa le̩ owñ abu kʼi fʼoluka che kpai Ebraham kpa; oñ Ebraham mudabi tʼe̩gu-wñ.
Lo̩t chʼamonuche̩ O̩jo̩ meji ojo So̩do̩m o̩mo̩
Oñ amonuche̩ meji le̩ lewa So̩do̩m e̩gbʼane̩; Lo̩t la gugu alaku So̩do̩m. Taku Lo̩t fʼuma li, oñ i kwane̩ ledo ma, i te̩kpe̩, i dʼoji lo̩,
oñ i kakini, Me̩ go ta, amodu-mi, nagbo̩ko̩bʼume̩, me̩ na tʼunyi adu-me̩-i, ku me̩ le̩, ku me̩ fʼe̩re̩-me̩ gwe̩; taku me̩ takpa kwane̩ odudu ku me̩ lo me̩. Oñ ma kakini, O̩da; a ale̩ ñw o̩jo̩ opee o̩do̩da emi.
I la kute̩ ma nana; taku ma na wʼugbo-wñ, oñ ma mugudu tef unyi-wñ; tak i fʼo̩je̩ ojo hi ñwu ma, i la fʼakala kʼo̩jo̩wu ma dʼo̩ n, che, oñ ma je̩.
O̩gba taku ma nyʼadachi, aboke̩le̩ ewo le̩ donyʼunyi le̩ daka, owñ chʼaboke̩le̩ So̩do̩m le̩ tʼimo̩to̩ tʼogijo, o̩chaka amone̩ kwʼugbo du wa.
Taku ma nomudala do̩ Lo̩t, ma ka ñw u kakini, Aboke̩le̩ ku ma gudu wʼugbo-we̩ ane̩-i, ugbo ma de̩ ke? Mʼuma kodufu wʼugbo-wa kʼa ma ma.
Taku Lo̩t ledufu wʼugbo ma alugbo̩na, oñ i fʼo̩na re ubi-wñ, i kakini,
Nagbo̩ko̩bʼume̩, amo̩maye-mi, me̩ ki che e̩wñ bibi abe̩i n.
Me̩ go ta, u chenʼamo̩ma onobule̩ meji ku ma ma mʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ n; agba, me̩ je̩ ñwu mi ko ma dufu wʼugbo-me̩ ku me̩ che ma alu ki rʼume̩ eju, i chʼe-aboke̩le̩-i, me̩ ki che ma abu du n; todabu kʼu mu ma gbanyi me̩.
Taku ma kakini, Te̩ubi! Oñ ma kakini, E̩ne̩ kate-i lewa emi kʼi ge̩ne̩, oñ i ache kʼi dʼo̩la-wñ chʼakajo̩-wa? Fai e-kʼa chʼuwe̩ abie̩ne̩ tʼe-kʼa che abo le̩ le. Oñ ma ke̩che̩ bʼe̩ne̩ le̩ ma bie̩ne̩ bie̩ne̩, owñ che Lo̩t le̩, oñ ma hi me̩rʼu ku ma kpʼolugbo̩na le̩ fo̩.
Ama aboke̩le̩ le̩ nʼo̩wo̩ dala dufu oñ ma mu Lo̩t du wʼef unyi ugbo-ma, taku ma fʼo̩na re.
Taku ma fʼaboke̩le̩ ku ma jo̩ alugbo̩na unyi le̩ eju chubi, tʼe-kekele tʼe-lile, abe̩le̩ etene alugbo̩na le̩ fʼuma hia.
Ma gu So̩do̩m kpai Go̩mo̩ra jo; Lo̩t mufu tane̩
Tak aboke̩le̩ le̩ ka ñwu Lo̩t kakini, Uwe̩ nʼe̩ne̩ du emi tʼame̩-i le? o̩ko̩ o̩ma-we̩ kpai amo̩ma-we̩ e-aboke̩le̩ kpai e-abobule̩ kpai e̩ne̩ du kʼe̩ ne̩ ewo-i, mʼuma ko kwʼemi dufu;
todu a che kʼa akpʼemi-i bie̩, todu ukwa-ma chenana ugbo Jihofa, Jihofa la fʼuwa kpe̩ wa kʼa fʼu kpabie̩.
Taku Lo̩t ledufu ako̩la ñw abo ku ma ne̩ amo̩ma-wñ, oñ i kakini, Kwane̩, me̩ kwʼemi dufu; todu Jihofa ache kʼi kpʼewo-i bie̩. Ama eju amo̩ko̩ amo̩ma-wñ, i dabe̩ne̩ kʼiyachi i ache.
Tak e̩gba kʼo̩jo̩ ñwa amonuche̩ le̩ nu Lo̩t aju, ma kakini, Kwane̩, mʼo̩ya-we̩ kpai amo̩ma-we̩ onobule̩ meji ku ma jʼemi ko, tode̩gba ku ma fʼuwe̩ lie̩ ef udu ku ma bu ñw ewo-i.
I muda fʼiñelebu che; tak aboke̩le̩ le̩ gwo̩nyʼu o̩wo̩ kpai o̩wo̩ o̩ya-wñ kpai o̩wo̩ amo̩ma-wñ onobule̩ meji le̩, abu ki Jihofa lʼejumomi-wñ, oñ ma mʼowñ du dufu ma mʼu du gugu ej o̩do̩da ewo le̩.
Oñ i lewatu abu ku ma mʼuma ko wʼo̩do̩da, i kakini, Ra lo tod oji-we̩; e̩ ki dʼej ubi n, e̩ ki dago ugbo du egbili-i n; ra tugbo uwo le̩, tode̩gba ku ma fʼuwe̩ lie̩.
Taku Lo̩t ka ñwu ma kakini, Aiya, i ki dʼabe̩le̩ n, Ondu-mi;
go ta, adu-we̩-i mud e̩ne̩ kʼuwe̩ li eju, uwe̩ je̩ ñw ufe̩do̩-e̩nyo̩-we̩ nana me̩, owñ chʼe-kʼe̩ du ña mi ejadu kʼe̩ jadu oji-mi-i; u la neke ra tugbo uwo le̩ n, tode̩gba kʼe̩wñ bie̩ne̩ ke̩re̩bʼumi, kʼu naku.
Go ta, ewo o̩mo̩-i chʼeme̩rʼo̩wo̩ kʼu nara tʼefu-wñ, i la de̩ ke̩ke̩. Je̩ ñwu mi ra tʼo̩mo̩—i de̩ ke̩ke̩ n?—tak onugo-mi adeju!
Tak i ka ñw u kakini, Go, e̩wñ kʼe̩ ka-i omi ño̩ mugba ge̩, ka kʼu nagu ewo kʼe̩ ko̩la-wñ le̩ lo̩ n.
Hiane̩, kʼe̩ ra tʼo̩mo̩; todu u neke che e̩wñ du gbogbo tak e̩ wʼo̩mo̩ n. Todule̩ ma dʼodu ewo le̩ ko̩ Zoar.
Olu kwodufu afu bʼile̩ ma e̩gba ku Lo̩t lewa Zoar.
E̩gbale̩ Jihofa je̩ ñw itolu kpai una lo̩ kwugbo Jihofa kwʼefojale bo̩ So̩do̩m kpai Go̩mora ma;
oñ i fʼewo ewo le̩ gulo̩ kpai egbili le̩ du kpai amone̩ ku ma jʼewo ewo le̩ kpai e̩wñ du ki tiga ane̩pe̩te̩.
O̩ya-wñ ki dʼubi-wñ muda dejubi go, oñ i mud ugbudu omu dago.
Ebraham la kwane̩ odudu odudu, i nyʼugbo kʼi dago o̩gba Jihofa le̩;
oñ i kejurʼo̩wo̩ So̩do̩m kpai Go̩mo̩ra kpai o̩wo̩ ane̩ egbili le̩ du, i la go, me̩ go, odudu ane̩ le̩ akwane̩ tʼate̩ tuu dabe̩ne̩ kʼodudu aido.
Oñ i lewatu, e̩gba kʼO̩jo̩ fʼewo ewo egbili le̩ kpabie̩, O̩jo̩ libekado Ebraham oñ i mu Lo̩t dudufu kwʼalumeji e̩gulo̩ le̩, e̩gba kʼi fʼewo ewo ku Lo̩t dodo efu-wñ le̩ gulo̩.
Taku Lo̩t mute̩gu kwo Zoar dufu, oñ i lewa dodo oj uwo le̩, amo̩ma-wñ onobule̩ meji la jʼugbo-wñ, todu i railo edodo Zoar; abe̩le̩ i gugu ef owo, owñ kpai amo̩ma-wñ onobule̩ meji le̩.
Tak o̩mo̩gba-wñ ka ñw okekele-wñ kakini, Ata-wa chʼogijo me̩, e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du la dʼile̩ kʼi awʼejefu ugbo wa alu kʼabo ile̩ du ache n.
Lewa, kʼa je̩ ñw ata-wa ñmʼo̩te̩, tak a abʼo̩ dachi, kʼa nʼugbe̩ tane̩ ñw ata-wa.
Taku ma je̩ ñw ata-ma ñmʼo̩te̩ odu o̩jo̩ le̩; oñ o̩mo̩gba le̩ le tʼejefu, i la bʼata-wñ dachi; Lo̩t la ma e̩gba kʼi dachi, abe̩k e̩gba kʼi kwane̩ n.
Oñ i lewatu o̩jo̩ñwa-wñ, o̩mo̩gba le̩ ka ñw okekele-wñ, kakini, Go, u bʼata-mi dachi odu o̩nale̩; a ñʼaje̩ ñw u ñmʼo̩te̩ odu eñini ge̩; tak e̩ nyʼejefu kʼe̩ bʼo̩ dachi, kʼa ki nʼugbe̩ tane̩ ñw ata-wa.
Abe̩le̩ ma ño̩ je̩ ñw ata-ma ñmʼo̩te̩ odu o̩jo̩ le̩ ge̩; oñ e-kekele kwane̩, i la bʼo̩ dachi; i la ma e̩gba kʼi wa dachi n, i la ma e̩gba kʼi kwane̩ n.
Abe̩le̩ amo̩ma Lo̩t meji le̩ fʼefu nyo̩ ñw ata-ma.
Oñ o̩mo̩gba le̩ fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi, i la dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Moab; owñ le̩ chʼata abo Moab gbogbo tʼeñini.
Tak e-kekele ño̩ fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Be̩nami; owñ le̩ chʼata amo̩ma Amo̩n gbogbo tʼeñini.
Ebraham re̩ ka ku Sara chʼo̩ya-wñ n
Tak Ebraham mʼe̩re̩ ko nyʼule̩ kwʼo̩mo̩ tʼo̩wo̩ o̩pata o̩gane̩, oñ i gugu agbagba Kede̩sh kpai Shur; i la ge̩ne̩ Ge̩rar.
Oñ Ebraham nʼo̩la o̩ya-wñ Sara aka kakini, Owñ chʼo̩maye-mi. Tak Abime̩le̩k, onu Ge̩rar, fʼone̩ kpe̩ wa oñ i mu Sara du.
Ama O̩jo̩ lewa ugbo Abime̩le̩k ef o̩na odu, oñ i ka ñw u kakini, Go, oku one̩ e̩ che, todu onobule̩ kʼe̩ du le̩; todu o̩ya one̩ i che.
Abime̩le̩k la te̩mʼo̩ ta n; oñ i kakini, Ondu, e̩ ñʼakpa abo uche̩ichi o̩kpakpa ge̩?
I chʼowñ onugo ka ñwu mi ka kʼo̩maye-wñ i che n? Tʼonobule̩ onugo, i ño̩ ka kʼo̩maye-wñ i che. Ef o̩foo e̩do̩-mi kpai o̩jali o̩wo̩-mi oñ u che-i.
Tak O̩jo̩ ka ñw u ef o̩na le̩ kakini, Ochochi, u chema ka kʼef ofoo e̩do̩-we̩ uwe̩ che-i, omi laño̩ gwo̩nyʼuwe̩ tode̩gba kʼe̩ du mi re; todule̩ u ma je̩ ñw e̩ do̩wo̩kadʼo n.
Todule̩ e̩ mʼo̩ya e̩ne̩ le̩ dudabi wa ñw u todu akache̩ i che, tak owñ achadua tod uwe̩, oñ uwe̩ adeju. I la che̩wñ kʼe̩ ma dʼowñ dabi tʼe̩gu-wñ n, e̩ ki ma ka kʼuwe̩ aku chuu, uwe̩ kpai abo du kʼuwe̩ ne̩.
Tak Abime̩le̩k takpa kwane̩ odudu oñ i fʼabuko̩lo̩-wñ chaka do̩ wa, i la fo̩la-i du ka ñwu ma gbo̩; tak aboke̩le̩ le̩ kwo chokpo ololo.
Tak Abime̩le̩k fʼEbraham do̩, oñ i ka ñw u kakini, E-kʼe̩ che wa-i fa? Ugbo omi la du we̩ re kʼuwe̩ mʼadure inaina kowa bʼomi kpai abo ojane̩-mi ma? E̩wñ kʼe̩ che mi-i, i dukpe̩ kʼone̩ ki che n.
Tak Abime̩le̩k ka ñw Ebraham kakini, Ibe e̩wñ dʼefu-we̩ kʼe̩ che e̩wñ-i?
Tak Ebraham kakini, Todu omi do̩ ka kʼe̩gahi O̩jo̩ dʼemi n, ma la adu mi kpa todu o̩ya-mi.
Anubi e-le̩ ge̩, o̩mata-mi i che ochochi, i chʼo̩ma ata-mi, a muda nʼiye n; oñ i mud o̩ya-mi.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba kʼO̩jo̩ je̩ ñwu mi kwo bʼunyi ata-mi te̩ tʼoko oko ale, e̩gbale̩ u ka ñw u kakini, E̩nyo̩ kʼe̩ che ñwu mi de̩: ugbo du kʼa lewa, uwe̩ ki nʼo̩la-mi aka kakini, O̩maye-mi de̩.
Tak Abime̩le̩k mʼamala kpai amo̩kokuno̩ kpai amadu e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩ ko ñw Ebraham oñ i mʼo̩ya-wñ Sara dudabi wa ñw u.
Tak Abime̩le̩k kakini. Go, ane̩-mi tʼo̩gba-we̩ le̩: ugbo kʼi nyʼe̩ eju e̩ gugu
Oñ i ka ñwu Sara, kakini, Go, omi mʼajifa icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ ko ñw o̩maye-we̩ me̩, go, owñ le̩ chʼe̩wñ ubʼeju-we̩ ma ugbo abo du ku ma jʼugbo-we̩; ale ma da ñw e̩ eju e̩ne̩ du le̩.
Tak Ebraham rodubʼO̩jo̩: oñ O̩jo̩ fʼo̩ga Abime̩le̩k che, kpai e-o̩ya-wñ, kpai e-amadu-wñ onobule̩; taku ma ño̩ chane̩ ebi o̩ma.
Todu Jihofa fʼabio̩ma abobule̩ unyi Abime̩le̩k chaka re, todu Sara o̩ya Ebraham le̩.
Ma fu Aise̩k bi
Taku Jihofa wa fejudo Sara alu kʼi ka le̩, Jihofa la che ñwu Sara alu kʼi ko̩la ñw u.
Oñ Sara fefunyo̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi ñw Ebraham o̩jo̩ ogijo-wñ, iko kʼO̩jo̩ ko̩la tane̩ ñw u kpakpa.
Ebraham la do̩ odu o̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ku ma bi ñw u, owñ chʼe-ki Sara bi ñw u le̩, ko̩ Aise̩k.
Tak Ebraham fʼe̩pi o̩ma-wñ Aise̩k da o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩jo̩-wñ, alu kʼO̩jo̩ ñwa ñw u.
O̩do̩ Ebraham la chʼo̩do̩ ogume̩lu e̩gba ku ma fʼo̩ma-wñ Aise̩k bi ñw u.
Taku Sara kakini, O̩jo̩ chʼe̩wñ kʼomi nyanyi; e̩ne̩ du ki la gbo̩ abʼumi nya-nyi.
I laño̩ kakini, E̩ne̩ ma ka ñw Ebraham ka ki Sara adʼe̩nya ñw o̩ma ñmo̩? Todu u la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi ñw u o̩jo̩ ogijo-wñ.
O̩ma le̩ naya nyo̩gba, i mʼalu e̩nya da; tak Ebraham fʼuje̩wñ uyo̩ elile che o̩jo̩ ku ma je̩ ñw Aise̩k dʼalʼe̩nya.
Ma fu Hega kpai Ishmae̩l ne
Sara fʼo̩ma ki Hega e̩ne̩ Ijipti le̩ bi ñw Ebraham li abu kʼi akʼo̩ ru.
Todule̩ i ka ñw Ebraham kakini, Mʼadu onobule̩-i du tinyo̩ kpai o̩ma-wñ; todu o̩ma adu onobule̩-i aje̩ e̩wñ ogu kpai o̩ma-mi Aise̩k in.
E̩wñ le̩ la bie̩ne̩ tabale eju Ebraham noji o̩ma-wñ le̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ ka ñw Ebraham kakini, I ki bie̩ne̩ eju-we̩ todu okolobia-i n, kpai tod adu onobule̩-we̩-i n; e̩wñ du ki Sara aka ñw e̩, e̩ nagbʼomu-wñ, todu efu Aise̩k ma ado̩ one̩ kʼugbe̩-we̩.
Omi año̩ che̩ kʼo̩ma adu onobule̩-i kʼi mud abo uche̩ichiʼka, todabu kʼi chʼugbe̩-we̩.
Abe̩le̩ Ebraham takpa kwane̩ odudu, oñ i mʼuje̩wñ kpai aiko omi du, oñ i mʼu du ñwu Hega, i la mʼu du nʼika-wñ, i laño̩ mʼimo̩to̩ le̩ du ñw u, tak i je̩ ñw u le. Oñ i kwʼo̩mo̩, i tale aje̩tachi Birshiba.
Tak omi ef aiko le̩ takpa, oñ i mʼimo̩to̩ le̩ du ro̩ tʼofe ejijiʼka o̩mo̩.
Oñ i le nyʼaguguane̩ o̩wo̩ʼka-wñ o̩najiji alu ku ma neke tʼo̩fa kʼi ale kade. I kakini, Todu kʼimo̩to̩ le̩ ki dʼiñmi nyʼumi o̩wo̩ n. Oñ i guguane̩ o̩wo̩ʼka-wñ, tak i dʼomu-wñ nyʼate̩ araku.
Oñ O̩jo̩ gbo̩ omu imo̩to̩ le̩; tak onuche̩ O̩jo̩ nomudala kwef ojale ado̩ Hega, I ka ñw u kakini, E̩wñ chʼuwe̩, Hega? E̩ ki chokpo n; todu O̩jo̩ gbo̩ omu imo̩to̩ le̩ ugbo kʼi de̩.
Kwane̩, kʼe̩ mʼimo̩to̩ le̩ du kwane̩, e̩ gwo̩wo̩nyʼu; todu nadʼowñ chʼuche̩ichi amone̩ ki nana.
Tak O̩jo̩ mʼe eju chi, oñ i fʼomi obuga li; tak i le nakpa omiofo nyʼaiko le̩ e̩ko̩, oñ i mʼu du ñw imo̩to̩ le̩ ñmo̩.
O̩jo̩ la dʼugbo imo̩to̩ le̩, oñ i nagbʼo̩kone̩; i la gugu aje̩tachi le̩, oñ i mud ato̩fa.
I la gugu aje̩tachi Paran, oñ iye-wñ fʼo̩ya ne̩ ñw u kwef abo Ijipti.
Ebraham kpai Abime̩le̩k kpalo
Oñ i lewatu iko le̩, Abime̩le̩k kpai Fiko̩l, agboji abo ogu-wñ, ka ñw Ebraham kakini, O̩jo̩ dʼugbo we̩ ef e̩wñ du kʼe̩ che;
todule̩ e̩ fʼO̩jo̩ go̩ ñwu mi emi, ka kʼe̩ ñache e̩wñ olemi kpai omi kpai o̩ma-mi kpai aaju-mi n, chai likpa alu kʼomi mo̩la ñw e̩ alu le̩ uwe̩ ache ñwu mi kpai ane̩ e-kʼe̩ ge̩ne̩ oji-wñ-i.
Tak Ebraham kakini, Nago̩ abe̩le̩.
Tak Ebraham dʼo̩la biu Abime̩le̩k todu omi obuga, owñ chʼe-kʼamadu Abime̩le̩k bʼo̩ gba afuma.
Tak Abime̩le̩k kakini, U ma e̩ne̩ ki che-i no; uwe̩ la ka ñwu mi n, omi la gbo̩ n, chai eñini-i.
Tak Ebraham mʼamala kpai amo̩kokuno̩ ko, oñ i mʼuma ko ñw Abime̩le̩k, tak ama meji kpalo.
Tak Ebraham mʼamo̩ma ala e-ole mebie kojo̩ kpai o̩la-ma.
Oñ Abime̩le̩k ka ñw Ebraham, kakini, Amo̩ma ala ole mebie kʼe̩ kojo̩ kpai o̩la-ma-i fa, e̩wñ chʼofe-wñ?
Oñ i kakini, Amo̩ma ala ole mebie-i uwe̩ agba o̩wo̩-mi, kʼi chʼijali-mi ka kʼomi gwa obuga-i.
Todule̩ oñ i do̩ ugbo ki de̩ ko̩ Birshiba; todabu kʼama meji go̩ o̩mo̩.
Abe̩le̩ ma fʼalo kpe̩ Birshiba. Tak Abime̩le̩k kpai Fiko̩l agboji abogu-wñ kwane̩, oñ ma mudabi tʼane̩ Amafilistia.
Ebraham la fʼoli tamarisk gbe̩ Birshiba le̩, oñ o̩mo̩ le̩ i do̩ odu Jihofa. O̩jo̩ Ogbegbele̩.
Ebraham la nʼo̩jo̩ je̩ ane̩ Amafilistia.
O̩jo̩ jʼe̩do̩ ekono Ebraham ma
Tak i lewatu ubi e̩wñ-i, oñ O̩jo̩ jʼEbraham ma, i ka ñw u kakini, Ebraham! Oñ i kakini, Omi de̩.
Tak i kakini, Fai e̩ mʼo̩ma-we̩ le̩ du, owñ chʼo̩ma okpono kʼe̩ fe̩do̩ le̩, owñ chʼAise̩k, kʼe̩ lo tʼane̩ Moraya, o̩mo̩ le̩ e̩ mʼowñ du wa chʼiche̩bo̩ e̩gujo noji uwoʼka kʼomi aka ñw e̩.
Tak Ebraham takpa kwane̩ odudu, i la fʼofidi ji mʼubi o̩ke̩ke̩te̩-wñ, i mʼabokolobia-wñ meji ko lebʼowñ, manyʼAise̩k o̩ma-wñ; i la fʼiji iche̩bo̩ e̩gujo le̩ kpana, tak i kwane̩, i le tʼugbo kʼO̩jo̩ ka ñw u.
O̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta-wñ Ebraham chi eju-wñ oñ i li ugbo le̩ o̩najiji.
Tak Ebraham ka ñw abokolobia-wñ kakini, Me̩ jʼemi kpai o̩ke̩ke̩te̩-i, oñ omi kpai imo̩to̩-i anyʼano̩mo̩-i, a la adojikane̩ ñw O̩jo̩, tak a adabiwa ugbo me̩.
Tak Ebraham mʼiji e̩wñ e̩gujo le̩ du, oñ i mudu nʼo̩ma-wñ Aise̩k oji; i la mʼuna kpai o̩be̩ du nʼo̩wo̩. Abe̩le̩ ama meji kpe̩re̩ alo.
Oñ Aise̩k ka ñw Ebraham ata-wñ kakini, Ata-mi! Oñ i kakini, Omi de̩, o̩ma-mi. I kakini, Go una kpai iji de̩; ama ugbo o̩mala todu iche̩bo̩ e̩gujo de̩?
Tak Ebraham kakini, O̩ma-mi, O̩jo̩ ali o̩mala ñw o̩la-wñ todu iche̩bo̩ e̩gujo. Abe̩le̩ amameji kpe̩re̩ alo.
Taku ma lewa ugbo kʼO̩jo̩ ka ñw u le̩; oñ Ebraham fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ kpa o̩mo̩, tak i fʼiji te̩ru, tak i fʼo̩ma-wñ Aise̩k ji, i la mʼu du dachi oj iji ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩.
Tak Ebraham nʼo̩wo̩ dala, oñ i mʼo̩be̩ du kʼi fʼo̩ma-wñ kpa.
Tak onuche̩ Jihofa efojale kwadʼo̩, i kakini, Ebraham, Ebraham! Oñ i je̩ kakini, Omi de̩.
Oñ i kakini, E ki dʼo̩wo̩-we̩ kad imo̩to̩ le̩ n, e̩ ki la chʼo abu du n; todu fai u chema ka kʼuwe̩ adiba ñw O̩jo̩, abu kʼuwe̩ ma do̩wo̩mʼo̩ma-we̩, e-okpono, ñw omi n.
Tak Ebraham mʼeju-wñ chi dago oñ i go, me̩ go, okoloʼka dago ubi-wñ o̩mo̩, igba-wñ gbaji tʼetutu; tak Ebraham le namʼokolo le̩ du, oñ i mʼu du wa chʼiche̩bo̩ egujo koji o̩ma-wñ.
Tak Ebraham dʼodu ugbo kide̩ ko̩ Jihofa-jire: alu ku ma ka tʼo̩jo̩ olu eñini, kakini, Oj uwo Jihofa ma aliʼu.
Tak onuche̩ Jihofa ño̩ dʼojale ado̩ Ebraham onuke̩ji
i kaklni, U fʼo̩la-mi go̩, Jihofa ka-i, todabu kʼe̩ fʼe̩wñ-i che, kʼe̩ ma la do̩wo̩mʼo̩ma-we̩ e-okpono-we̩ le̩ n,
ka kʼede̩nyo̩ nade̩nyo̩ ñw e̩, ewewe nyo̩gba naje̩ ñw ugbe̩-we̩ ki wewe nyo̩gba alu kʼawo ojale de̩, kpai alu kʼe̩lanyi ki dʼeti ohimini abadi de̩. Ugbe̩-we̩ la agbʼalaku ame̩nebi-ma,
ef ugbe̩-we̩ le̩ uche̩ichi amone̩ ojoji ojoji du ane̩-ile̩-i ali e̩nyo̩, todabu kʼe̩ gbʼomu-mi gbo̩.
Abe̩le̩ Ebraham mudabi tʼugbo abokolobia-wñ, taku ma kwane̩, ma kpe̩re̩ le̩ tu Birshiba; oñ Ebraham kwogugu Birshiba.
Oñ i lewatu anubi e̩wñ-i, ku ma ka ñw Ebraham kakini, Go, Milka ño̩ fʼamo̩ma bi ñw o̩maye-we̩ Ne̩ho̩r le̩:
Uz chʼo̩mo̩gba-wñ kpai Buz o̩maye-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai Kemue̩l ata Aram
kpai Che̩se̩d kpai Hazo kpai Pildash kpai Jidlaf kpai Be̩tue̩l.
Be̩tue̩l la fu Ribe̩ka bi. Ama me̩jo̩ le̩ Milka bi ñwu Ne̩ho̩r, o̩maye Ebraham.
Oñ abadu-wñ, kʼodu-wñ ko̩ Reuma, ño̩ bi Teba kpai Gaham kpai Tahash kpai Maaka.
Sara leku, oñ ma mʼu du ji Makpila
O̩do̩ udeju Sara la chʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩fa nyoke mebie; o̩do̩ udeju Sara la de̩.
Taku Sara leku Kiriat-arba (owñ che He̩bro̩n), ane̩ Kenan; tak Ebraham lewa ki nʼeku Sara ade̩ kʼi la rʼaku-wñ.
Tak Ebraham kwane̩ kwʼo̩gba okuegu-wñ le̩, oñ i ko̩la ñw amo̩ma He̩t kakini,
Ilowa omi che kpai e̩ne̩ ane̩ omune̩ kʼi dʼugbo me̩ ofofo; fʼane̩ ugbo kʼu nakʼabo-mi ji bu ñwu mi ugbo me̩-i, kʼu kʼabo-mi ki ku ji bʼeju-mi te̩.
Tak amo̩ma He̩t dohi ñw Ebraham kakini,
E̩ gbʼomu-wa, odu-mi; uwe̩ chʼidachi O̩jo̩ efu-wa-i. Dʼe̩ne̩-we̩ ki ku ji ef ojinoji-wa e-o̩me̩me̩le̩; i nʼe̩ne̩ du efu-wa kʼi ado̩wo̩mʼojinoji-wñ ñw uwe̩ kʼe̩ ma adʼe̩ne̩-we̩ ji n.
Tak Ebraham kwane̩, oñ i te̩kpe̩ ñw amone̩ ane̩ le̩, owñ chʼamo̩ma He̩t.
Oñ i ko̩la ñwu ma kakini, Iche̩wñ ki du me̩ e̩do̩ kʼu naji e̩ne̩-mi ki ku bʼeju-mi te̩, me̩ gbʼomu-mi, ku me̩ chologu bʼIfro̩n o̩ma Zohar ñwu mi,
kʼi mʼowo Makpila kʼi ne̩ le̩ du ñwu mi; owñ chʼe-kʼi dʼoj oko-wñ o̩mo̩ le̩; alu aja-wñ o̩gbolo i ata ñwu mi todu kʼu ne̩ ane̩ ugbo kʼu nakʼabo-mi ji, alumeji-me̩-i.
Ifro̩n la gugu alumeji amo̩ma He̩t o̩mo̩; tak Ifro̩n e̩ne̩ He̩t le̩ mʼohi du ñw Ebraham eju amo̩ma He̩t le̩, owñ chʼeju e̩ne̩ du ki gudu wa alaku ewo-wñ, kakini,
O̩da, odu-mi, e̩ gbʼe-mi ke; o̩ko̩ kide̩ nadu ñw e̩, owo ki dʼefu-wñ nadu ñw e̩; eju amo̩ma abo-mi-i nadʼu ñw e̩-i; dʼe̩ne̩-we̩ kʼi ku ji ke.
Tak Ebraham te̩kpe̩ wʼane̩ o̩gba amone̩ ane̩ le̩.
Oñ i ka ñw Ifro̩n eju amone̩ ane̩ le̩ kakini, Iche̩wñ ki dʼuwe̩ e̩do̩, nagbo̩ko̩bʼuwe̩, e̩ gbʼe̩-mi; alu aja oko kide̩ nadu ñw e̩; mʼu gba o̩wo̩-mi, tak u nadʼe̩ne̩-mi ki ku ji o̩mo̩.
Oñ Ifro̩n dohi ñw Ebraham, kakini,
Odu-mi, netirʼo̩la-mi; e̩bu ane̩ kʼo̩ko̩-wñ che she̩ke̩l ajifa ulo̩gwa, abʼe-le̩ ache agbagba omi kpai uwe̩? Todule̩ e̩ dʼe̩ne̩-we̩ ki ku ji ke.
Oñ Ebraham netirʼo̩la Ifro̩n; tak Ebraham fʼajifa le̩ ñwa ñw Ifro̩n, owñ chʼe-kʼi ka eju amo̩ma He̩t le̩, ajifa ulo̩gwa, owñ chʼo̩ko̩ amanyaja e̩gba le̩.
Abe̩le̩ oko Ifro̩n ki de̩ Makpila, ki dʼo̩gba Mamre le̩, o̩ko̩ le̩ kpai o̩wo̩ ki dʼefu-wñ kpai oli du ki jʼoko le̩, e-ki jʼejefu alo̩me̩-wñ daka,
mud e̩wñ kʼEbraham ne̩ eju amo̩ma He̩t, eju amone̩ du ku ma gudu wʼalaku ewo-wñ le̩.
Tak ubi e-le̩ Ebraham du Sara o̩ya-wñ ji ef owo oko Makpila e-ki dʼo̩gba Mamre̩ le̩ (owñ che He̩bro̩n), oj ane̩ Kenan.
Oñ amo̩ma He̩t mʼoko le̩ kpai owo kl dʼefu-wñ ko ñw Ebraham pioo kʼi ne̩ chʼane̩ ugbo kʼi akʼabo-wñ ji.
Aise̩k kpai Ribe̩ka nʼo̩la-ma
Oñ Ebraham mud ogijo, i chʼanagbo nana; Jihofa la de̩nyo̩ ñw Ebraham ef e̩wñ du.
Tak Ebraham ka ñw adu-wñ, kʼi chʼogijo unyi-wñ, e-kʼe̩wñ du kʼi ne̩ jʼef o̩wo̩-wñ kakini, Nagbo̩ko̩bʼuwe̩ kʼe̩ mʼo̩wo̩-we̩ ko nʼuta-mi,
oñ naje̩ ñw e̩ fu Jihofa, kʼi chʼO̩jo̩ efojale kpai ane̩-ile̩, go̩, ka kʼuwe̩ anʼo̩ya ñw o̩ma-mi kwef amo̩ma onobule̩ abo Kenan, e-kʼomi gugu efu-ma-i n,
e̩ muda alo tʼane̩-mi, tʼugbo amefu-mi, kʼe̩ fʼo̩ya ne̩ ñw o̩ma-mi Aise̩k.
Tak adu le̩ ka ñw u kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼonobule̩ le̩ ma je̩ tʼumi ubi wʼane̩-i n fa? i dukpe̩ kʼu nadabi dʼo̩ma-we̩ lo tʼane̩ ugbo kʼe̩ kwo wa le̩?
Tak Ebraham ka ñw u kakini, E̩ ki gbe̩do̩ edʼo̩ma-mi nyʼo̩mo̩ n.
Jihofa O̩jo̩ efojale, kʼi mʼumi du kwef unyi ata-mi, kpai kwoj ane̩ ugbo ku ma bi mi, kʼi ño̩ ko̩la ñwu mi, kʼi laño̩ fʼo̩la-wñ go̩ ñwu mi kakini, Omi adʼane̩ kide̩ ñw ugbe̩-we̩, owñ le̩ akpe̩ onuche̩-wñ tʼo̩gba-we̩, tak uwe̩ anʼo̩ya kwʼo̩mo̩ wa ñw o̩ma-mi.
Iche̩wñ kʼonobule̩ le̩ ma je̩ tʼe̩ ubi n, e̩gba le̩ ego̩ kʼe̩ go̩-i afʼuwe̩ oji; e̩ ki muda dʼo̩ma-mi nyʼo̩mo̩ ge̩ n.
Abe̩le̩ adu le̩ mʼo̩wo̩-wñ du nʼuta Ebraham, oñ i fu go̩ ñw u ugbo o̩la le̩.
Tak adu le̩ mʼaminyakulumi odu-wñ me̩gwa ko, oñ i le, e̩wñ e̩nyo̩ odu-wñ du jʼef o̩wo̩-wñ; oñ i kwane̩, i le tu Me̩sopotemia, ewo Neho̩r le̩,
tak i je̩ ñw aminyakulumi kʼokuku nyʼane̩ o̩do̩da ewo le̩ ugbo obuga omi e̩gba ane̩, owñ chʼiko kʼabobule̩ nyʼakpʼomi.
Tak i kakini, O Jihofa, O̩jo̩ odu-mi Ebraham, e̩ ki je̩ ñwu noji ñwu mi eñini, nagbo̩ko̩bʼe̩ kʼe̩ la mo̩la ñw odu-mi, Ebraham.
Go, omi dago alu e̩bi omi-i, oñ amo̩ma onobule̩ abo ewo-i dufu awa-i ku ma kpa omi.
E̩ ki je̩ ki wache kʼigbe̩le̩ kʼu naka ñw u kakini, E̩ dʼotube̩-we̩ wʼane̩ kʼu nañmo̩, agba, kʼowñ aka ñwu mi kakini, Ñmo̩, kʼu naño̩ du ñw aminyakulumi-we̩ ñmo̩ ge̩-owñ le̩ kʼi chʼe̩ne̩ kʼuwe̩ tu tane̩ ñw adu-we̩, Aise̩k. Lugbo kide̩ oñ nama ka kʼuwe̩ mo̩la ñw odu-mi.
Oñ i lewatu, o̩gba tak i fʼo̩la le̩ ka kpa, go, Ribe̩ka ku ma bi ñwu Be̩tue̩l, o̩ma Milka kʼi chʼo̩ya Neho̩r, o̩maye Ebraham le̩, kwodufu wa, oñ i nʼotube̩ ika-wñ.
Igbe̩le̩ le̩ la chʼuto̩ eju tabale, i mʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ mama ta n, e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du la mʼo̩ n. Owñ le̩ nyʼugbo e̩bi omi le̩, oñ i kpa omi nyʼotube̩-wñ e̩ko̩, oñ i mute̩gu wa.
Tak adu le̩ fule ledʼo, i kakini, Dʼomi otube̩-we̩ ñwu mi ñmo̩ pe̩, agba.
Tak i kakini, Ñmo̩, odu-mi; i la mʼotube̩-wñ ro̩gu nʼo̩wo̩-wñ piopio, oñ i du ñw u ñmo̩.
Tak e̩gba kʼi mudu ñw u ñmo̩ kpa, i kakini, Naño̩ kpa todu aminyakulumi-we̩ ge̩, gbogbo tak i bʼuma jo̩.
Tak i hiane̩ oñ i mʼomi otube̩-wñ dudanyʼagbada, tak i ño̩ dabi fule nyʼugbo obuga kʼi kpa, i la kpa todu aminyakulumi-wñ chaka.
Oñ e̩ne̩ le̩ kejurʼu chii; i chechi dago, kʼi ma abe̩ku Jihofa je̩ ñw ule̩-wñ la ra ñw u abe̩k i je̩ n.
Oñ i lewatu, abu kʼaminyakulumi fʼomi ñmo̩ kpa, tak e̩ne̩ le̩ mʼelika o̩jamalia kʼuwoji-wñ chʼukpeji she̩ke̩l oka, kpai ude̩ o̩wo̩ meji kʼuwoji-wñ chʼo̩jamalia she̩ke̩l me̩gwa ko tod o̩wo̩-wñ,
oñ i kakini, O̩ma e̩ne̩ uwe̩ che? Ka ñwu mi, agba. Uña do̩mo̩ unyi ata-we̩ kʼa ru?
Tak i ka ñw u kakini, O̩ma Be̩tue̩l kʼi chʼo̩ma ku Milka bi ñwu Neho̩r u che.
I ño̩ ka ñw u ge̩ kakini, A chene̩ e̩gbe ku ma dachi oji-wñ kpai ije̩ ki bʼuma jo̩, uña la dʼef unyi kʼe̩ ru.
Tak e̩ne̩ le̩ fʼoji dalo̩ i la dojikane̩ ñwu Jihofa.
Oñ i kakini, Jihofa, ki chʼO̩jo̩ odu-mi Ebraham kʼi nʼele, owñ chʼO̩jo̩ ki ma mʼufe̩do̩-e̩nyo̩-wñ kpai ochochi-wñ ko bʼodu-mi te̩ n. I chʼe-mi, Jihofa fʼumi ne̩ le o̩na tʼunyi amo̩maye odu-mi.
Tak igbe̩le̩ le̩ fule naka o̩la e̩wñ-i du ñw abo unyi iye-wñ.
Ribe̩ka la chene̩ o̩maye e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kʼodu-wñ ko̩ Leban; oñ Leban le̩ fule dufu nyʼugbo e̩ne̩ le̩, ugbo e̩bi omi kʼa ka le̩.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba kʼi fʼelika le̩ li kpai ude̩ o̩wo̩ ki jʼo̩wo̩ o̩maye-wñ, kʼi ño̩ gbʼo̩la Ribe̩ka o̩maye-wñ, ka kʼabe̩le̩ e̩ne̩ le̩ ka ñwu mi, i la wʼugbo e̩ne̩ le̩; me̩ go, i dago ugbo aminyakulumi alu e̩bi omi le̩.
Tak i kakini, Guduwa, uwe̩ ki Jihofa de̩nyo̩ ñw u le̩; e̩wñ chi kʼe̩ dago o̩doda-i? Todu omi fʼunyi ñwo̩che kpai uña todu aminyakulumi.
Tak e̩ne̩ le̩ mugudu wʼef unyi; oñ Leban mʼane̩ aminyakulumi tu jʼane̩, i la mʼegbe kpai ije̩ todu aminyakulumi ko ñw u, kpai omi kʼi adu gwe̩ e̩re̩-wñ, kpai e̩re̩ abo ku ma jʼugbo-wñ.
Taku ma dʼuje̩wñ gugu o̩gba-wñ kʼi je̩; ama i kakini, U je̩ ta n, i chʼe̩gba kʼu fʼuche̩-mi je̩ru me̩ ta. Oñ i kakini, Kwoka ke n.
Tak i kakini, Adu Ebraham omi che.
Jihofa mʼe̩nyo̩ du ñw odu-mi ololo, i la mud anana; i la mʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini kpai amokuno̩, kpai ajifa kpai o̩jamalia, kpai amadu e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩, kpai aminyakulumi, kpai amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩ ko ñw u.
Sara o̩ya odu-mi le̩ la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi ñw odu-mi o̩jo̩ ogijo-wñ; i la mʼe̩wñ du kʼi ne̩ ko ñw o̩ma le̩.
Oñ odu-mi je̩ ñwu mi fu go̩ kakini, Uwe̩ anʼo̩ya ñw o̩ma-mi kwef amo̩ma onobule̩ abo Kenan kʼu gugu oj ane̩-ma-i n;
e̩ muda nalo tʼunyi ata-mi ugbo abo-mi, kʼe̩ la fʼo̩ya ne̩ ñw o̩ma-mi.
Tak u ka ñw odu-mi kakini, Ikani onobule̩ le̩ aje̩ atʼumi ubi n.
Oñ i ka ñwu mi kakini, Jihofa kʼu nalule̩ o̩gba-wñ, owñ akpe̩ onuche̩-wñ lebʼuwe̩ kʼi je̩ ñw ule̩-we̩ ki ra ñw e̩; oñ uwe̩ anʼo̩ya ñw o̩ma-mi ugbo abo-mi kpai ugbo abo unyi ata-mi;
tak e-kʼe̩ go̩ ñwu mi afʼuwe̩ oji, owñ chʼe̩gba kʼe̩ lewa ogbo abo-mi, ku ma ma dʼu ñw e̩ n, mak ego̩ kʼe̩ go̩ ñwu mi afʼuwe̩ oji.
Oñ omi lewa eñini-i ugbo e̩bi omi le̩, u kakini, O Jihofa, O̩jo̩ odu-mi Ebraham, iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ je̩ kʼule̩-mi kʼu le-i ki ra ñwu mi,
go, omi dago alu e̩bi omi-i; e̩ che ki lewatu kʼigbe̩le̩ kʼi fʼo̩wo̩ mʼo̩la-wñ ne̩ kʼi adufu wa akpa omi e-kʼu naka ñw u kakini, Agba, e̩ che omi otube̩-we̩ ñwu mi ñmo̩ pe̩,
kʼowñ le̩ aka ñwu mi kakini, Uwe̩ ki ñmo̩, kʼu naño̩ kpa tod aminyakulumi-we̩ ge̩, e̩ne̩ le̩ ki mud onobule̩ ku Jihofa tu te̩ tod o̩ma odu-mi.
U la kʼo̩la le̩ ef e̩do̩-mi kpa n, go Ribe̩ka kwo dufu wa, otube̩-wñ nʼika-wñ; oñ i gwo̩ru nyʼugbo e̩bi omi le̩ akpa. Tak u ka ñw u kakini, O̩ko̩ nagba bʼe̩ kʼe̩ che mi ñmo̩.
Oñ i hika mʼotube̩-wñ ro̩gu wʼane̩ bʼojika-wñ te̩, i kakini, Ñmo̩, tak u naño̩ du ñw aminyakulumi-we̩ ñmo̩ ge̩. Abe̩le̩ u ñmo̩, tak i ño̩ je̩ ñw aminyakulumi ñmo̩ ge̩.
Tak omi tʼowñ ene kakini, O̩ma e̩ne̩ uwe̩ che? I kakini, O̩ma Be̩tue̩l, o̩ma Neho̩r ku Milka bi ñw u. Tak u mʼelika le̩ du tunyu iñmo̩-wñ, u ño̩ kʼude̩ nyʼu o̩wo̩.
Tak u fʼoji-mi dalo̩, oñ u dojikane̩ ñwu Jihofa, u laño̩ kele Jihofa, O̩jo̩ odu-mi Ebraham, kʼi du mi le̩ o̩na ochochi kʼu fʼo̩ma o̩maye odu-mi ne̩ ñw o̩ma-wñ.
Oñ ifai iche̩wñ ku me̩ amo̩la ñw odu-mi ku me̩ achʼochochi kpʼowñ, me̩ ka ñwu mi; i ma dʼabe̩le̩ n, ka ñwu mi; kʼu rida tʼo̩wo̩ awo̩to̩ abe̩k o̩wo̩ awohi.
E̩gba le̩ Leban kpai Be̩tue̩l dohi ñw u kakini, E̩te̩ e̩wñ-i kwʼugbo Jihofa; a neke ka e̩bie̩ne̩ abe̩k e̩nyo̩ ñw e̩ n.
Go, Ribe̩ka dʼo̩gba-we̩ le̩, mʼowñ du alo, kʼi chʼo̩ya o̩ma odu-we̩, alu ku Jihofa ka le̩.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba kʼadu Ebraham gbʼo̩la-ma le̩, i fʼeju-wñ bʼane̩ ma ñwu Jihofa.
Tak adu le̩ kʼe̩wñ ijaga dufu, e-ajifa kpai e-o̩jamalia, kpai ukpo, oñ i muko ñwu Ribe̩ka; i ño̩ kʼe̩wñ akoko ñw o̩maye-wñ kpai iye-wñ ge̩.
Tak owñ kpai abo ku ma jʼugbo-wñ fʼe̩wñ je̩, ma la ñmo̩, oñ ma fʼoluʼka le̩ o̩mo̩. Taku ma kwane̩ odudu-wñ, oñ i kakini, Me̩ je̩ ñwu mi lo tʼugbo odu-mi.
Tak o̩maye igbe̩le̩ le̩ kpai iye-wñ kakini, Je̩ ñw igbe̩le̩-i kʼi nʼo̩jo̩ je̩ kpai awa pe̩ ta, i ki nyarʼo̩jo̩ me̩gwa n; ubi le̩ tak i alo.
I muda ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ ki da mi hi n, todabu ku Jihofa je̩ ñw ule̩-mi ra ñwu mi; je̩ ñwu mi lo kʼu nanyʼugbo odu-mi.
Taku ma kakini, A adʼ igbe̩le̩-i wa kʼa gbʼalu-wñ.
Taku ma fu Ribe̩ka do̩ wa, oñ ma ka ñw u kakini, E̩ le bʼe̩ne̩-i alo? Oñ i kakini, Nale.
Taku ma je̩ ñwu Ribe̩ka o̩maye-ma le̩ kpai onobule̩ ki adejutʼo̩ kpai adu Ebraham kpai abo-wñ ku ma lo.
Oñ ma kadua ñwu Ribe̩ka, ma ka ñw u kakini, O̩maye-wa, ugbe̩-we̩ ki chʼicham icham o̩be̩le̩ke̩te̩; ugbe̩-we̩ ki ne̩ alaku abo ku ma chulaka ma.
Taku Ribe̩ka kwane̩, kpai amigbe̩le̩-wñ, ma la tano aminyakulumi, oñ ma tʼe̩ne̩ le̩ ubi; abe̩le̩ adu le̩ mu Ribe̩ka du, i le-wñ.
Oñ Aise̩k kwʼo̩na Bir-lehairo̩i wa, todu i gugu ane̩ owo o̩pata o̩gane̩ le̩.
Tak Aise̩k no̩lada nyʼoko e̩gba ane̩ kʼi kpibe; oñ i chi eju-wñ nyate̩, i la li, go, aminyakulumi awa.
Taku Ribe̩ka chi eju-wñ nyate̩, oñ abu kʼi fʼAise̩k li, i mudachi kwʼoj inyakulumi tane̩,
oñ i ka ñw adu le̩ kakini, E̩ne̩ tʼale oko kʼi aledo wa awa-i? Oñ adu le̩ kakini, Odu-mi le̩ de̩. Tak i mʼukpo-wñ du bʼoji-wñ ma wane̩.
Tak adu le̩ mʼe̩wñ du kʼi che du ka ñw Aise̩k.
Oñ Aise̩k mʼonobule̩ le̩ du tef unyabo Sara, iye-wñ, i la mu Ribe̩ka du oñ i mud o̩ya-wñ; i la fe̩do̩-wñ. Abe̩le̩ e̩do̩ Aise̩k nyi ubi kʼiye-wñ ku le̩.
Ebraham leku
Oñ Ebraham fʼo̩ya omune̩ ne̩, odu-wñ la ko̩ Ke̩tura.
Owñ le̩ fu Zimran kpai Jo̩kshan kpai Me̩dan kpai Midi an kpai Ishbak kpai Shua bi ñw u.
Oñ Jo̩kshan fu Shiba kpai Dedan bi. Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Dedan la chʼAshurim kpai Letushim kpai Leumim.
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Midian la chʼE̩fa kpai E̩fe̩r kpai Hano̩k kpai Abida kpai Eldaa. Abo-i chaka chʼamo̩ma Ke̩tura.
Ebraham la mʼe̩wñ du kʼi ne̩ ko ñw Aise̩k.
Ebraham muda kʼe̩wñ chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kʼamabadu Ebraham bi ñw u, ele lale, oñ abu kʼi adeju ta i je̩ ñwu ma kwo bʼo̩ma-wñ Aise̩k te̩ tʼo̩wo̩ olodudu tʼoj ane̩ olodudu le̩.
O̩jo̩ udeju Ebraham la chʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩jo̩ nyoke me̩gwe̩lu.
Tak Ebraham mʼiñmi da, i kwojolugbo nana tak i ku, i gbo, o̩do̩-wñ jo̩ kpa, oñ ma mʼu du atefu abo-wñ.
Tak Aise̩k kpai Ishmae̩l amo̩ma-wñ le̩ mʼowñ du ji ef owo Makpila, oko Ifro̩n o̩ma Zoar, e̩ne̩ abo He̩t le̩, owñ chʼe-ki dʼo̩gba Mamre.
Oko e-kʼEbraham la kwʼo̩wo̩ amo̩ma He̩t le̩. O̩mo̩ ma dʼEbraham ji, kpai Sara o̩ya-wñ.
Oñ i lewatu anubi uku Ebraham, kʼO̩jo̩ de̩nyo̩ ñw o̩ma-wñ Aise̩k. Aise̩k la gugu eti Bir-lehairo̩i.
O̩gba o̩gba e-Ishmae̩l, o̩ma Ebraham, e-ki Hega e̩ne̩ Ijipti kʼi chʼadu onobule̩ e-Sara bi ñw Ebraham le̩ de̩.
Odu amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Ishmae̩l la de̩, owñ chʼodu-ma alu ku ma bi ma aro̩ne aro̩ne; odu o̩mo̩gba Ishmae̩l ko̩ Nebayo̩t; kpai Ke̩dar kpai Adbie̩l kpai Mibsam
kpai Mishma kpai Duma kpai Masa,
kpai Hadad kpai Tema kpai Jetur kpai Nafish kpai Kedema.
Abo le̩ chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Ishmae̩l, e-le̩ chʼodu odu-ma ewo ewo-ma, kpai uru uru-ma; ma chʼamidachi me̩gweji o̩lo̩pu o̩lo̩pu-ma.
Edeju kʼIshmae̩l deju la chʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩fa nyoke me̩gwebie; tak i mʼiñmi da, oñ i leku, oñ ma mʼowñ du atefu abo-wñ.
Oñ ma dodo jo̩ akwo Hafila gbogbo wa Shur e-ki dʼo̩gba Ijipti abu kʼe̩ lo tʼo̩wo̩ Asiria: i filinyane̩ eju amo̩maye-wñ chaka.
Uchane̩ Iso̩ kpai Jeko̩b
E-i la chʼo̩gba o̩gba amo̩ma Aise̩k, o̩ma Ebraham: Ebraham fʼAise̩k bi,
o̩do̩ Aise̩k la chʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ meji e̩gba kʼi fu Ribe̩ka, o̩ma Be̩tue̩l, e̩ne̩ Siria e-Padan-aram, o̩maye Leban e̩ne̩ Siria le̩ ne̩ chʼo̩ya-wñ.
Tak Aise̩k rodubo̩ Jihofa tod o̩ya-wñ, todabu kʼi chʼagaji; Jihofa la mʼuro-dubo̩-wñ gbagbo̩, oñ Ribe̩ka o̩ya-wñ fefunyo̩.
Tak amo̩ma-wñ jʼefu-wñ akobʼo̩la-ma; oñ i kakini, Abe̩le̩? E̩wñ ache mi-i? Tak i nyʼatu Jihofa ene.
Oñ Jihofa ka ñw u kakini,
Amone̩ uche̩ichi meji jʼefu-we̩,
Abo meji la adaru bʼomune̩ te̩ kwef ifi-we̩;
Oka-wñ anʼukpahiu tʼekeji le; e-ogijo la are̩ e-kekele.
Tak e̩gba kʼo̩jo̩ o̩ma ebi-wñ jo̩, go, ukpejima meji jʼefu-wñ.
E-ki wane̩ ejodudu la chʼekpikpa, o̩chaka año̩la-wñ dabe̩ne̩ kʼukpo ku ma ne̩ edudu hi; oñ ma dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Iso̩.
Ubi le̩ tak o̩maye-wñ wʼane̩, o̩wo̩-wñ la tato̩ agbe̩re̩ Iso̩; oñ ma dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Jeko̩b: o̩do̩ Aise̩k la chʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩ta e̩gba kʼo̩ya-wñ bi ma.
Oñ abimo̩to̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ le̩ gbʼo̩kone̩ alo; Iso̩ la chʼado̩de̩ ki gbeju, e̩ne̩ oko i che; Jeko̩b la chʼe̩nami, i gugu ef unyabo.
