Aise̩k la fe̩do̩ Iso̩, todabu kʼe̩la o̩de̩-wñ arinyo̩ alu-wñ: Ribe̩ka muda fe̩do̩ Jeko̩b.
Jeko̩b la nʼo̩je̩ ahi ikoʼka oñ Iso̩ kwo oko awa, o̩la-wñ muda.
Tak Iso̩ ka ñwu Jeko̩b kakini, Agba, e̩ dʼuje̩wñ ekpikpa le̩ ñwu mi je̩, agba, todu o̩la-mi muda! Todu ku ma dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Ido̩m le̩ de̩.
Taku Jeko̩b kakini, E̩ mʼo̩da o̩mo̩gba-we̩ du ta ñwu mi la ejodudu ta.
Oñ Iso̩ kakini, Go, omi ache kʼu ku-i; ile e̩wñ oñ o̩da o̩mo̩gba ache ñwu mi ke?
Taku Jeko̩b kakini, Go̩ ñwu mi eñini-i ke. Tak i fu go̩ ñw u, oñ i mʼo̩da o̩mo̩gba-wñ du ta ñwu Jeko̩b la.
Taku Jeko̩b mʼakala kpai uje̩wñ e̩gwa le̩ du ñw Iso̩, oñ i je̩, i la ñmo̩, tak i kwane̩, i le wñ. Abe̩le̩ Iso̩ fʼo̩da o̩mo̩gba-wñ do̩ rʼibe̩te̩.
Aise̩k lewa Ge̩rar; owñ kpai Abime̩le̩k kpalo
Tak ukpo̩ta ño̩ dʼane̩ le̩ akpa, kʼi chʼojoji ñw ukpo̩ta ejodudu e-ki kpa adiko Ebraham le̩. Oñ Aise̩k nyi Ge̩rar ugbo Abime̩le̩k onu abo Filistia.
Taku Jihofa kwotejugede ñw u, i kakini, E̩ ki gwo̩ru nyʼIjipti no; e̩ kwogugu oj ane̩ e-kʼu naka ñw e̩.
Ge̩ne̩ ane̩-i, tak u nadʼugbo-we̩, oñ nade̩nyo̩ ñw e̩; todu nakʼane̩-i du ñw uwe̩ kpai ugbe̩-we̩, alu kʼu go̩ ñw Ebraham ata-we̩ le̩, abe̩le̩ nache.
Naño̩ je̩ ñw ugbe̩-we̩ ki wewe nyo̩gba dab awo ojale, oñ nakʼane̩-i du ñw ugbe̩-we̩; omi la ade̩nyo̩ ñw abo uche̩ichi du ane̩-ile̩-i lef ugbe̩-we̩:
todabu kʼEbraham gbʼomu-mi gbo̩, kʼi ño̩ fejute̩ e̩wñ kʼu du ñw u kʼi de kpai uko̩-mi kʼu te̩ ñw u, kpai uhio̩me̩-mi, kpai uko̩-o̩la-mi.
Abe̩le̩ Aise̩k kwogugu Ge̩rar.
Oñ abo unyi le̩ tʼe ene o̩la o̩ya-wñ, i kakini, O̩maye-mi i che; todu i chokpo eka kʼo̩ya-wñ, tode̩gba kʼabo emi adʼumi kpa todu Ribe̩ka, i ka; todu kʼowñ chʼuto̩ eju.
Oñ i lewatu abu kʼi do̩mo̩ kpo̩kpe̩ tak Abime̩le̩k, onu abo Filistia le̩, nyʼope go, oñ i li abu kʼAise̩k ache̩ñwe̩le̩ kpai Ribe̩ka o̩ya-wñ.
Tak Abime̩le̩k fʼAise̩k do̩, i ka ñw u kakini, Go, ochochi, o̩ya-we̩ i che; abʼe̩ le kʼe̩ ka kʼowñ chʼo̩maye-we̩? Tak Aise̩k ka ñw u kakini, Todabu kʼu kakini, Tode̩gba kʼu naku todu-wñ.
Oñ Abime̩le̩k kakini, E̩wñ chʼe-kʼe̩ che wa-i? I ma gbegbe n, e̩ne̩ʼka ma bʼo̩ya-we̩ dachi, oñ uwe̩ ma je̩ ñw a fʼudu fe̩.
Tak Abime̩le̩k hi amone̩ le̩ du owu kakini, E̩ne̩ du ki dʼo̩wo̩kado e̩ne̩ kide̩ abe̩k o̩ya-wñ, ekpa ma akpa e̩ne̩ le̩ chuu.
Tak Aise̩k fʼe̩wñ gbe̩ ane̩ le̩, oñ i nʼawo ñw u ogume̩lu o̩do̩ le̩ gbage̩de̩. Jihofa la de̩nyo̩ ñw u,
oñ e̩ne̩ le̩ mud anana, i nanana nana nyo̩gba waa gbogbo tak i mud anana ololo.
E̩wñ ukpa-wñ chʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini kpai amokuno̩, amikono-wñ laño̩ wewe; tak abo Filistia kwolie̩na-wñ. 15(Aluka obuga du kʼamadu ata-wñ gwa adiko Ebraham ata-wñ, abo Filistia nʼike̩te̩ fukaji.)
Tak Abime̩le̩k ka ñw Aise̩k kakini, Kwo bʼuwa te̩; todu e̩ gbiti tʼuwa le nana me̩.
Abe̩le̩ Aise̩k kwo̩mo̩ le̩, oñ i fʼunyabo-wñ fa o̩go̩wo Ge̩rar, i la kwogugu o̩mo̩.
Aise̩k laño̩ dabi fʼobuga omi le̩ gwa ge̩, owñ chʼe-ku ma gwa adiko Ebraham ata-wñ; todu abo Filistia fukaji abu kʼEbraham leku; i ño̩ dʼodu-wñ alu kʼata-wñ dʼodu-wñ lale.
Tak amadu Aise̩k gwa o̩go̩wo le̩, ma la fʼobuga e-kʼomi-wñ abi kwef ane̩ li.
Tak abo ku ma dejutʼame̩wño̩re̩ Ge̩rar tukana kpai abo ku ma dejutʼame̩wño̩re̩ Aise̩k, ma kakini, Omi le̩ awa ne̩. Abe̩le̩ i dʼodu obuga le̩ ko̩ E̩se̩k todabu ku ma tukana kpai owñ.
Taku ma ño̩ fʼobuga omune̩ gwa, ma laño̩ tukana e-le̩ ge̩; oñ i dʼodu e-le̩ ko Sitna.
Oñ i kwʼo̩mo̩, i fʼobuga omune̩ gwa, ma ño̩ tukana e-le ge̩ n; i la dʼodu e-le̩ ko Rehobo̩t,  i kakini, Todu Jihofa fʼuña fe̩ ñw a fai me̩, a ñʼabi amo̩ma wewe ane̩-i.
Tak i kwʼo̩mo̩ le tu Birshiba.
Oñ Jihofa kwotejugede ñw u odu o̩jo̩ le̩, i kakini, Omi, O̩jo̩ ata-we̩ Ebraham le̩ de̩; e̩ ki chokpo n, todu kʼomi dʼugbo-we̩, u ñʼade̩nyo̩ ñw e̩, nache kʼugbe̩-we̩ ki wewe nyo̩gba todu adu-mi Ebraham.
Tak i fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ kpa o̩mo̩, oñ i fʼodu Jihofa do̩, i laño̩ fʼunyabo-wñ fa o̩mo̩ ge̩. O̩mo̩ amadu Aise̩k laño̩ fʼobuga gwa ge̩.
Tak Abime̩le̩k kpai Ahusat, onuku-wñ, kpai Fiko̩l onu ogu-wñ kwo Ge̩rar nyʼugbo-wñ.
Oñ Aise̩k ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩wñ chi ku me̩ wʼugbo-mi, abu ku me̩ chʼulaka-mi ku me̩ la fʼumi ne kwugbo me̩?
Ma kakini, A li ejugede pee ka ki Jihofa dʼugbo-we̩; oñ a kakini, kʼawa ki go̩ ñw o̩la-wa, owñ chʼawa kpai uwe̩, kʼa kpʼalo kpai uwe̩,
ka kʼuwe̩ ache wa e̩bie̩ne̩ n, alu kʼawa ma do̩wo̩kado uwe̩ n, kʼawa ma che uwe̩ abu du n, chai e̩nyo̩ kate, kʼa ño̩ je̩ ñw e̩ lo kpai ure̩do̩. Uwe̩ mud e̩ne̩ ki Jihofa de̩nyo̩ ñw u fai me̩.
Tak i fʼo̩je̩ ojo hi ñwu ma, oñ ma fʼe̩wñ je̩, ma la ñmo̩.
Oñ ma takpa kwane̩ odudu-wñ, ma la go̩ ñw o̩la-ma; tak Aise̩k fʼahite̩-ma che, oñ ma kwʼugbo-wñ le kpai ure̩do̩.
Oñ i lewatu o̩jo̩ le̩, kʼamadu Aise̩k lewa ka o̩la obuga ku ma gwa le̩ ñw u, ma ka ñw u kakini, Awa fʼomi li me̩.
Tak i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Shiba; todule̩ odu ewo le̩ ko̩ Birshiba gbogbo tʼeñini.
Oñ e̩gba kʼo̩do̩ Iso̩ jo̩ o̩gbo̩ meji i ne̩ Judit o̩ma onobule̩ Biri e̩ne̩ abo He̩t kpai Basemat o̩ma onobule̩ E̩lo̩n e̩ne̩ abo He̩t chʼo̩ya.
Ama le̩ chʼe̩wñ kʼe̩do̩ Aise̩k kpai Ribe̩ka kpabie̩.
Jeko̩b gba Aise̩k ibe kʼi mʼe̩nyo̩ le̩ gba
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba kʼAise̩k mud ogijo, kʼeju-wñ de̩ bulubulu, kʼi ma ño̩ gane̩ ge̩ n, i fʼo̩ma o̩gba-wñ Iso̩ do̩ wa, i ka ñw u kakini, O̩ma-mi; oñ i dohi ñw u kakini, Omi de̩.
Tak i kakini, Go ta, omi mud ogijo me̩, u la ma o̩jo̩ uku-mi n.
Todule̩, agba, mʼe̩wñ o̩de̩-we̩ ko fai, owñ chʼahiagba-we̩ kpai o̩o̩do̩-we̩, kʼe̩ nyʼegbili kʼe̩ kpʼe̩la ñwu mi,
kʼe̩ fʼo̩je̩ e̩rinyo̩ hi ñwu mi, o̩gʼe-kʼu natene le̩, kʼe̩ muduwa ñwu mi kʼu naje̩; todu kʼonugo-mi ki kadua ñw e̩ o̩gba tak u ku.
Ribe̩ka la heti agbo̩ e̩gba kʼAise̩k ko̩la ñw Iso̩, o̩ma-wñ le̩. Oñ Iso̩ nyʼegbili kʼi do̩de̩ e̩la, kʼi mʼu duwa.
Taku Ribe̩ka ka ñwu Jeko̩b o̩ma-wñ kakini, Go, omi gbo̩ abu kʼata-we̩ ko̩la ñw Iso̩, o̩maye-we̩, i kakini,
Mʼe̩la-o̩de̩ duwa ñwu mi kʼe̩ fʼo̩je̩ e̩rinyo̩ hi ñw omi, kʼomi kʼu je̩ kʼu kadua ñw e̩ eju Jihofa o̩gba tak u ku.
Todule̩, o̩ma-mi, e̩ nagbʼomu-mi kʼe̩ che alu kʼu nañwa ñw e̩-i.
Nyʼugbo ame̩wño̩re̩ egini faifai kʼe̩ mʼamo̩ma ewo meji ki nyo̩ ko̩ kwʼo̩mo̩ wa ñwu mi, kʼu nako ma che o̩je̩ e̩rinyo̩ todu ata-we̩, alu kʼi atene le̩;
tak uwe̩ ki dʼu wʼugbo ata-we̩ kʼi je̩, todu kʼi kadua ñw e̩ o̩gba tak i ku.
Jeko̩b muda ka ñwu Ribe̩ka iye-wñ kakini, Go Iso̩, o̩maye-mi le̩ chene̩ edudu o̩la nana, o̩la-mi la de̩ bo̩lo̩bo̩lo̩.
Ikani ata-mi ado̩wo̩chʼo̩la-mi tak i adabe̩ne̩ kʼu nachʼo uke̩ eju-wñ oñ nafʼama fa wa bʼo̩la-mi ma, i chʼe̩nyo̩ n.
Tak iye-wñ ka ñw u kakini, Ama-we̩ ki dʼoji-mi, o̩ma-mi; omu-mi e̩ gbagbo̩ kate, lo kʼe̩ mʼu ko wa.
Oñ i le namʼuma ko wʼugbo iye-wñ; tak iye-wñ fʼo̩je̩ e̩rinyo̩ hi alu kʼata-wñ tene.
Taku Ribe̩ka mʼe̩wñ o̩la Iso̩ o̩ma o̩gba-wñ le̩ e-ki nyo̩ ko, owñ chʼe-ki jʼugbo-wñ ef unyi, oñ i mudu tʼo̩la Jeko̩b, o̩ma-wñ kekele;
tak i mʼaño̩ amo̩ma ewo le̩ ko wenyu o̩wo̩-wñ kpai o̩fa-wñ ugbo ki de̩ be̩lo̩bo̩lo̩:
tak i mʼo̩je̩ e̩rinyo̩ kpai akala kʼi che ko nyʼo̩wo̩ o̩ma-wñ Jeko̩b.
Tak i lewa ugbo ata-wñ, i kakini, Ata-mi; oñ i dohi ñw u kakini, Omi de̩; uwe̩ e̩ne̩ de̩, o̩ma-mi?
Taku Jeko̩b ka ñw ata-wñ kakini, Omi Iso̩, o̩mo̩gba-we̩ de̩. Alu kʼe̩ ka ñwu mi u che me̩; e̩ kwane̩ gugu kʼe̩ je̩ e̩la-o̩de̩-mi, kʼonugo-we̩ ki kadua ñwu mi.
Ama Aise̩k ka ñw o̩ma-wñ kakini, Ab i le kʼe̩ hika li piopio abe̩i, o̩ma-mi? Oñ i kakini, Todabu ki Jihofa O̩jo̩-we̩ je̩ ñwu mi kʼu hika hiane̩.
Tak Aise̩k ka ñwu Jeko̩b kakini, Agba, te̩wa kʼu do̩wo̩chʼo̩la-we̩, o̩ma-mi, abe̩k uwe̩ chʼo̩ma-mi Iso̩ pio̩ abe̩k i chʼuwe̩ n.
Taku Jeko̩b te̩wʼugbo Aise̩k ata-wñ, oñ i do̩wo̩chʼo, i kakini, Omuko̩la-i chʼomu Jeko̩b, o̩wo̩-wñ muda chʼo̩wo̩ Iso̩.
I la mejuma owñ n, todabu kʼo̩wo̩-wñ chʼedudu alu kʼo̩wo̩ o̩maye-wñ Iso̩ de̩; todabe̩le̩ i kadua ñw u.
Oñ i kakini, Uwe̩ chʼo̩ma-mi Iso̩, ochochi? I kakini, Omi de̩.
Tak i ka ñw u kakini, Dʼu wʼugbo-mi kʼu naje̩ e̩la o̩de̩ o̩ma-mi, todu kʼonugo-mi ki kadua ñw e̩. Tak i mʼu du wʼugbo-wñ, i la fʼu je̩; i ño̩ mʼomi achiwebe̩te̩ma du ñw u, i la ñmo̩.
Tak ata-wñ Aise̩k ka ñw u kakini, Te̩wa fai, o̩ma-mi, kʼe̩ dʼalu kʼumi alu.
Tak i lewa dʼalu kʼo̩ alu; oñ i gbo̩ ikpe̩ e̩wñ o̩la-wñ, i kadua ñw u, i kakini,
Go, ikpe̩ o̩ma-mi
dabe̩ne̩ kʼikpe̩ oko ki Jihofa de̩nyo̩ ñw u.
O̩jo̩ ki du eli kwʼefojale ñw e̩,
kpai uro̩je̩ kwef ane̩ ile̩-i,
kpai o̩ka ololo, kpai omi achiwebe̩te̩ma.
O̩jo̩ ki je̩ ñw amone̩ che e̩wñ ñw e̩,
abo uche̩ichi ki danyeku ñw e̩.
Uwe̩ ki chʼodu amo̩maye-we̩,
O̩jo̩ ki je̩ ñw amo̩ma iye-we̩ danyeku ñw e̩.
Ama ki mu e̩ne̩ du ki nama ñw e̩,
O̩jo̩ ki de̩nyo̩ ñw e̩ne̩ du kʼi kadua ñw e̩!
Oñ i lewatu abu kʼAise̩k kadua ñw Jeko̩b kpa, abu ku Jeko̩b dubigba kwugbo Aise̩k ata-wñ pe̩, ababale̩, Iso̩, o̩maye-wñ la mojida kwʼo̩de̩-wñ wa.
I ño̩ hi o̩je̩ e̩rinyo̩, oñ i mʼu du wʼugbo ata-wñ. I ka ñw ata-wñ kakini, Ata-mi ki kwane̩ kʼi je̩ e̩la-o̩de̩ o̩ma-wñ-i, kʼonugo-we̩ ki kadua ñwu mi.
Tak Aise̩k ata-wñ ka ñw u kakini, Uwe̩ e̩ne̩ de̩? Oñ ikakini, Omi o̩ma-we̩, o̩mo̩gba-we̩, Iso̩ de̩.
Tak o̩la Aise̩k ro̩wo̩ ega tabale, i kakini, Mak e̩ne̩ dʼe̩la o̩de̩ wʼugbo mi, kʼomi ño̩ je̩ chaka o̩gba tak e̩ wa-i? Omi la mʼadua ko ñw u me̩. Ochochi, ede̩nyo̩ ma ade̩nyo̩ ñw u chuu.
E̩gba kʼIso̩ gbʼo̩la kʼata-wñ ka, i kwo kwa anyanyi tabale̩, i ka ñw ata-wñ kakini, Kadua ñwu mi, ata-mi, omi onugo, ge̩.
Tak i kakini, O̩maye-we̩ wa dʼo̩wo̩ yʼumi eju, oñ i mʼe̩nyo̩-we̩ gba.
Tak i kakini, Odu-wñ ku ma do̩ ko̩ Jeko̩b chʼeju-wñ n? Todu onu meji kʼi dʼo̩wo̩ dʼomi agbe̩re̩-i de̩. I bʼumi gba ugugu o̩mo̩gba; fai, go i ño̩ mʼe̩nyo̩-mi gba, Oñ i ño̩ kakini, Uwe̩ do̩wo̩mʼe̩nyo̩ O̩jo̩ du tane̩ todu mi n?
Tak Aise̩k dohi ñw Iso̩ kakini, Go, u mʼowñ du chʼodu-we̩, u la mʼamo̩maye-wñ ko chʼabuko̩lo̩-wñ, o̩ka kpai omi achiwebe̩te̩ma etito̩ chʼo̩wo̩ kʼu ne̩ kʼo̩ dago. O̩ma-mi, e̩wñ nafiʼache todu we̩ ta?
Tak Iso̩ ka ñw ata-wñ kakini, Ata-mi, e̩nyo̩ kʼe̩ ne̩ chʼokate? Kadua ñwu mi, tʼomi onugo ge̩, O̩, ata-mi. Tak Iso̩ dʼomu dago, araku.
Tak Aise̩k, ata-wñ, dohi ñw u kakini,
Go, ef uro̩je̩ ane̩-ile̩-i oñ o̩do̩-we̩ ade̩,
i ñʼadʼef eli e-efojale ate̩-i.
O̩kwo̩chageli oñ uwe̩ ane̩ tene uje̩-wñ,
uwe̩ ñʼache e̩wñ ñw o̩maye-we̩ ge̩;
ama i awatu e̩gba kʼe̩ mujada tane̩,
uwe̩ agu oli uno̩lo̩-wñ che̩ bʼo̩lo̩-we̩ te̩.
Oñ Iso̩ chulaka Jeko̩b todu adua kʼata-wñ ko ñw u, tak Iso̩ ka ef e̩do̩-wñ kakini, O̩jo̩ kʼu nadeku ata-mi me̩ro̩wo̩; e̩gbale̩ tak u nadʼo̩maye-mi Jeko̩b kpa.
Ma muda dʼo̩la Iso̩, o̩mo̩gba-wñ le̩, ka ñwu Ribe̩ka; oñ i kpʼone̩ ado̩ Jeko̩b o̩ma-wñ kekele, i ka ñw u kakini. Go, Iso̩, o̩maye-we̩ anyi o̩la-wñ e̩do̩ ugbo we̩, kʼi adʼe̩ kpa.
Fai todule̩ o̩ma-mi, e̩ nagbʼomu-mi gbo̩; kwane̩, kʼe̩ ra nyʼugbo Le̩ban, o̩maye-mi e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, Haran,
kʼe̩ bʼo̩ nʼo̩jo̩ je̩ o̩mo̩ pe̩, gbogbo tʼe̩gba kʼuke̩do̩fulu o̩maye-we̩ murida;
gbogbo tʼe̩gba kʼuwe̩do̩ o̩maye-we̩ rida bʼe̩ te̩, kʼi gbenyo̩ e-kʼuwe̩ chʼo̩; e̩gbale̩ tak u nakpʼone̩ wa adʼe̩ kwo o̩mo̩. E̩wñ chi kʼu nadeku ame̩ meji o̩jo̩ kate?
Taku Ribe̩ka ka ñw Aise̩k kakini, Edeju kʼu deju-i kʼumi o̩la noji amo̩ma onobule̩ He̩t. Iche̩wñ ku Jeko̩b fʼo̩ya ne̩ ef amo̩ma onobule̩ He̩t kʼi dʼalu kʼabo-i de̩, owñ chʼonobule̩ ane̩-iʼka, e̩wñ chʼe̩nyo̩ kʼudeju-mi ali?
Jeko̩b nyʼatene o̩ya
Tak Aise̩k fu Jeko̩b do̩, oñ i kadua ñw u, i la fʼuko̩ te̩ ñw u, i ka ñw u kakini, E̩ ki nʼo̩ya ef abobule̩ Kenan-i no.
Kwane̩, kʼe̩ lo tu Padan-aram, tʼunyi Be̩tue̩l ata iye-we̩; o̩mo̩ e̩ nʼo̩ya-we̩ kwo, ef amo̩ma onobule̩ Leban, o̩maye iye-we̩ le̩.
O̩jo̩ Odo̩bao̩gagu ki de̩nyo̩ ñw e̩, kʼi je̩ ñw e̩ nʼugbe̩, kʼe̩ wewe nyo̩gba, todu kʼuwe̩ ki mud ujeju amone̩.
I ki ño̩ mʼe̩nyo̩ Ebraham du ñw e̩, kpai ugbe̩-we̩ manyʼuwe̩ ge̩, todu kʼuwe̩ ki nʼane̩ ugbo kʼe̩ ge̩ne̩-i, e-ki Jihofa du ñw Ebraham!
Abe̩le̩ Aise̩k fu Jeko̩b kpe̩ le; oñ i le tu Padan-aram ugbo Leban, o̩ma Be̩tue̩l, e̩ne̩ Siria le̩, owñ chʼe-kʼi chʼo̩maye Ribe̩ka, iye Jeko̩b kpai Iso̩.
Iso̩ la li abu kʼAise̩k kadua ñwu Jeko̩b kʼi ño̩ fʼu kpe̩ le tu Padan-aram, kʼi nʼo̩ya kwʼo̩mo̩, i ño̩ li abu kʼi kadua ñw u kʼi ño̩ fʼuko̩ te̩ ñw u kakini, Uwe̩ ki nʼo̩ya ef abobule̩ Kenan in.
I ño̩ li ka ku Jeko̩b la gbʼomu ata-wñ kpai iye-wñ gbo̩, kʼi la le tu Padan-aram.
Abu kʼIso̩ li ka kʼabobule̩ Kenan bie̩ne̩ eju Aise̩k ata-wñ,
tak Iso̩ le tugbo Ishmae̩l oñ i fu Mahalat o̩ma Ishmae̩l, ki chʼo̩ma Ebraham, o̩maye Nebaio̩t ne̩ chʼo̩ya-wñ, manyʼamo̩ya-wñ kʼi ne̩ akwoubi le̩.
Jeko̩b nʼo̩na Be̩te̩l
Oñ Jeko̩b kwo Birshiba, i le tʼo̩wo̩ Haran.
I lewa ugboʼka, oñ i ru o̩mo̩ gbogbo ñw o̩jo̩, todabu kʼolu tunyane̩. Oñ i mʼokuta o̩mo̩ oka du, i mʼoji-wñ du nʼo, oñ i kwodachi o̩mo̩ kʼi lolu.
Tak i nʼo̩na, go, agube dago ane̩-ile̩, oji-wñ la te̩ gbogbo kado efojale; go, amonuche̩ O̩jo̩ jʼo̩la-wñ ate̩gu, ma la agwo̩ru!
Go, Jihofa la dago ugbo oji-wñ ate̩, i kakini, Omi che Jihofa, O̩jo̩ Ebraham, ata-we̩ kpai O̩jo̩ Aise̩k; ane̩ kʼuwe̩ dachi oji-wñ le̩, nadu ñw e̩ kpai ugbe̩-we̩;
ugbe̩-we̩ la adabu ebutu ane̩. Uwe̩ la akpatuka tʼo̩wo̩ olane̩ kpai o̩wo̩ olodudu kpai o̩wo̩ o̩pata mejeji; oñ ef uwe̩ kpai ef ugbe̩-we̩ ma la ade̩nyo̩ ñw abo akwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi du ane̩-ile̩-i.
Go, omi la dʼugbo-we̩, nafʼe̩ de ugbo du kʼe̩ nyi, u ñʼadʼe̩ dabi tʼoj ane̩-i ge̩; todu natʼuwe̩ no̩ n, gbogbo tak ufʼe̩wñ kʼomi ka o̩la-wñ ñw e̩ che.
Taku Jeko̩b mʼolu ji, oñ i kakini, Ochochi, Jihofa dʼugbo-i; omi la ma n.
Tak i kwochokpo, i kakini, Emi nʼubailo gboo! Ugbo-i chʼugbo omune̩ n, unyi O̩jo̩ de̩, alaku e-efojale la de̩-i.
Taku Jeko̩b takpa kwane̩ odudu, oñ i mʼokuta kʼi dʼoji no le̩ du, i la mʼu du gwanyʼane̩ dago. I mʼekpo du-danyu oji-wñ.
I dʼodu ugbo kide̩ ko̩ Be̩te̩l; odu ewo le̩ muda ko̩ Luz e̩gba ejodudu.
Taku Jeko̩b fʼoji da kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼO̩jo̩ adʼugbo mi, kʼi ade mi o̩na kʼu nale-i, kʼi adʼuje̩wñ ñwu mi je̩, kʼi adʼukpo ñwu mi bʼo̩la ma,
todu kʼu ño̩ dabi wʼunyi ata-mi kpai ure̩do̩ ge̩, e̩gbale̩ taku Jihofa amud O̩jo̩-mi,
e̩gbale̩ tak okuta kʼomi gwanyane̩ dago-i achʼunyi O̩jo̩; e̩wñ du kʼuwe̩ ako ñwu mi nadʼukpe̩ke̩gwa-wñ ñw uwe̩ chuu.
Jeko̩b dʼugbo Leban; i mu Lea kpai Reche̩l ko chʼo̩ya
Taku Jeko̩b mʼe̩re̩ ko nyʼule̩-wñ, oñ i lewa ane̩ abo olodudu.
Oñ i go, go obugaʼka dʼoko le̩, i la go, ujo̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ egini me̩ta dachi kpe̩nyʼu o̩mo̩; todu ma kpa omi ñw ame̩wño̩re̩ egini kwef obuga le̩. Okuta ki nʼalu obuga le̩ chenana.
E̩gba kʼujo̩ ujo̩ a mala du jeju jʼo̩mo̩, taku ma mʼokuta li bʼalu obuga te̩, oñ ma kpa omi ñw amala, taku ma dʼokuta le̩ dabi nʼalu obuga e̩gu-wñ.
Oñ Jeko̩b ka ñwu ma kakini, Amo̩maye-mi, ugbo me̩ kwo? Oñ ma ka ñw u kakini, Abo Haran a che.
Oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, Ame̩ chema Le̩ban o̩ma Ne̩ho̩r? Oñ ma kakini, A chemʼo̩.
Tak i ka ñwu ma kakini, I raa? Oñ ma kakini, I raa gbo; go, Reche̩l o̩ma-wñ onobule̩, kpai ame̩wño̩re̩ egini awa-i!
Tak i kakini, Go, i chʼo̩ro̩ka gbaa ta, i la chʼiko kʼame̩wñ ukpa ajejujʼugbo okate de̩ n; me̩ fʼomiofo kpa ñw ame̩wño̩re̩ egini ku me̩ lo tekedu e̩wñ ñwu ma je̩.
Oñ ma kakini, A neke che n, gbogbo tak ujo̩ ujo̩ amala du jejujo̩, ku ma mʼokuta li bʼalu obuga te̩, e̩gba le̩ tak a kpʼomi ñw amala ñmo̩.
Abu kʼi do̩mo̩ ako̩la kpai ama ta, Reche̩l kʼame̩wño̩re̩ ata-wñ egini wa; todu owñ adejute̩ ma.
Abe̩le̩ e̩gba ku Jeko̩b li Reche̩l o̩ma onobule̩ e-Le̩ban o̩me̩nyi-wñ kpai ame̩wño̩re̩ egini Le̩ban o̩me̩nyi-wñ le̩, taku Jeko̩b te̩me̩ru, i la mʼokuta le̩ li bʼalu obuga te̩, oñ i kpʼomi ñw ame̩wño̩re̩ egini Le̩ban o̩me̩nyi-wñ ñmo̩.
Taku Jeko̩b dʼalu ko̩ Reche̩l alu, oñ i dʼomu-wñ dago, araku.
Taku Jeko̩b ka ñwu Reche̩l ka kʼowñ chʼefu ata-wñ, kʼowñ chʼo̩ma Ribe̩ka; tak i fule nyʼaka ñw ata-wñ.
Oñ i lewatʼe̩gba ku Le̩ban gbʼinabali Jeko̩b o̩ma o̩maye-wñ onobule̩, i ra ledʼo, i gbʼo̩ mʼe̩do̩, i dʼalu kʼo̩ alu, oñ i mʼu du wʼunyi-wñ. Tak i kʼe̩re̩ e̩wñ-i du ñwu Le̩ban.
Oñ Le̩ban ka ñw u kakini, Ochochi, uwe̩ chʼachiku-mi kpai o̩re̩la-mi! Tak i bʼo̩ gugu ochuʼka.
Taku Le̩ban ka ñwu Jeko̩b kakini, Todabu kʼuwe̩ chʼo̩maye-mi, todule̩ uwe̩ ñʼache e̩wñ ñwu mi ofofo? Ka ñwu mi, e̩wñ nadu rʼuwe̩ o̩me̩?
Leban la chenʼamo̩ma onobule̩ meji; odu e-ogijo ko̩ Lea, odu e-kekele ko̩ Reche̩l.
Eju Lea la de̩ no̩ko̩; ama año̩la Reche̩l chefe̩reju, eju-wñ la achʼuto̩.
Oñ Jeko̩b fe̩do̩ Reche̩l, i kakini, Nachʼuko̩lo̩ o̩do̩ mebie ñw e̩ todu Reche̩l o̩ma-we̩ kekele-i.
Taku Leban kakini, I nyo̩ kʼu nadʼu ñw e̩ tʼedʼu ñw e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ omune̩ le; e̩ bʼumi gugu ke.
Abe̩le̩ Jeko̩b chʼuko̩lo̩ o̩do̩ mebie todu Reche̩l, i dab o̩jo̩ ke̩ke̩ eju-wñ tod efe̩do̩ kʼi afe̩do̩ owñ.
Taku Jeko̩b ka ñwu Leban kakini, Mʼo̩ya-mi du ñwu mi todu o̩jo̩-mi jo̩ kpa me̩, kʼu nagudu nyʼejefu ugbo-wñ.
Taku Leban fʼabo ewo le̩ du do̩ jeju, oñ i fʼuje̩wñ uyo̩ hi.
Oñ e̩gba ane̩, i mu Lea, o̩ma-wñ du, oñ i mudu wʼugbo Jeko̩b; tak i nyʼejefu ugbo-wñ. 24(Leban ño̩ mu Zilpa, adu-wñ onobule̩, du ñwu Lea, o̩ma-wñ, kʼi chʼadu-wñ.)
Oñ i lewatʼodudu-wñ, go, Lea de̩, tak i ka ñwu Leban kakini, E̩wñ chʼe-kʼuwe̩ che mi-i? Omi chʼuko̩lo̩ ñw e̩ todu Reche̩l in? E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ chʼumi uji-i?
Oñ Leban kakini, I chʼabe̩le̩ oñ a che o̩ja-wa n, awa dʼe-kekele kpʼo̩ko̩ dʼo̩gba ñw o̩mo̩gba n.
O̩jo̩ mebie e-i ki jo̩, tak a ño̩ du ekeji-wñ ñw e̩ todu uko̩lo̩ kʼe̩ ñʼache ñwu mi o̩do̩ mebie omune̩.
Oñ Jeko̩b fʼabe̩le̩ che̩, i la fʼo̩jo̩ mebie-wñ je̩; tak i mu Reche̩l, o̩ma-wñ le̩ du ñw u chʼo̩ya ge̩. 29(Taku Leban mu Bilha, adu-wñ onobule̩, du ñwu Reche̩l, o̩ma-wñ, kʼi chʼadu-wñ.)
Tak i ño̩ le tejefu ugbo Reche̩l ge̩, i la fe̩do̩ Reche̩l tu Lea le. I ño̩ chʼuko̩lo̩ ñw u o̩do̩ mebie omune̩.
Oñ abu ku Jihofa li ka ku ma chulaka Lea, i mʼabio̩ma-wñ bi; Reche̩l muda chʼagaji.
Taku Lea fefunyo̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Rube̩n; todu i kakini, Todabu ku Jihofa fʼo̩bata-mi go; todu ifai tak o̩ko̩-mi afe̩do̩ mi.
Oñ i ño̩ fefunyo̩ ge̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi, i kakini, Todabu ku Jihofa gbo̩ ka ku ma chulaka-mi, todule̩ i ño̩ mʼe-i du ñwu mi ge̩, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Sime̩o̩n.
Tak i ño̩ fefunyo̩ ge̩ i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi ge̩, i kakini, Fai one̩de̩-i tak o̩ko̩-mi adama kpʼomi, todabu kʼomi fʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ me̩ta bi ñw u; todule̩ ma dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Lifai.
Oñ i ño̩ fefunyo̩ ge̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi, i kakini, O̩ne̩de̩-i nagogbodo̩ Jihofa; todule̩ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Juda; tak i we ebi o̩ma.
Amo̩ma Jeko̩b
Tak e̩gba ku Reche̩l li ka kʼi ma bi o̩ma ñwu Jeko̩b in, i kwojogu o̩maye-wñ; oñ i ka ñwu Jeko̩b kakini, Kʼamo̩ma ñwu mi cho̩kpo̩ni naku!
Tak e̩do̩ Jeko̩b kwane̩, i we̩do̩ ru Reche̩l. I kakini, Omi koji O̩jo̩, kʼi gbʼo̩na o̩ma ebi nyʼuwe̩?
Oñ i kakini, Adu-mi onobule, Bilha la de̩; nyʼejefu ugbo-wñ, kʼowñ ki bi o̩ma nʼumi kʼomi kʼu ño̩ ne amo̩ma lʼugbo-wñ.
Tak i mu Bilha, adu-wñ, du ñw u chʼo̩ya; oñ Jeko̩b le tejefu ugbo-wñ.
Taku Bilha fefunyo̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi ñwu Jeko̩b.
Taku Reche̩l kakini, O̩jo̩ fʼajo̩-mi ka me̩, i ño̩ gbʼomu-mi i la mʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du ñwu mi; todule̩ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Dan.
Taku Bilha, adu Reche̩l le̩, ño̩ fefunyo̩ ge̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ekeji bi ñwu Jeko̩b.
Taku Reche̩l kakini, Uja e-O̩jo̩ oñ u du bʼo̩maye-mi ja, u la fʼu du, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Naftali.
E̩gba ku Lea li ka kʼi ma ño̩ bi o̩ma ge̩ n, i mu Zilpa, adu-wñ onobule̩ du, oñ i mʼu du ñwu Jeko̩b, kʼi chʼo̩ya-wñ.
Taku Zilpa adu Lea le̩, fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi ñwu Jeko̩b.
Oñ Lea kakini, Ojile de̩! Oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Gad.
Taku Zilpa, adu Lea, ño̩ fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ekeji bi ñwu Jeko̩b.
Oñ Lea kakini, E̩do̩-mi bo̩ me̩! Todu amo̩ma onobule̩ ado̩ mi kʼe̩ne̩ ki gbede; oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Ashe̩r.
Taku Rube̩n le tʼoko iko ku ma jʼo̩ka, i fʼe̩ro oli o̩lafe̩ li oko o̩mo̩, oñ i mʼu ko wʼugbo iye-wñ, Lea. Taku Reche̩l ka ñwu Lea kakini, E̩ bu e̩ro oli o̩lafe̩ e-o̩ma-we̩ le̩ ñwu mi, agba.
Oñ i kakini, O̩ko̩-mi kʼe̩ gba, e̩wñ ke̩ke̩ i che eju-we̩? E̩ ño̩ tene kʼe̩ mʼe̩ro oli o̩lafe̩ e-o̩ma-mi du ge̩? Taku Reche̩l kakini, Todule̩ i abʼuwe̩ dachi odu-i koji e̩ro o̩lafe̩ e-o̩ma-we̩ le̩.
Tak e̩gba ku Jeko̩b doji kwʼoko awa e̩gba ane̩, oñ Lea dufu aledʼo, i kakini, E̩ wʼejefu ugbo mi chuu; todu omi mʼe̩ro oli o̩lafe̩ e-o̩ma-mi du rʼo̩me̩-we̩. Tak i bʼo̩ dachi odu o̩jo̩ le̩.
Oñ O̩jo̩ nyu Lea eti, oñ i fefunyo̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e̩ke̩lu bi ñwu Jeko̩b.
Taku Lea kakini, O̩jo̩ fʼo̩me̩ ra ñwu mi me̩, todabu kʼu mʼadu-mi onobule̩ du ñw o̩ko̩-mi; oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Isakar.
Taku Lea fʼefu omune̩ nyo̩ ge̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e̩ke̩fa bi ñwu Jeko̩b.
Oñ Lea kakini, O̩jo̩ mʼukpe̩ ki nyo̩ du chʼumi ele me̩; fai o̩ko̩-mi abʼumi gugu, todabu kʼomi fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ me̩fa bi ñw u; oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Ze̩biulo̩n.
Anubi e-le̩ i la fʼo̩ma onobule̩ bi, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Daina.
Tak O̩jo̩ libekado Reche̩l, O̩jo̩ la nyʼowñ eti, oñ i mʼuji o̩ma ebi-wñ chi.
Oñ i fefunyo̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi, i kakini, O̩jo̩ mʼumi anyo̩ eju ko me̩;
oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Jose̩f, kakini, Jihofa kʼi mʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ omune̩ du manyʼu ñwu mi ge̩!
Oñ i lewatu abu ku Reche̩l fu Jose̩f bi, Jeko̩b ka ñwu Leban kakini, Tʼumi no̩ kʼu nadabi tʼe̩gu-mi, kpai ane̩-mi.
Mʼamo̩ya-mi kpai amo̩ma-mi e-kʼomi chʼuko̩lo̩ ñw e̩ todu ma le̩ ko ñwu mi kʼe̩ je̩ ñwu mi lo; tod uwe̩ chemʼuko̩lo̩ kʼomi che ñw e̩.
Leban muda ka ñw u kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ li mi eju, gugu emi ta, agba; todu kʼu go go ño̩ go ka ki chʼutod uwe̩ oñ Jihofa de̩nyo̩ ñwu mi.
I ño̩ kakini, Fʼalu o̩me̩ kʼu nara ñw e̩ ka ñwu mi, kʼu nadu ñw e̩.
Oñ i ka ñw u kakini, Uwe̩ chemʼalu kʼomi chʼuko̩lo̩ ñw e̩, kpai alu kʼame̩wñ ukpa-we̩ de̩ ugbo mi.
Todu e̩wñ kʼuwe̩ ne̩ tak omi wa de̩ re, oñ i mud o̩be̩le̩ke̩te̩ jo̩-i; Jihofa la de̩nyo̩ ñw e̩ ugbo du kʼomi dʼe̩re̩ atʼo̩. E̩gba oñ omi ñʼachʼuko̩lo̩ unyi e-mi onugo ke?
Jeko̩b fʼugbeju che kʼane̩-wñ ki nyo̩gba
Oñ i kakini, E̩wñ nadu ñw e̩? Taku Jeko̩b kakini, Uwe̩ ñʼadʼe̩wñ du ñw omi ge̩ n; iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ ache e̩wñ-i kate todu mi mak u nadabi kʼuje̩wñ ñw ujo̩ ame̩wño̩re̩-we̩ je̩ kʼu ño̩ dejutʼo̩.
Nale gu ef ujo̩ ame̩wño̩re̩-we̩ du eñini, kʼu mʼe̩wño̩re̩ egini adibabala kpai e-e̩kina chaka ko kpai e̩wño̩re̩ egini edudu du ki jʼef amala, kpai e-e̩kina kpai e-adibabala ku ma jʼef amewo; tak abo e-le̩ achʼe̩wñ uro̩me̩-mi.
O̩kpakpa-mi adohi todu mi o̩jo̩ o̩na, e̩gba kʼe̩ wa tʼumi ene e̩wñ uro̩me̩-mi ki dʼo̩gba-we̩. E-du ki ma chʼadibabala kpai e-e̩kina ef amewo n, kpai e-edudu ef amala n, e-le̩ dʼugbo mi mak oji u ji.
Taku Leban kakini, I nyo̩! i ki de̩ alu kʼe̩ ka ke.
Tak o̩jo̩ le̩ Leban mʼamobuko̩ ku ma chʼe̩kina kpai e-adibabala ko, kpai amolewo du ku ma chʼadibabala kpai e̩kina, kpai e-du ki ne̩ efufu o̩la, kpai e-edudu du ku ma jʼef amala, oñ i mʼu ko jʼef o̩wo̩ amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩;
tak i mʼule̩ o̩jo̩ me̩ta du tʼagbagba owñ kpai Jeko̩b; Jeko̩b la nakʼuje̩wñ ñw ame̩wño̩re̩ Leban ki bo̩ je̩.
Taku Jeko̩b mʼe̩to̩ oli poplar kpai e-almo̩nd kpai e-plen emimi ko, oñ i fʼo̩la-wñ po̩ e̩kina efufu, i che kʼefufu ki dʼef oli le̩ ki kwotejugede.
Oñ i mʼoli kʼi po̩ le̩ ko dago o̩gba ame̩wño̩re̩ egini ef o̩go̩lo̩ ugbo kʼomi acha nyʼef agbada ugbo kʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini awa ñmʼomi. Oñ e̩gba ku ma wa ñmʼomi o̩ko̩ kpai o̩ya o̩mo̩.
Tak ame̩wño̩re̩ egini le̩ fefunyo̩ ugbo oli le̩, oñ ma fʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini e̩kina kpai e-adibabala kpai e-e̩kina pepepe bi.
Taku Jeko̩b fʼamala kpe̩ru meji, oñ i mʼeju ame̩wño̩re̩ egini le̩ ko kparu e-e̩kina kpai e-edudu ku ma jʼef ame̩wño̩re̩ Leban egini; tak i mʼujo̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ e-owñ ko jʼo̩wo̩ʼka, i la ko ma jʼef ame̩wño̩re̩ egini e-Leban in.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba du kʼabo ku ma chenʼukpahiu tule ef ujo̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ egini le̩ anyefu, Jeko̩b la mʼoli le̩ ko jʼo̩gba ame̩wño̩re̩ egini ef o̩go̩lo̩ ku ma jʼef oli le̩ anyefu o̩mo̩,
ama e̩gba kʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini ku ma chʼe̩gbo wa, i la ko ma jʼefu-wñ n; abe̩le̩ abo e̩gbo chʼe-Leban, abo ku ma nʼukpahiu chʼe-Jeko̩b.
Abe̩le̩ e̩ne̩ le̩ nana nyo̩gba ololo, i la nʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini wewe, kpai amadu onobule̩, kpai amadu e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, kpai aminyakulumi kpai amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩.
Jeko̩b ra bi Leban te̩
Tak i gbʼo̩la kʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Leban aka kakini, Jeko̩b mʼe̩wñ ata-wa du ko; e̩wñ ata-wa oñ i du nʼojima-i du.
Oñ Jeko̩b li eju Leban, go, eju-wñ la dʼalu ki de̩ ugbo owñ akwoubi n.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Jeko̩b kakini, Mudabi tʼane̩ amata-we̩, ugbo ame̩fu-we̩, oñ nadʼugbo-we̩.
Taku Jeko̩b kpʼone̩ ado̩ Reche̩l kpai Lea wʼoko ugbo ame̩wño̩re̩-wñ egini.
I ka ñwu ma kakini, U cheli eju ata-me̩, kʼi ma dʼalu ki de̩ ugbo mi akwoubi n. O̩jo̩ ata-mi muda te̩tadʼugbo-mi.
Ame̩ la chema kʼukpahiu-mi du oñ omi ne̩ chuko̩lo̩ ñw ata-me̩.
Ata-me̩ muda chʼumi uji, i la mʼe̩wñ uro̩me̩-mi rida onu me̩gwa, O̩jo̩ muda je̩ ñw u che mi e̩bie̩ne̩ du n.
Iche̩wñ kʼi fʼabe̩i ka kakini, Abo e-e̩kina pe pe pe chʼe̩wñ uro̩me̩-we̩, e̩gbale̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ egini le̩ chaka fʼo̩ma e̩kina pe̩ pe pe̩ bi; iche̩wñ kʼi ka abe̩i kakini, Abo e-e̩kina añmo̩ro̩ achʼe̩wñ uro̩me̩-we̩, mak ame̩wño̩re̩ egini du fʼamo̩ma e̩kina añmo̩ro̩ bi.
Abu kʼO̩jo̩ mʼame̩wñ ukpa ata-me̩ ko kʼi la muko ñwu mi de̩-i.
Oñ i lewatʼadiko kʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini anyefu, u chi eju-mi nyate̩, u li ef o̩na kʼu na, go, amobuko̩ ku ma roko nʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini le̩ ubi chʼe̩kina añmo̩ro̩, kpai adibabala, kpai e-a dacha.
Tak onuche̩ O̩jo̩ le̩ ka ñwu mi ef o̩na-mi kʼu na le̩ kakini, Jeko̩b, oñ u kakini, Omi de̩!
I kakini, Chi eju-we̩ nyate̩ kʼe̩ go, amobuko̩ du ku ma roko nʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini ubi chʼe̩kina añmo̩ro̩, kpai adibabala, kpai adacha; todu omi fʼe̩wñ du ku Leban achʼuwe̩ li me̩.
Omi chʼO̩jo̩ Be̩te̩l, ugbo kʼe̩ dʼekpo danyʼokuta kʼe̩ du gwanyane̩ dago, ugbo kʼe̩ fʼoji da ñwu mi le̩. Kwane̩ kwʼoj ane̩-i dufu, kʼe̩ mudabi tʼoj ane̩ ugbo ku ma bi we̩.
Taku Reche̩l kpai Lea dohi ñw u kakini, Ukpe̩ ʼka abe̩k e̩wñ ogu bo̩ ñw a unyi ata-wa ge̩?
Awa dab ononojo eju-wñ n? Todu i mʼuwa ko ta, i la mʼo̩ko̩ ku ma ko rʼo̩me̩-wa ko kpabie̩ kpa me̩.
Todu e̩wñ anana du kʼO̩jo̩ bʼata-wa gba, e-le̩ awa kpai amo̩ma-wa ne̩; todule̩, e̩wñ du kʼO̩jo̩ ka ñw e̩, e̩ che.
Taku Jeko̩b kwane̩, oñ i mʼamo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩-wñ kpai amo̩ya-wñ ko gugu oji inyakulumi;
oñ i mʼame̩wñ ukpa-wñ ko chaka, kpai ane̩-wñ du kʼi ne̩ jo̩, owñ chʼame̩wñ ukpa-wñ kʼi gba, e-kʼi gbajo̩ Padan-aram le̩, kʼi nyʼugbo Aise̩k ata-wñ oj ane̩ Kenan.
E̩gbale̩ Leban le tekeja edudu ame̩wño̩re̩-wñ egini, Reche̩l la mʼamude oji ata-wñ ji.
Taku Jeko̩b muji le. Leban, abo Siria le̩, ma n, abu kʼi ma ka ñw u kʼi ara n.
Abe̩le̩ i mʼe̩wñ du kʼi ne̩ ko ra, oñ i kwane̩, i mudaba Yufretis, i fʼeju kparu uwo o̩wo̩ Gilead alo.
Tak o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta-wñ ma mudu ka ñwu Leban kakini, Jeko̩b ra le.
Oñ i mʼamo̩maye-wñ ko rʼubi, i ranʼo o̩jo̩ mebie; tak i lewa fʼu mu uwo Gilead.
O̩jo̩ la wʼugbo Leban, e̩ne̩ Siria le̩, ef o̩na odu, i ka ñw u kakini, E̩ fʼo̩la-we̩ de, e̩ ki kʼo̩la du ñwu Jeko̩b in, tʼe̩nyo̩ tʼe̩bie̩ne̩.
Taku Leban fu Jeko̩b mu. E̩gbale̩ Jeko̩b la fʼunyabo-wñ fa ane̩ uwo le̩ me̩, Leban kpai amo̩maye-wñ laño̩ fʼuru-ma mu ane̩ uwo Gilead le̩.
Taku Leban ka ñwu Jeko̩b kakini, E̩wñ e̩ che kʼe̩ ji lʼolo kʼomi ma ma n, kʼe̩ mʼamo̩monobule̩-mi ko dabe̩ne̩ kʼabo kʼogu je̩?
E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ ra maja maja, kʼe̩ ji lʼolo kwugbo mi, kʼe̩ ma ka ñwu mi n? kʼomi ma je̩ ñw e̩ lo kpai anyi kpai eli kpai eicha kpai umo-lo n?
Uwe̩ la je̩ ñwu mi dʼalu kʼamo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩-mi kpai onobule̩ alu n. Idada uwe̩ che-i.
U chene̩ o̩wo̩ ukpahiu kʼu nachʼuwe̩ e̩bie̩ne̩; O̩jo̩ e-ata-we̩ muda ko̩la ñwu mi odu eñini-i, kakini, Fʼo̩la-we̩ de, e̩ ki kʼo̩la e̩nyo̩ abe̩k e̩bie̩ne̩ ñwu Jeko̩b in.
Elo uwe̩ lo-i ukpe̩ kʼeju abunyi ata-we̩ anʼe̩ tabale, e̩wñ chi kʼe̩ mʼamo̩jo̩-mi ko?
Taku Jeko̩b dohi ka ñwu Leban kakini, Todabu kʼomi chokpo, todu u kakini, Tode̩gba kʼe̩ bʼumi gba amo̩monobule̩-we̩ oji ukpahiu.
E̩ne̩ du kʼe̩ li amo̩jo̩-we̩ ugbo-wñ, e̩ne̩ le̩ adeju n. Eju amo̩maye-wa-i e̩ namejuma e̩wñ ki chʼe-we̩ ki dʼugbo mi, kʼe̩ mudu. Jeko̩b la ma ka ku Reche̩l fʼoji le̩ ji n.
Taku Leban le tef unyabo Jeko̩b kpai ef unyabo Lea, i ño̩ le tʼef unyabo amadu onobule̩ meji le̩, i muda li n. Tak i kwʼef unyabo Lea dufu oñ i le tʼef unyabo Reche̩l.
Reche̩l la mʼamude oji le̩ ko jʼef ofidi inyakulumi, oñ i kwogugu oji-wñ. Taku Leban do̩wo̩cho ugbo du ef unyabo le̩, i la li n.
Oñ i ka ñw ata-wñ kakini, I ki bi odu-mi eju, ukpe̩ kʼu ma neke kwane̩ o̩gba-we̩ nʼ todu o̩ga onobule̩ dʼo̩la-mi. Abe̩le̩ i tejane̩, i muda li amude le̩ n.
Taku Jeko̩b we̩do̩, i mʼe̩ro̩la kobo̩ Leban; Jeko̩b la ka ñwu Leban kakini, E̩wñ chʼada-we̩ kʼu je̩? Ugbo oñ u dʼuwe̩ re, tak e̩ ra nʼomi una una-i?
Abu kʼe̩ do̩wo̩chʼane̩-mi du, ugbo ane̩ unyi-we̩ du kʼe̩ li de̩? Mʼu du gugu o̩gba amo̩maye-mi kpai amo̩maye-we̩ emi, ku ma ki fʼajo̩ agbagba awa meji ka.
O̩do̩ ogu kʼomi dʼugbo we̩ de̩-i; amole ala-we̩, kpai amole ewo-we̩ la kʼo̩ma-ma rinyo̩ n, u la kʼamokolo ef ame̩wño̩re̩-we̩ egini je̩ n.
E-kʼame̩la fana, omi la du wʼugbo we̩ n; omi oñ ofu-wñ bu; ef o̩wo̩-mi oñ e̩ gba, dagba ma muji o̩ro̩ka, dagba ma muji odu.
Abe̩le̩ u de̩; e̩gba o̩ro̩ka olu bʼumi o̩la je̩, oñ afu kpa mi odu, eju-mi la gbe̩.
O̩do̩ ogu-i u te̩te̩dʼef unyi-we̩; omi chuko̩lo̩ ñw e̩ o̩do̩ me̩gwe̩le̩ todu amo̩ma onobule̩-we̩ meji, u ño̩ che o̩do̩ me̩fa tod ame̩wño̩re̩-we̩ egini ge̩, uwe̩ la mʼe̩wñ uro̩me̩-mi rida onu me̩gwa.
I ma chʼabu kʼO̩jo̩ e-ata-mi, owñ chʼO̩jo̩ e-Ebraham, kpai e̩gahi Aise̩k ki dʼugbo mi n, uwe̩ ma je̩ ñwu mi le o̩wo̩ ofo ochochi. O̩jo̩ fʼo̩bata-mi kpai akanya o̩wo̩-mi li, oñ i dʼo̩la bi uwe̩ odu eñini.
Taku Le̩ban dohi ñwu Jeko̩b kakini, Amo̩ma onobule̩ le̩ chʼamo̩ma-mi, abimo̩to̩ le̩ la chʼabimo̩to̩-mi, ame̩wño̩re̩ egini-i la chʼame̩wño̩re̩-mi, o̩gbo̩ e̩wñ du kʼe̩ li-i chʼe-mi. Eñini-i, e̩wñ omi neke che amo̩ma-mi onobule̩-i, abe̩k amo̩ma e-ma ku ma bi?
Lewa ta, kʼa kpʼalo, omi kpai uwe̩; kʼi chʼe̩wñ ibenu agbagba omi kpai uwe̩.
Taku Jeko̩b mʼokuta du, oñ i mudu gwanyane̩ dago.
Taku Jeko̩b ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ kakini, Me̩ rʼokuta jo̩, oñ ma mʼokuta ko kpʼugbudu dago; ma la fʼe̩wñ je̩ ugbo ugbudu o̩mo̩.
Taku Le̩ban dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Jegar-sahaduta ama Jeko̩b dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Galid.
Oñ Le̩ban kakini, Ugbudu-i chʼe̩wñ ibenu agbagba omi kpai uwe̩ eñini. Todule̩ ma dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Galid,
kpai Mizpa ge̩, todu i kakini, Jihofa ki de agbagba omi kpai uwe̩, e̩gba kʼa kwo bʼomune̩ te̩.
Iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ fʼamo̩ma onobule̩-mi dema, i la che̩wñ kʼuwe̩ nʼo̩ya omune̩ manyʼamo̩ma-mi-i, e̩ne̩ du dʼugbo wa-i n; go, O̩jo̩ chʼe̩nibenu agbagba omi kpai uwe̩.
Taku Le̩ban ka ñwu Jeko̩b kakini, Gʼugbudu-i, kʼe̩ laño̩ gʼokuta e̩gwanyane̩-i e-kʼomi dudago agbagba omi kpai uwe̩.
Ugbudu-i ki chʼe̩wñ ibenu, okuta e̩gwanyane̩-i ki ño̩ chʼe̩wñ ibenu ge̩, ka kʼomi alegʼugbu-du-i du wʼugbo we̩ n, kʼuwe̩ ñʼalegʼugbudu-ikpai okuta e̩gwanyane̩-i du wʼugbo mi tod e̩bie̩ne̩ n.
O̩jo̩ Ebraham kpai O̩jo̩ Ne̩ho̩r, O̩jo̩ e-ata-ma, kʼifʼajo̩ ki dʼagbagba-wa ka. Taku Jeko̩b fʼe̩gahi ata-wñ Aise̩k go̩.
Taku Jeko̩b dʼe̩wñ iche̩bo̩ wa che oj uwo le̩, oñ i fʼamo̩maye-wñ do̩ wa ajʼuje̩wñ; ma la fʼuje̩wñ je̩, oñ ma kpo̩kpe̩ oj uwo le̩ gbogbo ñw o̩jo̩.
Taku Le̩ban kwane̩ odudu odudu, oñ i dalukalu amaaju-wñ kpai amo̩ma-wñ onobule̩, i la kadua ñwu ma; taku Le̩ban kwo̩mo̩ le, i mudabi tʼe̩gu-wñ.
Jeko̩b fʼo̩la mu kʼi de kpai Iso̩
Taku Jeko̩b mʼe̩re̩ ko̩ nyʼule̩-wñ alo, oñ amonuche̩ O̩jo̩ de kpai owñ.
Tak e̩gba ku Jeko̩b fʼuma li i kakini, Uru e-O̩jo̩ de̩! oñ i dʼodu ugbo kide̩ ko̩ Mahanaim.
Jeko̩b la fʼamonuche̩ kpe̩ tʼo̩gba-wñ nyʼugbo Iso̩ o̩maye-wñ, ane̩ Seir, kʼi chʼegbili Ido̩m.
I ka ñwu ma kakini, Abu ku me̩ aka ñw odu-mi Iso̩ de̩, kakini, Abu kʼadu-we̩ Jeko̩b ka de̩, kakini, U te̩tage̩ne̩ ugbo Le̩ban, u kpo̩kpe̩ o̩mo̩ gbogbo wʼifai;
u la chenʼamo̩kokuno̩ kpai amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩ kpai ame̩wño̩re̩ ojoji ojoji kpai amadu e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩; oñ u fʼone̩ kpe̩ wa-i kʼi ka ñw odu-mi, todu kʼe̩ li mi eju.
Tak amonuche̩ le̩ mudabi wʼugbo Jeko̩b, ma kakini, Awa lewʼugbo o̩maye-we̩ Iso̩, owñ onugo ledʼuwe̩ awa-i, one̩ ulo̩ko̩ jʼugbo-wñ.
Taku Jeko̩b railo ololo, e̩do̩-wñ chane̩ echʼo o̩bata; i fʼamone̩ ku ma jʼugbo-wñ kpe̩rʼujo̩ meji, kpai ame̩wño̩re̩ egini kpai amokuno̩ kpai aminyakulumi,
oñ i kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼIso̩ lewʼugbo ujo̩ʼka kʼi fʼuma kpa, mak ujo̩ ekeji afʼo̩ o̩wo̩.
Oñ Jeko̩b kakini, O̩jo̩ e-ata-mi Ebraham, kpai O̩jo̩ e-ata-mi Aise̩k, uwe̩ Jihofa kʼe̩ ka ñwu mi kakini, Mudabi tʼane̩-we̩, ugbo amefu-we̩, tak u nachʼe̩nyo̩ ñw e̩,
omi nyarʼe̩wñ ke̩ke̩ ki dʼef ufe̩de̩nyo̩ kʼe̩ che kpai ochochi du kʼuwe̩ duña adu-we̩-i, todu omi kpai o̩kpa-mi daba Jo̩rdan-i; fai u la mud ujo̩ meji me̩.
Narodubʼe̩ kʼe̩ mʼumi gba kwef o̩wo̩ o̩maye-mi, kwef o̩wo̩ Iso̩, todu ailo-wñ aba mi, tode̩gba kʼi adʼumi kpa, tʼiye, tʼo̩ma.
Uwe̩ la ka kʼuwe̩ ache e̩nyo̩ ñwu mi chuu, kʼuwe̩ aje̩ ñw ugbe̩-mi ki dabu e̩lanyi ohimini abadi, e-ku ma ma neke gbaluka n todu uwewe-wñ.
Tak i ru o̩mo̩ odu o̩jo̩ le̩, oñ i mʼe̩wñ ko kwef e̩wñ kʼi ne̩ ugbo-wñ o̩mo̩ kʼi mud e̩wñ ele todu Iso̩ o̩maye-wñ:
ole ewo chʼo̩gwo̩ko, obuko̩ chʼogu, ole ala chʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ okolo chʼogu,
aminyakulumi kʼe̩nya-ma chenʼomi chʼogue̩gwa kpai amo̩ma e-ma, ole okuno̩ chʼo̩gbo̩ meji, o̩ko̩-wñ chʼe̩gwa, ole o̩ke̩ke̩te̩ chʼogu, o̩ma-ma chʼe̩gwa.
Tak i mʼuma ko nyʼamadu-wñ o̩wo̩, ujo̩ ujo̩ du jʼe-wñ ojoji. Oñ i ka ñw amadu-wñ kakini, Me̩ lale daba o̩gba-mi, me̩ bʼowe ujo̩ ujo̩ te̩.
Oñ i ka ñw abo ki dʼo̩gba kakini, E̩gba kʼIso̩ o̩maye-mi kpai uwe̩ de, kʼi tʼuwe̩ ene kakini, Abo e̩ne̩ uwe̩ che? Ugbo e̩ nyi? Ame̩wñ ki jʼo̩gba-we̩-i, e̩ne̩ ne̩ ma?
Tak uwe̩ akakini, E̩wñ adu-we̩ Jeko̩b jo̩-i; e̩wñ kʼi ko wa ache odu-mi Iso̩ ele i che; go, owñ onugo dʼubi awa.
Tak i ño̩ ka ñw ekeji kpai e̩ke̩ta ge̩, kpai abo du ku ma rʼamujo̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ ubi, kakini, Abe̩le̩ ame̩ ñʼaka ñw Iso̩ e̩gba ku me̩ fʼu li,
me̩ ki ka kakini, Go, adu-we̩ Jeko̩b la dʼubi awa ge̩. Todu i kakini, Nadʼe̩wñ ele ki tʼo̩gba-mi-i yʼowñ eju, ubile̩ tak u nali eju-wñ; ikani i fa agba mi.
Abe̩le̩ e̩wñ ele le̩ lale daba o̩gba-wñ; owñ onugo la ru ef uru le̩ odu o̩jo̩ le̩.
Tak i kwane̩ odu o̩jo̩ le̩, oñ i mʼamo̩ya-wñ meji kpai amadu-wñ onobule̩ meji kpai amo̩ma-wñ me̩gwaka ko, oñ i je̩ ñwu ma daba aji Jabo̩k ugbo kʼi de̩ hie̩hie̩le̩.
I la mʼuma ko oñ i je̩ ñwu ma daba aji le̩, kpai e̩wñ du kʼi ne̩ ge̩.
Jeko̩b kpai onuche̩ O̩jo̩ ja
Tak i bo̩ Jeko̩b kate ubi; oñ e̩ne̩ʼka bʼo̩ juja gbogbo tak ane̩ chane̩ e̩ne̩.
Tak e̩gba kʼe̩ne̩ le̩ li ka kʼi ma neke dʼu n, i do̩wo̩chʼoji ude-wñ; oñ oji ude Jeko̩b mukpare abu kʼi bʼo̩ juja le̩.
Tak i kakini, Tʼumi no̩, todu o̩jʼañwa me̩. Oñ i kakini, E̩ ma de̩nyo̩ ñwu mi n, u jʼatʼuwe̩ no̩ n.
Oñ i ka ñw u kakini, Ab odu-we̩ ko̩? I kakini, Jeko̩b.
Tak i kakini, Ma ñʼadʼodu-we̩ ko̩ Jeko̩b ge̩ n, chai Israe̩l, todu uwe̩ bʼO̩jo̩ kpai amone̩ ja me̩, e̩ la fu du.
Taku Jeko̩b tʼowñ ene kakini, Narodubʼe̩ kʼe̩ dʼodu-we̩ ñwu mi. Oñ i kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ tene odu-mi? Tak i de̩nyo̩ ñw u o̩mo̩.
Oñ Jeko̩b dʼodu ugbo kide̩ ko̩ Pe̩nie̩l, todu i kakini, Eju-mi kpai O̩jo̩ de me̩, iñmi-mi la do̩mo̩ ta.
Oñ olu kwane̩ bʼowñ ma abu kʼi lale gu Pe̩nie̩l du, i nachika ude-wñ.
Todule̩ oñ amo̩ma Israe̩l ma jʼili ude e̩la ugbo uka ude gbogbo tʼeñini n, todabu kʼi do̩wo̩chʼoji ude Jeko̩b ugbʼili ude-wñ.
Jeko̩b kpai Iso̩ de
Taku Jeko̩b chi eju-wñ nyate̩ kʼi go, go, Iso̩ awa me̩, one̩ ulo̩ko̩ la jʼugbo-wñ. Tak i fʼamo̩ma-wñ kpe̩ ñwu Lea kpai Reche̩l kpai amadu onobule̩ meji.
Tak i fʼamadu onobule̩ kpai amo̩ma-ma ko jo̩ o̩gba, taku Lea kpai amo̩ma-wñ ro̩ne, Reche̩l kpai Jose̩f la dʼubi otitala.
Tak owñ onugo mʼo̩gba du, oñ i dʼoji-wñ kad ane̩ onu mebie gbogbo tak i lewa ugbo o̩maye-wñ.
Tak Iso̩ ra ledʼo, i gbʼo̩ mʼe̩do̩, i fʼo̩wo̩ lo̩nyʼo̩lo̩-wñ, i la dʼalu kʼo̩ alu, taku ma mutu aku.
Tak i chi eju-wñ nyate̩ oñ i fʼabobule̩ kpai amo̩ma-ma li, i kakini, Abo ugbo jʼugbo-we̩-i? I kakini, Amo̩ma kʼO̩jo̩ du li adu-we̩ ejumomi le̩ de̩.
Tak amadu-wñ onobule̩ te̩ wa, ama kpai amo̩ma-ma, ma te̩kpe̩;
taku Lea kpai amo̩ma-wñ ño̩ te̩ wa ge̩, ma ño̩ te̩kpe̩; ubi-wñ otitala Jose̩f kpai Reche̩l te̩ wa, ma la te̩kpe̩ ge̩.
Tak Iso̩ kakini, E̩wñ chʼoji ujo̩ e̩wñ du kʼomi de kpai ama le̩ ta? I kakini, Todu kʼodu-mi kʼi li mi eju.
Tak Iso̩ kakini, E-kʼu ne̩ bʼumi jo̩, o̩maye-mi; e-kʼe̩ ne̩ ki chʼe-we̩.
Oñ Jeko̩b kakini, O̩da, agba, iche̩wñ kʼe̩ li mi eju, mak e̩ gba e̩wñ ele-mi o̩wo̩-mi-i; todabu kʼu fʼeju-we̩ li, dabe̩ne̩ kʼone̩ ali eju O̩jo̩, kʼe̩do̩-we̩ la bo̩rʼumi.
Agba, e̩ mʼe̩wñ ugwa-mi ku ma du wa le̩ gba, todabu kʼO̩jo̩ chʼufe̩de̩nyo̩ ñwu mi, kʼu laño̩ chenʼe̩wñ du. Abe̩le̩ i kutʼowñ, oñ i mu-gba.
Tak Iso̩ kakini, Wa kʼa chi e̩re̩ ule̩-wa, omi adʼo̩gba-we̩ alo.
Jeko̩b muda ka ñw u kakini, Odu-mi chema ka kʼe̩re̩ amo̩ma gbo mʼule̩ n, ame̩wño̩re̩ egini kpai amokuno̩ ki jʼugbo mi la che̩nʼamo̩ma; iche̩wñ ku ma nʼuma aju o̩jo̩ okate ame̩wño̩re̩ egini le̩ du aku.
Agba, odu-mi ki lale tʼo̩gba adu-wñ-i, tak u nane̩ ma wa ye̩e̩, alu kʼule̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ ki jʼo̩gba-mi de̩ kpai alu kʼule̩ amo̩ma de̩, gbogbo tak u lewa Se̩ir ugbo odu-mi.
Tak Iso̩ kakini, E̩ je̩ ñwu mi chi aboke̩le̩ ku ma jʼugbo-mi jane̩ ñw e̩ pe̩. I kakini, Tode̩wñ? Li mi eju, odu-mi.
Tak Iso̩ mudabi tʼo̩na Se̩ir le o̩jo̩ le̩.
Oñ Jeko̩b fʼule̩-wñ le tu Suko̩t, i la fʼunyi ko̩, oñ i fʼala ne ñw ame̩wñ ukpa-wñ, todule̩ ma dʼodu o̩mo̩ ko̩ Suko̩t.
Jeko̩b kwogugu Kenan
Taku Jeko̩b lewa ewo She̩ke̩m kʼi dʼoj ane̩ Kenan le̩ o̩lafia, abu kʼi kwo Padan-aram awa; i kwo ru o̩gbʼewo le̩.
Tak i fʼe̩bu ane̩ ugbo kʼi dʼunyabo-wñ fa le̩ la kwʼo̩wo̩ amo̩ma He̩mo̩r, ata She̩ke̩m, o̩ko̩ ogu me̩lu.
Tak i fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ kpa o̩mo̩, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ E̩l-e̩lo̩he Israe̩l.
Amo̩maye Daina fʼache̩-wñ na
Taku Daina, o̩ma onobule̩ ki Lea bi ñwu Jeko̩b, dufu nyʼafejudʼamo̩monobule̩ ane̩ le̩.
Oñ She̩ke̩m o̩ma He̩mo̩r, e̩ne̩ Hifai kʼi chʼidachi ane̩ le̩, fʼowñ li. Tak i mʼu du, i bʼo̩ dachi, i la fʼu kpabie̩.
Daina, o̩ma Jeko̩b le̩, che mʼonugo-wñ e̩do̩, i la fe̩do̩ igbe̩le̩ le̩, oñ i kpo̩te̩ rʼo̩ma igbe̩le̩ le̩ e̩do̩.
Taku She̩ke̩m ko̩la ñw ata-wñ Hemo̩r kakini, Tene igbe̩le̩-i ñwu mi chʼo̩ya.
Oñ Jeko̩b gbo̩ ka kʼi fʼo̩ma-wñ Daina o̩la daji; e̩gbale̩ amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la jʼoko ugbo ame̩-wñ ukpa-wñ, oñ Jeko̩b chechi gbogbo taku ma lewa.
Hemo̩r, ata She̩ke̩m, la dufu nyʼugbo Jeko̩b kʼi bʼo̩ choluka.
Oñ abu kʼamo̩ma Jeko̩b gbʼo̩ ma kwʼoko wʼunyi; e̩do̩ aboke̩le̩ le̩ kpabie̩, i bi ma eju tabale todabu kʼi fʼe̩wñ tuñ che efu Israe̩l, o̩ma Jeko̩b kʼi bʼo̩ dachi le̩; e̩wñ ki ma chʼukpe̩ ku ma che n le̩.
Taku Hemo̩r ka ñwu ma kakini. E̩do̩ o̩ma-mi, She̩ke̩m, lamo̩ o̩ma-we̩ onobule̩-i; narodubʼuwe̩ kʼe̩ mʼu du ñw u chʼo̩ya.
Awa ki ne̩ o̩la-wa ke; mʼamo̩monobule̩-me̩ ko ñw a, kʼame̩ ki mʼamo̩monobule̩ e-wa ne̩ ñw o̩la-me̩.
Ame̩ ki bʼuwa dodo, ane̩ la te̩ o̩gba-me̩-i; me̩ dodo ku me̩ nyaja o̩mo̩, kʼame̩ ki nʼe̩wñ o̩mo̩.
She̩ke̩m ño̩ ka ñw ata igbe̩le̩ le̩ kpai amo̩maye-wñ kakini, Ame̩ ki li mi eju ke, e̩wñ du ku me̩ ka ñwu mi nadu ñwu me̩.
Alu du kʼunana o̩me̩-wñ de̩ kpai ele kʼu nache koji, ka ñwu mi, alu du ku me̩ ka ñwu mi nadu. Me̩ ki muda dʼigbe̩le̩ le̩ ñwu mi chʼo̩ya ke.
Tak amo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Jeko̩b dʼohi abe̩lefu ñwu She̩ke̩m kpai ata-wñ Hemo̩r, todabu kʼi fʼo̩maye-ma Daina o̩la daji.
Ma ka ñwu ma kakini, Awa neke che e̩wñ-i n, kʼawa ki dʼo̩maye-wa ñw e̩ne̩ ki ma de̩pi n, todu e-le̩ ma chʼina ugbo wa.
Abu ki ade̩ kʼa aje̩ kpai ame̩ de̩; owñ che kakini, kʼame̩ ki dab awa, kʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du e̩fu-me̩ ki de̩pi.
E̩gbale̩ tak awa amʼamo̩monobule̩-wa ko ñwu me̩, kʼawa anʼamo̩monobule̩-me̩ ñw o̩la-wa, tak a adodo kpai ame̩, oñ awa amud uche̩ amone̩ okate.
I muda che̩wñ ku me̩ ma gbʼo̩la-wa gbo̩ ku me̩ de̩pi n, e̩gbale̩ a amʼo̩ma-wa-i du, a le wa.
O̩la-ma la cheru Hemo̩r kpai She̩ke̩m, o̩ma He̩mo̩r, eju.
Tak okolobia le̩ che̩du eche e̩wñ le̩ n, todabu kʼi ayo̩ ñw o̩ma Jeko̩b le̩. E̩ne̩ke̩le̩ le̩ la nʼojima tʼabo unyi ata-wñ du le.
Taku Hemo̩r kpai She̩ke̩m, o̩ma-wñ, lewa alaku ewo-ma oñ ma ka ñw aboke̩le̩ ewo-ma kakini,
E̩do̩ amone̩-i chemʼuwa; a ki je̩ ñwu ma dodo oj ane̩-i ku ma nyaja; go, ane̩-i chenana bʼuma jo̩; a ki mʼamo̩ma-ma ko chʼo̩ya, kʼa nakʼamo̩monobule̩-wa ñwu ma.
Ab i ade̩ tak ama aje̩ kpai awa ku ma abʼuwa dodo kʼa mud okate de̩: chai e̩gba kʼaboke̩le̩ du ki dʼefu-wa ki de̩pi alu kʼe-ma che̩da.
Tak ame̩wñ ukpa-ma kpai ane̩-ma kpai ame̩la-ma abe̩re̩me̩le̩ du amud e-wa n? Eje̩ a aje̩ dee tak ama abʼuwa dodo.
Tak e̩ne̩ tʼe̩ne̩ du kʼi dufu alaku ewo le̩ gbʼo̩la Hemo̩r kpai o̩la o̩ma-wñ She̩ke̩m; oñ aboke̩le̩ le̩ kʼe̩pi-ma da okoke, e̩ne̩ tʼe̩ne̩ du kʼi dufu alaku ewo le̩.
Oñ i lewatʼo̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta-wñ, e̩gba ki rʼe̩la, tak amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Jeko̩b meji, Simeo̩n kpai Lifai, amo̩maye Daina le̩, ejeji-ma mʼo̩kwo̩chageli-ma ko, oñ ma le umaja umaja wa ewo le̩, taku ma fʼaboke̩le̩-wñ du kpa.
Ma nʼalu o̩kwo̩chageli fu Hemo̩r kpai She̩ke̩m o̩ma-wñ kpa, ma mu Daina du kwef unyi She̩ke̩m taku ma kwʼo̩mo̩ dufu.
Tak amo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Jeko̩b lewa bʼabo ku ma kpa le̩ ma, oñ ma mʼane̩ ewo le̩ ko chʼe̩wñ aluje̩, todabu ku ma fʼo̩maye-ma onobule̩ o̩la daji.
Ma mʼame̩wño̩re̩-ma egini kpai amokuno̩-ma kpai amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩-ma kpai e̩wñ ki jʼef ewo le̩ kpai e-ki jʼoko kpa;
kpai e̩wñ anana-ma du kpai abo-ma egini kpai amo̩ya-ma du ma fʼuma mu, oñ ma mʼe̩wñ tʼe̩wñ du ki jʼef unyi le̩ ko chʼe̩wñ aluje̩.
Taku Jeko̩b ka ñwu Simeo̩n kpai Lifai kakini, Ame̩ mʼihianyi ko wa nyʼumi o̩la me̩, me̩ fʼumi kwuta ugbo abo ane̩-i, owñ chʼabo Kenan kpai abo Pe̩re̩z; tak abu kʼomi ma wewe n, ma ado̩ o̩la-ma jeju rʼumi o̩la akpa mi, ma afʼumi chile̩che̩, tʼomi tʼunyi-mi.
Oñ ma kakini, I dukpe̩ ku ma che o̩maye-wa alu ku ma chʼajo̩ko̩?
Oñ O̩jo̩ ka ñwu Jeko̩b kakini, Kwane̩, kʼe̩ te̩gu nyi Be̩te̩l kʼe̩ gugu o̩mo̩; e̩ ki fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ kpa ñw O̩jo̩ o̩mo̩, owñ chʼO̩jo̩ kʼi kwotejugede ñw e̩ e̩gba kʼe̩ ra bʼeju Iso̩ o̩maye-we̩ te̩ le̩.
Taku Jeko̩b ka ñw abʼo̩ja-wñ kpai abo du ku ma jʼugbo-wñ kakini, Me̩ ki mʼamo̩jo̩ ononojo ki jʼefu-me̩ ko jʼiba, ku me̩ fʼo̩la-me̩ gworinyo̩, me̩ mʼotogbo-me̩ gwo̩ jane̩ ku me̩ la ko omune̩ nyʼo̩la;
oñ a kwane̩ kʼa te̩gu nyi Be̩te̩l, o̩mo̩ nakpʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ñw O̩jo̩ kʼi dohi ñwu mi o̩jo̩ o̩pe̩cha-mi, kʼi laño̩ dʼugbo mi ugbo du kʼu le.
Taku ma mʼamo̩jo̩ ononojo ki jʼo̩wo̩-ma kpai elika ki dʼeti-ma ko ñwu Jeko̩b; oñ Jeko̩b mʼu ko maja of oli ok kʼi me̩ru She̩ke̩m le̩.
Oñ ma mʼe̩re̩ ko nyʼule̩-ma, ailo O̩jo̩ la bʼewo du ki lʼuma de ma, oñ ma ma ra nʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Jeko̩b n.
Abe̩le̩ Jeko̩b lewa Luz, (owñ che Be̩te̩l), e-ki dʼoj ane̩ Kenan, owñ kpai amone̩ du ku ma jʼugbo-wñ.
Tak i fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ kpa o̩mo̩, oñ i dʼodu ugbo kide̩ ko̩ E̩l-Be̩te̩l, todabu ki chʼo̩mo̩ oñ O̩jo̩ kwotejugede ñw u e̩gba kʼi ra bʼeju o̩maye-wñ te̩ le̩.
De̩bora, e̩ne̩ ki ne̩ Ribe̩ka gba, leku, oñ ma mʼu du ji of oli ok o̩wo̩ o̩gane̩ Be̩te̩l: oñ ma dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Alo̩n-bakut.
Tak O̩jo̩ ño̩ kwotejugede ñwu Jeko̩b e̩gba kʼi kwo Padan-aram wa ge̩, i la de̩nyo̩ ñw u.
Oñ O̩jo̩ ko̩la ñw u kakini, Odu-we̩ ko̩ Jeko̩b; ma ñʼadʼodu-we̩ ko̩ Jeko̩b ge̩ n, chai Israe̩l odu-we̩ ako̩. Abe̩le̩ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Israe̩l.
Tak O̩jo̩ ka ñw u kakini, Omi chʼO̩jo̩ Odobao̩gagu: bi o̩ma kʼe̩ wewe nyo̩gba; uche̩ amone̩ kpai uche̩ichi amone̩ ojoji ojoji akwef uwe̩ dufu, amonu la akwef uta-we̩ dufu.
Ane̩ kʼomi du ñw Ebraham kpai Aise̩k, uwe̩ nadʼu ñw u, naño̩ dʼane̩ kide̩ ñw ugbe̩-we̩ ubi-we̩ ge̩.
Tak O̩jo̩ mute̩gu kwʼugbo-wñ uña ugbo kʼi ko̩la kpʼowñ le̩.
Oñ Jeko̩b mʼe̩wñ du gwanyane̩ dago uña ugbo kʼi ko̩la kpʼowñ. E̩wñ kʼi du gwanyi le̩ chʼokuta; tak i dʼomi wa danyu oji-wñ o̩mo̩, i ño̩ mʼekpo du danyʼu.
Oñ Jeko̩b dʼodu uña ugbo kʼO̩jo̩ ko̩la ñw u le̩ ko̩ Be̩te̩l.
Reche̩l leku
Taku ma nʼule̩-ma ale kwo Be̩te̩l alo waa; abu kʼule̩-ma bo̩ re ku ma wa E̩frat ta, Reche̩l chane̩ echefu, efu le̩ chʼo akanya.
Abe̩le̩ e̩gba kʼi dʼef akanya efu le̩ eche, e̩ne̩ ki agba oji o̩ma ka ñw u kakini, E̩ chokpo n; todu fai uwe̩ ñʼanʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ omune̩ ge̩.
Oñ i lewatu abu kʼonugo-wñ che kʼi lo (todu i leku), i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Be̩noni; ata-wñ muda dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Be̩njamin.
Abe̩le̩ Reche̩l leku, oñ ma mʼu du ji eti o̩na ku ma le tu E̩frat (owñ che Be̩tle̩he̩m).
Oñ Jeko̩b fʼe̩wñ gwa-nyane̩ dago ojinoji-wñ; e-le̩ chʼegwa-nyane̩ dago ojinoji Reche̩l tʼo̩jo̩ oluñini.
Taku Israe̩l mʼe̩re̩ ko nyʼule̩ alo, oñ i fʼunyabo-wñ fa ejubi o̩do̩go̩ E̩de̩r.
Oñ i lewatʼabu kʼIsrae̩l ge̩ne̩ ane̩ le̩ Rube̩n le nabo̩ Bilha, abadu ata-wñ, dachi; Israe̩l la gbo̩.
Amo̩ma Jeko̩b e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la chʼe̩gweji.
Amo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Lea che Rube̩n, o̩mo̩gba Jeko̩b, kpai Simeon kpai Lifai kpai Juda kpai Isakar kpai Ze̩biulo̩n.
Amo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Reche̩l la che Jose̩f kpai Be̩njamin.
Amo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Bilha, adu Reche̩l, la che Dan kpai Naftali.
Amo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Zilpa, adu Lea, la che Gad kpai Ashe̩r. Abo-i chʼamo̩me̩ne̩kele̩ e-Jeko̩b ku ma bi ñw u Padan-aram.
Aise̩k leku
Taku Jeko̩b lewa Mamre ugbo Aise̩k, ata-wñ ugbo Kirio̩t-arba (owñ che He̩bro̩n) ugbo kʼEbraham kpai Aise̩k ge̩ne̩ le̩.
Oñ o̩do̩ Aise̩k ku ma bi chʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩la.
Tak Aise̩k mʼiñmi da; i leku oñ ma mʼowñ du atefu abo-wñ abu kʼi chʼogijo kʼo̩do̩-wñ jo̩ kpa; taku Iso̩ kpai Jeko̩b, amo̩ma-wñ le̩, mʼowñ du ji.
Amo̩ma Iso̩
Abo-i chʼo̩lo̩pu o̩lo̩pu Iso̩ (owñ chʼIdo̩m).
Amo̩ma onobule̩ Kenan oñ Iso̩ ne̩ chʼamo̩ya-wñ: Ada kʼi chʼo̩ma E̩lo̩n abo He̩t kpai Oholi-bama kʼi chʼo̩ma Ana kʼi chʼo̩ma Zibeo̩n abo Hifai
kpai Basemat, o̩ma Ishmae̩l, o̩maye Ne̩baio̩t.
Ada la bi Elaifaz ñw Iso̩; Basemat la bi Rue̩l;
Oholibama la bi Jeush kpai Jalam kpai Ko̩ra. Abo-i chʼamo̩ma Iso̩ e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ku ma bi ñw u ane̩ Kenan.
Tak Iso̩ mʼamo̩ya-wñ kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai amo̩ma-wñ onobule̩ kpai onugo abo unyi-wñ du kpai ame̩wñ ukpa-wñ kpai ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩-wñ chaka, kpai ane̩-wñ du ko, owñ chʼe-kʼifiye̩ jo̩ oj ane̩ Kenan; oñ i kwo bʼo̩maye-wñ Jeko̩b te̩ le tʼane̩ omune̩.
Todu e̩wñ-ma ku ma ne̩ chenana, i je̩ ñwu ma dodo ugbʼokate n; ane̩ ugbo ku ma ge̩ne̩ le̩ la neke gba ma n todu ame̩wñ ukpa-ma.
Abe̩le̩ Iso̩ dodo ane̩ uwo Se̩ir; Iso̩ chʼIdo̩m.
Abo-i la chʼo̩lo̩pu o̩lo̩pu Iso̩ kʼi chʼata abo Ido̩m ane̩ uwo Seir.
Odu amo̩ma Iso̩ e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ jo̩-i: Elaifaz o̩ma Ada kʼi chʼo̩ya Iso̩, Rue̩l o̩ma Basemat kʼi chʼo̩ya Iso̩.
Oñ amo̩ma Elaifaz che Teman kpai Omar kpai Zefo kpai Gatam kpai Kenaz. 12(Timna la chʼabadu Elaifaz, o̩ma Iso̩; owñ bi Amale̩k ñw Elaifaz.) Abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Ada, o̩ya Iso̩.
Oñ abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Rue̩l: Nahat kpai Zera kpai Shama kpai Miza. Abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Basemat, o̩ya Iso̩.
Oñ abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Oholibama o̩ma Ana kʼi chʼo̩ma Zibeo̩n, o̩ya Iso̩, owñ bi Jeush kpai Jalam kpai Ko̩ra ñw Iso̩.
Abo-i chʼamo̩ma Iso̩ ku ma mud ame̩ne̩fe̩nyi: amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Elaifaz kʼi chʼo̩mo̩gba Iso̩ che: Teman chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Omar chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Zefo chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Kenaz chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi,
Ko̩ra chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Gatam chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Amale̩k chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, abo-i chʼame̩ne̩fe̩nyi abo Elaifaz ane̩ Ido̩m; abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Ada.
Abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Rue̩l, o̩ma Iso̩ le̩; Nahat chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Zera chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Shama chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Miza chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi; abo-i chʼame̩ne̩fe̩nyi ku Rue̩l bi ane̩ Ido̩m; ama le̩ chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Basemat, o̩ya Iso̩.
Oñ abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Oholibama, o̩ya Iso̩: Jeush chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Jalam chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Kpra chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi; ama le chʼame̩ne̩fe̩nyi kʼOholibama kʼi chʼo̩ma Ana o̩ya Iso̩ bi.
Abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Iso̩, ama le̩ la chʼame̩ne̩fe̩nyi-ma: Iso̩ le̩ chʼIdo̩m.
Abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Seir e̩ne̩ Ho̩r kʼi chʼo̩mane̩ o̩mo̩: Lotan kpai Shobal kpai Zibeo̩n kpai Ana
kpai Dishon kpai Eze̩r kpai Dishan; abo-i chʼame̩ne̩fe̩nyi abo Ho̩r, ma chʼamo̩ma Seir oj ane̩ Ido̩m.
Oñ amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Lotan che Hori kpai Heman; o̩maye Lotan e-onobule̩ che Timna.
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Shobal la de̩: Alfan kpai Manahat kpai Ebal kpai Shefo kpai Onam.
Abo ku ma chʼamo̩ma Zibeo̩n la de̩: Aiya kpai Ana; owñ chʼAna kʼi li e̩bi omi-una aje̩tachi abu kʼi akʼamo̩ke̩ke̩te̩ Zibeo̩n ata-wñ nyʼokije̩ le̩.
Abo-i la chʼamo̩ma Ana: Dishon kpai Oholibama o̩ma Ana onobule̩.
Oñ abo-i chʼamo̩ma Dishon: Hemdan kpai Eshban kpai Itran kpai Che̩ran.
Abo-i chʼamo̩ma Eze̩r: Bilhan kpai Zafan kpai Akan.
Abo-i chʼamo̩ma Dishan: Uz kpai Aran.
Abo-i chʼame̩ne̩fe̩nyi abo Ho̩r: Lotan chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Shobal chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Zibeon chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Ana chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi,
Dishon chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Ezer chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Dishan chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi; abo-i chʼame̩ne̩fe̩nyi abo Hpr, alu kʼame̩ne̩fe̩nyi-ma do̩ ane̩ Seir.
Abo-i chʼabo ku ma jʼonu ane̩ Ido̩m o̩gba tak e̩ne̩ du jʼonu amo̩ma Israe̩l.
Bila, o̩ma Beo̩r e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, jʼonu Ido̩m, odu ewo-wñ la ko̩ Dinhaba.
Taku Bila leku oñ Jobab o̩ma Zera e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ abo Bo̩zra jʼonu koji-wñ.
Taku Jobab leku, oñ Husham abo ane̩ Teman jʼonu koji-wñ.
Taku Husham leku, oñ Hadad, o̩ma Bedad e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, e-ki fu Midian gwoda egbili Moab, jʼonu koji-wñ, odu ewo-wñ la ko̩ Afit.
Taku Hadad leku oñ Samla, abo Masreka, jʼonu koji-wñ.
Taku Samia leku, oñ Sho̩l abo Rehobo̩t eti ohimini Yufretis le̩, jʼonu koji-wñ.
Taku Sho̩l leku, oñ Beal-hanan, o̩ma Akbo̩r e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, jʼonu koji-wñ.
Taku Beal-hanan, o̩ma Akbo̩r e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, leku, oñ Hadar jʼonu koji-wñ, odu ewo-wñ la ko̩ Pau; odu o̩ya-wñ ko̩ Me̩he̩tabe̩l, o̩ma Matred onobule̩, kʼi chʼo̩ma Me̩zahab onobule̩.
Odu-i chʼodu ame̩ne̩fe̩nyi abo Iso̩, alu kʼakwo̩ra unyi, akwo̩ra unyi-ma kpai ugbo ku ma je̩ kpai odu odu-ma de̩: Timna chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Alfa chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Jete̩t chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi,
Oholibama chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Ela chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Pinon chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi,
Kenaz chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Teman chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Mibzar chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi,
Magdie̩l chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi, Iram chʼe̩ne̩fe̩nyi; abo-i chʼame̩ne̩fe̩nyi abo Ido̩m, alu ku ma gugu je̩ oj ane̩ e-ma ku ma ne̩. Owñ le̩ chʼIso̩ kʼi chʼata Ido̩m.
Amo̩maye Jose̩f chʼulaka-wñ
Abe̩le̩ Jeko̩b gugu oj ane̩ ugbo kʼata-wñ ge̩ne̩ le̩, owñ chʼane̩ Kenan.
O̩gba o̩gba Jeko̩b de̩-i:
Abu kʼo̩do̩ Jose̩f chʼe̩gwebie, i do̩mo̩ kpai amo̩maye-wñ adejutʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini; owñ la chʼokolobia kpai amo̩ma Bilha kpai amo̩ma Zilpa, amo̩ya ata-wñ le̩; taku Jose̩f mʼinabali e̩bie̩ne̩-ma du ñw ata-ma.
Israe̩l la fe̩do̩ Jose̩f tʼamo̩ma-wñ du le, todabu kʼi chʼo̩ma kʼi bi o̩jʼogijo-wñ; oñ i fʼafe̩ e-kʼina-wñ chʼojoji ojoji ga ñw u.
Amo̩maye-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ cheli kʼata-ma afe̩do̩-wñ tʼamo̩maye-wñ du le; oñ ma chane̩ echulaka-wñ, ma la neke hi e̩do̩ wane̩ ako̩la ñw u n.
Jose̩f la fʼo̩na na, oñ i mʼu du ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ, taku ma kwochulaka-wñ tule.
I ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ agba, gbo̩ o̩na kʼu na-i:
todu me̩ go, awa jʼoko aji oti o̩ka, oñ go, oti-mi kwane̩, i kwodago kpakpa; me̩ la go, oti e-me̩ donyʼu, oñ ma dʼoji le̩ agwa oti e-mi.
Tak amo̩maye-wñ ka ñw u kakini, Uwe̩ ajʼonu-wa, ochochi? abe̩k uwe̩ achʼodu-wa, ochochi? Taku ma ño̩ chulaka-wñ tule noji o̩na-wñ kpai o̩la-wñ kʼi ka.
I ño̩ fʼo̩na omune̩ na ge̩, oñ i mʼu du ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ, i kakini, Go, omi ño̩ fʼo̩na omune̩ na ge̩; me̩ go, olu kpai ochu kpai awo me̩gwaka la jʼadʼoji kad ane̩ ñwu mi.
I la mʼu du ka ñw ata-wñ kpʼamo̩maye-wñ, tak ata-wñ dejurʼu, i kakini, E̩wñ chʼofe o̩na kʼe̩ na-i? Omi kpai iye-we̩ kpai amo̩maye-we̩ ñʼadʼoji kad ane̩ ñw e̩ ochochi?
Tak amo̩maye-wñ lie̩na-wñ, ama ata-wñ mʼo̩la le̩ du tʼef ibe-wñ.
Tak amo̩maye-wñ le namʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini ata-ma ko nyʼoko ije̩ She̩ke̩m.
Tak Israe̩l ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Amo̩maye-we̩ jʼoko ekʼije̩ ñw ame̩wño̩re̩ je̩ She̩ke̩m in? Lewa kʼu nakpʼe̩ uche̩ nyʼugbo ma. Tak i ka ñw u kakini, Omi de̩-i.
Oñ i ka ñw u kakini, Lo fai, kʼe̩ gʼamo̩maye-we̩, kpai ame̩wño̩re̩ egini, ma ra? kʼe̩ dʼohi wa ñwu mi. Abe̩le̩ i kpʼowñ uche̩ kwef o̩go̩ He̩bro̩n le̩ oñ i lewa She̩ke̩m,
tak e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ʼka fʼowñ li, go, i tale egbili le̩; tak e̩ne̩ le̩ tʼo̩ ene kakini, E̩wñ e̩ feju?
Tak i kakini, Natene amo̩maye-mi, agba, e̩ ka ñwu mi ugbo ku ma jo̩ akʼije̩ ñw ame̩wño̩re̩ je̩.
Tak e̩ne̩ le̩ ka ñw u kakini, Ma kwʼemi le me̩, todu omi gbo̩ abu ku ma kakini, A ki nyi Dotan. Taku Jose̩f gbe̩re̩ amo̩maye-wñ, oñ i fʼuma li Dotan.
Ma la fʼowñ li o̩najiji, gbogbo tak i me̩ru ma mafʼalu jo̩nyʼu kumafʼu kpa.
Oñ ma ko̩la ñw o̩la-ma kakini. Go, ano̩na-i awa me̩.
Me̩ lewa fai kʼa mʼu du kpa, kʼa mʼu du rikpolo tef o̩fe̩ʼka; tak a akakini, E̩wñ iñmi e̩bie̩ne̩ʼka fʼu kpa je̩, tak a ali abu kʼo̩na-wñ ache̩.
Taku Rube̩n gbo̩, oñ i mʼu gba kwef o̩wo̩-ma, i kakini, A ki bʼo̩ gbʼoji n.
Taku Rube̩n ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ ki dʼe̩bie̩ dafo n; mʼowñ du rikpolo tef o̩fe̩ ki dʼef aje̩tachi-i; me̩ ki muda dʼo̩wo̩ kadʼowñ n; todu kʼi li uña kʼi mʼowñ gba kwef o̩wo̩-ma (oñ i ka-i) kʼi mʼu du dabi wa ñw ata-wñ.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba ku Jose̩f wʼugbo amo̩maye-wñ, ma la gwo̩ko̩ rʼu o̩la, ma mʼafe̩-wñ gwo̩, owñ chʼafe̩ kʼina-wñ chʼojoji ojoji ki dʼo̩la-wñ le̩;
taku ma mʼowñ du rikpolo tef o̩fe̩. Efu o̩fe̩ le̩ te̩ ofofo, omi dʼefu-wñ n.
Taku ma kwoguane̩ ku ma jʼuje̩wñ; oñ ma chi eju-ma nyʼate̩ ago, me̩ la go, abelo̩na ku ma chʼabo Ishmae̩l kwo Gilead awa, aminyakulumi-ma nʼadu e̩wñ ido̩ro̩ kpai o̩bia oguʼka kpai otulale mur, oñ ma che ku ma ne̩ agwo̩ru nyʼIjipti.
Taku Juda ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼa dʼo̩maye-wa kpa kʼa du e̩bie̩-wñ maja, ugbo ile-wñ de̩?
Me̩ lewa kʼa mʼowñ du ta ñw abo Ishmae̩l-i; o̩wo̩ e-wa ki kadʼo n, todabu kʼowñ chʼo̩maye-wa, o̩re̩la-wa onugo. Tak amo̩maye-wñ netirʼu.
Tak abo Midian ku ma chʼamanyaja alale; ma la fu Jose̩f fa kwef o̩fe̩ le̩ dufu, oñ ma mʼu du ta ñw abo Ishmae̩l le̩ la o̩ko̩ ajifa ogu. Tak ama le̩ mu Jose̩f du wa ane̩ Ijipti.
Taku Rube̩n mudabi tʼalu o̩fe̩ le̩; go, Jose̩f la dʼef o̩fe̩ n; oñ i fʼukpo-wñ fana.
Tak i mudabi wʼugbo amo̩maye-wñ, i kakini, Imo̩to̩ le̩ do̩mo̩ ge̩ n; abʼomi ale ke?
Taku ma mʼafe̩ Jose̩f ko, ma la fʼo̩mʼewo kpa, oñ ma mʼafe̩ le̩ ko tunyʼe̩bie̩-wñ;
taku ma mʼafe̩ kʼina-wñ chʼojoji ojoji le̩ ko kpuche̩, oñ ma mʼu ko wʼugbo ata-ma, ma kakini, E̩wñ kʼa li de̩-i; todu kʼe̩ mejuma abe̩k afe̩ o̩ma-we̩ de̩, abe̩k i chʼe-owñ n?
Oñ i mejuma, i kakini, Afe̩ o̩ma-mi de̩; e̩wñ iñmi e̩bie̩ne̩ʼka dʼu kpa je̩; i nʼabu du ki che n, ma fu Jose̩f fana rinyo̩ pe̩le̩ pe̩le̩ me̩.
Taku Jeko̩b fʼotogbo-wñ fana, i mʼe̩gbanukpo ko lʼago, oñ i deku o̩ma-wñ o̩jo̩ wewe.
Tak amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩ chaka kwane̩ ku ma nyʼi e̩do̩; i muda ko̩ eje̩ ñwu ma nyʼi e̩do̩; i kakini, Todu, omi kpai eku o̩ma-mi ede̩ akpe̩re̩ nyʼef o̩jegu ugbo o̩ma-mi. Abe̩le̩ ata-wñ rʼaku-wñ.
Oñ abo Midian le̩ mʼowñ du le tʼane̩ Ijipti ata ñwu Po̩tife̩r, onoji Fero, kʼi chʼagboji amaganyi-wñ.
Inabali Juda
Oñ i lewatu adiko le̩ ku Juda kwugbo amo̩maye-wñ nyʼo̩gane̩, oñ i muna tʼejefu ugbo abo Adulam oka kʼodu-wñ ko̩ Haira.
Taku Juda fʼo̩ma onobule̩ abo Kenan oka li, odu-wñ ko̩ Shua; i la ne̩ chʼo̩ya oñ i nyʼejefu ugbo-wñ.
Tak i fefunyo̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi; oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ E̩r.
Tak i ño̩ fefunyo̩ ge̩, i la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi; tak i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Onan.
Tak i ño̩ fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ omune̩ bi ge̩, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Shila. I la de̩ Che̩zib e̩gba kʼi biʼi.
Taku Juda fʼo̩ya ne̩ ñw o̩mo̩gba-wñ E̩r, odu-wñ la ko̩ Temar.
E̩r, o̩mo̩gba Juda le̩, la chʼe̩ne̩bie̩ne̩ eju Jihofa; taku Jihofa mʼu du kpa.
Taku Juda ka ñw Onan kakini, Nyʼejefu ugbo o̩ya o̩maye-we̩ le̩ kʼe̩ che o̩wo̩ o̩maye o̩ko̩ ñw u, kʼe̩ ne̩ ugbe̩ ñw o̩maye-we̩ le̩.
Onan la chema ka kʼugbe̩ le̩ achʼe-wñ n; abe̩le̩ e̩gba kʼi nyʼejefu ugbo o̩ya o̩maye-wñ, i mudu dajane̩ tode̩gba kʼi anʼugbe̩ ñw o̩maye-wñ.
Oñ e̩wñ kʼi che le̩ chʼe̩bie̩ne̩ eju Jihofa, oñ i ño̩ fʼowñ kpa ge̩.
E̩gbale̩ taku Juda ka ñwu Temar, o̩ya o̩ma-wñ kakini, Gugu unyi ata-we̩ kʼe̩ chʼo̩ya ukuo̩ko̩ gbogbo taku Shila, o̩ma-mi, gbakpa; todu, i kakini, tode̩gba kʼi año̩ ku dab amo̩maye-wñ ge̩. Taku Temar le nagugu unyi ata-wñ.
Gboogbo i wa tʼe̩gba kʼo̩monobule̩ Shua, o̩ya Juda, leku; oñ e̩gba kʼe̩do̩ Juda nyi, tak i nyʼugbo abo ku ma ja edudu ame̩wño̩re̩-wñ egini Timna, owñ kpai onuku-wñ Haira kʼi chʼabo Adulam le̩.
Taku ma mudu ka ñwu Temar kakini, Go, ata o̩ko̩-we̩ alo tʼate̩ Timna kʼi fʼedudu ame̩wño̩re̩-wñ egini ja.
Tak i mʼukpo eku ko̩ bʼo̩la te̩, oñ i mʼo̩chada ki de̩ fe̩ne̩ fe̩ne̩ ko bʼoji ma oñ i fʼu wenyʼo̩la-wñ abʼoji-wñ ma wʼane̩, oñ i kwogugu alaku E̩naim, e-ki dʼej o̩na Timna; todu kʼi cheli ku Shila gbakpa me̩, ma la dʼowñ ñw u kʼi chʼo̩ya-wñ n.
E̩gba ku Juda fʼowñ li i do̩kʼajo̩ko̩ de̩, todabu kʼi kʼe̩wñ bʼeju-wñ ma.
Tak i muna wʼugbo-wñ ej o̩na le̩, i kakini, Agba, lewa, kʼe̩ je̩ ñwu mi wʼejefu ugbo-we̩, todu i ma ka kʼowñ chʼo̩ya o̩ma-wñ n. Tak i ka ñw u kakini, E̩wñ e̩ du ñwu mi, kʼe̩ wʼejefu ugbo mi?
I kakini, Nadʼo̩mʼewoʼka kwef ame̩wño̩re̩ egini kpuche̩ rʼuwe̩. Tak i kakini, Uwe̩ adʼe̩wñʼka hiʼumi o̩wo̩ gbogbo tak e̩ dʼu kpuche̩ wa n?
Tak i kakini, E̩wñ nadu hiʼuwe̩ o̩wo̩? Oñ i kakini, E̩wñ uhiuko̩-we̩, kpai iyagba-we̩, kpai o̩kpa ki dʼo̩wo̩-we̩ le̩. Tak i mʼu ko ñw u, oñ i nyʼejefu ugbo-wñ i la fefunyo̩ ñw u.
Tak i kwane̩, i le owñ, i mʼukpo fe̩ne̩ fe̩ne̩ le̩ ko bʼo̩la-wñ te̩, oñ i dʼukpo eku le̩ bʼo̩la ma.
Taku Juda mʼo̩ma ewo du kpuche̩ lʼo̩wo̩ onuku-wñ abo Adulam le̩, kʼi mʼe̩wñ uhio̩wo̩ le̩ gba kwʼe̩wo̩ onobule̩ le̩, i muda liʼu n.
Tak i tʼaboke̩le̩ ugbo kʼonobule̩ le̩ de̩ ene kakini, Ugbo ajo̩ko̩ le̩ de̩? e-kʼi te̩te̩de̩ E̩naim me̩rʼej o̩na o̩mo̩? Oñ ma kakini, Ajo̩ko̩ du dʼemi mama ta n.
Tak i mudabi nyʼugbo Juda, i kakini, Omi liʼu n; tʼaboke̩le̩ o̩mo̩ le̩ ño̩ kakini, Ajo̩ko̩ du dʼemi mama ta n.
Taku Juda kakini, Owñ ki gwo̩nyʼu ke, tode̩gba kʼanyo̩ mʼuwa, go, omi dʼo̩ma ewo-i kpuche̩rʼu, uwe̩ la liʼu n.
Oñ i lewatu gbogbo me̩rʼochu me̩ta, ku ma ka ñwu Juda kakini, Temar, o̩ya o̩ma-we̩ le̩, fʼo̩ko̩ je̩; go, i la fefunyo̩ o̩ko̩ kʼi je̩ le̩. Taku Juda kakini, Mʼu du dufu wa ku ma fʼu gujo.
E̩gba ku ma mʼu du dufu, i fʼuche̩ kpe̩ rʼata o̩ko̩-wñ kakini, E̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ki ne̩ e̩wñ-i oñ u nyefu ñw u; i kakini, Narodubʼe̩ kʼe̩ mejuma e̩ne̩ kʼi ne̩ e̩wñ-i, e̩wñ uhiuko̩-i kpai iyagba-i kpai o̩kpa-i.
Taku Juda je̩ ka kʼowñ ne̩, i kakini, Owñ chʼe̩no̩kpakpa tʼumi le, todabu kʼomi ma dʼu ñwu Shila o̩ma-mi n. Tak i ño̩ dabi mʼo̩ ge̩ n.
Oñ i lewatʼe̩gba kʼiko o̩ma ebi-wñ jo̩, go, ukpejima jʼefu-wñ.
Abe̩le̩ e̩gba kʼi achefu le̩, oka dʼo̩wo̩ dufu; tak e̩ne̩ kʼi agbʼoji o̩ma mʼowu ekpikʼpa du ji mʼo̩wo̩-wñ, i kakini, E-ki dufu wa ejodudu de̩.
Abe̩le̩ abʼi mʼo̩wo̩ dudabi, go, o̩maye-wñ kwodufu wa; oñ i kakini, Abile kʼe̩ fʼuña ñw o̩la-we̩? Todule̩ ma dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Pe̩re̩z.
Ubi le̩ tak o̩maye-wñ dufu wa, owñ chʼe-kʼowu ekpikpa dʼo̩wo̩-wñ le̩; oñ ma dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Zera.
Jose̩f dʼunyi Po̩tife̩r
Oñ ma mu Jose̩f du gwo̩ru nyʼIjipti, taku Po̩tife̩r, onoji Fero kʼi chʼagboji amaganyi-wñ, kʼi chʼe̩ne̩ Ijipti, mʼu gba la kwʼo̩wo̩ abo Ishmae̩l ku ma dʼu gwo̩ru nyʼo̩mo̩.
Jihofa la dʼugbo Jose̩f, oñ i mud e̩ne̩ kʼe̩wñ du ara nyʼu o̩wo̩; i la dʼef uñyi odu-wñ, e̩ne̩ Ijipti le̩.
Tak odu-wñ li ka ku Jihofa dʼugbo-wñ, i ño̩ li ka ku Jihofa la je̩ ñw e̩wñ du kʼi che ra nyʼu o̩wo̩.
Oñ i li Jose̩f eju, Jose̩f la chʼe̩wñ ñw u, oñ i mʼowñ du chʼadejutʼunyi-wñ, e̩wñ du kʼi ne̩ i la ko jʼef o̩wo̩-wñ.
Abe̩le̩ akwe̩gba kʼi mʼowñ du chʼadejutʼunyi-wñ kpai e̩wñ du kʼi ne̩, Jihofa la de̩nyo̩ ñw unyi e̩ne̩ Ijipti le̩ todu Jose̩f; e̩nyo̩ Jihofa la dʼoji e̩wñ du kʼi ne̩, tʼe-unyi, tʼe-oko,
i tʼe̩wñ du kʼi ne̩ no jʼo̩wo̩ Jose̩f; i ño̩ ma e̩wñ du kʼi dʼugbo-wñ n, chai uje̩wñ kʼi aje̩.
Jose̩f la che̩nʼeju e̩nyo̩, año̩la-wñ achʼuto̩.
Oñ i lewatu ubi e̩wñ-i, kʼeju o̩ya odu-wñ kado Jose̩f, oñ i kakini, E̩ bʼumi dachi.
Jose̩f muda ko̩; i ka ñw o̩ya odu-wñ kakini, Go, odu-mi ma e̩wñ du ki dʼugbo-mi ef unyi-i n, i la mʼe̩wñ du kʼi ne̩ ko jʼo̩wo̩-mi;
i nʼe̩ne̩ du ki tʼumi le ef unyi-i n; i la dʼo̩wo̩ bʼe̩wñ du ma ugbo mi n, chai uwe̩, todabu kʼuwe̩ chʼo̩ya-wñ. Ab u nale kʼu nachʼe̩wñ bie̩ne̩ inaina-i, kʼu dʼO̩jo̩re?
Tak abu kʼi tu Jose̩f o̩la o̩jo̩ñwa o̩jo̩ñwa, i la nyeti kʼi abʼo̩ dachi n; i je̩ atʼugbo-wñ n.
Oñ o̩jo̩ʼka i le tef unyi kʼi chʼuko̩lo̩-wñ, aboke̩le̩ unyi le̩ du dʼef unyi o̩mo̩ n,
onobule̩ le̩ gwo̩nyʼukpo-wñ kakini, E̩ bʼumi dachi. I muda tʼukpo-wñ no̩ nyʼu o̩wo̩, i ra le tʼo̩lo̩fe̩.
Oñ e̩gba kʼi li kʼi tʼukpo-wñ no̩ nyʼu o̩wo̩ kʼi ra tʼo̩fe̩,
i la nomudala do̩ aboke̩le̩ unyi-wñ, i ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ go, owñ dʼe̩ne̩ Hibruʼka wʼugbo wa kʼi chʼuwa uke̩; i wʼejefu ugbo mi kʼi bʼumi dachi, tak omi dʼomu nyate̩ akpogu;
oñ abu kʼi gbo̩ abʼu chʼomu nyate̩ akpogu, i tʼe̩wñ o̩la-wñ no̩ nyʼumi o̩wo̩, oñ i ra le tʼo̩lo̩fe̩.
Tak onobule̩ le̩ mʼe̩wñ o̩la-wñ ko jʼugbo-wñ gbogbo tak odu-wñ lewʼunyi.
Tak i ño̩ ka ñw u alu kʼi ka le̩, kakini, Adu abo Hibru kʼe̩ du wʼugbo wa le̩, wa ejefu ugbo mi kʼi che mi uke̩;
abu kʼu dʼomu nyate̩ akwa i la tʼe̩wñ o̩la-wñ no̩ nyʼumi o̩wo̩, oñ i ra tʼo̩lo̩fe̩.
Oñ abu kʼodu-wñ gbo̩ o̩la kʼo̩ya-wñ ka ñw u kakini, Alu kʼadu-we̩ che mi de̩, uwe̩do̩-wñ mutajo.
Tak odu Jose̩f mʼowñ du tef unyi uga, ugbo ku ma ji ame̩namu e-onu jo̩, abe̩le̩ i dʼef unyi uga o̩mo̩.
Jihofa muda dʼugbo Jose̩f, i dʼufe̩de̩nyo̩-wñ ñʼo̩, i je̩ ñw agboji unyi uga le̩ liʼu eju.
Tak agboji unyi uga mʼame̩namu du ku ma jʼef unyi uga le̩ ko nyu Jose̩f o̩wo̩; e̩wñ du ku ma che o̩mo̩ mak owñ che.
Agboji unyi uga le̩ dʼeju-wñ gʼe̩wñ du ki dʼo̩wo̩ Jose̩f ge̩ n, todabu ki Jihofa dʼugbo-wñ; e̩wñ du kʼi ache Jihofa la je̩ ñw u ki ra ñw u.
Jose̩f dʼunyi uga akʼoji o̩na ñwu ma
Oñ i lewatʼanubi e̩wñ-i, kʼe̩ne̩ ki adʼomi ñw onu Ijipti ñmo̩, kpai e̩ne̩ ki ache uje̩wñ egini ñw u, fʼo̩la che bi odu-ma onu Ijipti le̩ eju.
Taku Fero we̩do̩ rʼamonoji-wñ meji-i, owñ chʼagboji abo ku ma dʼomi ñw u ñmo̩ kpai agboji abo ku ma che uje̩wñ egini ñw u je̩.
Oñ i mʼuma ko nyʼone̩ o̩wo̩ ef unyi agboji amaganyi le̩, ef unyi uga ugbo ku ma ji Jose̩f te̩.
Tak agboji amaganyi mʼudu edejute̩ ma du ñwu Jose̩f, oñ i che e̩wñ ñwu ma; ma jʼef amu le̩ kpo̩kpe̩ pe̩.
Tak ejeji-ma fo̩na na, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ nʼo̩na e-wñ odu o̩jo̩ okate, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ nʼalu kʼoji o̩na-wñ kʼi na de̩, owñ chʼadʼomi ñw onu ñmo̩ kpai ache uje̩wñ egini e-onu Ijipti ku ma ji ma jʼef unyi uga le̩.
Taku Jose̩f wʼejefu ugbo ma odudu, oñ i li ma, go, eju-ma che̩bu nyʼo̩wo̩.
Tak i tʼamonoji Fero ku ma jʼef o̩wo̩ one̩ ef unyi odu-wñ kpʼowñ ene kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼeju-me̩ chʼekpa jo̩ abe̩i eñini-i?
Taku ma ka ñw u kakini, A fʼo̩na na, i la nʼe̩ne̩ du kʼi neke kʼoji-wñ ñwa n. Taku Jose̩f ka ñwu ma kakini, I chʼO̩jo̩ nʼoji e̩wñ eka n? narodubʼume̩ ku me̩ ka ñwu mi.
Tak agboji abo ku ma dʼomi ñw onu ñmo̩ mʼo̩na-wñ du ka ñwu Jose̩f, i ka ñw u kakini, Ef o̩na-mi, go, ikeli achiwebe̩te̩maʼka dʼo̩gba-mi,
ikeli achiwebe̩te̩ma le chenʼe̩to̩ me̩ta; oñ i dabe̩ne̩ kʼi abu, ebu-wñ mutu dufu; ugbo kʼi mujo̩ mujo̩ le i mʼe̩ro achiwebe̩te̩ma ki kpa ko dufu.
Ago omi Fero la dʼef o̩wo̩-mi; oñ u mʼe̩ro achiwebe̩te̩ma le̩ ko, ufʼu pili nyʼef ago omi e-Fero, tak u mʼago le̩ du tʼo̩wo̩ Fero.
Taku Jose̩f ka ñw u kakini, Oji-wñ de̩: E̩te̩ me̩ta le̩ chʼo̩jo̩ me̩ta;
gbogbo tak o̩jo̩ me̩ta ki jo̩ Fero adʼuwe̩ oji dago, kʼi adʼuwe̩ dabi tʼe̩gu ugugu-we̩; oñ uwe̩ adʼago Fero tʼo̩wo̩-wñ alu ki de̩ o̩gbo̩gba e̩gba kʼuwe̩ dʼomi ñw u ñmo̩ le̩.
Ama uwe̩ ki nadibekado mi e̩gba ki ra ñw e̩, narodubʼe̩ kʼe̩ chʼe̩nyo̩ ñwu mi kʼe̩ mʼinabali-mi du ñwu Fero, kʼe̩ mʼumi gba kwef unyi-i dufu.
Todu eji ma mʼumi ji kwʼoj ane̩ abo Hibru; tʼemi ge̩, u la che e̩wñ du taku ma dʼumi tef ura-i n.
Egba kʼagboji abo ku ma che uje̩wñ egini le̩ li kʼoji o̩na-wñ kʼi ka chenyo̩, i ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Omi ño̩ fʼo̩na na ge̩; go, agba akala efufu me̩ta la jʼoji-mi,
oñ ef agba ki dʼate̩ otitala, uje̩wñ egini ku ma che ojoji ojoji du jʼefu-wñ todu Fero, oñ ame̩we̩ jʼaje̩ kwef agba ki dʼoji-mi.
Taku Jose̩f dohi kakini, Oji e-le̩ de̩: agba me̩ta le̩ chʼo̩jo̩ me̩ta;
gbogbo tak o̩jo̩ me̩ta ki jo̩ Fero adʼoji-we̩ dago bʼuwe̩ o̩la te̩! i la adʼuwe̩ lo̩ko̩li olʼoli; ame̩we̩ la agbe̩ o̩re̩la-we̩ je̩ bʼachiku-we̩ te̩.
Oñ o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta-wñ, ki chʼo̩jo̩ kʼo̩do̩ ku ma bi Fero mudako, i la fʼuje̩wñ uyo̩ hi ñw amadu-wñ chaka, oñ i mʼoji agboji abo ku ma dʼomi ñw u ñmo̩ kpai agboji abo ku ma che e̩wñ ayaga ñw u du dago ef amadu-wñ.
I mʼagboji abo ku ma dʼomi ñw u le̩ du dabi tʼe̩gu-wñ, oñ i mʼago le du tʼo̩wo̩ Fero;
ama i mʼagboji abo ku ma che uje̩wñ ayaga ñw u je̩ du lo̩ko̩li dabalu ku Jose̩f kʼoji-wñ ñwu ma.
Abu ki chaka chʼabe̩le̩ agboji abo ku ma dʼomi ñw onu ñmo̩ la dibekado Jose̩f in, i fʼu gbenyo̩.
Jose̩f kʼoji o̩na Fero ñw u
Oñ i lewatʼe̩gba kʼo̩do̩ odokulu meji muda, Fero la nʼo̩na; go, i dago etʼohimini Naye̩l.
Me̩ go, amokuno̩ mebie kwef ohimini dufu, año̩la-ma de̩ bo̩lo̩bo̩lo̩, ma chʼeyoyo, oñ ma jʼef icho̩lo̩ alʼije̩.
Taku me̩ go, amokuno̩ mebie omune̩ te nʼuma ubi kwef ohimini dufu, año̩la-ma chʼekenyi, ma chʼe̩gbo̩gbe̩ jo̩, ma la dago me̩rʼamokuno̩ ekeji le̩ etʼo̩ba ohimini.
Tak amokuno̩ kʼaño̩la-ma chʼe̩kenyi ku ma chʼe̩gbo̩gbe̩ mʼamokuno̩ kʼaño̩la-ma de bo̩lo̩bo̩lo̩ ku ma chʼeyoyo le̩ ko je̩. Oñ Fero mʼolu ji.
Tak i mʼolu du, i ño̩ nʼo̩na onu keji ge̩; go, acha o̩ka mebie ki cheru jigbo̩jigbo̩ kwodufu wʼoj oli o̩ka okate.
Me̩ la go, acha mebie ki chʼekwire̩ e-kʼafu olodudu fʼu gʼuna ño̩ kwane̩ tʼo̩ ubi.
Tak acha o̩ka e̩kwire̩ le mʼacha o̩ka mebie ki de jigbo̩jigbo̩ le ko mi. Taku Fero mʼolu ji. Go, i mud o̩na ena.
Oñ i lewatʼodudu-wñ i kwodejiji; tak i kpuche̩ nado̩ amachobochi Ijipti chaka wa, kpai amanibe o̩mo̩ chaka: taku Fero mʼo̩na-wñ kʼi na du ka ñwu ma, ama e̩ne̩ du do̩mo̩ kʼi aneke kʼofe-wñ ñwu Fero n.
Tak agboji abo ku ma dʼomi ñw onu ñmo̩ le ka ñwu Fero kakini, Edure kʼu dure, ibe-mi lewa kado eñini.
Fero we̩do̩ rʼamadu-wñ, i la mʼumi kpai agboji abo ku ma che uje̩wñ ayaga du nyʼone̩ o̩wo̩ ef unyi agboji amaganyi,
oñ a fʼo̩na na odu o̩jo̩ kate, omi kpʼowñ; awa nʼo̩na alu kʼofe o̩na e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ de̩.
Okolobia abo Hibruʼka la dʼugbo wa o̩mo̩, adu agboji amaganyi i che; oñ a ka ñw u tak i kʼofe o̩na-wa ñw a, i ka ofe e-e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ñw u alu kʼo̩na-wñ de.
Abe̩le̩ alu kʼi kʼofe-wñ ñw a alu le̩ i de̩; i mʼumi du dabi tʼe̩gu-mi, i mʼowñ du lo̩.
Taku Fero kpʼone̩ ado̩ Jose̩f, oñ ma mʼu du kwef ura le̩ wa piopio; abi fʼilagba-wñ la, kʼi la mʼukpo omune̩ ko nyʼo̩la, tak i wʼejefu ugbo Fero.
Oñ Fero ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Omi fʼo̩na na, i la nʼe̩ne̩ du kʼi aneke kʼofe-wñ n; omi chegbo̩ abu ku ma ka o̩la-we̩, kakini, E̩gba kʼuwe̩ gbo̩ o̩na kʼone̩ na e̩ neke kʼofe-wñ.
Taku Jose̩f dohi ñwu Fero kakini, I chʼefu-mi i de̩ n; O̩jo̩ adohi ugbe̩do̩ ñwu Fero.
Taku Fero ko̩la ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Ef o̩na kʼu na, go, omi dago oj ugbogbo ohimini Naye̩l.
E̩ la go, amokuno̩ mebie kwef omi ohimini dufu, ma chʼeyoyo, año̩la-ma de̩ bo̩lo̩bo̩lo̩; oñ ma jʼef icho̩lo̩ alʼije̩.
E̩ la go, amokuno̩ mebie omune̩ dufu wa ubi-ma, año̩la-ma chʼelo̩ma te̩, año̩la-ma chʼe̩kenyi tabale, ma chʼe̩gbo̩gbe̩, u li e̩bie̩ne̩ e̩gʼe-ma ane̩ Ijipti du mama ta n.
Tak amokuno̩ ku ma chʼe̩gbo̩gbe̩, kʼaño̩la-ma chʼe̩kenyi mʼamokuno̩ mebie ejodudu ku ma chʼeyoyo le̩ koje̩.
E̩gba ku ma fʼuma je̩ kpa, one̩ me̩ma ka ku ma je̩ e̩wñ du n, ama o̩la-ma chʼe̩ke̩nyi alu ki de̩ ejodudu; tak u mʼolu ji.
U ño̩ fʼe̩wñ li ef o̩na-mi ge̩, go, acha mebie la wʼoji oli o̩ka okate, i chʼere̩yo̩ o̩me̩me̩le̩;
go, acha mebie ki chʼe̩gbe̩ mʼakpo, ki chʼe̩kwire̩, e-kʼafu olodudu fʼu gʼuna te̩ nʼuma ubi dufu.
Tak acha e̩kwire̩ le̩ mʼacha mebie e-ki nyo̩ ko mi. Oñ u mudu ka ñw amachobochi, i muda nʼe̩ne̩ du kʼi neke kʼofe-wñ ñwu mi n.
Taku Jose̩f ka ñwu Fero kakini, O̩na Fero chʼokate; e̩wñ kʼO̩jo̩ ache kʼi che i je̩ ñwu Fero ki ma de̩.
Amokuno̩ mebie e-ki nyo̩ le̩ chʼo̩do̩ mebie, acha o̩ka mebie e-ki nyo̩ le̩ laño̩ chʼo̩do̩ mebie; o̩na le̩ chʼokate.
Amokuno̩ mebie e-ku ma gbo̩gbe̩, kʼaño̩la-ma chʼe̩kenyi ku ma ate̩gu anʼuma ubi wa le̩, la chʼo̩do̩ mebie, kpai acha o̩ka e̩kpafolo mebie, e-kʼafu olodudu fu guna le̩ ge̩, ño̩ chʼo̩do̩ ukpo̩ta mebie.
E̩wñ kʼomi ka ñwu Fero le̩ de̩, kakini, E̩wñ kʼO̩jo̩ ache kʼi che, i mʼu du ña Fero.
Go, o̩do̩ mebie e̩gba kʼe̩wñ akpo̩rane̩ o̩be̩le̩ke̩te̩ ugbo du ane̩ Ijipti awa,
tak o̩do̩ ukpo̩ta mebie anʼubi-wñ, oñ ma agbenyo̩ e̩wñ ki kpo̩rane̩ oj ane̩ Ijipti chaka; ukpo̩ta le̩ la amʼane̩ Ijipti ko mi,
taku ma ñʼama uro̩je̩ ane̩ le̩ ge̩ n, todu ukpo̩ta ki dʼubi-wñ, todu i abie̩ne̩ ololo.
Todabu kʼo̩na le̩ chʼugbo meji ñwu Fero chʼutodabu kʼe̩wñ le̩ fʼoji ne̩ ugbo O̩jo̩ me̩, oñ O̩jo̩ adʼu wa faifai.
Todule̩ Fero ki natene e̩ne̩ʼka kʼi nʼibe kʼi meju e̩wñ eche, kʼi dʼo̩da ane̩ Ijipti-ʼi ñw u.
Fero ki nache abe̩le̩, kʼi chi amone̩ ku ma nagʼane̩, ku ma gbʼukpe̩ e̩ke̩lu ane̩ Ijipti ef o̩do̩ uro̩je̩ mebie le̩.
Kʼi naje̩ ñwu ma mʼuje̩wñ e-o̩do̩ ki nyo̩ ki awa-i yajo̩, ku ma mʼe̩wñ e̩yo̩ ko maja o̩wo̩ Fero todu ki chʼuje̩wñ abewo, kʼi je̩ ñwu ma fejutʼo̩.
Uje̩wñ le̩ ki najʼef aka ñw abane̩ todu o̩do̩ ukpo̩ta mebie e-ki adʼoj ane̩ Ijipti-i du; todu kʼane̩-i ki we ekpabie̩ lugbo ukpo̩ta le̩.
Oñ e̩wñ kʼi ka le̩ che̩nyo̩ Fero kpai abuko̩lo̩-wñ chaka eju.
Taku Fero ka ñw abuko̩lo̩-wñ kakini, Awa neke li e̩ne̩ ki dab e̩ne̩-i, one̩ kʼAfu O̩jo̩ dʼefu-wñ-i?
Taku Fero ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Todabu kʼO̩jo̩ kʼe̩wñ-i du ñʼuwe̩, i nʼe̩ne̩ du kʼi nʼibe kʼi ño̩ meju e̩wñ eche dab uwe̩ n;
uwe̩ anʼo̩da unyi-mi alu kʼo̩la-we̩ de̩ alu le̩ oñ amone̩-mi du aleru; chai oj ede kate omi du tʼuwe̩ le.
Taku Fero ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini. Go, omi dʼo̩da ane̩ Ijipti du ñw e̩.
Taku Fero mʼelika-uhiuko̩-wñ gwo̩ kwʼo̩wo̩-wñ, i la mʼu du tunyʼo̩wo̩ Jose̩f, I la mʼotogbo line̩n ku ma hi reju du tʼo̩la-wñ, i ño̩ mʼiyagba o̩jamalia du tʼo̩fa-wñ;
tak i je̩ ñw u kwo tʼo̩ko̩ ogu ekeji kʼi ne̩; oñ ma kwa rʼo̩ o̩gba kakini, Me̩ kʼoku-ku nyʼane̩! Abe̩le̩ i dʼo̩da ane̩ Ijipti le̩ du ñw u.
Fero ño̩ ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Omi Fero de̩, i ma chʼuwe̩ n, e̩ne̩ du a chi o̩wo̩-wñ abe̩k e̩re̩-wñ nyate̩ ugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti n.
Taku Fero dʼodu Jose̩f ko̩ Zafe̩nat-pane̩a, oñ i mʼAse̩nat o̩ma Po̩tife̩ra, atama kʼi de̩ On, du ñw u chʼo̩ya. Taku Jose̩f dufu lʼugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti.
O̩do̩ Jose̩f la chʼogue̩gwa e̩gba kʼi dago o̩gba Fero onu Ijipti le̩. Taku Jose̩f le dufu kwʼo̩gba Fero, oñ i nyʼugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti.
O̩do̩ uro̩je̩ mebie le̩ ane̩-ile̩-i la bi e̩wñ dufu e̩kʼe̩ko̩.
Oñ i fʼuje̩wñ o̩do̩ mebie le̩ e-du ki jʼoj ane̩ Ijipti yajo̩, i la mʼuje̩wñ le̩ ko maja ewo ewo; owñ chʼuje̩wñ oko ki lʼewo ewo daka, e-le̩ i ko jo̩ ewo ewo le̩.
Jose̩f la kʼe̩wñ e̩yo̩ maja dab e̩lanyi ohimini abadi, i nana tabale, gbogbo tak i to̩no̩ ekaluka; todu i nʼaluka n.
Ase̩nat, o̩ma Po̩tife̩ra atama On, la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ meji bi ñwu Jose̩f o̩gba tak o̩do̩ ukpo̩ta le̩ wa.
Taku Jose̩f dʼodu e-ku ma bi o̩gba ko̩ Manasa, i kakini, todu O̩jo̩ je̩ ñwu mi gbenyo̩ akanya-mi kʼu che kpai abʼunyi ata-mi du.
I la dʼodu o̩ma-wñ ekeji ko Ifraim, todu O̩jo̩ je̩ ñwu mi nʼugbe̩ oj ane̩ o̩bata-mi.
Tak o̩do̩ uroje̩ mebie ki dʼoj ane̩ Ijipti le̩ lewa kpoji.
Oñ o̩do̩ ukpo̩-ta mebie le̩ chane̩ ewa, dabalu ku Jose̩f ka. Ukpo̩ta la dʼoj ane̩ oj ane̩ du akpa; ama oj ane̩ Ijipti du uje̩wñ do̩mo̩.
Tak e̩gba kʼelu abo ane̩ Ijipti du muda, amone̩ le̩ raku nyu Fero o̩la tod uje̩wñ; taku Fero ka ñw abo Ijipti du kakini, Me̩ nyʼugbo Jose̩f; e̩wñ kʼi aka ñwu me̩ me̩ che.
Oñ ukpo̩ta le̩ mʼile̩ du gba nyʼo̩wo̩, taku Jose̩f mʼo̩na aka du bi, i ko ta ñw abo Ijipti la, todu ukpo̩ta nakpa ololo ane̩ Ijipti.
Tak abo ile̩ du wʼane̩ Ijipti ugbo Jose̩f ku ma la e̩wñ e̩yo̩, todabu kʼukpo̩ta akpa ololo ile̩ du.
Amo̩ma Jeko̩b nyʼIjipti alʼuje̩wñ
E̩gbale̩ Jeko̩b li ka kʼe̩wñ e̩yo̩ dʼIjipti; taku Jeko̩b ka ñw amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kakini, E̩wñ chi ku me̩ kejurʼo̩la-me̩ jo̩-i?
Oñ i kakini, Go, omi gbo kʼe̩wñ e̩yo̩ dʼIjipti me̩ gwo̩ru nyʼo̩mo̩ ku me̩ la kwʼo̩mo̩ wa ñw a, todu kʼa deju kʼa we eku.
Tak amo̩maye Jose̩f me̩gwa nyʼo̩gane̩ ku ma la e̩wñ e̩yo̩ kwo Ijipti wa.
Jeko̩b muda kpe̩ Be̩njamin, o̩maye Jose̩f, uche̩ tef amo̩maye-wñ le̩ n, todu i kakini, Tode̩gba kʼe̩wñʼka ake̩re̩bʼo̩.
Abe̩le̩ amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Israe̩l jʼef abo ku ma wa Ijipti ala, todu ukpo̩ta le̩ dʼane̩ Kenan akpa.
Jose̩f la chʼigo̩bina ane̩ le̩; owñ chʼe̩ne̩ ki ata e̩wñ ñw amone̩ ane̩ le̩ du la. Tak amo̩maye Jose̩f lewa, ma danyeku o̩gba owñ, oñ ma fʼeju bʼane̩ ma ñw u.
Jose̩f fʼamo̩maye-wñ le̩ li, i la fʼuma ma, i muda che o̩la-wñ dabe̩ne̩ kʼononojo ejaduña, i la ko̩la o̩ko̩ko̩ ñwu ma. I ka ñwu ma kakini, Ugbo me̩ kwo? Ma kakini, A kwʼane̩ Kenan wa kʼa lʼuje̩wñ.
Abe̩le̩ Jose̩f chema amo̩maye-wñ le, ma muda mʼowñ n.
Taku Jose̩f libekado o̩na-ma kʼi na; oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, Ame̩ chʼabo ku ma atu ane̩, me̩ wa ku me̩ go alu kʼane̩ te̩ ofofo.
Taku ma ka ñw u kakini, O̩da, odu-mi, chai todu uje̩wñ ela, oñ amadu-we̩ wa-i.
O̩chaka-wa chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ kate, one̩ ochochi awa che, amaduwe̩-i chʼabo ku ma atu ane̩ n.
Tak i ka ñwu ma kakini, O̩da, chai todu ku me̩ go alu kʼane̩ te̩ ofofo, tod e-kide̩ oñ me̩ wa-i.
Taku ma kakini, Amadu-we̩ chʼamo̩maye me̩gweji, a chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ kate ane̩ Kenan; go, e-kekele la dʼugbo ata-wa eñini, oka la de̩ n.
Taku Jose̩f ka ñwu ma kakini, I chʼe-kʼomi ka ñwu me̩ ka kʼane̩ me̩ wa tu-i de n?
Ef e-kide̩ najʼume̩ ma: Oji Fero, me̩ ñʼakwʼemi ge̩ n chai e̩gba kʼokekele-me̩ lewa.
Me̩ fʼe̩ne̩ʼka efu-me̩ kpe̩ lo kʼi dʼo̩maye-me̩ wa, ma aji me̩ ku ma jʼo̩la-me̩ ma abe̩k ochochi dʼefu-me̩; cho̩kpo̩ni, oji Fero, ame̩ chʼabo ku ma wa tu ane̩ ochochi.
Tak i mʼuma ko jʼef o̩wo̩ amadide o̩jo̩ me̩ta.
Tak o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta-wñ Jose̩f ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩wñ ku me̩ che kʼoji-me̩ ado̩mo̩ de̩, todu ailo O̩jo̩ aba mi.
Iche̩wñ kʼame̩ chʼone̩ ochochi, me̩ je̩ ñwu ma fʼo̩maye-me̩ʼka ji tef unyi uga-me̩ le̩, tak ame̩ kibo̩ ki lo, ku me̩ mʼe̩wñ e̩yo̩ ko alo todu ukpo̩ta ki dʼunyi-me̩.
Oñ me̩ mʼokekele-me̩ du wʼugbo mi; abe̩le̩ tak o̩la-me̩ achʼo̩kpakpa oñ ame̩ ñʼaku ge̩ n. Taku ma fʼabe̩le̩ che.
Ma la ka ñw o̩la-ma kakini, A fʼudu fe̩ ugbo o̩la o̩maye-wa le̩ ochochi, todu a li o̩bata onugo-wñ e̩gba kʼi gbo̩ko̩bʼuwa, kʼa ma gbo̩ n; todule̩ o̩pe̩cha-i lewa bʼuwa ma.
Taku Rube̩n dohi ñwu ma kakini, Omi ka ñwu me̩ ka kʼame̩ ki we edʼo̩ma le̩ re n? Me̩ je̩ gbo̩ n. Todule̩, me̩ go, ma tene e̩bie̩-wñ me̩.
Ma la ma ka ku Jose̩f agbʼichi-ma n, todu agbo̩laka dʼagbagba-ma.
Tak i murida i kwugbo ma, i mutu aku; tak i mudabi wʼugbo ma, oñ i ko̩la ñwu ma. Tak i mu Simeo̩n du kwefu-ma, oñ i fʼowñ ji eju-ma.
Taku Jose̩f ñwa ñw abo-wñ ku ma ko e̩wñ e̩yo̩ nyʼe̩wñ ku ma ne̩ wa e̩ko̩, ku ma ño̩ mʼo̩ko̩ e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ko dabi tef akpulu-wñ, ku ma laʼko e̩wñ ku ma aje̩ ej o̩na ñwu ma. Abe̩le̩ ma che ñwu ma.
Taku ma mʼadu e̩wñ e̩yo̩ ko ji mʼubi amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩-ma, oñ ma kwʼo̩mo̩ le.
Abu kʼe̩ne̩ʼka efu-ma mʼalu akpulu-wñ tu kʼi kʼuje̩wñ ñw o̩ke̩ke̩te̩-wñ je̩ ugbo ku ma ru, i fʼo̩ko̩-wñ li alu akpulu-wñ.
Tak i ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ kakini, O̩ko̩-mi mudabi wa me̩; go i dʼef akpulu-mi-i! tak e̩do̩-ma mudeji, ma rejuda go o̩la-ma, o̩la-ma aga, ma kakini, E̩wñ chʼe-kʼO̩jo̩ che wa-i?
Taku ma lewʼugbo Jeko̩b, ata-ma, ane̩ Kenan, oñ ma fʼe̩wñ du ki ke̩re̩bʼuma choli ñw u, ma kakini,
E̩ne̩ ki chʼodu ane̩ le̩ ko̩la o̩ko̩ko̩ ñw a, eju-wñ a chʼabo ku ma wa tu ane̩.
Tak a ka ñw u kakini, Awa chʼone̩ ochochi, awa chʼabo ku ma tu ane̩ n;
amo̩maye me̩gweji oñ a che, amo̩ma ata-wa; oka de̩ n, eñini-i e-kekele dʼugbo ata-wa ane̩ Kenan.
Tak e̩ne̩ ki chʼodu ane̩ le̩ ka ñw a kakini, Ugbo kʼu nale kʼu nama ku me̩ chʼone̩ ochochi de̩: me̩ tʼo̩maye-me̩ oka no̩ ugbo mi, me̩ mʼe̩wñ ko todu ukpo̩ta ki dʼunyi-me̩, ku me̩ lo me̩.
Me̩ dʼokekele-me̩ wʼugbo mi; e̩gbale̩ tak u nama ka kʼame̩ ma chʼabo ku ma atu ane̩ n, ku me̩ la chʼabo ochochi, abe̩le̩ tak u nadʼo̩maye-me̩ ñwu me̩, oñ ame̩ anyaja ane̩-i.
Oñ i lewatʼe̩gba ku ma mʼe̩wñ ki dʼef akpulu-ma ko dajane̩, go, o̩ko̩ e̩ne̩ du efu-ma chʼe̩ji tef akpulu-wñ; tak e̩gba kʼama kpai ata-ma li o̩ko̩-ma ki chʼe̩ji te̩ ma kwochokpo.
Taku Jeko̩b, ata-ma, ka ñwu ma kakini, Ame̩-fʼamo̩ma-mi kpa: Jose̩f de̩ n, Simeo̩n la de̩ n, fai ame̩ ño̩ che ku me̩ mu mi n du kwʼemi ge̩? e̩wñ du bʼumima-i.
Taku Rube̩n ka ñw ata-wñ kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼomi ma dʼowñ dabi wa ugbo we̩ n, e̩ fʼo̩ma-mi meji kpa; e̩ mʼu du nyʼumi o̩wo̩, nadʼu dabi wa ñw e̩.
Tak i kakini, O̩ma-mi ale bʼume̩ nyʼo̩gane̩ n, todu o̩maye-wñ leku me̩, owñ kate bo̩. Iche̩wñ ku me̩ alo kʼe̩wñ bie̩ne̩ ke̩re̩bʼo̩ ej o̩na, e̩gbale̩ ame̩ adʼi-loji-mi efufu tef o̩jegu kpai e̩do̩dudu.
O̩TAKADA O̩LA O̩JO̩
Amo̩maye Jose̩f nyʼIjipti onu keji
Oñ ukpo̩ta dʼane̩ le̩ akpa ololo.
Tak i lewatʼe̩gba ku ma fʼe̩wñ e̩yo̩ ku ma ko kwʼIjipti wa je̩ kpa, ata-ma ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ ño̩ lo ku me̩ la uje̩wñ wa ñw a pe̩.
Taku Juda ka ñw u kakini, E̩ne̩ le̩ ka ñwu wa kpaka kakini, Me̩ ñʼali eju-mi ge̩ n, chai e̩gba kʼo̩maye-me̩ dʼugbo me̩.
Iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ je̩ kʼe̩ kpe̩ o̩maye-wa lebʼuwa, tak a nyʼo̩gane̩ kʼa la uje̩wñ wa ñw e̩;
ama iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ ma je̩ kpʼo̩ lebʼuwa n, mak a nyʼo̩gane̩ n, todu e̩ne̩ le̩ ka ñw a kakini, Me̩ ñʼali eju-mi n, chai e̩gba kʼo̩maye-me̩ dʼugbo me̩.
Tak Israe̩l kakini, E̩wñ chi ku me̩ che mi e̩bie̩ne̩ abe̩i, eka ku me̩ ka ñw e̩ne̩ le̩ ka ku me̩ nʼo̩maye omune̩ ta?
Taku ma kakini, E̩ne̩ le̩ tʼuwa ene o̩la o̩la-wa ogbolo, kpai o̩la amefu-wa, i kakini, Ata-me̩ deju ta? Me̩ nʼo̩maye? Tak a ka ñw u alu kʼo̩la le̩ de̩; i nʼugbo kʼa neke ma ka kʼi aka ñw a kʼa dʼo̩maye-wa gwo̩ru wa?
Taku Juda ka ñw Israe̩l, ata-wñ, kakini, E̩ kpʼokolobia le̩ lebʼumi, tak a kwane̩ alo, todu kʼa deju kʼa we eku, tʼawa, tʼuwe̩, tʼabimo̩to̩-wa egini kpo̩fo̩.
Omi onugo achʼe̩wñ uhio̩wo̩-wñ; e̩ tene-wñ o̩wo̩-mi. Iche̩wñ kʼomi ma dʼu dabi wa ñw e̩ n, kʼomi ma dʼu gugu o̩gba-we̩ n, mak adure ogbegbele̩ omi du we̩ re le̩;
todu i ma chʼiñelebu kʼa che-i n, a ma le mudabi wa onu ekeji me̩.
Tak ata-ma, Israe̩l, ka ñwu ma kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼi adʼabe̩le̩ tila mak e̩wñ ku me̩ che de̩-i; me̩ mʼe̩ro o̩me̩me̩le̩ ane̩-i ko nyʼefu akpulu-me̩, ku me̩ muko nyʼo̩gane̩ ache e̩ne̩ le̩ ele, o̩bia bam pe̩, kpai iño̩ pe̩, e̩wñ ido̩ro̩ kpai otulale mur, kpai e̩yo̩ oli ku ma je̩, kpai almond.
Me̩ mʼo̩ko̩ alu o̩me̩-wñ meji ko nyʼo̩wo̩-me̩ alo; o̩ko̩ ki dabi wʼef alu akpulu-me̩ le̩, me̩ muko nyʼo̩wo̩-me̩ alo ge̩; ikani i chʼibe legudu le̩.
Me̩ ki ño̩ mʼo̩maye-me̩ du ku me̩ kwane̩ alo tʼugbo e̩ne̩ le̩ ge̩.
Oñ O̩jo̩ Odobao̩gagu kʼi je̩ ñw e̩ne̩ le̩ li me̩ ejumomi todu kʼi tʼo̩maye-me̩ ekeji no̩ ñwu me̩ kpai Be̩njamin. Iche̩wñ kʼuku mʼamo̩ma-mi ko, mak eko i ko le̩.
Tak aboke̩le̩ le̩ mʼe̩wñ ele ko, ma ño̩ mʼo̩ko̩ alu o̩me̩ meji ko nyʼo̩wo̩-ma, kpai Be̩njamin; oñ ma kwane̩, ma le tʼo̩gane̩ Ijipti, ma la kwodago o̩gba Jose̩f.
Tak e̩gba ku Jose̩f fu Be̩njamin li ugbo ma, i ka ñw adejutunyi-wñ, kakini, Mʼabo le̩ ko wʼef unyi, fʼela kpa kʼe̩ fʼu ñwo̩che, todu aboke̩le̩-i aje̩ e̩wñ kpai omi o̩ro̩ka-i.
Tak e̩ne̩ le̩ che alu ku Jose̩f ka, oñ i mʼaboke̩le̩ le̩ ko nyʼunyi Jose̩f.
Tak aboke̩le̩ le̩ kwochokpo todabu ku ma mʼuma ko wʼunyi Jose̩f, oñ ma kakini, Tod o̩ko̩ ku ma mudu dabi tefu akpulu-wa e̩gba ejodudu le̩, todule̩ oñ ma ko wa wʼejefu-i, todu kʼi li uña kʼi agulo̩ bʼuwa ma, kʼi mʼuwa ko chʼadu, kpai amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩-wa.
Taku ma te̩ me̩ru adejutunyi Jose̩f le̩ ma ko̩la ñw u alugbo na unyi le̩,
kakini, Odu-mi, awa wʼo̩gane̩ emi ala uje̩wñ e̩gba ejodudu le̩ ochochi,
oñ i lewatu e̩gba kʼa lewa uru kʼa mʼakpulu-wa tu, go, o̩ko̩ e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ dʼalu akpulu-wñ, o̩ko̩-wa du jo̩ kpa; oñ a ño̩ du nʼo̩wo̩ dabi wa-i.
A la nʼo̩ko̩ omune̩ o̩wo̩-wa wa kʼa du la uje̩wñ ge. Awa ma e̩ne̩ kʼi kʼo̩ko̩-wa nyʼef akpulu-wa n.
Tak i kakini, Ugbe̩do̩ ki dʼugbo me̩, me̩ chokpo n; O̩jo̩-me̩ kpai O̩jo̩ ata-me̩, owñ du odochia tʼef akpulu-me̩ le̩; omi mʼo̩ko̩-me̩ gba me̩. Tak i mu Simeon dudufu wʼugbo ma.
Abe̩le̩ e̩ne̩ le̩ mʼaboke̩le̩ le̩ ko wʼef unyi Jose̩f, oñ i mʼomiofo du ñwu ma, ma la fʼe̩re̩-ma gwe̩; tak i mʼije ko ñw amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩-ma le̩.
Taku ma fʼe̩wñ ele le̩ ñwo̩che te anede Jose̩f e̩gba kʼi awa o̩ro̩ka; todu ma chegbo̩ ku ma aje̩ uje̩wñ o̩mo̩.
Oñ e̩gba ku Jose̩f lewʼunyi, ma mʼe̩wñ ele ki dʼo̩wo̩-ma ko wʼugbo-wñ ef unyi, ma lewa bʼane̩ ma ñw u.
Tak i tene o̩lafia-ma, i kakini, Ata-me̩ ra? ogijo e-ku me̩ kʼo̩la-wñ le̩, i deju ta?
Taku ma kakini, Adu-we, ata-wa, chʼo̩lafia, i deju ta. Taku ma mʼoji dalo̩, ma fʼu gwa.
Tak i dʼeju dago, oñ i fu Be̩njamin, o̩ma iye-wñ li, i kakini, Okekele-me̩ e-ku me̩ kʼo̩la-wñ ñwu mi le̩ de̩? Tak i kakini, O̩jo̩ ki chʼufe̩de̩nyo̩ ñw e̩, o̩ma-mi.
Taku Jose̩f naju, todu udo̩laga o̩maye-wñ je̩ ñw u n, oñ i tene ugbo kʼi anyʼaraku. Tak i mugudu tef unyi olu-wñ, i kworaku o̩mo̩.
Tak i fʼeju-wñ gwe, oñ i kwodufu; i mʼo̩la-wñ ne, i kakini. Kʼuje̩wñ wa.
Taku ma mʼe-owñ du gugu ojoji ñw u, e-ma la dʼugbo e-ma, e-abo Ijipti ku ma je̩ e̩wñ kpai owñ dʼugbo e-ma, todabu ki ma dugbo kʼabo Ijipti aje̩ e̩wñ kpai abo Hibru n, tod e̩wñ ibie̩ne̩ i che ñw abo Ijipti.
Taku ma kwogugu o̩gba-wñ, o̩mo̩gba gugu uña ogijo, e-kekele la gugu uña imo̩to̩-wñ; oñ i mud e̩wñ awuwu ñw aboke̩le̩ le̩.
Tak i je̩ ñwu ma mʼeli o̩je̩ chi kwef e-ki dʼo̩gba-wñ, ku ma du wa ñwu ma, eli o̩je̩ Be̩njamin muda tʼe-e̩ne̩ du ki dʼefu-ma le onu me̩lu. Abe̩le̩ ma ñmo̩, ma chane̩ eyo̩ kpai owñ.
Jose̩f jʼamo̩maye-wñ ma
Tak i ñwa ñw adejutunyi-wñ kakini, E̩ kʼuje̩wñ nyʼakpulu aboke̩le̩-i eko̩, alu ku ma neke ne̩, e̩ la mʼo̩ko̩ e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ko jʼef alu akpulu-wñ.
Tak e̩ mʼago-mi, ago e-ajifa le̩, du tʼef alu akpulu e-kekele, kpai o̩ko̩ e̩wñ e̩yo̩-wñ ge̩. Tak i che alu ku Jose̩f ka ñw u.
Odudu e̩gba kʼane̩ ne̩, ma fʼaboke̩le̩ le̩ kpe̩ lolo, ama kpai amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩-ma.
E̩gba ku ma kwʼewo le̩ ku ma ma le jiji ta n, Jose̩f ka ñw adejutunyi-wñ kakini, Kwane̩, rano aboke̩le̩ le̩; e̩gba kʼe̩ fʼuma mu e̩ ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩wñ chi ku me̩ dʼe̩bie̩ne̩ ro̩me̩ e̩nyo̩?
I chʼe̩wñ kʼodu-mi añmo̩ omi efu-wñ de̩ n? kpai e̩wñ kʼi adu ñw e̩ñwa n? e̩wñ ku me̩ che le̩, me̩ fʼe̩bie̩ne̩ che me̩.
Tak i fʼuma mu, oñ i fʼo̩la-i ka ñwu ma.
Oñ ma ka ñw u kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼodu-mi akʼo̩la abe̩i? Eche e̩wñ abe̩i che̩jijiru amadu-we̩-i!
E̩ go, o̩ko̩ kʼa li alu akpulu-wa, a mudu kwʼane̩ Kenan dabiwa ñw e̩; ab i le kʼawa neke joji ajifa abe̩k o̩jamalia kwef unyi odu-we̩ ge̩?
E̩ne̩ du ef amadu-we̩ ku ma liʼu ugbo-wñ kʼi leku, tʼawa, a ñʼache adu odu-mi ge̩.
Tak i kakini, Alu ku me̩ ka abe̩le̩ i ade̩: e̩ne̩ ku ma liʼu ugbo-wñ e̩ne̩ le̩ amud adu-mi; tak ame̩ amufu.
Taku ma hiane̩, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ mʼakpulu-wñ ro̩gu wʼane̩, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩-ma mʼalu akpulu-wñ tu.
Oñ i tejane̩, i chane̩ ugbo e-ogijo, i kpoji ugbo e-imo̩to̩; ma la fʼago le̩ li ef akpulu Be̩njamin.
Taku ma fʼe̩wñ o̩la-ma fana, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ mʼadu-wñ ko nʼubi o̩ke̩ke̩te̩-wñ, oñ ma mudabi tʼewo le̩.
E̩gba ku Juda kpai amo̩maye-wñ lewa unyi Jose̩f, i la dʼe̩gu-wñ ta; ma fʼo̩la-ma ro̩ fiane̩ o̩gba-wñ.
