Taku Jose̩f ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩wñ chʼe-ku me̩ che-i ta? Ame̩ ma kʼe̩ne̩ e̩gʼe-mi chʼuli n?
Taku Juda kakini, E̩wñ a aka ñw odu-mi ke̩? ab a aka? Ab a ale kʼa gbʼo̩la-wa te̩? O̩jo̩ fʼudu kʼamadu-we̩ fe̩ li me̩; go, awa chʼadu odu-mi, tʼawa, tʼe̩ne̩ ku ma fʼago le̩ li o̩wo̩-wñ ge̩.
Tak i kakini, Echʼabe̩le̩ ki jiji rʼumi! e̩ne̩ ku ma li ago le̩ o̩wo̩-wñ, e̩ne̩ le̩ achʼadu-mi; i chʼe-me̩, me̩ kwane̩ alo tʼugbo ata-me̩ kpai ure̩do̩.
Taku Juda te̩me̩rʼu, I kakini, Aiya, odu-mi, narodubʼuwe̩ kʼe̩ je̩ ñw adu-we̩-i ka o̩laʼka nyʼodu-mi eti, e̩ ki we̩do̩ rʼadu-we̩ n; todu uwe̩ dabe̩ne̩ ku Fero onugo.
Odu-mi, tʼamadu-wñ ene kakini, Ame̩ nʼata abe̩k o̩maye e̩ne̩ke̩le̩?
Tak a ka ñw odu-mi kakini, Awa nʼata, i chʼogijo, i la nʼo̩maʼka o̩jʼogijo-wñ, o̩ma ke̩ke̩ i che; o̩maye-wñ la leku, e-kate chʼo̩ma iye-wñ kibo̩; ata-wñ la fe̩do̩-wñ.
Tak uwe̩ ka ñw amadu-we̩ kakini, Me̩ mʼu du gwo̩ru wʼugbo mi emi todu kʼeju-mi ki dʼo.
Tak awa ka ñw odu-mi kakini, Imo̩to̩ le̩ neke tʼata-wñ no̩ n, todu iche̩wñ kʼi kwo bʼata-wñ te̩, ata-wñ aku.
Tak uwe̩ ka ñw amadu-we̩ kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼokekele-me̩ ma wa o̩gane̩ emi kpai ame̩ n, ame̩ ñʼali eju-mi ge̩ n.
Oñ i lewatʼe̩gba kʼa wʼate̩ ugbo adu-we̩, ata-mi, awa mʼo̩la odu-mi du ka ñw u.
Tak ata-wa kakini, Me̩ ño̩ lo ku me̩ lʼuje̩wñ wa ñw a pe̩.
Tak awa kakini, Awa neke nyʼo̩gane̩ n: iche̩wñ kʼokekele-wa dʼefu-wa tak a anyʼo̩gane̩; todu ma aje̩ ñw a li eju e̩ne̩ le̩ n, chai e̩gba kʼokekele-wa dʼugbo wa.
Tak adu-we̩, ata-mi, ka ñw a kakini, Ame̩ chema kʼo̩ya-mi fʼamo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ meji bi ñwu mi;
oñ oka kwo bʼumi te̩, u la kakini, Ma fʼowñ fana rinyo̩ pe̩le̩pe̩le̩ ochochi; akwihi le̩ u ño̩ liʼu ge̩ n.
I la che̩wñ ku me̩ ño̩ mʼe-ki de̩ du kwʼugbo mi, kʼe̩wñ bie̩ne̩ ke̩re̩bʼo̩, ame̩ adu iloji efulu-mi tef o̩jegu bie̩ne̩.
Todule̩ fai, e̩gba kʼu lewa ugbo adu-we̩, ata-mi, kʼimo̩to̩ Je̩ ma dʼugbo wa n, todabu kʼiñmi-wñ che̩wenyu onugo iñmi imo̩to̩-i,
abe̩le̩ e̩gba kʼi ali kʼimo̩to̩ le̩ ma dʼugbo wa n, i aku; oñ amadu-we̩ adʼiloji efufu e-adu-we̩, ata-wa, tef o̩jegu kpai e̩do̩dudu.
Todu adu-we̩ dʼo̩la-wñ chʼe̩wñ uhio̩wo̩ imo̩to̩ le̩ ñw ata-mi, u ka ñw u kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼomi ma dʼu dabi wa ñw e̩ n, e̩gbale̩ mak adure ogbegbele̩ oñ u du ata-mi re le̩.
Todule̩ fai, narodubʼe̩, e̩ je̩ ñw adu-we̩-i kʼi gugu chʼadu ñw odu-mi-i koji okolobia le̩; kʼe̩ je̩ ñw okolobia le̩ lo tʼate̩ kpai amo̩maye-wñ.
Todu abʼu nnle̩ kʼu nanyʼate̩ ugbo ata-mi kʼokolobia le̩ ma dʼugbo mi n? tode̩gba kʼu nali e̩bie̩ne̩ ki abʼata-mi ma.
Jose̩f je̩ ñw amo̩maye-wñ ma e̩ne̩ kʼi che
E̩gbale̩ Jose̩f neke ño̩ fʼo̩wo̩ mʼo̩la-wñ ne̩ eju abo ku ma dago kpenyʼu ge̩ n; tak i ka nana kakini, Me̩ je̩ ñw e̩ne̩ du ki kwobʼumi te̩ nyʼo̩do̩da. Oñ e̩ne̩ du bo̩ ugbo-wñ e̩gba ku Jose̩f dʼo̩la-wñ dufu ñw amo̩maye-wñ n.
Tak i naraku taa, oñ abo Ijipti gbo̩, abo unyi Fero ño̩ gbo̩ du.
Taku Jose̩f ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ kakini, Omi Jose̩f de̩; ata-mi deju ta? Amo̩maye-wñ la neke dohi ñw u n, todu ugoju mu ma da eli ku ma liʼi.
Taku Jose̩f ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ kakini, Agba, me̩ te̩me̩ru mi. Taku ma te̩me̩rʼu. Oñ i kakini, Omi che Jose̩f o̩maye-me̩, e-ku me̩ mudu ta tʼIjipti.
E̩do̩-me̩ ki kpabie̩ n, me̩ ki we̩do̩ rʼo̩la-me̩ ukpe̩ ku me̩ ta mi wʼemi n; todu O̩jo̩ kpe̩ mi wa o̩gba-me̩ kʼoji one̩ ki do̩mo̩.
Todu, o̩do̩ meji kʼukpo̩ta chane̩ ekpa ane̩-i de̩ ta; i laño̩ bo̩ o̩do̩ me̩lu tak i anʼuche̩ elo, ma la ane̩ e̩wñ ku ma ko nyʼaka n.
O̩jo̩ la kpe̩ mi dʼo̩gba-me̩ wa kʼu fʼejutʼame̩ ku me̩ chʼabubo̩ amone̩ ile̩, kʼu mʼoji-me̩ gba lʼef ujadu elile.
Todule̩ i la chʼame̩ kpe̩ mi wʼemi n, chai O̩jo̩; owñ la mʼumi du chʼata Fero kpai odu abunyi-wñ du, kpai agboji ane̩ Ijipti chaka.
Me̩ hiane̩ ku me̩ nyʼate̩ ugbo ata-mi, ku me̩ ka ñw u kakini, Abu kʼo̩ma-we̩ Jose̩f ka de̩ kakini, O̩jo̩ mʼumi du chʼodu Ijipti du; gwo̩ru wʼugbo mi, e̩ ki fo̩kpane̩ n;
uwe̩ ki dodo ane̩ Goshe̩n, tak uwe̩ ame̩rʼumi, uwe̩ kpai amo̩ma-we̩, kpai amaaju-we̩, kpai ame̩wño̩re̩-we̩ egini kpai amokuno̩-we̩ kpai e̩wñ du kʼe̩ ne̩;
o̩mo̩ nane̩ uwe̩, todu o̩do̩ ukpo̩ta bo̩ e̩lu ta; tode̩gba kʼi agwʼuwe̩ e̩nale, uwe̩ kpai abunyi-we̩, kpai e̩wñ du kʼe̩ ne̩.
Me̩ go, eju-me̩ cheli, kpai eju o̩maye-mi, Be̩njamin, ka kʼalu e-mi u nʼako̩la ñwu me̩-i.
Me̩ ki dʼojima-mi ane̩ Ijipti du ka ñw ata-mi, kpai e̩wñ du ku me̩ liʼi. Me̩ nahiane̩ ku me̩ dʼata-mi gwo̩ru wʼemi.
Tak i fʼo̩wo̩ lo nyʼo̩lo̩ o̩maye-wñ Be̩njamin, i chane̩ eraku; Be̩njamin la raku nʼowñ o̩lo̩.
Tak i dʼalu-wñ ko̩ amo̩maye-wñ alu chaka, oñ i raku nyʼuma o̩la; ubi le̩ tak amo̩maye-wñ ko̩la kpai owñ.
Fero do̩ ata kpai amo̩maye Jose̩f wʼIjipti
E̩gba ku ma gbo̩ uwohi-wñ ef unyi Fero kakini, Amo̩maye Jose̩f lewa me̩, i la chenyo̩ Fero eju nana, kpai amadu-wñ.
Taku Fero ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, E̩ ka ñw amo̩maye-we̩ ka kʼabu ku me̩ ache de̩: me̩ mʼadu ko nʼubi ame̩la ki anʼadu-me̩, ku me̩ mudabi tʼane̩ Kenan;
me̩ ki mʼata-me̩ kpai abunyi-me̩ ko wa ugbo mi, tak u nadʼugbo ki nyo̩ ane̩ Ijipti ñwu me̩, oñ ame̩ ajʼura ane̩-i.
U ñwa ñw e̩ me̩, abu ku me̩ ache de̩: me̩ ki mʼo̩ko̩ane̩ kʼamanya afo̩ ko kwo ane̩ Ijipti todu abimo̩to̩-me̩, kpai amo̩ya-me̩, me̩ ki la mʼata-me̩ du ku me̩ lewa.
Me̩ ki kula kpʼe̩wñ e-me̩ n, todu e̩wñ e̩nyo̩ du ane̩ Ijipti chʼe-me̩.
Tak amo̩ma Israe̩l chʼabe̩le̩; oñ Jose̩f kʼo̩ko̩ane̩ ñwu ma alu ku Fero ka kpʼalu-wñ, i ño̩ kʼe̩wñ ku ma aje̩ ej o̩na ñwu ma.
I mʼukpo alomuda ko ñw o̩chaka-ma okʼoke; i rnuda mʼajifa oli me̩fa ko ñwu Be̩njamin kpai ukpo alomuda me̩lu.
Alu kʼi du kpuche̩ rʼata-wñ de̩: o̩ke̩ke̩te̩ me̩gwa kʼadu ki nʼubi-ma che̩ko̩ e̩wñ e̩nyo̩ ane̩ Ijipti, kpai amole o̩ke̩ke̩te̩ me̩gwa kʼadu ki nʼubi-ma che̩ko̩ ñw e̩wñ e̩yo̩ kpai uje̩wñ kpai e̩fiye̩ e̩wñ kʼata-wñ aje̩ ej o̩na.
Abe̩le̩ i fʼamo̩maye-wñ kpuche̩ lelo, oñ abu ku ma alo i ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ nago edareji ej o̩na.
Taku ma mute̩gu kwʼane̩ Ijipti dufu, oñ ma lewa ane̩ Kenan ugbo Jeko̩b ata-ma.
Taku ma ka ñw u kakini, Jose̩f deju ta, owñ la nʼo̩da ane̩ Ijipti chaka. Tak e̩do̩-wñ muda kpu, todu i dʼo̩la-ma rʼochochi n.
Taku ma mʼo̩la Jose̩f e-kʼi ka ñwu ma chaka du ka ñw u, tak e̩gba kʼi fʼo̩ko̩ane̩ e-ku Jose̩f du kpuche̩ wa ku ma du dʼowñ alo li, iñmi Jeko̩b ata-ma ruko;
tak Israe̩l kakini, I nyo̩ me̩; Jose̩f, o̩ma-mi deju ta; nanyʼali owñ o̩gba tak u ku.
Jeko̩b kpai abo-wñ ño̩ wʼIjipti
Abe̩le̩ Israe̩l mʼe̩wñ du kʼi ne̩ ko, oñ i mʼo̩na ule̩-wñ du, oñ i lewa Birshiba, tak i kʼe̩wñ kpa ñw O̩jo̩ e-Aise̩k ata-wñ.
O̩jo̩ la ko̩la ñw Israe̩l ef ane̩ ego odu, kakini, Jeko̩b, Jeko̩b. Oñ i kakini, Omi de̩.
Tak i kakini, Omi chʼO̩jo̩, O̩jo̩ e-ata-we̩; e̩ ki railo egwo̩ru nyʼIjipti n; todu o̩mo̩ nadʼuwe̩ chʼuche̩ichi lile.
Nagwo̩ru nyʼIjipti kpai uwe̩; nañʼadʼuwe̩ te̩gu kwo o̩mo̩ wa chuu; Jose̩f la adʼo̩wo̩-wñ bʼuwe̩ eju ma.
Taku Jeko̩b kwo Birshiba alo; oñ amo̩ma Israe̩l mu Jeko̩b ata-ma du, kpai abimo̩to̩-ma, kpai amo̩ya-ma ef o̩ko̩ane̩ e-ku Fero du kpuche̩ wa adʼu.
Ma ño̩ mʼame̩wñ ukpa-ma kpai ane̩-ma ku ma fiye̩ jo̩ ane̩ Kenan ko, oñ ma lewa Ijipti, Jeko̩b kpai ugbe̩-wñ du,
amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, kpai amaaju-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, amo̩ma-wñ onobule̩, kpai amaaju-wñ onobule̩, e-kʼamo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi; i la mʼamugbe̩-wñ chaka ko wʼIjipti kpai owñ.
Odu abimo̩to̩ Israe̩l ku ma wʼane̩ Ijipti le̩ de̩, Jeko̩b kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩. Rube̩n, o̩mo̩gba Jeko̩b,
amo̩ma Rube̩n e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che Hano̩k kpai Palu kpai He̩zro̩n kpai Karmi.
Amo̩ma Simeo̩n e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: Jemue̩l kpai Jamin kpai Ohad kpai Jachin kpai Zohar kpai Sho̩l ki chʼo̩ma kʼonobule̩ Kenan oka bi ñw u.
Amo̩ma Lifai e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che̩: Ge̩rsho̩n kpai Ko̩hat kpai Me̩rari.
Amo̩ma Juda e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: E̩r kpai O̩nan kpai Shela kpai Pe̩re̩z kpai Zera (Er kpai Onan muda leku ane̩ Kenan); amo̩ma Pe̩re̩z e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: He̩zro̩n kpai Hamul.
Amo̩ma Isakar e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: To̩la kpai Pufa kpai Job kpai Shimro̩n.
Amo̩ma Ze̩biulo̩n e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: Se̩re̩d kpai E̩lon kpai Jalee̩l. 15(Abo-i chʼamo̩ma Lea e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-kʼi bi ñwu Jeko̩b Padan-aram, manyʼo̩ma-wñ onobule̩ Daina; onugo amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩ du chʼogue̩gwa nyoke me̩ta.)
Amo̩ma Gad e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: Zifion kpai Hagi kpai Shuni kpai E̩zbon kpai Eri kpai Arodi kpai Areli.
Amo̩ma Ashe̩r e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: Imna kpai Ishfa kpai Ishfi kpai Be̩raya kpai Sera o̩maye-ma onobule̩. Amo̩ma Be̩raya e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che̩: Hebe̩r kpai Malkie̩l. 18(Abo-i chamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Zilpa, ku Le̩ban du ñwu Lea o̩ma-wñ onobule̩; abo-i chʼabo kʼi la bi ma ñwu Jeko̩b—owñ chʼonugo one̩ me̩gwe̩fa.)
Amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Reche̩l o̩ya Jeko̩b che: Jose̩f kpai Be̩njamin.
Ane̩ Ijipti ma bi Manasa kpai Ifraim ñwu Jose̩f, ama chʼe-kʼAse̩nat o̩ma Potife̩ra kʼi chʼatama On le̩, bi ñw u.
Amo̩ma Be̩njamin e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: Bila kpai Be̩ke̩r kpai Ashbe̩l kpai Gera kpai Neaman kpai Ehi kpai Rosh kpai Muppim kpai Huppim kpai Ard. 22(Abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-ki Reche̩l bi ñwu Jeko̩b—onugo one̩ le̩ du chʼe̩gwe̩le̩.)
Amo̩ma Dan e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: Hushim.
Amo̩ma Naftali e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: Jazee̩l kpai Guni kpai Jeze̩r kpai Shile̩m. 25(Abo-i chʼamo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-Bilha ku Leban du ñwu Reche̩l o̩ma-wñ onobule̩, abo-i la chʼabo kʼi bi ma ñwu Jeko̩b—onugo one̩ le̩ du chʼebie.)
Onugo one̩ du ku ma lebo̩ Jeko̩b wa Ijipti, owñ chʼabo ku ma kwo uta-wñ dufu, amo̩ya amo̩ma Jeko̩b la dʼo̩ n; onugo one̩ du le̩ chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩ta nyoke me̩fa;
amo̩ma Jose̩f e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ku ma bi ñw u Ijipti chʼonugo one̩ meji; onugo one̩ du ki chʼabunyi Jeko̩b ki wʼIjipti chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩ta nyoke me̩gwa.
Tak i fu Juda kpe̩ tʼo̩gba-wñ nyʼugbo Jose̩f, kʼi jiwe o̩na Goshe̩n ñwu ma; oñ ma lewa ane̩ Goshe̩n.
Taku Jose̩f ko ane̩ nyef o̩ko̩ ogu-wñ, i mute̩gu aledo Israe̩l ata-wñ nyi Goshe̩n; oñ i dʼo̩la-wñ dufu ñw u, i la fʼo̩wo̩ lo nyʼo̩lo̩-wñ, oñ i nʼo̩lo̩-wñ araku gbane̩ gbane̩.
Tak Israe̩l ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Dagba u leku ke, abu kʼu fʼeju-we̩ li, kʼe̩ la deju-i.
Taku Jose̩f ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ kpai abo unyi ata-wñ, kakini, Nate̩gu nyʼaka ñwu Fero, oñ naka ñw u kakini, Amo̩maye-mi kpai abo unyi ata-mi ku ma jʼane̩ Kenan lewa ugbo-mi me̩;
aboke̩le̩ le̩ che abo ku ma kʼije̩ ñw ame̩wño̩re egini je̩; todu ama chʼabo ku ma nʼame̩wñ ukpa; ma la nʼame̩wño̩re̩-ma egini kpai amokuno-ma kpai e̩wñ du ku ma ne wa.
Oñ i awatu e̩gba ku Fero ado̩ me̩ kʼi kakini, Uko̩lo̩ e̩wñ me̩ che?
Ame̩ ki kakini, Ame̩wñukpa e̩ne̩ chʼobe amadu-we̩-i, akwo o̩jo̩ imo̩to̩-wa gbogbo wa ifai, tʼawa, tʼamata-wa, todu kʼame̩ ki dodo ane̩ Goshen; todu adide ame̩wño̩re̩ egini du chʼe̩wñ ihie̩ne̩ ugbo abo Ijipti.
Taku Jose̩f nyʼugbo Fero aka ñw u, kakini, Ata-mi kpai amo̩maye-mi kpai ame̩wño̩re-ma egini kpai amokuno̩-ma kpai e̩wñ du ku ma ne̩, kwʼane̩ Kenan lewa me̩; go, ma jʼoj ane̩ Goshe̩n.
Oñ i mʼaboke̩le̩ me̩lu chi kwef amo̩maye-wñ kʼi ko ma wʼugbo Fero kʼi ma ma.
Taku Fero ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ, kakini, Obe e̩wñ me̩ che? Taku ma ka ñwu Fero, kakini, Amadu-we̩-i chʼamadide ame̩wño̩re egini, tʼawa, tʼamata-wa.
Ma ño̩ ka ñwu Fero, kakini, A lewa kʼa ge̩ne̩ ane̩-i, todu ugbo kʼame̩wño̩re amadu-we̩ egini ajije̩ de̩ ge̩ n: todu ukpo̩ta akpa ololo ane̩ Kenan; todule̩ a rodubʼe̩, kʼe̩ je̩ ñw amadu-we̩ gugu ane̩ Goshe̩n.
Taku Fero ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Ata-we̩ kpai amo̩maye-we̩ lewa ugbo-we̩ me̩.
Ane̩ Ijipti te̩ ñw e̩-i; ugbo kʼane̩ nyo̩ tule e̩ dʼata-we̩ kpai amo̩maye-we̩ gugu; je̩ ñwu ma gugu ane̩ Goshe̩n; i la che̩wñ kʼe̩ ma abo ki le efu-ma, mak e̩ ko ma chʼamagboji abo ku ma de ame̩wñ ukpa e-mi.
Taku Jose̩f mu Jeko̩b ata-wñ duwa, oñ i mʼu du gugu o̩gba Fero; taku Jeko̩b kadua ñwu Fero.
Oñ Fero ka ñwu Jeko̩b, kakini, O̩do̩ onu ma biʼe̩?
Taku Jeko̩b ka ñwu Fero kakini, O̩do̩ o̩jo̩ ege̩ne̩-mi kʼu ge̩ne̩-i chʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩fa nyoke me̩gwa; o̩jo̩ o̩do̩ udeju-mi la wewe n, i ño̩ chʼe̩bie̩ne̩, i la tu alu o̩jo̩ o̩do̩ udeju amata-mi ef ege̩ne̩ ku ma ge̩ne̩ le ta n.
Taku Jeko̩b kadua ñwu Fero, oñ i kwʼo̩gba Fero dufu.
Taku Jose̩f hiʼata-wñ kpai amo̩maye-wñ gugu, i la bʼane̩ ñwu ma ku ma ne̩ ane̩ Ijipti, ugbo kʼane̩ nyo̩ tule, oj ane̩ Ramese̩s, alu ku Fero ñwa te̩.
Oñ Jose̩f dʼuje̩wñ ñw ata-wñ kpai amo̩maye-wñ, kpai abo unyi ata-wñ du je̩, alu kʼuwewe abo unyi unyi-ma de̩.
Uje̩wñ ño̩ bo̩ ane̩ o̩mo̩ du ge̩ n; todu ukpo̩ta le̩ akpa ololo, oñ o̩la abo ane̩ Ijipti kpai abo ane̩ Kenan muda noji ukpo̩ta ki akpa.
Jose̩f la mʼo̩ko̩ du ku ma li ane̩ Ijipti yajo̩ kpai e-ane̩ Kenan, tod e̩wñ e̩yo̩ ku ma la; oñ Jose̩f mʼo̩ko̩ le̩ ko wʼef unyi Fero.
Tak e̩gba ku ma mʼo̩ko̩ du ki dʼane̩ Ijipti ko la e̩wñ kpa, kpai e-ki dʼane̩ Kenan, abo ane̩ Ijipti chaka lewʼugbo Jose̩f, ma kakini, Dʼuje̩wñ ñw a; e̩wñ chi kʼa ku rinyo̩ eju-we̩-i? todu o̩ko̩-wa takpa.
Taku Jose̩f kakini, O̩ko̩-me̩ takpa maku me̩ kʼame̩wñ ukpa-me̩ wa, tak u nadʼuje̩wñ koji ñwu me̩.
Abe̩le̩ ma kʼame̩wñ ukpa-ma wʼugbo Jose̩f; taku Jose̩f kʼuje̩wñ koji amanya-ma kpai koji ame̩wñ ukpa ki chʼala kpai ewo kpai ame̩wñ ukpa ki chʼokuno̩ kpai amo̩ke̩ke̩te̩ ñwu ma: abe̩le̩ i kʼuje̩wñ ñwu ma je̩ koji ame̩wñ ukpa-ma du o̩do̩ le̩.
E̩gba kʼo̩do̩ le muda ma ño̩ lewʼugbo-wñ o̩do̩ ekeji, ma la ka ñw u kakini, Awa adu maja ñw odu-mi alu kʼa kʼo̩ko̩-wa la e̩wñ kpa n; ame̩wñ ukpa ki chʼabe̩re̩me̩le̩ du la mud e-odu-mi; e̩wñ du bo̩ eju odu-mi n, chai año̩la-wa kpai ane̩-wa kate;
tode̩wñ a ku rinyo̩ eju-we̩ meji? tʼawa tʼane̩-wa? Fʼawa kpai ane̩-wa la tod uje̩wñ, tak awa kpai ane̩-wa ache amadu ñwu Fero; e̩ la mʼulu e̩wñ ko ñw a kʼa deju kʼa we eku, todu kʼane̩ ki we echʼalache̩.
Abe̩le̩ Jose̩f fane̩ Ijipti du la ñwu Fero; todu e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ abo Ijipti du mʼane̩ uche̩-wñ duta, todabu kʼukpo̩ta akpa ololo, oñ ane̩ le̩ mud e-Fero.
I chʼe-amone̩ le̩ i mʼuma ko kpe̩ jo̩ ewo ewo kwo alo̩me̩ ane̩ Ijipti oka gbogbo wʼalo̩me̩ ekeji.
Chai ane̩ amatama kate oñ i ma gba la n; todu amatama che̩nʼo̩da e-ma ugbo Fero, ma la je̩ e̩wñ o̩da e-ma ku Fero du ñwu ma; todule̩ oñ ma ma kʼane̩-ma ta n.
Taku Jose̩f ka ñw amone̩ le̩ kakini, Me̩ go, omi fʼame̩ kpai ane̩-me̩ la ñwu Fero eñini. Go, ulu e̩wñ-me̩ de̩ ku me̩ gbe̩ ane̩.
Oñ i awatu e̩gba ku me̩ ako e̩wñ oko wʼunyi, ame̩ ki kʼukpe̩ e̩ke̩lu ñwu Fero, oñ ukpe̩ me̩le̩ kibo̩ achʼe-me̩ o̩to̩to̩la-me̩, todu ulu oko kpai uje̩wñ-me̩, todu abo unyi-me̩ kpai uje̩wñ todu abo-me̩ egini.
Taku ma kakini, Uwe̩ mʼoji-wa gba te̩ me̩; odu-mi kʼi li wa eju dee, mak amadu Fero awa che ke.
Taku Jose̩f mʼe-le̩ du chʼe̩wñ uhio̩me̩ ane̩ Ijipti gbogbo tʼojolu eñini, ka ku Fero anʼukpe̩ e̩ke̩lu e̩wñ du, chai ane̩ amatama kate ma chʼe-Fero n.
Abe̩le̩ Israe̩l gugu Ijipti, oj ane̩ Goshe̩n; oñ ma chane̩ e̩wñ ene̩ o̩mo̩, ma la bi o̩ma oñ ma wewe nyo̩gba ololo.
Jeko̩b la dʼo̩do̩ me̩gwebie ane̩ Ijipti; abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ Jeko̩b, owñ chʼo̩do̩ kʼi da tak i ku, chʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ mebie nyoke mebie.
Oñ iko e̩gba kʼIsrae̩l adʼiñmi me̩ru awa, i la fʼo̩ma-wñ Jose̩f do̩ wa, i ka ñw u kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼe̩ li mi eju, narodubʼe̩, e̩ ki dʼo̩wo̩-we̩ nʼuta-mi ka kʼe̩ che e̩wñ e̩nyo̩ kpai ochochi ugbo mi. Narodubʼe̩, e̩ ki du mi ji ane̩ Ijipti n,
ama e̩gba kʼu kwo dachi manyʼamata-mi, uwe̩ ki mʼumi du kwʼ Ijipti alo, kʼe̩ mʼumi du ji ane̩ ojinoji amata-mi. Tak i dohi, Nache alu kʼe̩ ka.
Tak i kakini, E̩ fu go̩ ñwu mi; oñ i fu go̩ ñw u. Tak Israe̩l fʼoji-wñ dalo̩ nʼoji ate̩-wñ le̩.
Jeko̩b kadua ñwu Manasa kpai Ifraim
Oñ i lewatʼubi e̩wñ le̩ ge̩, kʼe̩ne̩ʼka ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Go, ata-we̩ acho̩ga; tak i mʼamo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ meji, Manasa kpai Ifraim, ko rubi alo.
Oñ ma ka ñwu Jeko̩b, kakini. Go, o̩ma-we̩ Jose̩f awʼugbo-we̩-i; tak Israe̩l fʼeju gbiti gugu oj ate̩.
Oñ Jeko̩b ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, O̩jo̩ Odobao̩gagu dʼo̩la-wñ tejugede ñwu mi Luz oj ane̩ Kenan, i la de̩nyo̩ ñwu mi,
oñ i ka ñwu mi kakini. Go, nakʼamo̩ma ñw e̩ wewe, naje̩ ñw e̩ wewe nyo̩gba, naño̩ dʼuwe̩ che o̩wo̩ amone̩, oñ nadʼane̩ kide̩ ñw ugbe̩-we̩ ubi-we̩ ku ma ne̩ ogbegbele̩.
Fai amo̩ma-we̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ meji, e-ku ma bi ñw e̩ ane̩ Ijipti o̩gba tak u wʼugbo-we̩ Ijipti-i, chʼe-mi; Ifraim kpai Manasa achʼe-mi alu ku Rube̩n kpai Sime̩o̩n de̩.
Tak e-kʼuwe̩ adʼato̩ bi ubi-ma achʼe-we̩; oñ ma adʼodu amo̩maye-ma manyu ma ef e̩wñ ogu-ma.
I chʼe-mi, e̩gba kʼu kwo Padan wa, Reche̩l leku bʼumi te̩ ane̩ Kenan ej o̩na o̩mo̩, e̩gbale̩ ule̩ E̩frat bo̩ re ta; oñ u mʼu du ji o̩na E̩frat o̩mo̩ (owñ che Be̩tle̩he̩m).
Tak Israe̩l go amo̩ma Jose̩f e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ le̩, i kakini, Abo ugbo de̩-i?
Taku Jose̩f ka ñw ata-wñ kakini, Amo̩ma-mi, kʼO̩jo̩ ko ñwu mi emi, jo̩-i. Oñ i kakini, Narodubʼe̩, kʼe̩ ko ma wʼugbo mi-i, kʼu nakadua ñwu ma.
Abu kʼeju Israe̩l gbe̩ noj ogijo-wñ, i neke li e̩wñ n. Taku Jose̩f mʼuma ko me̩ru ugbo-wñ; oñ i dʼalu kʼuma alu, i la gba ma kʼe̩do̩.
Tak Israe̩l ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Ibe dʼedʼumi efu ka kʼu nali eju-we̩ n; e̩ la go, O̩jo̩ ño̩ je̩ ñwu mi li ugbe̩-we̩ ge̩.
Taku Jose̩f mʼuma ko kwo agada-wñ dufu, i te̩kpe̩ gbogbo wa fʼeju-wñ bʼane̩ ma.
Taku Jose̩f mʼama meji ko, Ifraim dʼo̩wo̩ awo̩to̩-wñ ugbo o̩wo̩ awohi Israe̩l, Manasa la dʼo̩wo̩-wñ awohi ugbo o̩wo̩ Israe̩l awo̩to̩, oñ i mʼuma ko me̩ru ugbo-wñ.
Tak Israe̩l nʼo̩wo̩ awo̩to̩-wñ dala i mʼu du ne̩ Ifraim, e-ki chʼimo̩to̩, oji, o̩wo̩ awohi-wñ la nʼoji Manasa, i gwejugede dʼo̩wo̩-wñ kofi omune̩ da, todu Manasa chʼo̩mo̩gba.
Tak i kadua ñwu Jose̩f, i kakini, O̩jo̩ e-kʼamata-mi Ebraham kpai Aise̩k lule̩ o̩gba-wñ le̩, O̩jo̩ e-ki ne̩ mi akwʼe̩gba ku ma bi mi gbogbo tʼeñini,
onuche̩ O̩jo̩ e-ki gba mi tane̩ bʼef e̩wñ e̩bie̩ne̩ du te̩, Owñ le̩ kʼi de̩nyo̩ ñw abokolobia-i; ama ki dʼodu-mi manyu ma, kpai odu amata-mi Ebraham kpai Aisek; ama ki mud o̩wo̩ one̩ o̩ge̩ge̩de̩ ile̩-i.
Tak e̩gba ku Jose̩f li kʼata-wñ dʼo̩wo̩-wñ awo̩to̩ nʼoji Ifraim, i bie̩ne̩ eju-wñ; tak i gwo̩nyu o̩wo̩ ata-wñ, kʼi mʼu du bʼoji Ifraim te̩ tʼoji Manasa.
Oñ Jose̩f ka ñw ata-wñ kakini, Ata-mi, i chʼabe̩le̩ no, todu e-kide̩ chʼo̩mo̩gba; mʼo̩wo̩ awo̩to̩-we̩ du nʼo oji.
Ata-wñ muda ko̩, oñ i kakini, U chema, o̩ma-mi, u chema; owñ le año̩ chʼuche̩ amone̩ kpo̩fo̩, owñ año̩ chʼelile ge̩; okekele-wñ muda anana tʼowñ le, oñ ugbe̩-wñ amud ukpe̩ko̩ amone̩ uche̩ uche̩.
Abe̩le̩ i kadua ñwu ma o̩jo̩ le̩, i kakini, Lugbo we̩ oñ abo Israe̩l akadua, kakini, O̩jo̩ ki je̩ ñw e̩ kʼe̩ dab Ifraim kpai Manasa; abe̩le̩ i dʼugugu Ifraim tʼo̩gba ñwu Manasa.
Tak Israe̩l ka ñwu Jose̩f kakini, Go, eku naku-i, O̩jo̩ muda adʼugbo we̩, i adʼuwe̩ dabi tʼane̩ amata-we̩ ge̩.
U la mʼukpe̩ ane̩ʼka, kʼomi nʼo̩kwo̩chageli-mi kpai o̩o̩do̩-mi bʼabo Amo̩r le̩ gba du ñw e̩ tʼamo̩maye-we̩ le.
Jeko̩b kadua ñw amo̩ma-wñ me̩gweji
Taku Jeko̩b nomudala do̩ amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ i kakini, Me̩ dʼo̩la-me̩ jeju, kʼu naka ñw me̩ e̩wñ ki ake̩re̩bʼume̩ e̩gba o̩jo̩ otitala.
Me̩ dʼo̩la-me̩ jeju ku me̩ gbo̩, ame̩ amo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Jeko̩b,
me̩ ki netirʼomu Israe̩l, ata-me̩.
Rube̩n, uwe̩ chʼo̩mo̩gba-mi
kpai ukpahiu-mi kpai ejo̩ga ugbiti-mi,
ehi nyate̩-we̩ kpai echo̩ko̩-we̩ tʼuma le.
Uwe̩ ana rinyo̩ dab omiofo, uwe̩ atʼo̩gba n
todabu kʼuwe̩ mute̩gu tʼoj ate̩ ata-we̩;
e̩gbale̩ e̩ fʼu daji—i mute̩gu tʼoj o̩kpo̩kpo̩-mi!
Simeo̩n kpai Lifai chʼo̩maye;
o̩lachi eche chʼo̩kwo̩chageli-ma.
O-o onugo-mi, e ki wʼef ojuju-ma n;
O ojima-mi, uwe̩ ki dama kpai ujeju-ma n;
todu ma kpʼamone̩ ef uwe̩do̩-ma,
ef e̩do̩fulu-ma ma mʼamo̩kokuno̩ ili e̩re̩ da.
Ama ki mu uwe̩do̩-ma, todu i bie̩ne̩;
kpai o̩fu-ma todu i chʼo̩lachi!
Nafʼuma kpe̩ru efu Jeko̩b
nafʼuma kpatuka efu Israe̩l.
Juda, amo̩maye-we̩ agogbodʼe̩;
o̩wo̩-we̩ adʼame̩nebi-we̩ o̩lo̩;
amo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ata-we̩ adanyeku o̩gba-we̩.
Juda chʼo̩ma idu;
o̩ma-mi, e̩ kwugbo e̩la o̩de̩ le̩ mute̩gu le me̩.
I te̩kpe̩, i hi e̩do̩ mʼane̩ dab idu,
dabe̩ne̩ kʼo̩ya idu; e̩ne̩ gbe̩do̩ adʼu kwane̩?
Okute̩ akwo bo̩ Juda te̩ n,
e̩ne̩ ki adʼo̩da wa akwo bʼagbagba e̩re̩-wñ te̩ n,
gbogbo taku Shailo lewa;
owñ le̩ oñ amone̩ du agbʼo̩la-wñ gbo̩.
I mʼo̩ma o̩ke̩ke̩te̩-wñ du ro tʼoli achiwebe̩te̩ma
o̩ma o̩ke̩ke̩te̩-wñ le i la ro tʼoli achiwebe̩te̩ma e-o̩me̩me̩le̩,
i agwʼotogbo-wñ ef omi achiwebe̩te̩ma
i la agwʼafe̩-wñ ef e̩bie̩ achiwebe̩te̩ma;
eju-wñ akpa ñw omi achiwebe̩te̩ma,
enyi-wñ achʼefufu ñw omi enya.
Zebiulo̩n agugu o̩la ohimini abadi;
owñ la achʼugbo ku ma adʼo̩ko̩ mane̩,
alo̩me̩-wñ ade̩ Saidon.
Isakar chʼo̩ke̩ke̩te̩ ki gbiti,
i la do̩mo̩ ahi e̩do̩ mane̩ agbagba iga amala;
i la li uña uñmi ki nyo̩,
kpai ane̩ kʼi abʼe̩do̩
oñ i hi ika-wñ wane̩ kʼi nʼadu,
oñ i mud adu kʼi arʼire̩.
Dan akajo̩ amone̩-wñ
owñ chʼo̩lo̩pu Israe̩l oka.
Dan achʼejo ki dʼej o̩na,
i achʼolijo ej o̩kpa,
kʼi alo̩ agbe̩re̩ amanya
todu kʼe̩ne̩ ki tanʼo kʼi ñwa lubi anane̩.
O Jihofa, omi anede ujadu-we̩.
Gad abo ku ma kpʼane̩ fo̩ ake̩che̩ bʼowñ ma,
owñ muda ake̩che̩ bʼuma agbe̩re̩ ma.
Uje̩wñ Ashe̩r chʼula ula,
i akʼe̩wñ uñeju kʼone̩ aje̩ dufu.
Naftali chʼole egbi ku ma to̩no̩ tane̩,
i akʼo̩la e̩te̩le̩.
Jose̩f chʼe̩to̩ oli ki aro nana,
e̩to̩ oli ki dago alu e̩bi omi aro nana;
e̩to̩-wñ ata lʼoji o̩gba.
Amato̩fa kpʼowñ e̩do̩ bie̩ nana,
ma tʼo̩fa ñw u, ma la doli owñ;
ukpahiu o̩o̩do̩-wñ muda dabu n,
ugbogbolo o̩wo̩-wñ la ale̩
lʼo̩wo̩ E̩nugbiti e-Jeko̩b le̩
(o̩mo̩ adidala kwo, owñ chʼOkuta e-Israe̩l),
lugbo O̩jo̩ e-ata-we̩ e-kʼi abʼuwe̩ che,
lugbo Odobao̩gagu kʼi ade̩nyo̩ ñw e̩
e̩nyo̩ ki chʼe-ojale ate̩,
e̩nyo̩ e-o̩lulu ki hie̩do̩ mane̩ o̩gane̩,
e̩nyo̩ e-e̩nya, kpai e̩nyo̩ e-abio̩ma.
E̩nyo̩ kʼO̩jo̩ du ñw ata-we̩
dʼoji dufu tʼe̩nyo̩ amo̩ra-mi le,
gbogbo kad ukpoji otitala e-uwo ogbegbele̩;
e-le̩ anʼoji Jose̩f,
e̩-le ki nʼakpe̩te̩ oji e̩ne̩ ku ma fʼu
daru bʼamo̩maye-wñ te̩ le̩.
Be̩njamin chʼo̩gu ki afʼe̩wñ na,
odudu i akpa e̩wñ je̩,
i akpe̩ e̩wñ e̩gba ane̩.
Abo-i chaka chʼo̩lo̩pu Israe̩l me̩gweji, e̩wñ kʼata-ma ka ñw ma abu kʼi akadua ñw ma la de̩; alu kʼe̩nyo̩ e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ de̩ i du ñw ma.
Tak i ñwa ñw ma, i ka ñw ma kakini, Ma che ku ma mʼumi du amanyu abo-mi; fʼumi ji ugbo amata-mi ef owo ki dʼoko Ifro̩n abo He̩t le̩,
ef owo ki dʼoko Makpila, e-ki dʼo̩wo̩ olodudu Mamre, ane̩ Kenan, e-kʼEbraham la manyu oko le̩ kwʼo̩wo̩ Ifro̩n abo He̩t, todu kʼi nʼugbo kʼi aji oku abo-wñ.
O̩mo̩ ma fʼEbraham kpai Sara o̩ya-wñ ji; o̩mo̩ ma fʼAise̩k kpai Ribe̩ka o̩ya-wñ ji; o̩mo̩ omi la du Lea ji ge̩—
ma la oko le̩ kpai owo ki dʼefu-wñ o̩wo̩ amo̩ma He̩t.
Tak e̩gba ku Jeko̩b fʼoji e̩ñwa kʼi ñwa ñw amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ le̩ kpa, i mʼe̩re̩-wñ ko jʼoj ate̩, i mʼiñmi-wñ da, oñ ma mʼowñ du amanyu abo-wñ.
Ma du Jeko̩b ji—Jose̩f leku
Taku Jose̩f lewa bʼata-wñ eju ma, i kworʼaku-wñ, oñ i dʼalu-wñ kʼo̩ alu.
Taku Jose̩f ñwa ñw abuko̩lo̩-wñ ku ma chʼamobochi ku ma dʼata-wñ kpe̩ka. Abe̩le̩ amobochi le̩ mʼIsrae̩l du kpe̩ka.
Oñ o̩jo̩ o̩gbo̩ meji-wñ jo̩, todu abe̩le̩ o̩jo̩ ku ma du kpe̩ka ajo̩. Abo Ijipti la dʼeku-wñ o̩jo̩ e̩te̩gwa.
Tak e̩gba kʼo̩jo̩ eku ede̩-wñ jo̩, Jose̩f ko̩la ñw abo unyi Fero kakini, Iche̩wñ ku me̩ li mi eju, narodubʼume̩ ku me̩ ko̩la nyu Fero eti, kakini,
Ata-mi je̩ ñwu mi go̩, i kakini, Go, eku naku: ef ura-mi e-kʼomi gwa ñw o̩la-mi ane̩ Kenan, o̩mo̩ e̩ dʼumi ji. Todule̩, ifai narodubʼe̩ kʼe̩ je̩ ñwu mi nyʼate̩ o̩mo̩ kʼu fʼata-mi ji; tak u nadakubiwa ge̩.
Taku Fero kakini, Te̩gu nyʼo̩mo̩ kʼe̩ fʼata-we̩ ji, alu kʼi je̩ ñw e̩ go̩ le̩.
Abe̩le̩ Jose̩f mute̩gu le kʼi dʼata-wñ aji; abuko̩lo̩ Fero chaka, kpai abogijo unyi-wñ, kpai abogijo ane̩ Ijipti chaka du, mute̩gu le kpai owñ.
Kpai abo unyi Jose̩f chaka kpai amo̩maye-wñ kpai abo unyi ata-wñ, chai abimo̩to̩-ma egini, kpai ame̩wño̩re̩-ma egini kpai amokuno̩-ma, ma to̩no̩ jʼane̩ Goshe̩n.
Tʼo̩ko̩ane̩ ogu kpai amananya mute̩gu le kpai owñ; ma la chʼo̩wo̩ one̩ o̩temeje.
Taku ma lewa ugbo ajita Atadi ugbo ku ma gwo̩ka, e-ki dʼudaba Jordan, o̩mo̩ ma dinaku, inaku-wñ chenana ololololo; oñ i deku ata-wñ o̩jo̩ mebie.
E̩gba kʼabo ane̩ le̩, abo Kenan ma che, e̩gba ku ma li eku ku ma de̩ ugbo ajita Atadi le̩, ma kakini, Eku kide̩ chekpuna ugbo abo Ijipti. Todule̩ ma dʼodu o̩mo̩ ko̩ Ebe̩l-mizraim, i dʼudaba Jordan.
Abe̩le̩ amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ le̩ la che ñw u alu kʼi ñwa ñwu ma;
todu amo̩ma-wñ mʼowñ du tʼane̩ Kenan, ma la fʼu ji ef owo oko Makpila, e-kʼEbraham la manyʼoko o̩wo̩ olodudu Mamre o̩wo̩ Ifro̩n abo He̩t le̩, todu kʼi ne̩ ugbo kʼi akʼabo-wñ ji.
Taku abu ku Jose̩f fʼata-wñ ji, owñ kpai amo̩maye-wñ mudabi nyʼIjipti, kpai abo du ku ma le bʼowñ nyʼaji ata-wñ.
Tak e̩gba kʼamo̩maye Jose̩f li kʼata-ma leku, ma kakini, Ikani Jose̩f achulaka wa, kʼi adʼe̩bie̩ne̩ du kʼa chʼo rʼuwa o̩me̩ kpa.
Oñ ma kpʼuche̩ nyʼugbo Jose̩f kakini, Ata-we̩ ñwa ñw a o̩gba tak i ku kakini,
Abu ku me̩ aka ñwu Jose̩f de̩ kakini, Narodubʼe̩ fai kʼe̩ mʼe̩do̩ kpako kʼamo̩maye-we̩ chʼe̩ du chʼuma ele, kpai adure-ma, todu ma chʼe̩ e̩bie̩ne̩ gbe̩. Tak ifai a rodubʼe̩ kʼe̩ mʼe̩do̩ kpako kʼamadu O̩jo̩ e-ata-we̩ chʼe̩ le̩ du chʼuma ele. Jose̩f la mutʼaku e̩gba ku ma ko̩la ñw u.
Tak amo̩maye-wñ ño̩ lewa bʼane̩ ma o̩gba-wñ, oñ ma kakini, Go, amadu-we̩ a che.
Taku Jose̩f ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ ki railo n, todu omi koji O̩jo̩?
I chʼe-me̩, e̩bie̩ne̩ ame̩ ñwa nyʼumi, O̩jo̩ muda fʼu ñwa rʼe̩nyo̩, todu kʼi mudu che alu ki de̩ eñini kʼi fʼamone̩ wewe jadu kʼoji-ma ki do̩mo̩.
Todule̩ me̩ ki railo n; nane̩ me̩ kpai amo̩ma-me̩ egini. Abe̩le̩ i nyʼuma e̩do̩, i la kpo̩te̩rʼuma e̩do̩.
Abe̩le̩ Jose̩f dodo Ijipti, owñ kpai abo unyi ata-wñ; oñ Jose̩f dʼo̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ me̩lu nyoke me̩gwa
Jose̩f la li amaaju Ifraim; ma laño̩ bi amo̩ma Makir kʼi chʼo̩ma Manasa no Jose̩f e̩re̩.
Taku Jose̩f ka ñw amo̩maye-wñ kakini, Eku naku; O̩jo̩ muda awa fejudo me̩ chuu, i la ako me̩ kwʼoj ane̩-i tʼoj ane̩ e-kʼi go̩ ñw Ebraham kpai Aise̩k kpai Jeko̩b.
Taku Jose̩f je̩ ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l go̩, i kakini, O̩jo̩ awa fejudo me̩ chuu, ame̩ ki kʼachiku-mi kwʼemi alo tʼate̩.
Abe̩le̩ Jose̩f leku, o̩do̩-wñ la chʼogu me̩lu nyoke me̩gwa; oñ ma mʼu du kpe̩ka, ma la dʼoku-wñ tef akpati Ijipti.
Akwodufu 1
Ma fʼabo Israe̩l dema Ijipti
Odu amo̩ma Israe̩l e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kʼama kpai Jeko̩b kpe̩re̩ wʼIjipti la de̩, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ nʼabo unyi-wñ wa:
Rube̩n kpai Simeo̩n kpai Lifai kpai Juda,
Isakar kpai Ze̩biulo̩n kpai Be̩njamin,
Dan kpai Naftali kpai Gad kpai Ashe̩r.
Onugo one̩ du ku ma kwef uta Jeko̩b chʼone̩ e̩te̩gwa; todu Jose̩f la dʼIjipti e̩gbale̩ me̩.
Oñ Jose̩f leku, kpai amo̩maye-wñ chaka, kpai abo o̩gba le̩ du.
Amo̩ma Israe̩l muda chʼabio̩ma, oñ ma wewe ololo; ma la wewe nyʼo̩gba, oñ ukpahiu-ma kwane̩ tabale; oñ ane̩ le̩ la che̩ko̩ ñwu ma.
Tak onu Ijipti etito̩, e-kʼi ma ma Jose̩f in kwane̩.
Oñ i ka ñw amone̩-wñ kakini, Me̩ go, amo̩ma Israe̩l wewe tʼuwa le, ma ño̩ nʼukpahiu tʼuwa le.
Me̩ lewa kʼa che ma ugbeju, tode̩gba ku ma wewe nyo̩gba, kʼi awa atʼe̩gba kʼogu achi ku ma ma kpai ame̩nebi-wa, ku ma kʼogu bʼuwa ku ma kwo bʼane̩-i te̩.
Taku ma chi amagboji ku ma ñwʼuko̩lo̩ o̩pe̩cha ñwu ma ku ma fʼuma dema; oñ ma fʼewo Pitam kpai Raamse̩s, ugbo ku Fero akʼane̩ jo̩, ko̩ ñw u.
Ama alu ku ma fʼuma dema tule alu le̩ ma wewe nyo̩gba tule, ma ño̩ kpatuka bʼane̩ ma tule. Tak i chane̩ ekʼuma o̩la noji amo̩ma Israe̩l.
Tak abo Ijipti ñwa uko̩lo̩ o̩lachi ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l che,
oñ ma che kʼudeju-ma chʼelañu noji uko̩lo̩ adu eche, ma je̩ ñwu ma chʼuko̩lo̩ adu ef ike̩te̩ egwa kpai o̩tubeli ebo̩ kpai uko̩lo̩ oko ojoji ojoji du. Uko̩lo̩ adu du ku ma je̩ ñwu ma che chʼuko̩lo̩ o̩lachi.
Tak onu Ijipti ka ñw abobule̩ amaHibru ku ma gba oji o̩ma, kʼoduʼka-wñ ko̩ Shifra, kʼodu ekeji la ko̩ Pua,
kakini, E̩gba ku me̩ dʼugbo ku me̩ bʼabobule̩ Hibru che ku me̩ li ma o̩gbe̩, iche̩wñ kʼi chʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, me̩ mʼu du kpa; iche̩wñ kʼi chʼonobule̩, tak i adeju.
Abobule̩ ku ma gba oji o̩ma le̩ muda railo O̩jo̩, ma la ko̩ eche alu kʼonu Ijipti ka ñwu ma, oñ ma je̩ ñw amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ki deju.
Tak onu Ijipti fʼabobule̩ ku ma gba oji o̩ma do̩ wa, oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩wñ chi ku me̩ che-i? ku me̩ la je̩ ñw amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ deju?
Tak abobule̩ ku ma gba oji o̩ma le̩ ka ñwu Fero kakini, Todabu kʼabobule̩ Hibru ma dʼalu kʼabobule̩ Ijipti de̩ n; o̩la-ma chʼele̩, oñ ma fʼo̩ma bi tane̩ tak e̩ne̩ kʼi agba oji o̩ma ki wʼo̩mo̩.
Abe̩le̩ O̩jo̩ chʼo̩wo̩ e̩nyo̩ ñw abobule̩ ku ma gba oji o̩ma, oñ amone̩ le̩ awewe nyo̩gba, ukpahiu-ma laño̩ nana.
Oñ abu kʼabobule̩ ku ma gba oji o̩ma le̩ railo O̩jo̩, i la je̩ ñwu ma nʼunyi e-ma.
Taku Fero ñwañwu amone̩-wñ chaka kakini, O̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du ku ma bi, me̩ mʼu du ro̩ tʼefu ohimini Naye̩l, me̩ ki muda tʼo̩ma onobule̩ du no̩ kʼi deju.
Ma fu Mose̩s bi: kpai o̩jo̩ okolobia-wñ
Oñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ abo Lifaiʼka le nyʼanʼo̩ma onobule̩ Lifai chʼo̩ya.
Tak onobule̩ le̩ fefunyo̩ oñ i fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi; oñ e̩gba kʼi li ka kʼi chʼo̩ma alifia, i mʼu du maja ochu me̩ta.
Tak e̩gba kʼi ma ño̩ neke dʼu maja ge̩ n, i mʼo̩ko̩ ke̩ke̩ ku ma nʼuma ño̩ du, oñ i dʼo̩bia bitume̩n kpai kolta kuru; tak i mʼo̩ma le̩ du tʼefu-wñ, oñ i dʼu tʼef e̩gbe̩ e̩tʼo̩ba ohimini Naye̩l.
O̩maye-wñ onobule̩ la dago o̩najiji kʼi ma e̩wñ ki achʼo.
Abe̩le̩ o̩ma Fero onobule̩ lewa Naye̩l kʼi gwo̩la, oñ abigbe̩le̩-wñ tale eti Naye̩l; tak i fʼo̩ko̩ le̩ li ef egbe o̩mo̩ oñ i fʼimo̩to̩-wñ oka kpe̩ nyʼamʼu du wa.
Oñ abu kʼi mʼu chi i fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ le̩ li; me̩ la go, o̩me̩kpa le̩ araku. Ejumomi-wñ la je̩ ñw u n, oñ i kakini, O̩ma abo Hibruʼka de̩.
Tak o̩maye-wñ ka ñw o̩ma Fero kakini, U lo kʼu fʼonobule̩ Hibruʼka do̩ wa kʼi ne̩ o̩ma le̩ ñw e̩?
Tak o̩ma Fero le̩ ka ñw u kakini, Lo. Tak igbe̩le̩ kʼi fʼo̩wo̩ mʼo̩la-wñ ne̩ le̩ le nyʼado̩ iye o̩ma le̩ wa.
Oñ o̩ma Fero ka ñw u kakini, Mʼo̩ma-i du, kʼe̩ nʼe̩ñwu mi, tak u narʼo̩me̩ ñw e̩. Abe̩le̩ onobule̩ le̩ mʼo̩ma du, oñ i fʼu ne̩.
O̩ma le̩ la naya eju alo waa tak i mʼowñ du wʼugbo o̩ma Fero le̩, oñ i mud o̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩; i la dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Mose̩s, i kakini, Todabu kʼu dʼu kwef omi.
Mose̩s fʼe̩ne̩ Ijipti kpa
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba ku Mose̩s gbakpa, i dufu nyʼugbo amo̩maye-wñ, i la go uko̩lo̩ o̩pe̩cha-ma ku ma che; oñ i li e̩ne̩ Ijiptiʼka kʼi agwo e̩ne̩ Hibru, o̩maye-wñʼka.
Tak i gʼemi, gʼemi, oñ abu kʼi ma li e̩ne̩ du n, i fʼe̩ne̩ Ijipti le̩ kpa, tak i mʼu du maja ef e̩lanyi o̩mo̩.
O̩jo̩ñwa-wñ i ño̩ ledufu, me̩ la go, aboke̩le̩ abo Hibru meji jʼajuja; oñ i ka ñw e̩ne̩ kʼi achʼe̩bie̩ne̩ kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼuwe̩ agwo ekeji-we̩-i?
Tak e̩ne̩ le̩ kakini, E̩ne̩ dʼuwe̩ chʼagboji kpai akajo̩-wa? I dʼe̩do̩-we̩ kʼe̩ kpa mi alu kʼe̩ kpa e̩ne̩ Ijipti le̩? Taku Mose̩s kwochokpo, I kakini, Ma fʼe̩wñ le̩ ma me̩.
Oñ e̩gba ku Fero gbʼo̩, i che kʼi du Mose̩s kpa.
Mose̩s muda ra bʼeju Fero te̩, oñ i kwogugu ane̩ Midian;
i lewa gugu me̩rʼobugaʼka. Atama Midian o̩mo̩ la nʼamo̩ma onobule̩ mebie; oñ ma lewʼo̩mo̩ akpa omiofo. Ma la kpa nyʼagbada e̩ko̩ kʼame̩wño̩re̩ ata-ma egini ki ñmo̩.
Tak amadide ala lewa fʼuma ne kwʼo̩mo̩; Mose̩s muda kwane̩ ate̩ko ma, oñ i je̩ ñw ame̩wño̩re̩-ma egini ñmo̩.
Tak e̩gba ku ma lewa ugbo Rue̩l, ata-ma, i kakini, Abu me̩ le ku me̩ takpa wa eñini-i?
Oñ ma kakini, E̩ne̩ Ijiptiʼka mʼu wa gba ugbo amadidala, i laño̩ fʼomiofo kpa ñw a kʼame̩wño̩re̩-wa egini kʼi ñmo̩.
Tak i ka ñw amo̩ma-wñ onobule̩ kakini, Ugbo i de̩? E̩wñ chi ku me̩ tʼe̩ne̩ le̩ no̩ tʼubi? Me̩ dʼo̩ wa kʼi jʼe̩wñ.
I la du Mose̩s e̩do̩ kʼi bʼe̩ne̩ le̩ gugu, tak i mʼo̩ma-wñ Zipo̩ra du ñwu Mose̩s.
I la fʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ bi, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Ge̩rsho̩m; todu i kakini, Omi te̩tachʼilowa oj ane̩ omune̩.
Oñ i lewatu iko ki kpo̩kpe̩-i, onu Ijipti le̩ leku. Oñ amo̩ma Israe̩l jʼañmiru noji uko̩lo̩ adu ku ma che, ma kwokwa, tak ukwa ku ma kwa noji o̩bata adu ku ma che mute̩gu wʼugbo O̩jo̩.
O̩jo̩ la gbo̩ ifi-ma, oñ O̩jo̩ libekado alo kʼi kpe̩ kpai Ebraham kpai Aise̩k kpai Jeko̩b.
O̩jo̩ la go amo̩ma Israe̩l, oñ O̩jo̩ ma.
O̩jo̩ fu Mose̩s do̩ kʼi jadu abo Israe̩l
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s do̩mo̩ adejute̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ egini e-ana-wñ, Je̩tro, atama Midian le̩; i la ne̩ ame̩wño̩re̩ egini le̩ alo tʼejubi aje̩tachi, oñ i lewa Ho̩re̩b, uwo O̩jo̩ le̩.
O̩mo̩ onuche̩ Jihofa kwotejugede ñw u ef o̩go̩ una alumeji oli ye̩e̩le̩ʼka; oñ i go, una le̩ la dʼef oli ye̩e̩le̩ le̩ ajo, oli le̩ la jo n.
Taku Mose̩s kakini, Namuna cho, kʼu go igo inaina-i, e̩wñ chi kʼoli ye̩e̩le̩ le̩ ma jo n?
Jihofa la li abu kʼi muna nyʼago, oñ O̩jo̩ nʼomudala dʼo̩ kwef alumeji oli yeele̩ le̩, i kakini, Mose̩s, Mose̩s! Tak i kakini, Omi de̩.
Tak i kakini, E̩ ki te̩me̩rʼemi n; mʼe̩da-we̩ gwo̩ bʼe̩re̩-we̩ te̩, todu uña ugbo kʼe̩ dago le̩ chʼane̩ ki afo̩.
I ño̩ kakini, Omi chʼO̩jo̩ ata-we̩, O̩jo̩ Ebraham kpai O̩jo̩ Aise̩k kpai O̩jo̩ Jeko̩b. Taku Mose̩s mʼeju-wñ du maja, todu i chokpo ekejurʼO̩jo̩.
Taku Jihofa kakini, Omi fʼo̩bata amone̩-mi ku ma jʼIjipti li me̩, u la gbo̩ ukwa-ma noji abo ku ma chi tu ma ofe; u chema iwo̩-ma,
omi la gwo̩ru wa kʼu mʼuma gba kwef o̩wo̩ abo Ijipti-i, kʼu laño̩ mʼuma ko kwʼoj ane̩ le̩ tʼane̩ ki nyo̩, kʼi laño̩ chenana, owñ chʼoj ane̩ ugbo kʼomi e̩nya kpai iño̩ acha, tʼuña abo Kenan kpai abo He̩t kpai abo Amo̩r kpai abo Pe̩re̩z kpai abo Hifai kpai abo Je̩bius.
Ifai, go, ukwa amo̩ma Israe̩l lewa ugbo mi me̩, u laño̩ li ekpama kʼabo Ijipti fʼuma kpama le̩.
Fai, e̩ lewa kʼu kpʼe̩ nyʼugbo Fero kʼuwe̩ ki mʼamone̩-mi, amo̩ma Israe̩l le̩, ko kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti dufu.
Mose̩s muda ka ñw O̩jo̩ kakini, E̩ne̩ omi che, kʼu nanyʼugbo Fero, kʼu nakʼamo̩ma Israe̩l kwʼ Ijipti dufu?
I kakini, Nadʼugbo we̩ chuu; e̩wñ ki chʼijali ñw e̩ ka kʼomi kpʼuwe̩ uche̩ de̩ kakini, E̩gba kʼe̩ mʼamone̩ le̩ ko kwʼIjipti dufu, me̩ are̩ O̩jo̩ oj uwo kide̩.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw O̩jo̩ kakini, Go, u lewʼugbo abo Israe̩l kʼu ka ñwu ma kakini, O̩jo̩ e-amata-me̩ kpe̩ mi wʼugbo me̩, ku ma la tʼumi ene kakini, Ab odu-wñ ko̩? E̩wñ naka ñwu ma?
Oñ O̩jo̩ ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, OMI KʼU CHʼOMI DE̩ LE̩ DE̩. I ño̩ kakini, Abu kʼuwe̩ aka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l le̩ de̩, ka kʼOMI DE̩ kpe̩ mi wʼugbo me̩.
O̩jo̩ ño̩ ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Alu kʼuwe̩ aka ñw abo Israe̩l le̩ de̩, ka ki Jihofa, O̩jo̩ e-amata-me̩, O̩jo̩ e-Ebraham kpai O̩jo̩ e-Aise̩k kpai O̩jo̩ e-Jeko̩b kpe̩ mi wʼugbo me̩-i: e-le̩ chʼodu-mi ogbegbele̩, e-le̩ laño̩ chʼurewa-mi tʼo̩gba o̩gba du.
Lo, kʼe̩ dʼabogijo Israe̩l jeju, kʼe̩ la ka ñwu ma kakini, Jihofa kʼi chʼO̩jo̩ e-amata-me̩, O̩jo̩ e-Ebraham kpai e-Aise̩k kpai e-Jeko̩b, kwotejugede ñwu mi, i kakini. Omi wa go me̩, ochochi; u la fʼe̩wñ ku ma che me̩ Ijipti li.
Eka omi ka, ka kʼu nako me̩ kwʼef o̩bata Ijipti dufu wʼane̩ abo Kenan kpai e-abo He̩t kpai e-abo Amo̩r kpai e-abo Pe̩re̩z kpai e-abo Hifai kpai e-abo Je̩bius, owñ chʼane̩ ugbo kʼomi e̩nya kpai iño̩ acha.
Ma la agbo̩ omu-we̩: tak uwe̩ kpai abogijo Israe̩l anyʼugbo onu Ijipti, oñ ame̩ aka ñw u kakini, Jihofa, O̩jo̩ e-amaHibru, de kpai awa; agba, e̩ je̩ ñw a nyʼef aje̩tachi ule̩ o̩jo̩ me̩ta kʼa che iche̩bo̩ ñwu Jihofa, O̩jo̩-wa.
U chema ka kʼonu Ijipti jʼatʼume̩ no̩ ku me̩ lo n. I aje̩ n, chai e̩gba kʼo̩wo̩ ukpahiu dufu.
Abe̩le̩ u la anʼo̩wo̩-mi dala oñ nanʼe̩wñ aye-mi du kʼu nache alumeji o̩mo̩ gwo Ijipti; ubi e-le̩ tak i aje̩ ñwu me̩ lo.
U la aje̩ ñw abo Ijipti li amone̩-i eju; oñ i awatu e̩gba ku me̩ alo, me̩ la atʼo̩wo̩ ofo lo n,
onobule̩ du abi e̩wñ ijaga e-ajifa kpai e-o̩jamalia kpai ukpo, ugbo ekeji-wñ kpai ugbo e̩ne̩ ki ge̩ne̩ ef unyi-wñ, me̩ la akʼe̩wñ le̩ nyʼamo̩ma-me̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩ o̩la; abe̩le̩ me̩ la bʼabo Ijipti gbʼe̩wñ-ma.
Mose̩s tene kʼi lo n, oñ O̩jo̩ du Aro̩n manyʼu o̩la
Taku Mose̩s dohi, kakini, Ama, go, ma jʼadʼo̩la-mi rʼochochi n, ma la agbʼomu-mi n, todu ma aka kakini, Jihofa tejugede ñw e̩ n.
Taku Jihofa ka ñw u kakini, E̩wñ dʼef o̩wo̩-we̩ le̩? I kakini, O̩kpa de̩.
Tak i kakini, Mʼu du ro̩ tʼane̩. Oñ i mʼu du ro̩ tʼane̩, i la mud ejo; taku Mose̩s ra bʼo̩ te̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Nʼo̩wo̩-we̩ dala kʼe̩ gwo̩nyʼotihi-wñ—i la nʼo̩wo̩-wñ dala oñ i gwo̩nyʼu tak i mud o̩kpa ef o̩wo̩-wñ.
Todu ku ma ki dʼo̩ rʼochochi ka ku Jihofa, O̩jo̩ e-amata-ma, owñ chʼO̩jo̩ e-Ebraham kpai O̩jo̩ e-Aise̩k kpai O̩jo̩ e-Jeko̩b, kwotejugede ñw e̩.
Jihofa laño̩ ka ñw u kakini, Fai, e̩ mʼo̩wo̩-we̩ du tunyʼagbe̩do̩-we̩. Tak i mʼo̩wo̩-wñ du tunyʼagbe̩do̩-wñ; oñ e̩gba kʼi mʼu du dufu, me̩ go, o̩wo̩-wñ chʼo̩ga ikpemute, i chefufu dabu sno.
Tak i kakini, Mʼo̩wo̩-we̩ du dabi tʼagbe̩do̩-we̩. Oñ i dʼo̩wo̩-wñ dabi tʼagbe̩do̩-wñ; tak e̩gba kʼi mʼu du kwʼagbe̩do̩-wñ dufu, go, i murida dab alu kʼaño̩la-wñ de̩.
Iche̩wñ ku ma ma jʼadʼo̩la-we̩ rʼochochi n, ku ma la anyʼujiwe ejodudu le̩ eti n, ma ado̩ ujiwe otitala rʼochochi.
I la che̩wñ kʼama ma do̩ ujiwe meji-i rʼochochi n, ku ma ma agbʼomu-we̩ n, mak e̩ mʼomi Naye̩l du kʼe̩ mʼu du dajʼane̩ e̩gbe̩; tak omi kʼe̩ kpa kwefu Naye̩l le̩ amud e̩bie̩ tʼane̩ e̩gbe̩ le̩.
Ama Mose̩s ka ñwu Jihofa kakini, Aiya, Ondu, omi chʼe̩ne̩ o̩la eka n, dagba i chʼakwoubi, dagba kʼi chʼabu kʼuwe̩ ako̩la ñw adu-we̩-i; todu narubo̩ o̩la eka, ukpalu-mi la chʼewoji.
Taku Jihofa ka ñw u kakini, E̩ne̩ che alu one̩? abe̩k e̩ne̩ je̩ ñw one̩ ki chʼajialu, abe̩k ajeti, abe̩k agane̩, abe̩k akpejufo̩? I chʼomi, Jihofa-i n?
Todule̩, e̩ kwolo ke, omi la adʼugbo alu-we̩ oñ nakʼuwe̩ o̩la kʼuwe̩ aka.
I muda kakini, Aiya, Ondu, e̩ne̩ omune̩ du ki dʼuwe̩ e̩do̩, e̩ kpʼe̩, agba.
Tak uwe̩do̩ Jihofa mutajo bu Mose̩s ma, oñ i kakini, Aro̩n, abo Lifai le̩, chʼo̩maye-we̩ n? U chema kʼi meju o̩la eka nyo̩nyo̩. E̩ la go, owñ dufu le dʼuwe̩ awa-i, e̩gba kʼi fʼe̩ li, e̩do̩-wñ abo̩.
Uwe̩ la ako̩la ñw u, kʼe̩ dʼo̩la tef alu-wñ; omi la adʼugbo alu-we̩ kpʼalu e-wñ, oñ nakʼuwe̩ e̩wñ kʼame̩ ache.
Owñ la akʼomu-we̩ ñw amone̩ le̩. Owñ la achʼalu ñw e̩, uwe̩ adab O̩jo̩ ñw owñ.
Uwe̩ ki dʼo̩kpa-i nʼo̩wo̩, owñ chʼe-kʼuwe̩ ane̩ che ujiwe le̩.
Taku Mose̩s mudabi nyʼugbo Je̩tro ana-wñ, oñ i ka ñw u kakini, Agba, e̩ je̩ ñwu mi mudabi nyʼugbo amo̩maye-mi ku ma jo̩ Ijipti, kʼu li abe̩ku ma deju ta. Taku Je̩tro ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Lo kpai ure̩do̩.
Oñ Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s Midian o̩mo̩ kakini, Mudabi tʼIjipti; todu abo ku ma feju oji-we̩ le̩ leku kpa me̩.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s mʼo̩ya-wñ kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ko, oñ i ko ma gugu oj o̩ke̩ke̩te̩, tak i mudabi tʼane̩ Ijipti; Mose̩s la mʼo̩kpa O̩jo̩ le̩ du nʼo̩wo̩-wñ alo.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Abu kʼe̩ dabi tʼIjipti, e̩ nago kʼe̩ che e̩wñ uno̩ du kʼomi du tʼef o̩wo̩-we̩ le̩ eju Fero; omi muda ache kʼe̩do̩-wñ ki gbiti. I la atʼamone̩ le̩ no̩ ku ma lo n.
Tak uwe̩ aka ñwu Fero kakini, Abu ki Jihofa aka de̩ kakini, Israe̩l chʼo̩mo̩gba-mi e̩ne̩ke̩le̩,
omi la aka ñw e̩-i kakini, E̩ ki tʼo̩ma-mi no̩ kʼi lo, todu kʼi re̩ mi; uwe̩ muda ko̩ etʼo̩ no̩, go, nadʼo̩mo̩gba e-we̩ kpa.
Taku Jihofa de kpʼowñ ef uruʼka ejo̩na le̩, oñ i che kʼi dʼu kpa.
Taku Zipo̩ra mʼokuta o̩mu du oñ i mʼaño̩ kʼi bʼo̩gba e̩pi o̩ma-wñ ma ko̩da, oñ i mʼu du rikpolo tʼane̩ e̩re̩-wñ, i kakini, U we̩ chʼo̩ko̩ e̩bie̩ ñwu mi, ochochi!
Abe̩le̩ tak i tʼo̩ no̩, oñ onobule̩ le̩ kakini, O̩ko̩ e̩bie̩ e̩ che, todu e̩pi-wñ kʼi da le̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñw Aro̩n kakini, Lo kʼuwe̩ kpai Mose̩s ki de ef aje̩tachi le̩. Tak i le, oñ i de kpai owñ oj uwo O̩jo̩, i la dalu kʼalu.
Taku Mose̩s mʼo̩la uche̩ du ku Jihofa kpʼo̩ du ka ñw u kpai ujiwe du kʼi ñwa ñw u kʼi che.
Taku Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n le oñ ma fʼabogijo amo̩ma Israe̩l do̩ jeju chaka.
Tak Aro̩n mʼo̩la du ku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s du ka ñwu ma, i laño̩ che ujiwe le̩ eju amone.
Amone̩ le̩ la dʼo̩ rʼochochi; oñ e̩gba ku ma gbo̩ ka ku Jihofa lewa fejudo amo̩ma Israe̩l, kʼi la go o̩bata-ma, ma fʼoji-ma dalo̩, oñ ma la dojikane̩ ñw u.
Uche kʼO̩jo̩ kpe̩ru Fero— o̩bata-ma anyo̩gba
Ubile̩ taku Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n mugudu nyʼugbo Fero aka ñw u kakini, Abu ku Jihofa, O̩jo̩ Israe̩l, aka de̩ kakini, Tʼamone̩-mi no̩ ku ma nyʼahi uje̩wñ uyo̩ ñwu mi ef aje̩tachi.
Taku Fero kakini, Jihofa chʼe̩ne̩? kʼu nagbʼomu-wñ gbo̩ kʼu tʼabo Israe̩l no̩? Omi ma Jihofa n, u jʼatʼabo Israe̩l no̩ n.
Taku ma kakini, O̩jo̩ e-amaHibru de kpai awa me̩; a rodubʼe̩, kʼe̩ je̩ ñw a le ule̩ o̩jo̩ me̩ta nyʼef aje̩tachi, kʼa fʼiche̩bo̩ che ñwu Jihofa, O̩jo̩-wa, tode̩gba kʼi anʼe̩wñ ibi abe̩k o̩kwo̩chageli wa abʼuwa ma.
Tak onu Ijipti ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼame̩, Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n, mʼamone̩ le̩ o̩wo̩ ta bʼuko̩lo̩-ma te̩? Me̩ nyʼugbo uko̩lo̩ adu-me̩ le̩.
Taku Fero kakini, Me̩ go, amone̩ ane̩-i chewewe, oñ me̩ je̩ ñwu ma ñmi ugbo uko̩lo̩ adu-ma!
O̩jo̩ le̩ gbage̩de̩ Fero ñwa ñw abo ku ma chi tʼamone̩ le̩ ofe, kpai amako̩takada-ma kakini,
Me̩ ki ño̩ kʼegbe ñw amone̩ le̩ ku ma bo̩ otubeli alu ku me̩ che akwoubi le̩ ge̩ n; je̩ ñwu ma nyʼayʼegbe ñw o̩la-ma.
Aluka otubeli ku ma te̩tabo̩ akwoubi, me̩ ki bu ñwu ma abe̩le̩ waa, me̩ ki bʼu wane̩ kilikili n; todu o̩kpo̩ ma che le̩; todule̩ ma kwa kakini, Je̩ ñw a lo kʼa fʼiche̩bo̩ che ñw O̩jo̩-wa.
Bʼuko̩lo̩ le̩ tʼo̩ ki wo̩ aboke̩le̩ le̩ ku ma ki chʼakanya-wñ kʼama ki ño̩ nyʼolemi le̩ eti n.
Oñ abo ku ma chi tʼamone̩ le̩ ofe kpai amako̩takada-ma ledufu, oñ ma ka ñw amone̩ le̩ kakini, Abu ku Fero ka de̩ kakini, Nakʼegbe ñwu me̩ ge̩ n.
Ame̩ onugo ki lo ku me̩ tene egbe ugbo du ku me̩ li; uko̩lo̩-me̩ muda abu wane̩ kilikili n.
Abe̩le̩ amone̩ le̩ mukpatuka bʼane̩ Ijipti du ma ku ma ya o̩kakpunu egbe jo̩ koji egbe otubeli.
Abo ku ma chi tʼuma ofe la nanʼuma aju, ma kakini, Me̩ ki chʼuko̩lo̩-me̩ kpa o̩jo̩ du, me̩ che tʼalu o̩jo̩ʼka alu ku me̩ che e̩gba ku ma kʼegbe ñwu me̩.
Taku ma fʼamako̩takada amo̩ma Israe̩l kʼabo Fero ku ma chi tʼuma ofe kʼamone̩ le nyʼuma o̩wo̩ ja, oñ ma ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼame̩ ma fʼukpe̩ otubeli-me̩ bo̩ kpa o̩nale̩ kpʼeñini-i dab akwoubi n?
Tak amako̩takada abo Israe̩l le̩ lewa raku nyu Fero o̩la, ma kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼuwe̩ ache amadu-we̩-i abe̩i?
Ma la kʼegbe ñw amadu-we̩-i n, ma muda aka ñw a kakini, Me̩ bʼotubeli! E̩ la go, ma ja amadu-we̩-i; e̩bie̩ne̩-wñ muda adʼugbo abo e-we̩ onugo.
Ama i kakini, O̩kpo̩ me̩ che le̩, o̩kpo̩ me̩ che! todule̩ oñ me̩ kakini, Je̩ ñw a lo kʼa chʼiche̩bo̩ ñwu Jihofa.
Me̩ nyʼachʼuko̩lo̩ ke! Ma la akʼegbe du ñwu me̩ n. Me̩ muda akʼaluka otubeli abe̩le̩ wa pio̩o̩.
Tak amako̩takada abo Israe̩l le̩ li ka kʼi bie̩ne̩ ñwu ma, owñ chʼabu ku ma kakini, Me̩ ñʼabu aluka otubeli-me̩ wane̩ ef uko̩lo̩-me̩ ku me̩ che o̩jo̩ du le̩ n.
Taku ma de kpai Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n ku ma dago anede ma abu ku ma kwʼugbo Fero dufu;
oñ ma ka ñwu ma kakini, Jihofa ki go me̩, kʼi fʼajo̩-wa ka, todabu ku me̩ je̩ ñw ekpo kʼa kpo ki mud e̩wñ ki alu eju Fero kpai amadu-wñ, me̩ la dʼo̩kwo̩chageli nyʼuma o̩wo̩ ku ma kpa wa.
Taku Mose̩s mudabi tʼugbo Jihofa, oñ i kakini, Aiya, Ondu! E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ che amone̩-i e̩bie̩ne̩? E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ kpe̩ mi wa-i?
Todu akwe̩gba kʼu lewa ako̩la ñwu Fero ef odu-we̩, i te̩tache amone̩-i e̩bie̩ne̩, e̩ la gba amone̩-we̩ re n.
Jihofa dabi ka ñw abo Israe̩l alu kʼi ache ñwu ma
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Ifai tak uwe̩ ali e̩wñ kʼu nache Fero; todu i anʼo̩wo̩ ukpahiu tʼuma no̩, ochochi, i la anʼo̩wo̩ ukpahiu ane ma kwo bʼane̩-wñ te̩.
Oñ O̩jo̩ ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Omi che Jihofa.
Omi kwotejugede ñw Ebraham kpai Aise̩k kpai Jeko̩b, kʼu chʼO̩jo̩ Odobao̩gagu; i muda chʼe-odu-mi Jihofa, u je̩ ñwu ma ma ka kʼomi de̩ n.
U laño̩ fʼalo-mi kpe̩ kpai ama, todu kʼu dʼane̩ Kenan ñwu ma, owñ chʼane̩ ugbo ku ma ge̩ne̩ efu-wñ ale le̩.
U laño̩ gbo̩ ifi amo̩ma Israe̩l, e-kʼabo Ijipti gwo̩nyu ma jʼef adu le̩, oñ ibe-mi kado alo-mi kʼu kpe̩ le̩.
Todule̩ e̩ naka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l kakini, Omi Jihofa de̩, nako me̩ kwef uko̩lo̩ adu e-abo Ijipti, oñ nagba me̩ kwef uko̩lo̩ adu-ma eche, nanʼo̩wo̩ ki nadala te̩ kpai udu elile ebu ñwu ma gba me̩ tane̩.
Tak u nako me̩ chʼabo-mi, oñ omi achʼO̩jo̩-me̩; taku ame̩ ama ka kʼomi che Jihofa, O̩jo̩-me̩, kʼi ko me̩ kwʼef uko̩lo̩ adu e-abo Ijipti eche le̩.
Omi ñʼako me̩ wa oj ane̩ e-kʼomi dʼo̩wo̩-mi nyate̩ ago̩ ñw Ebraham kpai Aise̩k kpai Jeko̩b ka kʼu nadu ñwu ma; nadʼu ñwu me̩ ku me̩ ne̩. Omi Jihofa de̩.
Taku Mose̩s ko̩la abe̩le̩ ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l; ma muda nyi Mose̩s eti n, noji ubie̩do̩, kpai uko̩lo̩ adu ki bie̩ne̩ ñwu ma le̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
Nyʼejefu, kʼe̩ ka ñwu Fero, onu Ijipti, kʼi tʼamo̩ma Israe̩l no̩ ku ma kwo bʼane̩-wñ te̩.
Taku Mose̩s ka o̩gba Jihofa o̩mo̩, kakini, Go, amo̩ma Israe̩l la netirʼumi n; ab u nale ki Fero anetirʼumi? Omi, kʼuko̩la ma ya alu-mi n-i?
Jihofa muda ko̩la ñwu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n, oñ i ñwañwu ma alu ku ma aka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l kpai alu ku ma aka ñwu Fero, onu Ijipti, ku ma kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l kwo bʼane̩ Ijipti te̩.
Amata Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n
Abo kuma dʼoji dufu unyi unyi amata-ma jo̩-i: amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Rube̩n kʼi chʼo̩mo̩gba Israe̩l che: Hano̩k kpai Palu kpai He̩zro̩n kpai Karmi; abo-i chʼabo akwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi Rube̩n.
Amo̩ma Simeo̩n e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ la che: Jemue̩l kpai Jamin kpai Ohad kpai Jachin kpai Zohar kpai Sho̩l kʼi che o̩ma kʼonobule̩ Kenan bi ñw u; abo-i chʼabo akwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi Simeo̩n.
Odu odu amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Lifai o̩gba o̩gba-ma jo̩-i: Ge̩rsho̩n kpai Kohat kpai Me̩rari, o̩do̩ udeju Lifai la chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩fa nyoke me̩gwebie.
Amo̩ma Ge̩rsho̩n e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ che: Libni kpai Shimeai, akwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi-ma.
Amo̩ma Kohat e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ che: Amram kpai Izhar kpai He̩bro̩n kpai Uzie̩l, o̩do̩ udeju Kohat la chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩fa nyoke me̩gwe̩ta.
Amo̩ma Me̩rari e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ che: Mali kpai Mushi. Abo-i chʼakwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi abo Lifai o̩gba o̩gba-ma.
Amram la ne̩ Jo̩kebe̩d, o̩maye ata-wñ, chʼo̩ya, owñ le̩ fʼAro̩n kpai Mose̩s bi ñw u; o̩do̩ udeju Amram la chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩fa nyoke me̩gwebie.
Amo̩ma Izhar e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ che: Ko̩ra kpai Nefe̩g kpai Zikri.
Amo̩ma Uzie̩l e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ che: Mishae̩l kpai E̩lzafan kpai Sitri.
Tak Aro̩n ne̩ E̩lisheba, o̩ma Aminadab o̩maye Nasho̩n, chʼo̩ya; i la fu Nedab kpai Abaihiu kpai E̩leaza kpai Itamar bi ñw u.
Amo̩ma Ko̩ra e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ che: Asir kpai E̩lkana kpai Abiasaf; abo-i chʼabo akwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi abo Ko̩ra.
Oñ E̩leaza, o̩ma Aro̩n, ne̩ o̩ma Putie̩l oka chʼo̩ya; i la fu Finehas bi ñw u. Abo ku ma dʼoji dufu ef amata abo Lifai, akwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi-ma de̩.
Abo-i che Aro̩n kpai Mose̩s e-ku Jihofa ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ ko amo̩ma Israe̩l kwo oj ane̩ Ijipti dufu wa, udala udala-ma.
Ama chʼabo ku ma ko̩la ñwu Fero onu Ijipti, ku ma ko amo̩ma Israe̩l kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti dufu wa, Mose̩s le̩ kpai Aro̩n le̩ de̩.
Oñ o̩jo̩ ku Jihofa ko̩la ñwu Mose̩s ane̩ Ijipti,
Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Omi Jihofa de̩; o̩la du kʼu naka ñw e̩-i, e̩ naka ñwu Fero, onu Ijipti.
Mose̩s muda ka o̩gba Jihofa kakini, Go, kʼo̩la ma ya alu-mi n-i, ab u na le ku Fero anyʼumi eti ge̩?
Mose̩s nyʼugbo Fero
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Go, omi dʼuwe̩ che dab O̩jo̩ ñwu Fero; Aro̩n, o̩maye-we̩ la ache akache̩-we̩.
O̩la du kʼu nañwa ñw e̩, uwe̩ ki ka; oñ Aro̩n o̩maye-we̩ aka ñwu Fero kʼi tʼamo̩ma Israe̩l no̩ ku ma kwobʼoj ane̩-wñ te̩.
Omi muda ache e̩do̩ Fero ki gbiti, oñ nache kʼujiwe-mi kpai e̩wñ uno̩-mi ki wewe nyo̩gba oj ane̩ Ijipti.
Fero muda anyʼuwe̩ eti n; tak u nadʼo̩wo̩-mi no ane̩ Ijipti, kʼu ko abudala udala-mi, owñ chʼamone̩-mi amo̩ma Israe̩l-i, kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti lugbo udu lile kʼu nabu ñwu ma.
Tak abo Ijipti ama ka kʼomi Jihofa de̩, e̩gba kʼu fʼo̩wo̩-mi nadala nʼIjipti, kʼu nako amo̩ma Israe̩l kwʼefu-ma dufu.
Taku Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n fʼabe̩le̩ che; ma che alu ku Jihofa ñwa ñwu ma.
O̩do̩ Mose̩s la chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩le̩, oñ o̩do̩ Aro̩n chʼo̩gbo̩ me̩le̩ nyoke me̩ta e̩gba ku ma ko̩la ñwu Fero le̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n kakini,
E̩gba ku Fero aka ñwu me̩ kakini, Chʼuno̩-me̩ʼka kʼu go, e̩gbale̩ uwe̩ aka ñw Aro̩n kakini, Mʼo̩kpa-we̩ du ro̩ tane̩ o̩gba Fero, kʼi mud ejo.
Taku Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n nyʼugbo Fero, oñ ma che alu ku Jihofa ñwa ñwu ma le̩. Aro̩n la mʼo̩kpa-wñ du ro̩tane̩ o̩gba Fero kpai o̩gba abuko̩lo̩-wñ, oñ i mud ejo.
Taku Fero fʼamanibe kpai amachobochi do̩ wa; oñ ama, amachifamu Ijipti le̩, ño̩ ne̩ e̩wñ ifamu-ma chʼabe̩le̩ ge̩.
Todu e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩-ma mʼo̩kpa-wñ du ro̩ tane̩, oñ i mud ejo. O̩kpa Aro̩n muda mʼo̩kpa-ma ko mi.
Oñ e̩do̩ Fero ño̩ gbiti kpo̩, i ko̩ enetirʼuma; alu ki Jihofa ka le̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩do̩ Fero chʼokuta, i ko̩ etʼamone̩-i no̩.
E̩ nyʼugbo Fero odudu, go, i adufu nyʼaji; tak uwe̩ ki dago eti o̩ba ohimini anede owñ, kʼe̩ la dʼo̩kpa kʼi rida ejo le̩ nʼo̩wo̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki ka ñw u kakini, Jihofa, O̩jo̩ amaHibru, kpe̩ mi wʼugbo we̩-i, kakini, Tʼamone̩-mi no̩ ku ma re̩ mi aje̩tachi; e̩ go, uwe̩ la nyeti ta n.
Abu ku Jihofa aka de̩, kakini, Ef e-i oñ uwe̩ ama ka kʼomi Jihofa de̩: go, nadʼo̩kpa ki dʼo̩wo̩-mi-i gwo omi Naye̩l-i, oñ i arida e̩bie̩,
tak e̩ja ki jʼefu Naye̩l-i aku, omi Naye̩l-i la alu, oñ omi Naye̩l-i achʼabo Ijipti ihie̩ne̩ eñmo̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩ ka ñw Aro̩n kakini, E̩ mʼo̩kpa-we̩ du kʼe̩ fʼo̩wo̩ nadala nʼeju omi Ijipti, noji ohimini ohimini-ma, noji aji aji-ma kpai noji oduda oduda omi-ma kpai noji ugbo du kʼomi-ma agbagu, kʼi mud e̩bie̩; abe̩le̩ e̩bie̩ ado̩mo̩ ugbo du ane̩ Ijipti, tʼef e̩wñ eku oli tʼe-okuta.
Atulubo̩ ejodudu
Taku Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n che alu ku Jihofa ñwa ñwu ma le̩; i la mʼo̩kpa le̩ du nyate̩, oñ i mʼu du gwo omi Naye̩l eju Fero kpai eju abuko̩lo̩-wñ du, tak omi Naye̩l le̩ du mud e̩bie̩.
E̩ja ki la jʼefu Naye̩l leku, taku Naye̩l le̩ kwolu, oñ abo Ijipti ma ño̩ neke ñmo̩ omi Naye̩l le̩ ge̩ n; e̩bie̩ la dʼugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti.
Tak amachifamu Ijipti ño̩ fʼe̩wñ ifamu-ma che abe̩le̩ ge̩; oñ e̩do̩ Fero ño̩ gbiti waa, i la ko̩ enyʼuma eti; alu ki Jihofa ka le̩.
Taku Fero murida le tef unyi-wñ, tʼabe̩le̩, tʼabe̩le̩, i dʼe̩do̩ tʼo̩ n.
Tak abo Ijipti chaka fʼura gwa o̩la Naye̩l ku ma kpa ñmo̩, todu ma neke ñmo̩ omi Naye̩l le̩ n.
Tak abu ku Jihofa fu Naye̩l gwo le̩, i ño̩ jʼo̩jo̩ mebie.
Atulubo̩ ekeji
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Nyʼugbo Fero kʼe̩ ka ñw u kakini, Abu Jihofa aka de̩, kakini, Tʼamone̩-mi no̩ ku ma re̩ mi.
E̩ muda ko̩ eje̩ ñwu ma lo, go, nanʼo̩bana kpʼane̩-we̩ bie̩ gbogbo kad alo̩me̩-wñ du;
Naye̩l-i ako̩ ñw amo̩bana, ama ate̩gu nyʼef unyi-we̩ kpai ef unyi olu-we̩ kpai oj ate̩-we̩ kpai ef unyi abuko̩lo̩-we̩ kpai abʼamone̩-we̩ o̩la ma, kpai ef igbeli-we̩ kpai ef agu-we̩;
amo̩bana le̩ la awa bʼuwe̩ kpai amone̩-we̩ kpai abuko̩lo̩-we̩ ma chaka.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩ ka ñw Aro̩n kakini, Nʼo̩wo̩-we̩ kʼo̩kpa-we̩ dʼo̩ le̩ dala nʼohimini ohimini kpai nʼaji aji kpai noji oduda oduda omi, kʼe̩ la je̩ ñw amo̩bana lewa abʼane̩ Ijipti ma!
Abe̩le̩ Aro̩n fʼo̩wo̩-wñ nadala nʼomi omi Ijipti; tak amo̩bana lewa bʼane̩ Ijipti ma.
Tak amachifamu lewa nʼe̩wñ ifamu e-ma che abe̩le̩ ge̩, oñ ma mʼamo̩bana ko wa abʼane̩ Ijipti ma.
Taku Fero fu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n do̩ wa, oñ i kakini, Me̩ gbo̩ko̩bo̩ Jihofa, kʼi mʼamo̩bana ko bʼo̩la-mi kpai amone̩-mi te̩; tak u naje̩ ñw amone̩ le̩ lo ku ma che iche̩bo̩ ñwu Jihofa.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñwu Fero kakini. Mʼe le̩ bu mo̩ ñwu mi ta, kʼe̩ dʼiko-wñ ñwu mi kʼu nagbo̩ko̩bʼo̩ todu uwe̩ kpai abuko̩lo̩-we̩ kpai amone̩-we̩, ku ma fʼamo̩bana kpa bʼuwe̩ kpai unyi unyi-we̩ te̩, ku ma bo̩ efu Naye̩l kate.
Tak i kakini, O̩na. Taku Mose̩s kakini, I ki de̩ alu kʼe̩ ka, todu kʼuwe̩ ki ma ka kʼe̩ne̩ du kʼi dabu Jihofa, O̩jo̩-wa, do̩mo̩ n.
Amo̩bana le̩ akwo bʼuwe̩ kpai unyi unyi-we̩ kpai abuko̩lo̩-we̩ kpai amone̩-we̩ te̩; ma la abo̩ efu Naye̩l kate.
Taku Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n kwʼugbo Fero dufu; oñ Mose̩s kwado̩ Jihofa todu amo̩bana kʼi wa abu Fero ma le̩.
Jihofa la che teju o̩la Mose̩s; oñ amo̩bana leku bʼef unyi unyi te̩ kpai ologbo ologbo kpai oko oko te̩.
Taku ma fʼuma yajo̩ aido aido, oñ ane̩ le̩ alu.
Ama e̩gba ku Fero li ka kʼi bulo̩, i fʼe̩do̩-wñ no̩, oñ i ko̩ enyʼuma eti; alu ku Jihofa ka le̩.
Atulubo̩ e̩ke̩ta
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s, kakini, E̩ ka ñw Aro̩n kakini, Fʼo̩kpa-we̩ nadala kʼe̩ du gwo ebutu ane̩ ile̩-i, kʼi mud amahiama ugbo du ane̩ Ijipti.
Taku ma f abe̩le̩ che; Aro̩n fʼo̩wo̩-wñ nadala oñ i dʼo̩kpa-wñ gwo ebutu ane̩-ile̩, tak amahiama wa jʼo̩la one̩ kpai e̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩; ebutu ane̩ ile̩ chaka mud amahiama ugbo du ane̩ Ijipti.
Amachifamu ño̩ ne̩ e̩wñ ifamu e-ma che ku ma ko amahiama dufu wa, ma muda neke che n. Abe̩le̩ amahiama jʼo̩la one̩ kpai e̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩.
Tak amachifamu ka ñwu Fero kakini, O̩mo̩wo̩ e-O̩jo̩ de̩. E̩do̩ Fero muda gbiti, oñ i ko̩ enyʼuma eti; alu ku Jihofa ka le̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩ takpa kwane̩ odudu, kʼe̩ dago anede Fero, go, i adufu nyʼaji le̩, kʼe̩ la ka ñw u kakini, Abu ku Jihofa aka de̩ kakini, Tʼamone̩-mi no ku ma re̩ mi.
Cho̩kpo̩ni, iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ ma je̩ tʼamone̩-mi no̩ ku ma lo n, go, nakpe̩ amachichi ku ma dutu wa abʼuwe̩ kpai abuko̩lo̩-we̩ kpai amone̩-we̩ ma, ma la atʼef unyi unyi-we̩, unyi unyi abo Ijipti du la ako̩ ñw amachichi ku ma dutu wa kpai ane̩pe̩te̩ ugbo ku ma dago ge̩.
O̩jo̩ le̩ omi la afʼane̩ Goshe̩n, ugbo kʼamone̩-mi jo̩ le̩, date̩ ojoji, todu kʼamachichi du kʼi we ejʼo̩mo̩; todu kʼuwe̩ ki ma ka kʼomi che Jihofa o̩ge̩ge̩de̩ ane̩-ile̩-i.
Abe̩le̩ u la afʼo̩me̩ hi tʼagbagba amone̩-mi kpai amone̩-we̩. Gbogbo nyʼo̩na oñ ujiwe-i ade̩.
Atulubo̩ e̩ke̩le̩
Oñ Jihofa fʼabe̩le̩ che; amachichi mudutu wʼef unyi Fero kpai ef unyi unyi abuko̩lo̩-wñ e̩kute̩, ugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti le̩ mukpabie̩ te̩ noji amachichi le̩.
Taku Fero fu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n do̩ wa, oñ i kakini, Me̩ lo ku me̩ fʼe̩wñ e̩bie̩ kpa ñw O̩jo̩-me̩ oj ane̩-i.
Mose̩s muda kakini, I chʼeju-wñ kʼa che abe̩le̩ n; todu e̩wñ kʼabo Ijipti la ahihie̩ne̩-wñ le̩ oñ a akpa ñwu Jihofa, O̩jo̩-wa. Iche̩wñ kʼa kʼe̩wñ ihie̩ne̩ Ijipti chʼiche̩bo̩ eju-ma, ma arʼokuta ñw an?
Awa anyʼef aje̩tachi ule̩ o̩jo̩ me̩ta chuu, kʼa kpa e̩wñ e̩bie̩ ñwu Jihofa, O̩jo̩-wa, alu kʼi añwa ñw a.
Taku Fero kakini, Naje̩ ñwu me̩ lo ku me̩ kpʼe̩wñ e̩bie̩ ñwu Jihofa, O̩jo̩-me̩, ef aje̩tachi; me̩ ki muda le jiji n. Me̩ ki gbo̩ko̩bʼo̩ ñwu mi.
Taku Mose̩s kakini, Go, nakwʼugbo we̩ dufu-i oñ nagbo̩ko̩bo̩ Jihofa kʼamachichi-i ki kwo bi Fero kpai abuko̩lo̩-wñ kpai amone̩-wñ te̩ o̩na; Fero ki muda ño̩ dabi che wa ayechi kʼi we etʼamone̩ no̩ ku ma nyʼakpa e̩wñ ñwu Jihofa ge̩ no.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s kwʼugbo Fero dufu, oñ i gbo̩ko̩bo̩ Jihofa.
Taku Jihofa che alu ku Mose̩s bi le̩, i la mʼamachichi ko kwo bi Fero kpai abuko̩lo̩-wñ kpai abo-wñ o̩la te̩; okate-ma bo̩ n.
Fero muda ño̩ fʼe̩do̩-wñ no̩ e̩ne̩de̩-i ge̩. I la tʼamone̩ le̩ no̩ ku ma lo n.
Atulubo̩ e̩ke̩lu
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩ nyʼugbo Fero kʼe̩ ka ñw u kakini, Abu ku Jihofa, O̩jo̩ e-amaHibru, ka de̩ kakini, E̩ ki tʼamone̩-mi no̩ ku ma re̩ mi.
Todu iche̩wñ kʼe̩ ko̩ eje̩ ñwu ma lo kʼe̩ la gwo̩nyu ma waa,
go, o̩wo̩ Jihofa anʼe̩wñ ibi wa gulo̩ bʼame̩-wñ ukpa-we̩ ku ma jʼoko ma, tʼamanya, tʼamo̩ke̩ke̩te̩, tʼaminyakulumi, tʼamokuno̩, tʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini.
Jihofa muda afʼame̩wñ ukpa abo Israe̩l kpai ame̩wñ ukpa Ijipti kpe̩ru ojoji, ef e̩wñ du kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l ne̩ e-du aku n.
Taku Jihofa fʼiko-wñ date̩, i kakini, O̩na, Jihofa ache e̩wñ-i ane̩-i.
Taku Jihofa fʼe̩wñ-i che o̩jo̩ñwa-wñ; ame̩wñ ukpa Ijipti chaka leku, i muda chʼe-ame̩wñ ukpa amo̩ma Israe̩l, okate-wñ ku n.
Taku Fero fʼonuche̩ kpe̩ nyʼo̩mo̩, me̩ la go, ame̩wñ ukpa abo Israe̩l okate ku n. E̩do̩ Fero muda no̩, i la tʼamone̩ le̩ no̩ n.
Atulubo̩ e̩ke̩fa
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n kakini, Me̩ bʼelulu adido nyʼo̩wo̩-me̩, ku Mose̩s ki nakwʼu rʼojale eju Fero.
Tak e-le̩ amud ebutu ki akwu bʼane̩ Ijipti du ma, oñ i amud iketo̩ko̩ ki amʼone̩ kʼi ate̩ño̩ jʼaño̩la one̩ kpai e̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ ugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti.
Abe̩le̩ ma mʼelulu adido ko, oñ ma kwodago o̩gba Fero, taku Mose̩s fʼu kwu rʼojale, oñ i mud iketo̩ko̩ ki ate̩ño̩ jʼaño̩la one̩ kpai e̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩.
Amachifamu le̩ la neke dago o̩gba Mose̩s in, todu iketo̩ko̩ le̩, todu iketo̩ko̩ le̩ jʼo̩la amachifamu kpai abo Ijipti du.
Jihofa muda ño̩ che e̩do̩ Fero ki gbiti, i la netirʼuma n; alu ku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s le̩.
Atulubo̩ e̩kebie
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩ takpa kwane̩ odudu kʼe̩ dago o̩gba Fero, kʼe̩ ka ñw u kakini, Abu ki Jihofa, O̩jo̩ e-amaHibru, ka de̩ kakini, Tʼamone̩-mi no̩ ku ma re̩ mi.
E̩ne̩de̩-i nakpe̩ atulubo̩-mi chaka wa bʼe̩ e̩do̩ ma, kpai abʼabuko̩lo̩-we̩ ma, kpai abʼamone̩-we̩ ma, todu kʼuwe̩ ki ma ka ki nʼe̩ne̩ kʼi dab omi ugbo du ane̩-ile̩-i n.
Todu i ma nʼugbo kʼomi ma dʼo̩wo̩-mi dufu anʼe̩wñ ibi gwo abo-we̩ da e̩gba-i me̩, taku ma ma fʼuwe̩ ko̩da rinyo̩ bʼane̩-ile̩-i te̩;
i muda chʼutodu e̩wñ-i gbage̩de̩ oñ omi dʼuwe̩ kwane̩, todu kʼu dʼukpahiu-mi ñʼuwe̩, todu ku ma ki dʼodu-mi kpogo ugbo du ane̩-ile̩-i.
Uwe̩ te̩tahi o̩la-we̩ ne ugbo amone̩-mi ta, e̩ la aje̩ ñwu ma lo n.
Go, dab iko-i o̩na, naje̩ ñw okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha ki wane̩ akiliwo, e-kʼe̩go̩-wñ ma dʼane̩ Ijipti akwe̩gba ku ma chʼunyane̩-wñ gbogbo wʼifai n.
Todule̩, e̩ fʼuche̩ kpe̩ fai, ku ma kʼame̩wñ ukpa-we̩ kpai e̩wñ du kʼe̩ ne̩ oko maja nyo̩nyo̩; todu okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha le̩ awane̩ bʼone̩ kpai e̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ du ku ma li oko ku ma ma ko wa unyi n ma, ma la aku.
Tak e̩ne̩ kʼi dʼefu abuko̩lo̩ Fero ki railo o̩la Jihofa, je̩ ñw amadu-wñ kpai ame̩wñ ukpa-wñ ra jʼef unyi unyi;
e̩ne̩ kʼo̩la Jiliofa ma wʼeju n tʼamadu-wñ kpai ame̩wñ ukpa-wñ no̩ jʼoko.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Fʼo̩wo̩-we̩ nadala rʼojale, kʼokuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha ki wane̩ bʼane̩ Ijipti chaka ma, abʼoji one̩ kpai e̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ kpai e̩wñ oko kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ du ma, ugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti.
Taku Mose̩s fʼo̩kpa-wñ nadala rʼojale; oñ Jihofa fʼakpabana kpai okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha kpuche̩ wa, una lewa gbʼane̩ nyʼo̩wo̩ tʼemi tʼemi. Jihofa la je̩ ñw okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha lewa bʼane̩ Ijipti ma.
Abe̩le̩ okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha do̩mo̩ manyʼuna ki adʼo̩go̩ tʼemi tʼemi ef okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha le̩, akiliwo-wñ tabale, e̩go̩-wñ de̩ ane̩ Ijipti akwʼe̩gba ki mud uche̩ichi amone̩ mama ta n.
Okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha le̩ fʼe̩wñ du ki jʼoko ugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti gwo mʼane̩, tʼone̩, tʼe̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩; okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha le̩ laño̩ fu e̩wñ kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ oko du gwo mʼane̩, i la fʼoli du kʼi jo̩ oko kpanya rinyo̩.
Chai ane̩ Goshe̩n, ugbo kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l jo̩ le̩, o̩mo̩ kate oñ okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha ma wa n.
Taku Fero fʼonuche̩ kpe̩, oñ i fu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n do̩ wa, i ka ñwu ma kakini, U dure iko-i me̩; Jihofa chʼe̩no̩kpakpa, omi kpai abo-mi la chʼame̩ne̩bibi.
Gbo̩ko̩bo̩ Jihofa; todu omu O̩jo̩ kpai okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha-i bʼuwa jo̩ me̩; natʼume̩ no̩, me̩ ñʼajo̩ emi ge̩ n.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw u kakini, Ababa kʼu kwʼef ewo-i dufu nanʼo̩wo̩-mi dala ñwu Jihofa; akpabana le̩ awe, okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha awa ge̩ n, kʼuwe̩ ki ma ka kʼane̩-ile̩-i chʼe-Jihofa.
I la chʼuwe̩ kpai abuko̩lo̩-we̩, u chema ka kʼame̩ arailo O̩jo̩ ta n. 31(Flaks kpai o̩ka barli mukpabie̩, todu o̩ka barli le̩ mutoji, flaks la adikoko.
O̩ka wit kpai o̩ka spe̩lti muda kpabie̩ n, todu abo e-le̩ ache̩du etiga.)
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s kwʼef ewo ugbo Fero dufu, oñ i fʼo̩wo̩-wñ nadala ñwu Jihofa; tak akpabana kpai okuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha le̩ we, omi ojale laño̩ lo̩ akiliwo bʼile̩ ma ge̩ n.
Tak e̩gba ku Fero li ka kʼomi ojale kpai okuta omo̩jo̩cha kpai akpabana we, i nadure alo waa, i la fʼe̩do̩-wñ no̩, owñ kpai abuko̩lo̩-wñ.
Abe̩le̩ e̩do̩ Fero gbiti, i la je̩ ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l ku ma lo n; alu ki Jihofa ka lugbo Mose̩s le̩.
E̩do̩ Fero kpa ololo
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Nyʼejefu ugbo Fero todu omi fʼe̩do̩-wñ no̩ kpai e̩do̩ abuko̩lo̩-wñ, todu kʼu du ujiwe-mi-i ñʼe̩ña efu-ma,
todu kʼuwe̩ ki kʼinabali alu kʼu che abo Ijipti kpai ujiwe kʼomi che efu-ma nyʼo̩ma-we̩ kpai aaju-we̩ e̩ti; todu kʼuwe̩ ama ka kʼomi Jihofa de̩.
Taku Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n nyʼejefu ugbo Fero, oñ ma ka ñw u kakini, Abu ku Jihofa, O̩jo̩ amaHibru aka de̩ kakini, Gbogbo nyʼe̩gba uwe̩ ako̩ ehi o̩la-we̩ wane̩ o̩gba-mi kade taa? Tʼamone̩-mi no̩ ku ma re̩ mi.
Cho̩kpo̩ni iche̩wñ kʼe̩ ko̩ eje̩ ñw abo-mi lo, go, nakʼamimiejo wa oj ane̩-we̩ o̩na,
ma la abʼeju ane̩ ma gbogbo tak one̩ ma ali ane̩pe̩te̩ ge̩ n; tak ama le̩ aje̩ abubo̩ e̩wñ ki bo̩ ñwu me̩ kʼokuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha ma kpa n, oli-me̩ du kʼi atiga oko ma la aje̩.
Oñ ef unyi-we̩ ako̩ ñwu ma, kpai ef unyi abuko̩lo̩-we̩ chaka kpai ef unyi unyi abo Ijipti chaka du; alu kʼamata-we̩ kpai amokwo̩-we̩ ma li akwe̩gba ku ma wʼile̩ gbogbo tʼojolu eñini n. Tak i mubidagba, oñ i kwʼugbo Fero dufu.
Tak abuko̩lo̩ Fero ka ñw u kakini, Gbogbo nyʼe̩gba oñ e̩ne̩-i achʼoku ñw a kade taa? Je̩ ñw aboke̩le̩ le̩ lo kʼama ki re̩ Jihofa, O̩jo̩-ma; uwe̩ ma ka kʼIjipti mud alache̩ te̩-i n?
Taku ma ño̩ mu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n ko dabi wa ugbo Fero; oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ lo ku me̩ re̩ Jihofa, O̩jo̩-me̩; ama e̩ne̩ chʼabo ki alo?
Taku Mose̩s kakini, A alo, tʼimo̩to̩-wa, tʼogijo-wa; awa kpai amo̩ma-wa e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai amo̩ma-wa onobule̩ kpai ame̩wño̩re̩-wa egini kpai amokuno̩-wa alo; todu awa ahi uje̩wñ uyo̩ ñwu Jihofa tila.
Tak i ka ñwu ma kakini, Jihofa ki dʼugbo me̩! Omi kʼu je̩ ñwu me̩ lo kpai amo̩ma-me̩ egini? me̩ go, e̩bie̩ne̩ dʼo̩gba-me̩-i!
Gbe̩do̩! Ame̩ aboke̩le̩, me̩ lo ku me̩ re̩ Jihofa, todu e̩wñ ki dʼume̩ e̩do̩ le̩ de̩. Taku ma fu ma ne bʼeju Fero te̩.
Atulubo̩ e̩ke̩jo̩
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Fʼo̩wo̩ nadala nʼane̩ Ijipti tod amimiejo, kʼama ki lewa abʼane̩ Ijipti ma, ku ma je̩ e̩wñ eñmi kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ du ki jʼane̩-i, e-du kʼokuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha le̩ to̩no̩.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s fʼo̩kpa-wñ nadala nʼane̩ Ijipti, oñ Jihofa je̩ ñw afu ju kwʼo̩wo̩ olodudu wa bʼane̩ le̩ ma gbogbo dʼo̩jo̩, gbogbo ñw o̩jo̩; tak e̩gba kʼo̩jo̩ muñwa afu o̩wo̩ olodudu le̩ mʼamimiejo ko wa jʼo̩mo̩.
Oñ amimiejo lewa bʼane̩ Ijipti du ma, ma la dade jo̩ ugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti; ma tabale; amimiejo e̩go e-ma de̩ mama ta n, ma ñʼade̩ abe̩le̩ ate̩to̩gba ge̩ n.
Todu ma mʼeju olu ane̩ le̩ du gba, todu abe̩le̩ ane̩ kwochubi, oñ ma mʼe̩wñ eñmi kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ du ane̩ le̩ ko je̩, kpai e̩ro oli kʼokuta o̩mo̩jo̩cha to̩no̩ du; e̩wñ emimi du la bo̩ n, tʼoli, tʼe̩wñ eñmi kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ ef uche̩, ugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti.
Taku Fero fu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n do̩ wa unaju, unaju; oñ i kakini, Omi fu Jihofa, O̩jo̩-me̩, dure, kpai ame̩ ge̩.
Todule̩, agba, e̩ ki dʼadure-mi tinyo̩ bʼumi o̩la te̩ onukate-i ta, kʼe̩ la gbo̩ko̩bo̩ Jihofa, O̩jo̩-me̩, kʼi mʼuku-i kate gba bʼumi oji te̩.
Tak i kwʼugbo Fero dufu, oñ i gbo̩ko̩bo̩ Jihofa.
Taku Jihofa mʼafu rida tʼolane̩ kʼi ju nana, oñ e-le̩ mʼamimiejo ko, i la fu ma ne rʼef Ohimini Ekpikpa; imiejo okate bo̩ ejefu alʼo̩me̩ Ijipti du n.
Jihofa muda ño̩ che e̩do̩ Fero kʼi gbiti, i la tʼamo̩ma Israe̩l no̩ ku ma lo n.
Atulubo̩ e̩ke̩la
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Fʼo̩wo̩-we̩ nadala rʼojale kʼe̩chubi ki bʼane̩ Ijipti ma, kʼi chʼe̩chubi kʼone̩ adʼo̩wo̩kado.
Taku Mose̩s fʼo̩wo̩-wñ nadala rʼojale; oñ e̩chubi ki jukpa dʼugbo du ane̩ Ijipti gbogbo o̩jo̩ me̩ta;
ma li o̩la-ma n, e̩ne̩ du la kwane̩ kwʼe̩gu-wñ n gbogbo o̩jo̩ me̩ta; abo Israe̩l du muda nʼugane̩ ugbo ku ma gugu le̩.
Taku Fero fu Mose̩s do̩ wa, i kakini, Me̩ lo ku me̩ re̩ Jihofa; amo̩ma-me̩ ki ño̩ lebʼume̩; chai ame̩wño̩re̩-me̩ egini kpai amokuno̩-me̩ ki bo̩ jʼane̩.
Ama Mose̩s kakini, I dukpe̩ kʼe̩ ño̩ kʼe̩wñ iche̩bo̩ kpai e̩wñ iche̩bo̩ e̩gujo nyʼuwa o̩wo̩ tila, todu kʼawa ki ko che ñwu Jihofa O̩jo̩-wa.
Ame̩wñ ukpa-wa ñʼale bʼuwa tila; etikpaʼkate ama ubi n; todu ef e-le̩ oñ a chi kwo kʼa ko re̩ Jihofa O̩jo̩-wa tila; awa la ma e̩wñ kʼa ne̩ re̩ Jihofa abu kʼa ma nyʼo̩mo̩ ta ni n.
Ama Jihofa ño̩ che kʼe̩do̩ Fero ki gbiti waa, oñ i ko̩ etʼuma no̩.
Taku Fero ka ñw u kakini, Kwo bʼumi te̩; fʼo̩la-we̩ de; e̩ ki ño̩ go mi eju ogbegbele̩ ge̩ n; todu o̩jo̩ kʼe̩ fʼe u-mi li eku e̩ ku.
Taku Mose̩s kakini, O̩me̩me̩le̩ e̩ ka le̩! u ñʼali eju-we̩ ge̩ n.
O̩jo̩ ka kʼamo̩mo̩gba aku
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, I bo̩ atulubo̩ okate kʼu nadu wa abʼi Fero kpai Ijipti oji ma ta; ubi e-le̩ tak i aje̩ ñwu me̩ kwʼemi alo: e̩gba kʼi aje̩ ñwu me̩ lo le̩ ene i ane me̩ kwʼemi hioko.
Ifai tak e̩ ko̩la ki tʼamone̩-i eti, ka kʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du, kpai onobule̩ du, ki bi e̩wñ eku ajifa kpai e̩wñ eku o̩jamalia ugbo ekeji-wñ.
Oñ Jihofa je̩ ñw abo Ijipti li amone̩ le̩ eju. Anoji e-le̩ ge̩ Mose̩s chʼe̩ne̩ lile oj ane̩ Ijipti le̩ eju abuko̩lo̩ Fero kpai eju amone̩ oj ane̩ Ijipti.
Taku Mose̩s kakini, Abu ku Jihofa aka de̩ kakini, Ame̩ru iñaliña odu nadufu tʼalumeji Ijipti;
tak amo̩mo̩gba du oj ane̩ Ijipti aku, akwʼo̩mo̩gba Fero kʼi gugu oj e̩de̩-wñ le̩ gbogbo wa o̩mo̩gba adu onobule̩ kʼi dʼo̩dokuta; kpai o̩mo̩gba ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ du.
Tak o̩li lile achi ugbo du oj ane̩ Ijipti, e-kʼe̩go̩-wñ ma de̩ mama ta n, i ñʼade̩ ej o̩gba ge̩ n.
I muda che e-abo Israe̩l du, tʼone̩, tʼe̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩, abia du ako̩ ru ma n; todu kʼame̩ ki ma ka kʼabo Ijipti kpai abo Israe̩l chʼojoji eju Jihofa.
Tak abo ku ma chʼamadu-we̩-i du agwo̩ru wʼugbo mi, ku ma dojikane̩ ñwu mi; ma akakini, E̩ kwʼemi alo, uwe̩ kpai amone̩ du ku ma tʼuwe̩ ubi. Ubi le̩ tak u nadufu alo. Tak i we̩do̩ kwʼo̩gba Fero dufu.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Fero anyʼuwe̩ eti n; todu kʼe̩wñ uno̩-mi ki wewe nyo̩gba oj ane̩ Ijipti.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n fʼe̩wñ uno̩-i chaka che eju Fero; oñ Jihofa che e̩do̩ Fero ki gbiti, i la tʼabo Israe̩l no̩ ku ma kwo bʼane̩-wñ te̩ n.
Elaloji edu wane̩
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n ane̩ Ijipti o̩mo̩, kakini,
Ochu-i achʼagboji ochu du ñwu me̩; ochu ejodudu o̩do̩ du, i ache ñwu me̩.
Me̩ ka ñw abo o̩gbadu Israe̩l chaka ka kʼo̩jo̩ e̩ke̩gwa ochu-i e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ki mʼe̩wño̩re̩ egini du alu kʼuwewe akwo̩ra unyi ata-wñ de̩, e̩wño̩re̩ eginiʼka todu akwo̩ra unyiʼka;
i la che̩wñ kʼakwo̩ra unyi le̩ nyaru e̩wño̩re̩ eginiʼka, e̩gbale̩ tak one̩ kpai ekeji-wñ kʼunyi-wñ ro̩ne amʼoka du alu kʼuwewe amone̩-ma de̩; alu kʼe̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ neke je̩ alu le̩ me̩ akaluka one̩-wñ todu e̩wño̩re̩ eginiʼka.
E̩wño̩re̩-we̩ egini amufu, i achʼo̩ko̩ kʼi chʼo̩ma o̩do̩ʼka; ame̩ ki mʼu du kwef amala abe̩k o̩mewo;
tak ame̩ ade gbogbo wʼo̩jo̩ e̩ke̩gwe̩le̩ ochu-i, e̩gbale̩ ujeju o̩gbadu abo Israe̩l chaka akpa e̩gba ane̩.
Taku ma adʼe̩bie̩-wñ kuru oli udago o̩wo̩ meji alugbo̩na kpai akofida-wñ ate̩, ef unyi ugbo ku ma aje̩ e̩la-wñ.
Ma aje̩ e̩la-wñ odu o̩jo̩ le̩, ero̩ ma aro̩; ma aje̩ manyʼe̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma dʼefu-wñ n manyʼe̩wñ ki alukoko.
Me̩ ki je̩ emimi-wñ n kpai e̩hi-wñ n, chai e-ku ma ro̩; tʼoji-wñ, tʼe̩re̩-wñ, tʼifi-wñ.
Me̩ ki je̩ ñw e-du bo̩bo̩ nyʼodudu n, e-du kʼi la bo̩ nyʼodudu me̩ fʼu gujo.
Abu ku me̩ aje̩ de̩: iñmi-me̩ ki chʼe̩ji, e̩da-me̩ ki dʼe̩re̩-me̩, o̩kpa-me̩ ki la dʼef o̩wo̩-me̩; me̩ hika je̩ unaju unaju: Elaloji e-Jihofa de̩.
Todu omi alale gu ef ane̩ Ijipti du odu o̩jo̩ le̩, oñ nagwʼamo̩mo̩gba du oj ane̩ Ijipti dajane̩, tʼone̩, tʼe̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩; u la abʼudu ñw amo̩jo̩ Ijipti-i chaka; omi Jihofa de̩.
E̩bie̩ le̩ la achʼujiwe ñwu me̩ o̩la unyi unyi ugbo ku me̩ jo̩ le̩; oñ e̩gba kʼu fʼe̩bie̩ le̩ li nalʼume̩ oji lale tak e̩wñ e̩bie̩ne̩ du abʼume̩ ma kʼi kpa me̩ bie̩ e̩gba kʼu fʼabo oj ane̩ Ijipti-i gwoda n.
Eñini-i ache o̩jo̩ urewa ñwu me̩, me̩ la ade kʼi che̩ o̩jo̩ uje̩wñ uyo̩ ñwu Jihofa; me̩ ki dʼuko̩-wñ te̩ ki che e̩wñ o̩hio̩gu-me̩ ogbegbele̩.
O̩jo̩ mebie me̩ aje̩ e̩wñ ki ma nʼo̩jo̩wu efu-wñ n; o̩jo̩ ejodudu-wñ me̩ akʼo̩jo̩wu kwef unyi-me̩ dufu, todu e̩ne̩ du kʼi fʼe̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu bie̩ nyʼu je̩ akwo o̩jo̩ ejodudu gbogbo wa o̩jo̩ e̩kebie-wñ, ma akʼonugo e̩ne̩ le̩ da bʼIsrae̩l te̩.
O̩jo̩ ejodudu-wñ me̩ achʼujeju kiafo̩, o̩jo̩ e̩kebie laño̩ chʼujeju kiafo̩ ge̩; me̩ achʼuko̩lo̩ du o̩jo̩ meji kʼa ka le̩ n, chai e̩wñ kʼe̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ aje̩, e-le̩ kate me̩ ache.
Me̩ ki fejutʼe̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma dʼo̩ n-i; todu o̩jo̩ kide̩ gbage̩de̩ oñ omi ko me̩ kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti dufu, udala udala: todule̩ me̩ afejutʼo̩jo̩-i gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-me̩ kʼi chʼuko̩ ogbegbele̩ kʼu te̩ ñwu me̩.
E̩gba ane̩, o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩gwe̩le̩ ochu ejodudu le̩, me̩ aje̩ e̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma dʼo̩ n, abe̩le̩ me̩ aje̩ gbogbo wa ane̩ o̩jo̩ ogu nyokeʼka ochu le̩.
Ma ki li o̩jo̩wu du ef unyi-me̩ gbogbo o̩jo̩ mebie le̩ n; todu e̩ne̩ du kʼi aje̩ e̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu dʼo̩, ma akʼonugo e̩ne̩ le̩ da bʼabo o̩gbadu Israe̩l te̩, dagba i chʼilowa dagba i chʼo̩mane̩.
Me̩ ki je̩ e̩wñ du kʼo̩jo̩wu dʼo̩ n, ugbo du ku me̩ dodo me̩ ki je̩ e̩wñ du kʼo̩jo̩wu dʼo̩ n.
E̩bie̩ o̩mala etafio̩ alu o̩na
Taku Mose̩s fʼabogijo Israe̩l du do̩ wa, oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, Me̩ ki tu ame̩wño̩re̩ egini ku me̩ ko alu kʼabo akwo̩ra unyi akwo̩ra unyi-me̩ de̩, ku me̩ fʼElaloji kpa.
Me̩ ki chi eñmi oli hiso̩p nyʼo̩wo̩ ku me̩ dʼu tunyu e̩bie̩ ki dʼef ugba le̩, taku me̩ dʼe̩bie̩ kʼi dʼef ugba le̩ kado oli alugbo̩na akofida-wñ ate̩ kpai o̩wo̩-wñ mejeji; e̩ne̩ du efu-me̩ ki dufu lʼalugbo̩na unyi-wñ gbogbo tak o̩jo̩ ki ñwa n.
Todu Jihofa alale gu ef ane̩-i du kʼi fʼabo Ijipti kpa; tak e̩gba kʼi ali e̩bie̩ o̩la oli akofida ate̩ kpai oli o̩wo̩ alugbo̩na mejeji, Jihofa alʼalugbo̩na le̩ oji lale, i ñʼaje̩ ñw akpʼone̩ bie̩ le̩ kʼi wa ef unyi-me̩ kʼi kpa me̩ n.
Ame̩ ki fejutʼe̩wñ-i ki chʼe̩wñ uhio̩me̩ ñw e̩ kpai amo̩ma-we̩ ogbegbele̩.
Oñ i awatu e̩gba ku me̩ lewa oj ane̩ ku Jihofa adu ñwu me̩ alu kʼi kʼo̩la-wñ tane̩ le̩, ame̩ ki de e̩wñ ku me̩ che-i.
Tak e̩gba kʼamo̩ma-me̩ aka ñwu me̩ kakini, E̩wñ chʼoji e̩wñ ku me̩ che-i?
Ame̩ akakini, Owñ chʼe̩la Elaloji Jihofa ekpa, todabu kʼi lʼoji unyi amo̩ma Israe̩l lale Ijipti, e̩gba kʼi fʼabo Ijipti le̩ gwo da kʼi la gbʼunyi e-wa tane̩. Tak amone̩ le̩ fʼoji-ma dalo̩, oñ ma dojikane̩ ñw O̩jo̩.
Tak amo̩ma Israe̩l nyʼache abe̩le̩; alu ku Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n, alu le̩ ma che.
Atulubo̩ e̩ke̩gwa; abo Israe̩l le̩
Oñ t lewatu iñaliña odu Jihofa fʼamo̩mo̩gba du oj ane̩ Ijipti gwoda, akwo o̩mo̩gba Fero kʼi gugu oj ede-wñ gbogbo wa o̩mo̩gba e̩namu kʼi dʼef ura ef unyi uga, kpai amo̩mo̩gba ame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ du ge̩.
Taku Fero kwane̩ odu o̩jo̩ le̩, owñ kpai abuko̩lo̩-wñ chaka kpai abo Ijipti chaka; tak o̩li lile chi Ijipti, todu i nʼunyi du kʼoku one̩ ma dʼefu-wñ ni n.
Tak i fu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n do̩ wa odu, oñ i kakini, Me̩ kwane̩, me̩ kwʼef abo-mi dufu, tʼame̩, tʼamo̩ma Israe̩l; me̩ lo, ku me̩ re̩ Jihofa alu ku me̩ ka le̩.
Me̩ maʼame̩wño̩re̩-me̩ egini kpai amokuno̩-me̩ ko alu ku me̩ ka le̩ ku me̩ lo me̩ ke; me̩ ki no̩ kadua ñwu mi ge̩!
Abo Ijipti la nakʼamone̩ le̩ e̩che̩ unaju unaju ku ma kwʼoj ane̩ le̩; todu ma kakini, O̩chaka-wa mud oku one̩ me̩.
Abe̩le̩ amone̩ le̩ fʼe̩kpo uje̩-wñ-ma kʼo̩jo̩wu ma dʼo̩ n ko, agu-ma chʼe̩ji jʼef ukpo-ma nʼika-ma.
Oñ amo̩ma Israe̩l ño̩ che alu ku Mose̩s ka le̩, ma fʼe̩wñ eku e-ajifa, e-o̩jamalia kpai e̩wñ ku ma ko nyʼo̩la bi ugbo abo Ijipti;
Jihofa la je̩ ñw abo Ijipti li amone̩ le̩ eju, oñ ma mʼe̩wñ ku ma bi le̩ ko ñwu ma. Abe̩le̩ ma bʼabo Ijipti gba e̩wñ-ma kpa.
Tak amo̩ma Israe̩l le kwo Ramese̩s nyi Suko̩t, amo̩kone̩ ku ma le e̩re̩ ofo dab icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ ulo̩gwa, manyʼabo-ma egini.
O̩wo̩ amone̩ ojoji ojoji ño̩ te̩gu le bʼuma ge̩, kpai ame̩wñ ukpa otemeje, tʼame̩wño̩re̩ egini, tʼamokuno̩,
taku ma ne̩ e̩kpo uje̩wñ ku ma ko kwo Ijipti wa le̩ che akala kʼo̩jo̩wu ma dʼo̩ n, todu ma dʼo̩jo̩wu tʼo̩ ta n, todabu ku ma kʼuma e̩che̩ kwʼIjipti dufu, ma la neke che̩du ubi n, ma la ñw ane̩ uje̩wñ che tane̩ ñw o̩la-ma n.
Iko kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l jo̩ Ijipti le̩ chʼo̩do̩ ulo̩ko̩ nyʼogue̩gwa.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba kʼo̩do̩-wñ jo̩ ulo̩ko̩ nyʼogue̩gwa, o̩jo̩ le̩ gbage̩de̩, o̩gbo̩ abo Jihofa du kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti dufu.
E-le̩ chʼodu ku ma dejute̩ ñwu Jihofa gbali abu kʼi mʼuma ko kwʼane̩ Ijipti wa; abe̩le̩ odu le̩ gbage̩de̩ chʼodu kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l du adejute̩ ñwu Jihofa gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-ma.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n kakini, Uko̩ e-Elaloji le̩ de̩: Ononojo du aje̩ n;
adu du ku ma nʼo̩ko̩ la, kʼe̩ fʼe̩pi-wñ da, muda aje̩.
E̩ne̩ ane̩ omune̩ du kpai e̩ne̩ uko̩lo̩ ku ma rʼo̩me̩ ñw u, aje̩ n.
Ef unyi okate oñ ma aje̩; e̩ ki ko̩ e̩la-wñ du kwef unyi nyʼo̩do̩da n; me̩ ki la gu achiku-wñ okate che̩ n.
O̩gbadu abo Israe̩l chaka ade.
E̩gba kʼilowa ge̩ne̩ ugbo we̩ kʼi neku ede Elaloji le̩ ñwu Jihofa, aboke̩le̩-wñ chaka ki fʼe̩pi da ejodudu, tak i ate̩me̩ru ade; i adab o̩mane̩. E̩ne̩ du ki ma da e̩pi n muda aje̩ n.
Uko̩ o̩mane̩ kpai e-ilowa ki ge̩ne̩ efu-me̩ achʼoka.
Abe̩le̩ amo̩ma Israe̩l chaka che; alu ku Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n, abe̩le̩ ma che.
O̩jo̩ le̩ gbage̩de̩ oñ Jihofa mʼamo̩ma Israe̩l ko kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti dufu, udala udala-ma.
Ma kʼamo̩mo̩gba jo̩ ñw O̩jo̩
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
E̩ fʼamo̩mo̩gba chaka che ku ma fo̩ ku ma mud e-mi; e-du ki dʼef amo̩ma Israe̩l kʼi kpʼo̩gba iye-wñ na, tʼone̩, tʼe̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩, e-mi i che.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw amone̩ le̩ kakini, Me̩ nadibekado o̩jo̩ eñini-i, kʼi chʼo̩jo̩ ku me̩ kwo Ijipti dufu, kwʼef unyi adu le̩, todu lugbo ukpahiu o̩wo̩-wñ oñ Jihofa ko me̩ kwo ugbo kide̩ dufu; me̩ ki je̩ uje̩wñ du kʼo̩jo̩wu dʼefu-wñ n.
Eñini, ochu Abib-i, me̩ akwʼemi adufu.
Tak e̩gba ku Jihofa mʼume̩ ko wa ane̩ abo Kenan kpai abo He̩t kpai abo Amo̩r kpai abo Hifai kpai abo Je̩bius, owñ chʼe-kʼi go̩ ñw amata-me̩ ka kʼi adu ñwu me̩, ane̩ kʼomi e̩nya kpai iño̩ acha efu-wñ le̩, ame̩ ade e̩wñ ucholo kide̩ ochu-i.
Me̩ aje̩ e̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma do̩ n gbogbo o̩jo̩ mebie, tak o̩jo̩ e̩kebie-wñ achʼuje̩wñ uyo̩ ñwu Jihofa.
Ma aje̩ e̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma do̩ n gbogbo o̩jo̩ mebie; ama ki li e̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu dʼefu-wñ ugbo we̩ n, ama ki la li o̩jo̩wu du ugbo du oj ane̩-we̩ n.
Tak uwe̩ ki ka ñw o̩ma-we̩ o̩jo̩ le̩ kakini, E-le̩ chʼutodu e̩wñ ku Jihofa che ñwu mi e̩gba kʼu kwʼIjipti dufu.
I la ache ujiwe o̩wo̩-we̩ ñw e̩, i ñʼachʼutodu urewa o̩gba oji-we̩, todu kʼuko̩-o̩la Jihofa ki nadʼef alu-we̩; todu o̩wo̩ ukpahiu-wñ oñ Jihofa ne̩ mʼuwe̩ du kwʼIjipti dufu.
Todule̩ e̩ ki de uko̩ kide̩ iko-wñ o̩do̩ tʼo̩do̩ du.
Oñ e̩gba ku Jihofa mʼe̩ du wa ane̩ abo Kenan, alu kʼi go̩ ñw e̩ kpai amata-we̩, kʼi la mʼu du ñw e̩,
tak uwe̩ achi e̩ne̩ du ki kpʼo̩gba iye-wñ na jo̩ ñwu Jihofa. O̩mo̩gba e̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩-we̩ du kʼi chʼo̩ko̩ ache e-Jihofa.
O̩mo̩gba o̩ke̩ke̩te̩ du e̩ nʼe̩wño̩re̩ egini la tane̩, i la che̩wñ kʼe̩ ma neku ela tane̩ n mak e̩ fʼo̩lo̩-wñ guche̩. O̩mo̩gba one̩ du ki jʼef amo̩me̩ne̩ke̩le̩-we̩, uwe̩ alatane̩.
Tak e̩gba kʼo̩ma-we̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ atʼuwe̩ ene ejo̩gba-i kakini, E̩wñ che oji e-le̩? Uwe̩ aka ñw u kakini, Lʼugbo ukpahiu o̩wo̩-wñ oñ Jihofa mʼuwa ko kwʼIjipti dufu, kwef unyi adu le̩.
Todu e̩gba ku Fero fʼe̩do̩-wñ no̩ kʼi ma je̩ tʼuwa no̩ kʼa lo n le̩, Jihofa fʼamo̩mo̩gba du oj ane̩ Ijipti kpa, tʼo̩mo̩gba e-one̩, tʼo̩mo̩gba e-e̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩. Todule̩ nako e-du ki chʼo̩ko̩ ki chʼo̩ma ki kpʼo̩gba iye-wñ na kpa ñwu Jihofa; omi muda ala amo̩mo̩gba e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e-amo̩ma-mi tane̩.
E-le̩ ache ujiwe ef o̩wo̩-we̩ kpai e̩wñ urewa o̩gba oji-we̩; todu lugbo ukpahiu o̩wo̩-wñ oñ Jihofa mʼuwa ko kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti wa.
Abo Israe̩l nyʼEtam
Oñ i lewatu, e̩gba ku Fero tʼamone̩-i no̩, O̩jo̩ la ne̩ ma lʼo̩na oj ane̩ abo Filistia n, dagba o̩na le̩ chaka me̩; todu O̩jo̩ kakini, To̩de̩gba kʼamone̩ afʼeju dʼogu kʼibe-ma rida ku ma dabi tʼIjipti.
Ama O̩jo̩ fʼamone̩ le̩ ne̩ dagbala lʼo̩na aje̩tachi lʼo̩wo̩ Ohimini Ekpikpa. Amo̩ma Israe̩l la fʼo̩la ogu ji kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti dufu alo.
Achiku Jose̩f
Mose̩s ño̩ mʼachiku Jose̩f ko le̩. Todu Jose̩f je̩ ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l go̩ o̩me̩me̩le̩, i kakini, O̩jo̩ awa fejudo me̩ chuu; e̩gba le̩ ame̩ ki mʼachiku-mi ko kwʼemi alo.
Taku ma kwo Suko̩t alo, oñ ma lewa ru Etam, iba aje̩tachi le̩.
Jihofa la tʼuma o̩gba, o̩ro̩ka i dʼef akpa ki dago waala o̩gba-ma kʼi ne̩ ma alʼo̩na le̩, odu i dʼef una kʼi dago waala kʼi mud ugane̩ ñwu ma, ku ma nʼugbo ku ma le o̩ro̩ka kpai odu;
akpa ki dago waala o̩ro̩ka le̩ kpai una ki dago waala odu la kwo bʼamone̩ le̩ o̩gba te̩ n.
Mohimini Ohimini Ekpikpa daba
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
E̩ ka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l ku ma mudabi wʼubi ku ma rujʼo̩gba Pihahiro̩t, agbagba Migdol kpai ohimini le̩, o̩gba Beal-zefo̩n; me̩ ki ru ru jo̩ o̩la ohimini me̩ru o̩mo̩.
Todu Fero anʼo̩la amo̩ma Israe̩l aka kakini, Ma chila jo̩ oj ane̩-i me̩; aje̩tachi le̩ re nyu ma.
Oñ nache kʼe̩do̩ Fero ki gbiti, tak i arano ma; tak omi anʼojima ugbo Fero kpai ugbo abogu-wñ chaka; tak abo Ijipti ama ka kʼomi Jihofa de̩. Ma la fʼabe̩le̩ che.
Oñ ma mudu ka ñw onu Ijipti ka kʼamone̩ le̩ ra le, tak e̩do̩ Fero kpai e̩do̩ abuko̩lo̩-wñ rida ugbo amone̩ le̩, oñ ma kakini, E-kʼa che-i chʼe̩wñ taa? kʼa tʼabo Israe̩l no̩ ku ma we uko̩lo̩ adu eche ñw a?
Abe̩le̩ i fʼo̩ko̩ ogu-wñ ñwo̩che, oñ i mʼabogu-wñ ko lebʼowñ,
i la fʼo̩ko̩ ogu-wñ tu, oñ i mʼulo̩gwa-wñ ko, manyʼo̩ko̩ ogu abo Ijipti ki bo̩ chaka kpai amagboji-ma chaka.
Jihofa la che e̩do̩ Fero onu Ijipti ki gbiti, tak i rano amo̩ma Israe̩l todu amo̩ma Israe̩l dufu kpai o̩wo̩ edago.
Oñ abo Ijipti rano ma, amanya Fero chaka kpai o̩ko̩ ogu-wñ kpai abo-wñ ku ma ta nʼanya kpai abogu-wñ, i la fu ma mu ugbo ku ma ruru jo̩ o̩la ohimini me̩ru Pihahiro̩t, o̩gba Beal-zefo̩n.
Tak e̩gba ku Fero me̩ru awa, amo̩ma Israe̩l chi eju-ma nyate̩, me̩ la go, abo Ijipti dʼe̩re̩ rʼane̩ rʼuma ubi awa; oñ okpo chʼuma ofe. Tak amo̩ma Israe̩l kwado̩ Jihofa;
oñ ma ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Ukpe̩ kʼugbo ku ma dʼone̩ ji ma dʼIjipti n, oñ e̩ kowa kwʼo̩mo̩ wa kʼa ku aje̩tachi-i? E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ che wa abe̩i, kʼe̩ ko wa kwʼ Ijipti wa-i?
I chʼe-kʼa ka ñw e̩ Ijipti le̩ de̩ ka kʼe̩ tʼuwa no̩ kʼa chʼuko̩lo̩ adu ñw abo Ijipti n? Todu i ma nyo̩ tule ñw a kʼa chʼuko̩lo̩ adu ñw abo Ijipti tʼeku ef aje̩tachi-i le.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw amone̩ le̩ kakini, Me̩ ki chokpo n, me̩ dago ka, ku me̩ li ujadu Jihofa, owñ chʼe-kʼi ache ñwu me̩ eñini; todu i chʼe-abo Ijipti ku me̩ li ma eñini-i, me̩ ñʼali ma ogbegbele̩ ge̩ n.
Jihofa la ajogu todu me̩, me̩ chʼechi jo̩ ofo.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ raku do̩ mi-i? Ka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l ku ma chʼe̩re̩ nyʼo̩gba.
E̩ mʼo̩kpa-we̩ du nyʼate̩, kʼe̩ la fʼo̩wo̩ nadala nʼoji ohimini, kʼe̩ fʼu kpe̩ rʼeji, kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l ki le ane̩ e̩gbe̩ alumeji ohimini daba.
I la chʼomi, go, nache e̩do̩ abo Ijipti ki gbiti, kʼama ki rʼuma ubi nyʼefu-wñ, tak u nanʼojima ugbo Fero kpai abogu-wñ chaka kpai ugbo o̩ko̩ ogu o̩ko̩ ogu-wñ kpai ugbo amanʼanya-wñ.
Tak abo Ijipti ama ka kʼomi Jihofa de̩, owñ chʼe̩gba kʼu fʼojima ne̩ ugbo Fero kpai o̩ko̩ ogu o̩ko̩ ogu-wñ kpai ugbo amanʼanya-wñ.
Tak onuche̩ O̩jo̩ kʼi tʼabo Israe̩l o̩gba le̩ kwʼo̩gba-ma lale tʼubi-ma; tak akpa ojale ki dago waala le̩ kwʼo̩gba-ma, oñ i lewa dago ubi-ma,
oñ i lewatʼagbagba uru abo Israe̩l kpai uru abo Ijipti. Abe̩le̩ akpa kpai e̩chubi do̩mo̩, oñ i je̩ ñw ane̩ ne̩ odu oñ e̩ne̩ du ma te̩ me̩ru ekeji gbogbo ñw o̩jo̩ n.
Taku Mose̩s fʼo̩wo̩-wñ nadala nʼoj ohimini le̩; oñ Jihofa je̩ ñw afu olodudu ki ju nana gbogbo ñw o̩jo̩ kʼi kʼohimini e̩che̩ dabi, i la je̩ ñw ohimini le̩ ki mud ane̩ e̩gbe̩, omi-wñ mukpe̩ rʼeji.
Tak amo̩ma Israe̩l lʼane̩ e̩gbe̩ alumeji ohimini, omi le̩ la chʼo̩do̩ dago o̩wo̩ awo̩to̩ kpai o̩wo̩ awohi-ma.
Tak abo Ijipti rano ma, oñ ma tʼuma ubi gbogbo nyʼalumeji ohimini, ananya Fero chaka kpai o̩ko̩ ogu-wñ kpai amanʼanya-wñ.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba ide inajo̩, Jihofa dʼef una ki dago waala kpai e-akpa le̩ ago abo Ijipti, oñ i fʼabogu Ijipti le̩ dutu.
I la fʼo̩da o̩ko̩ ogu-ma chi rinyo̩, tak ule̩ ele̩-ma mud akanya ñwu ma; oñ abo Ijipti kakini, A ki ra bʼeju abo Israe̩l te̩; todu Jihofa akʼogu bʼabo Ijipti todu ma.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Fʼo̩wo̩ nadala nʼoj ohimini, todu kʼomi-wñ ki dabi wa abʼabo Ijipti kpai o̩ko̩ogu o̩ko̩ogu-ma kpai amanʼanya-mama.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s fʼo̩wo̩-wñ nadala nʼoj ohimini le̩, tak e̩gba kʼo̩jo̩ muñwa ohimini le̩ mu dabi tʼe̩gu-wñ; abo Ijipti la che ku ma ra bʼo̩ te̩, oñ Jihofa fʼabo Ijipti gbanyo̩ rʼalumeji ohimini le̩.
Tak omi le̩ mudabi, i bʼoji o̩ko̩ogu o̩ko̩ogu-ma kpai amanʼanya-ma kpai abogu Fero chaka ku ma rʼuma ubi tʼef ohimini le̩ ma; i chaka chʼokate-ma bo̩ n.
Ama amo̩ma Israe̩l lule̩ ane̩ e̩gbe̩ legu ohimini le̩ du, omi la mud o̩do̩ dago ñwu ma o̩wo̩ awo̩to̩ kpai o̩wo̩ awohi-ma.
Abe̩le̩ Jihofa fʼabo Israe̩l jadu kwef o̩wo̩ abo Ijipti o̩jo̩ le̩; oñ abo Israe̩l fʼoku abo Ijipti li abu ma de̩le̩gba jʼoj e̩lanyi o̩la ohimini le̩.
Oñ abo Israe̩l li o̩wo̩ Jihofa inaina kʼi lewa bʼabo Ijipti ma le̩, tak amone̩ le̩ kwo railo Jihofa; taku ma dʼo̩la Jihofa kpai o̩la Mose̩s, adu-wñ, rʼochochi.
Eli Mose̩s
Taku Mose̩s kpai amo̩ma Israe̩l kʼeli-i do̩ Jihofa, ma kakini,
Nakeli do̩ Jihofa, todu edu i du ma;
i mʼanya kpai e̩ne̩ kʼi tanʼo ko ro̩ nyʼef ohimini.
Jihofa che ukpahiu-mi kpai eli-mi,
i laño̩ mud ujadu-mi me;
O̩jo̩-mi de̩, oñ nañwulo̩-wñ,
O̩jo̩ e-ata-mi i che, oñ nahi u ne tʼatate̩.
Jihofa chʼagbiti ogu;
Jihofa, oñ odu-wñ ko̩.
O̩ko̩ ogu Fero kpai abogu-wñ i muko rikpolo jʼef ohimini;
amagboji ogu kʼi chi ma ji ef Ohimini Ekpikpa.
Unefu le̩ bʼuma ma;
ma ji tʼef unefu le̩ dab okuta.
O Jihofa, o̩wo̩ awo̩to̩-we̩ che̩nʼojima ef ukpahiu-wñ,
O Jihofa, o̩wo̩-we̩ awo̩to̩ agʼe̩nebi ye̩ge̩ye̩ge̩ me̩.
Ef unana e̩gahi-we̩, e̩ la ko abo ku ma kwane̩ tʼuwe̩ o̩la ro̩ jamʼane̩;
uwe̩ kpe̩ e̩do̩fulu-we̩ dufu, i la fʼuma lie̩ dabe̩ne̩ kʼo̩kakpunu e̩gbe̩.
Iñmo̩ kʼe̩ bu oñ omiofo kwane̩ dago go̩mu go̩mu,
uwobi omi le̩ mud ugbudu dago;
unefu le̩ ma te̩ e̩do̩ ohimini le̩.
E̩nebi le̩ kakini, Narano ma, namu ma,
nakpe̩ e̩wñ kʼogu je̩, e̩wñ kʼi dʼumi e̩do̩ le̩ nane̩ ki bʼumi jo̩. Nawo̩ o̩kwo̩chageli-mi, o̩wo̩-mi akpa ma bie̩.
Uwe̩ je̩ ñw afu-we̩ ju, oñ ohimini lewa bʼuma oji ma;
ma lawo̩nye̩ dab o̩de̩le̩ma ef omi ki nʼukpahiu le̩.
E̩ne̩ dʼef amo̩jo̩ kʼi dab uwe̩, O Jihofa?
E̩ne̩ dab uwe̩, kʼe̩fo̩ kʼe̩ fo̩ chʼojima-we̩?
Kʼuñwulo̩-wñ abailo, kʼi ache e̩wñ awuwu?
Uwe̩ fʼo̩wo̩-we̩ awo̩to̩ nadala,
oñ ane̩ ile̩ mʼuma ko mi.
Ef ufe̩de̩nyo̩-we̩ oñ e̩ nʼamone̩ kʼe̩ gbatane̩ le̩ le̩,
uwe̩ nʼukpahiu-we̩ ko ma le o̩na o̩na tʼugbo ugugu-we̩ kiafo̩.
Amone̩ ojoji ojoji gbo̩ me̩, o̩la-ma naga;
abo ku ma dodo Filistia jʼarʼefu nyʼukpo.
Tak ugoju mʼamidachi Ido̩m da dago;
o̩la amagbiti e-Moab chane̩ ega;
abo ku ma dodo Kenan du muyo̩ rinyo̩.
Okpo kpai ailo lewa bʼuma ma;
lʼugbo unana ugbo̩lo̩ o̩wo̩-we̩ ma chemane̩ jo̩ dab okuta, gbogbo tak amone̩-we̩ lale gudu, O Jihofa,
gbogbo tak amone̩ kʼe̩ la ñw o̩la-we̩ lale.
Uwe̩ la akʼuma wa kʼe̩ ko ma gbe̩ oj uwo ki chʼe̩wñ ogu kʼe̩ je̩ le̩,
owñ chʼuña kʼe̩ che ñw o̩la-we̩ kʼe̩ dodo efu-wñ le̩, Jihofa,
owñ chʼuña kiafo̩ kʼo̩wo̩-we̩ fu lonyane̩ le̩, O Ondu.
Jihofa ajʼonu tʼogbegbele̩ nyile̩wa.
Todu e̩gba kʼamanya Fero kpai o̩ko̩ogu o̩ko̩ogu-wñ kpai amanʼanya-wñ nyʼef ohimini le̩, Jihofa mʼomi ohimini du dabiwa abʼuma oji ma; abo Israe̩l muda lule̩ ane̩ e̩gbe̩ alumeji ohimini le̩.
Eli Miriam
Taku Miriam o̩maye Aro̩n, kʼi chʼakache̩ onobule̩, mʼeicha du nʼo̩wo̩; oñ abobule̩ du kwodufu tʼo̩ ubi kpai eicha kpai ido eta.
Taku Miriam dohi ñw ma kakini: Me̩ keli do̩ Jihofa, todu edu i du ma i mʼanya kpai e̩ne̩ kʼi tanʼo ko ro̩ nyʼef ohimini.
Taku Mose̩s nʼabo Israe̩l kwʼo̩la Ohimini Ekpikpa alo, oñ ma nyʼaje̩tachi Shur; ma la fʼule̩ o̩jo̩ me̩ta le aje̩tachi o̩mo̩, ma la li omiofo n.
Ma nyi Mara kpai Elim
