Tak e̩gba ku ma lewa Mara, ma neke ñmo̩ omi Mara le̩ n, todu elukoko kʼi lukoko; todu ku ma do̩ odu-wñ ko̩ Mara le̩ de̩.
Tak amone̩ le̩ kwokeñmini nyu Mose̩s o̩la, ma kakini, E̩wñ a ñmo̩?
Tak i raku do̩ Jihofa; oñ Jihofa dʼoliʼka ñʼo̩, tak i mʼe-le̩ du ro̩ tef omi le̩, oñ omi le̩ chane̩ erinyo̩.
O̩mo̩ i fʼo̩me̩ʼka hi ñwu ma, i la mʼoji ajo̩ʼka dute̩ ñwu ma, i laño̩ jʼuma ma o̩mo̩ ge̩,
i kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼe̩ agbʼomu Jihofa O̩jo̩-we̩ ogbolo, kʼe̩ la ache e̩wñ kʼi tʼo̩kpakpa eju-wñ, kʼe̩ nʼeti rʼuko̩ kʼi te̩, kʼe̩ la ade o̩me̩ kʼi hi du, mak u nadʼo̩ga du kʼu du nʼabo Ijipti oji nʼuwe̩ n; todu omi che Jihofa kʼi achʼo̩ga-we̩ kpa.
Taku ma lewa Elim, ugbo kʼe̩bi omi me̩gweji kpai oli ki dab e̩kpe̩ e̩te̩gwa jo̩; oñ ma ru ru jo̩ alu omi o̩mo̩.
Abo Israe̩l keñmini ef aje̩tachi
Taku ma kʼe̩re̩-ma nyʼule̩ kwo Elim, oñ o̩gbadu amo̩ma Israe̩l le̩ chaka lewa aje̩tachi Sin, e-ki dʼagbagba Elim kpai Sainai, o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩gwe̩lu ochu ekeji ku ma kwo bʼane̩ Ijipti te̩.
Tak o̩gbo̩ o̩gbadu amo̩ma Israe̩l le̩ du kwokeñmini nyu Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n o̩la aje̩tachi o̩mo̩,
ma la ka ñwu ma kakini, Awa ma leku o̩wo̩ Jihofa ane̩ Ijipti e̩gba kʼa gugu kpenyʼucha e̩la kʼa la jʼuje̩wñ kʼefu le̩ i ma me̩; todu ame̩ ko wa dufu wʼef aje̩tachi-i, kʼebi ki kpa o̩gbo̩ abo ujeju-i du rinyo̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Go, omi akʼuje̩wñ kwʼefojale wa dab omi ojale ñwu me̩; tak amone̩-i anyʼo̩lo̩fe̩ ku ma fʼukpe̩ o̩jo̩ʼka yajo̩ o̩jo̩ du, kʼu najʼuma ma, abe̩ku ma jʼalule̩ tikpa uko̩-o̩la-mi, abe̩ku ma aje̩ n.
Oñ o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩fa-wñ ma la añwʼuje̩wñ ku ma ko wʼunyi le̩ che, e-o̩jo̩ le̩ achʼukpe̩ o̩jo̩ meji.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n ka ñw abo Israe̩l du kakini, Ane̩-i ame̩ ama ka ku Jihofa chʼe̩ne̩ kʼi ko me̩ kwʼane̩ Ijipti dufu,
odudu-wñ me̩ la ali ojima Jihofa, todabu kʼi gbo̩ eñmini ku me̩ ka nyu Jihofa o̩la. Todu e̩ne̩ awa che taa, ku me̩ kʼeñmini nyʼuwa o̩la?
Taku Mose̩s kakini, E̩gba ku Jihofa akʼe̩la ñwu me̩ je̩ e̩gba ane̩, kʼi laño̩ kʼuje̩wñ ñwu me̩ kʼefu-me̩ ki ko̩ odudu, todu Jihofa gbo̩ eñmini-me̩ ku me̩ ka nyʼowñ o̩la me̩— e̩ne̩ awa che? Eñmini-me̩-i i chʼawa me̩ ka nyu n, chai Jihofa.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñwu Aro̩n kakini, E̩ ka ñw o̩gbadu amo̩ma Israe̩l chaka kakini, Me̩ te̩me̩ru o̩gba Jihofa-i, todu i fʼeñmini-me̩ gbo̩ me̩.
Oñ i lewatu abu kʼAro̩n nako̩la ñw o̩gbo̩ o̩gbadu amo̩ma Israe̩l du le̩, ama mʼeju korʼo̩wo̩ aje̩tachi, me̩ la go, ojima Jihofa kwotejugede ef akpa le̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
Omi gbo̩ eñmini amo̩ma Israe̩l me̩; e̩ naka ñwu ma kakini, E̩gba kʼo̩jo̩ adu bulu-bulu ame̩ aje̩ e̩la, efu-me̩ la ako̩ ñw uje̩wñ odudu, tak ame̩ ama ka kʼomi che Jihofa, O̩jo̩-me̩.
Amagbailo kpai mana lewa
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba ane̩ amagbailo muwu wa fʼuru le̩ gwebo; odudu-wñ eli la chʼo̩tuu bʼane̩ ma lʼuru le̩ daka.
Tak e̩gba kʼeli le̩ gbe̩ rʼane̩, me̩ go, e̩wñ fe̩fe̩le̩ bʼeju aje̩tachi le̩ ma, i dab eli efufu kʼi chi jʼane̩pe̩te̩ re re re.
Oñ e̩gba kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l fʼu li, ma ka ñw o̩la-ma kakini, E̩wñ de̩? Todu ma mʼe̩wñ kʼi che n. Taku Mose̩s ka ñwu ma kakini, Uje̩wñ ku Jihofa ko ñwu me̩ ku me̩ je̩ de̩.
Uko̩-wñ ku Jihofa te̩ de̩: E̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩-me̩ ki fʼu yajo̩ alu kʼi neke je̩; e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ kʼi du e̩ñwa omaʼka omaʼka alu kʼuwewe one̩-wñ de̩, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ki ko todu abo unyabo e-wñ.
Tak amo̩ma Israe̩l fʼabe̩le̩ che; ma fʼu rejo̩, e-abo iche̩ka chenana, e-iche̩ka la de̩ ke̩e̩.
Ama e̩gba ku ma ne̩ oma le̩ fʼu ñwa, e̩ne̩ ki gbajo̩ nana la nʼe̩bo̩ n, e̩ne̩ ki la gbajo̩ re, i nyarʼowñ n; e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩-ma fʼu rejo̩ alu kʼi neke je̩.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñwu ma kakini, E-e̩ne̩ du ki bo̩ nyʼodudu n.
Ma muda nyi Mose̩s eti n; iche̩ka efu-ma je̩ ñw u bo̩ nyʼodudu, oñ i kwochʼide̩, i chane̩ elu; taku Mose̩s we̩do̩ bʼuma.
Odudu o̩jo̩ du, o̩jo̩ du, ma la rejo̩, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ re alu kʼi neke je̩; ama e̩gba kʼolu kpa nyane̩ i muyo̩.
Oñ i lewatu o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩fa-wñ ma fʼuje̩wñ o̩jo̩ meji rejo̩, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ne̩ oma meji; tak e̩gba kʼamidachi o̩gbadu le̩ chaka lewa ka ñwu Mose̩s,
i ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩wñ ki Jihofa ka le̩ de̩, kakini, O̩na chʼuñmi, uñmi kiafo̩ todu Jihofa i che; e̩wñ ku me̩ neku ede̩ me̩ de̩, me̩ neku hi, me̩ hi; e̩wñ du ki la kwʼume̩bo̩, me̩ denyʼodudu.
Abe̩-le̩ ma mʼu du gugu nyʼodudu, alu ku Mose̩s ka ñwu ma; i la lu n, i la nʼide̩ n.
Taku Mose̩s kakini, Me̩ fʼe-le je̩ eñini, todu eñini chʼo̩jo̩ uñmi ñwu Jihofa; me̩ ñʼaliʼi oko eñini ge̩ n.
O̩jo̩ me̩fa me̩ rejo̩; ama o̩jo̩ e̩kebie, kʼi che o̩jo̩ uñmi, e-du ado̩mo̩ n.
Oñ i lewatu, o̩jo̩ e̩kebie le̩, amone̩ iche̩ka dufu ku ma rejo̩, ma la li e-du n.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Gbogbo nyʼe̩gba oñ ame̩ ako̩ ede uko̩ kʼu te̩ kpai uko̩-o̩la-mi kade taa?
Go! Jihofa mʼo̩jo̩ uñmi du ñwu me̩ me̩, todule̩ oñ i akʼuje̩wñ o̩jo̩ meji ñwu me̩ o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩fa; e̩ne̩ du efu-me̩ ki nagugu e̩gu-wñ, e̩ne̩ du ki kwʼe̩gu-wñ o̩jo̩ e̩kebie n.
Abe̩le̩ amone̩ le̩ ñmi o̩jo̩ e̩kebie.
Oñ abo unyi Israe̩l fʼodu e-le̩ do̩ ko̩ mana; i la dab e̩yo̩ ko̩rianda, i chʼefufu, e̩ du tʼalu i arinyo̩ dab akala ku ma nʼiño̩ che.
Taku Mose̩s kakini, E̩wñ ku Jihofa ñwa ñw a de̩ kakini, Me̩ ki dʼo̩ma-wñ oka tʼade kʼi mud e̩wñ o̩hio̩gu-me̩ gbogbo alo, kʼama ki li uje̩wñ kʼu du ñwu me̩ je̩ aje̩tachi e̩gba kʼu ko me̩ kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti wa le̩.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw Aro̩n kakini, Mʼucha du kʼe̩ du oma manaʼka tʼefu-wñ, kʼe̩ mʼu du ne e̩gba Jihofa, ku me̩ de kʼi mud e̩wñ o̩hio̩gu-me̩ gbogbo alo.
Alu ku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s, alu le̩ Aro̩n mʼu du ne o̩gba E̩wñ Ibenu le̩, ku ma fʼu de.
Amo̩ma Israe̩l la je̩ mana le̩ o̩do̩ o̩gbo̩ meji, gbogbo taku ma lewa ane̩ ugbo kʼone̩ adodo, ma je̩ mana le̩ gbogbo taku ma lewa alu o̩me̩ ane̩ Kenan. 36(Oma la chʼukpe̩gwa e̩fa.
Mose̩s gwo okuta oñ omi dufu wa
Tak o̩gbadu amo̩ma Israe̩l le̩ du kad ule̩-ma ubi ale pe̩ pe̩ akwʼaje̩tachi Sin, alu ku Jihofa dʼalu ñwu ma, oñ ma ru jo̩ Refidim; omiofo la dʼo̩mo̩ kʼamone̩ añmo̩ n.
Todule̩ amone̩ le̩ kobo̩ Mose̩s, oñ ma kakini, Dʼomi ñw a ñmo̩. Taku Mose̩s ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩wñ chi ku me̩ kobʼumi? E̩wñ chi ku me̩ chajama Jihofa abe̩-i?
Ama alugbe̩ nakpa amone̩ o̩mo̩ waa, oñ amone̩ le̩ kʼeñmini nyu Mose̩s o̩la, ma kakini, E̩wñ chi kʼe̩ ko wa kwʼIjipti wa kʼe̩ nʼalugbe̩ akpa wa kpai amo̩ma-wa kpai ame̩wñ ukpa-wa-i?
Taku Mose̩s raku do̩ Jihofa, kakini, Ab u nache kpai amone̩-i ta? I bo̩ pe̩ ku ma akʼokuta ro̩ do̩ mi.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Lale tʼo̩gba amone̩ le̩ kʼe̩ mʼabogijo Israe̩l iche̩ka ko le bʼuwe̩; o̩kpa-we̩ e-kʼe̩ du gwo Naye̩l kʼi nʼo̩wo̩-we̩, kʼe̩ lo.
Go, omi adago o̩gba-we̩ oj okuta o̩mu Ho̩re̩b o̩mo̩; tak uwe̩ ki gwo okuta le̩, oñ omiofo akwʼefu-wñ dufu kʼamone̩-i ki ñmo̩. Taku Mose̩s fʼabe̩le̩ che eju abogijo Israe̩l.
Oñ i do̩ odu ugbo kide̩ ko̩ Masa kpai Me̩riba, tod e̩kobo̩ kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l kobʼo̩ kpai todabu ku ma chʼajama Jihofa, owñ chʼe-ku ma kakini, Jihofa dʼefu-wa? abe̩k i dʼefu-wa n?
Amale̩k kobʼuma Refidim
Tak Amale̩k lewa kʼogu bo̩ Israe̩l Refidim.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñwu Jo̩shua kakini, Fʼaboke̩le̩ chi ñw a kʼe̩ dufu nyʼajogu kpai Amale̩k; nadago oj uwo-i o̩na, o̩kpa O̩jo̩ adʼef o̩wo̩-mi.
Abe̩le̩ Jo̩shua che alu ku Mose̩s ka ñw u, oñ i jogu kpai Amale̩k; Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n kpai He̩r la nyʼoj uwo le̩.
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba du ku Mose̩s dʼo̩wo̩-wñ dago ukpahiu Israe̩l tule, e̩gba du kʼi tʼo̩wo̩-wñ no̩ wane̩, ukpahiu Amale̩k tule.
Ama o̩wo̩ Mose̩s chane̩ egbogu; oñ ma mʼokuta du, ma mʼu du tʼofe-wñ, oñ i gugu oji-wñ, tak Aro̩n kpai He̩r kʼo̩wo̩-wñ e̩che̩ dago, e̩ne̩ʼka dʼo̩wo̩ʼka, e̩nekeji la dʼo̩wo̩ ekeji; abe̩le̩ o̩wo̩-wñ lodago gbogbo tak olu tunyʼane̩.
Oñ Joshua nʼalu o̩kwo̩chageli fʼAmale̩k kpai abo-wñ gwo dajane̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Fʼe-i ko̩ nyʼef ubuku ki chʼe̩wñ urewa, kʼe̩ ka ño̩ ka nyu Jo̩shua eti ka kʼomi akpa urewa Amale̩k lu bʼo̩gane̩ efojale te̩ hioko.
Taku Mose̩s fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ kpa, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Jihofa chʼAgaliga-mi,
i kakini, Abu kʼo̩wo̩ no ede Jihofa! Jihofa ajʼogu kpai Amale̩k gbogbo nyʼo̩gba o̩gba-wñ.
Je̩tro wa fejudo Mose̩s
Oñ Je̩tro, atama Midian, ana Mose̩s le̩, gbʼinabali e̩wñ du kʼO̩jo̩ che ñwu Mose̩s, kpai Israe̩l, abo-wñ le̩, owñ chʼalu ku Jihofa mʼabo Israe̩l ko kwʼIjipti dufu.
Taku Je̩tro, ana Mose̩s le̩, mu Zipo̩ra, o̩ya Mose̩s kʼi je̩ ñw u mudabi tʼunyi, du,
kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ meji; e-kʼoduʼka ko̩ Ge̩rsho̩m; (todu i kakini, Ilowa omi te̩tache oj ane̩ ononojo),
odu ekeji la ko E̩lieza; (todu O̩jo̩ e-ata-mi chʼe̩ne̩ ki bʼumi che, i la mʼumi gba bʼo̩kwo̩chageli Fero te̩).
Taku Je̩tro, ana Mose̩s le̩, kpai amo̩ma-wñ kpai o̩ya-wñ lewʼugbo Mose̩s aje̩tachi ugbo kʼi ru e̩re̩ uwo O̩jo̩.
Oñ e̩ne̩ʼka ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Go, Je̩tro, ana-we̩, awʼugbo-we̩-i, kpʼo̩ya-we̩ kpai amo̩ma-wñ meji manyʼowñ.
Taku Mose̩s ledufu aledo ana-wñ, i dojikane̩, oñ i dʼalu-wñ kʼo̩ alu; ma la tʼo̩la-ma ene o̩lafia-ma, oñ ma le tʼef unyabo.
Taku Mose̩s mʼe̩wñ du ki Jihofa che Fero kpai abo Ijipti todu Israe̩l du ka ñw ana-wñ, kpai ihianyi du ki ke̩re̩bʼuma ej o̩na le̩, kpai alu ku Jihofa mʼuma gba.
Oñ Je̩tro kwoyo̩ todu e̩nyo̩ du ku Jihofa che ñw Israe̩l, owñ chʼabu kʼi mʼuma gba kwef o̩wo̩ abo Ijipti.
Taku Je̩tro kakini, Jihofa ki nʼele, owñ kʼi gbʼuwe̩ kwef o̩wo̩ abo Ijipti, kpai kwef o̩wo̩ Fero le̩; owñ kʼi mʼamone̩-i gba kwef o̩wo̩ abo Ijipti.
Ifai tak u chema ka ku Jihofa tʼamo̩jo̩ du le; ochochi, efu e̩wñ ku ma du buba ñwu ma le̩ owñ tʼuma le.
Taku Je̩tro, ana Mose̩s le̩, mʼe̩wñ e̩gujo kpai e̩wñ iche̩bo̩ kibo̩ ko wa ñw O̩jo̩; oñ Aro̩n kpai abogijo Israe̩l chaka lewa ku ma je̩ uje̩wñ kpai ana Mose̩s o̩gba O̩jo̩.
Je̩tro kʼo̩la ibe ñwu Mose̩s
Oñ i lewatu o̩jo̩ñwa-wñ, Mose̩s la gugu kʼi kʼajo̩ amone̩ le̩, oñ amone̩ le̩ donyu Mose̩s akwo odudu gbogbo nyʼane̩.
Tak e̩gba kʼana Mose̩s li e̩wñ kʼi ache ñw amone̩ le̩ du, i kakini, E̩wñ chʼe-kʼuwe̩ ache ñw amone̩-i? E̩wñ chi kʼuwe̩ kate gugu kʼamone̩ le̩ chaka donyʼuwe̩ akwʼodudu gbogbo nyʼane̩?
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw ana-wñ kakini, Todabu kʼamone̩-i awʼugbo-mi ku ma tene e̩wñ kʼO̩jo̩ ka;
e̩gba kʼiñwa chi ñwu ma, ma wʼugbo-mi, tak u nakʼajo̩ one̩ kpai ekeji-wñ oñ naje̩ ñwu ma ma e̩wñ uhio̩me̩ O̩jo̩ kpai uko̩-o̩la-wñ.
Tak ana Mose̩s ka ñw u kakini, E̩wñ kʼuwe̩ ache-i nyo̩ n.
Uwe̩ kpai amone̩ ku ma jʼugbo-we̩ abo che̩che̩le̩che̩ fai, todu e̩wñ-i woji tʼuwe̩ le; uwe̩ kate neke che n.
E̩ nagbo̩ omu-mi ta, nako̩ we̩ ali-mi, O̩jo̩ ki la dʼugbo we̩! uwe̩ ki koji amone̩ ugbo O̩jo̩, kʼe̩ kʼo̩la-ma wʼugbo O̩jo̩;
uwe̩ ki la ko̩ ma e̩wñ uhio̩me̩-wñ kpai uko̩-o̩la-wñ, kʼe̩ la je̩ ñwu ma mʼo̩na ku ma ale tila, kpai e̩wñ ki dukpe̩ ku ma che.
Uwe̩ ki ño̩ tu amone̩ le̩ kʼe̩ chi aboke̩le̩ ku ma bʼe̩wñ-i jo̩, kʼama la bʼe̩gahi O̩jo̩, aboke̩le̩ ochochi, kʼe̩wñ e̩gbaje̩ chʼe̩wñ ulaka-ma; e̩ ki ko ma nyʼabo abe̩i o̩wo̩, kʼama ki chʼamagboji one̩ icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩, kpai amagboji ogu me̩lu, ogume̩lu, kpai amagboji one̩ ooje ooje, kpai amagboji one̩ me̩gwa e̩gwa.
E̩ ki je̩ ñwu ma kajo̩ amone̩-i iko du; O̩la elile du, ma ki ko wʼugbo-we̩, ama onugo ki muda kpʼoji ajo̩ re re du; abe̩le̩ tak i ame̩ ñw e̩, oñ ama abʼuwe̩ nʼadu-wñ.
Iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ ache abe̩le̩, kʼO̩jo̩ la ñwa ñw e̩ abe̩le̩, e̩gba le̩ uwe̩ ne̩kʼadago, oñ amone̩-i du alo tʼuña e-ma kpai ure̩do̩.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s gbʼomu ana-wñ gbo̩, oñ i fʼe̩wñ kʼi ka le̩ du che.
Mose̩s fʼaboke̩le̩ ku ma bʼe̩wñ-i jo̩ chi kwef abo Israe̩l chaka, i la mʼuma ko chʼoji amone̩ le̩, amagboji one̩ icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ kpai amagboji one̩ ogume̩lu ogume̩lu kpai amagboji one̩ ooje ooje, kpai amagboji one̩ me̩gwa e̩gwa.
Tak ama kʼajo̩ amone̩ le̩ e̩gba du; ajo̩ ki gbiti ma ko wʼugbo Mose̩s, ama o̩la re re du ama onugo kpʼoji-wñ.
Taku Mose̩s je̩ ñw ana-wñ kwʼo̩mo̩ le; oñ i le tʼane̩ e-wñ.
Abo Israe̩l lewa ere uwo Sainai; o̩la emu tod o̩lo̩da
Ochu e̩ke̩ta kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l kwʼoj ane̩ Ijipti dufu, o̩jo̩ le̩ gbage̩de̩ ma lewa aje̩tachi Sainai.
Oñ abu ku ma kwo Refidim ku ma lewa aje̩tachi Sainai, ma ru ru jʼaje̩tachi le̩; abo Israe̩l la rujo̩ o̩gba uwo o̩mo̩.
Taku Mose̩s mute̩gu nyʼugbo O̩jo̩, oñ Jihofa kʼi dʼoj uwo le̩ nʼomudala dʼo̩, i kakini, Abu kʼuwe̩ aka ñw abunyi Jeko̩b de̩, kʼe̩ laño̩ ka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l, kakini,
Ame̩ fʼe̩wñ kʼomi che abo Ijipti li me̩, kpai alu kʼomi ne̩ me̩ oj ika amo̩re̩, kʼu la ko me̩ wʼugbo-mi-i.
Todule̩, ifai, iche̩wñ ku me̩ agbʼomu-mi gbo̩ ochochi, ku me̩ la ade alo-mi, ame̩ achʼabo-mi kʼu ne̩ kwef amone̩ du; todu ane̩ ile̩ du chʼe-mi,
me̩ la achʼamatama ku me̩ chʼabo ojane̩ʼka kpai uche̩ichi amone̩ kiafo̩ ñwu mi. O̩la kʼuwe̩ aka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l la de̩.
Taku Mose̩s lewa fʼabogijo amone̩ le̩ do̩ jeju, oñ i fʼo̩la du ku Jihofa ñwa ñw u-i kajane̩ ñwu ma.
Tak amone̩ le̩ du dohi alukate kakini, E̩wñ du ku Jihofa ka le̩, awa ache. Taku Mose̩s mʼohi o̩la kʼamone̩ ka le̩ du wa ñwu Jihofa.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini. Go, nawʼugbo-we̩ ef akpa ki chubi te̩ fioo, todu kʼamone̩ le̩ ki gbo̩ e̩gba kʼu nako̩la ñw e̩, ku ma ki ño̩ dʼo̩la-we̩ rʼochochi ogbegbele̩.
Taku Mose̩s mʼo̩la amone̩ le̩ du ka ñwu Jihofa.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Nyʼugbo amone̩ le̩ kʼe̩ fʼuma o̩la gworinyo̩ eñini kpai o̩na ku ma fo̩, kʼe̩ la je̩ ñwu ma fʼe̩wñ o̩la-ma gwe̩,
ku me̩ fʼo̩la-me̩ mu tane̩ nede o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta-wñ; todu o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta le̩ Jihofa agwo̩ru wa oj uwo Sainai eju amone̩ le̩ du.
Uwe̩ ki la bʼo̩gba nyʼu daka todu amone̩ le̩, kakini, Me̩ nafʼo̩la-me̩ de ku me̩ we enyʼe̩re̩ uwo le̩, me̩ ki dʼo̩wo̩ himʼo̩ n; e̩ne̩ du ki la dʼo̩wo̩ kado uwo le̩ ekpa ma akpa.
O̩wo̩ du akadʼo n, chai okuta ma aro̩ ñw u, cho̩kpo̩ni ma atʼo̩fa ñw u; dagba i chʼe̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ dagba i chʼone̩, i adeju n. E̩gba ku ma fʼopo fa taa, ama ki wʼe̩re̩ uwo le̩.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s gwo̩ru kwo oj uwo le̩ tane̩ nyʼugbo amone̩, oñ i fʼamone̩ le̩ o̩la gworinyo̩ ku ma fo̩; ma la fʼe̩wñ o̩la-ma gwe̩.
Tak i ka ñw amone̩ le̩ kakini, Me̩ fʼo̩la-me̩ mu tane̩ nede o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta; me̩ ki te̩ me̩rʼonobule̩ n.
Oñ i lewatu odudu o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩ta-wñ, kʼakpabana ako̩la, o̩mamanya nada, akpa ki chubi te̩ fioo la bʼoji uwo le̩ ma, tak opo chane̩ eko̩la nana tabale, oñ o̩la amone̩ du ku ma jʼef uru le̩ kwoga.
Taku Mose̩s ko amone̩ le̩ kwef uru dufu ku ma ledʼO̩jo̩; oñ ma kwodago e̩re̩ uwo le̩.
Uwo Sainai le̩ chaka la kpʼodudu, todabu ku Jihofa gwo̩ru wa oji-wñ ef una; oñ odudu-wñ nate̩gu tʼate̩ dabe̩ne̩ kʼodudu aido, o̩chaka uwo le̩ la naga liga liga.
Tak abu kʼuko̩la opo anana nana nyo̩gba, Mose̩s fʼo̩la ka; O̩jo̩ la nʼomu akpabana dohi ñw u.
Abe̩le̩ Jihofa gwo̩ru wa uwo Sainai, tʼoji uwo le̩; taku Jihofa fu Mose̩s do̩ wa oj uwo le̩; Mose̩s la mute̩gu nyʼo̩mo̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Mugwo̩ru tane̩ kʼe̩ juka ñw amone̩ le̩, tode̩gba ku ma gulo̩ wʼugbo Jihofa ku ma gigo, kʼuwewe-ma alenyo̩.
E̩ ki laño̩ je̩ ñw amatama ku ma te̩me̩ru Jihofa, ku ma fʼo̩la-ma gworinyo̩ ku ma fo̩, tode̩gba ku Jihofa gwo̩ko̩ tʼuma o̩la.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñwu Jihofa kakini, Amone̩ le̩ neke wʼugbo uwo Sainai-i n; todu uwe̩ onugo ñwa ñw a kakini, Me̩ ki bʼo̩gba nyʼuwo-i daka ku me̩ che ki fo̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñw u kakini, Gwo̩ru alo, tak uwe̩ kpʼAro̩n ki kpe̩re̩ te̩gu wa, e̩ ki muda je̩ ñw amatama kpai amone̩ gulo̩ wʼugbo Jihofa n, tode̩gba kʼi a gwo̩ko̩ tʼuma o̩la.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s mugwo̩ru nyʼugbo amone̩ le̩ oñ i ka ñwu ma.
O̩la me̩gwa le̩
Tak O̩jo̩ fʼo̩la-i du ka kakini,
Omi che Jihofa O̩jo̩-we̩, kʼi dʼuwe̩ kwʼane̩ Ijipti wa, kwef unyi adu le̩ dufu.
E̩ ki ne̩ amo̩jo̩ omune̩ eju-mi n.
E̩ ki gbe̩ ojibo ñw o̩la-we̩ n, abe̩k e̩wñ du ki biu e̩wñ ki dʼefojale ate̩ n, abe̩k e̩wñ ki dʼef ile̩ o̩gane̩-i n, abe̩k e-ki dʼef omi o̩gane̩ ile̩ n;
e̩ ki dojikane̩ ñwu ma n, e̩ ki re̩ ma n; todu omi Jihofa, O̩jo̩-we̩, O̩jo̩ ajogu u che, nadʼudu kʼamata-ma fe̩ nʼamo̩ma abo ku ma chʼulaka-mi oji gbogbo tʼo̩gba e̩ke̩ta kpai e̩ke̩le̩,
u muda adʼufe̩de̩nyo̩ ña abo icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ ku ma fe̩do̩ mi, ku ma la fʼuko̩ kʼu te̩ de.
E̩ ki dʼodu Jihofa, O̩jo̩-we̩, tʼalu adʼo̩ ofofo n; todu Jihofa adale ñw e̩ne̩ ki dʼodu-wñ tʼalu adʼo̩ ofofo n.
E̩ nadibekado o̩jo̩ uñmi kʼe̩ fʼu de kʼi fo̩.
O̩jo̩ me̩fa e̩ nachʼe̩wñ-we̩ kʼe̩ la fʼuko̩lo̩-we̩ du che;
o̩jo̩ e̩kebie-wñ muda chʼo̩jo̩ uñmi ñwu Jihofa O̩jo̩-we̩; e̩ ki chʼuko̩lo̩ du o̩jo̩ le̩ n, tʼuwe̩, tʼo̩ma-we̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, tʼo̩ma-we̩ onobule̩, tʼadu-we̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, tʼadu-we̩ onobule̩, tʼame̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩-we̩, tʼilowa kʼi dʼejefu alaku-we̩;
todu o̩jo̩ me̩fa Jihofa che efojale kpai ane̩-ile̩, tʼohimini abadi kpai e̩wñ du ki jʼefu-wñ, tak i ñmi o̩jo̩ e̩kebie-wñ; todule̩ Jihofa de̩nyo̩ ñw o̩jo̩ uñmi, oñ i fʼu che kiafo̩.
E̩ ki bʼojima mʼata-we̩ kpai iye-we̩ kʼuwe̩ ki kwʼojolugbo oj ane̩ ki Jihofa, O̩jo̩-we̩, adu ñw e̩.
E̩ ki kpa one̩ n.
E̩ ki te̩ mʼo̩ya e̩ne̩ omune̩ n.
E̩ ki joji n.
E̩ ki gba ibenu olemi nyʼekeji-we̩ n.
Unyi ekeji-we̩ ki nyo̩ we̩ eju kʼe̩ ne̩ n; o̩ya ekeji-we̩ ki nyo̩ we̩ eju kʼe̩ ne̩ n, abe̩k adu-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ n, abe̩k adu-wñ onobule̩ n, abe̩k o̩kokuno̩-wñ n abe̩k o̩ke̩ke̩te̩-wñ n, abe̩k e̩wñ du kʼekeji-we̩ ne̩ n.
Oñ abu kʼibe amone̩ le̩ chaka tʼakpabana kpai o̩mamanya kpai omu o̩po kpai uwo ki akpodudu, o̩la-ma naga, oñ ma kwodago jʼo̩najiji,
oñ ma ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Uwe̩ ko̩la ñw a oñ awa agbo̩; O̩jo̩ ki muda ko̩la ñw a n, tode̩gba kʼa ku.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw amone̩ le̩ kakini, Me̩ ki railo n; todu O̩jo̩ wa kʼi jʼume̩ ma de̩, todu kʼe̩gahi-wñ ki mu me̩, ku me̩ we edure.
Tak amone̩ le̩ kwodago jʼo̩najiji, oñ Mose̩s te̩me̩ru ugbo e̩chubi gbe̩m ugbo kʼO̩jo̩ de̩ le̩.
E̩wñ o̩da ojoji ojoji
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Abu kʼuwe̩ aka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l le̩ de̩, kakini, Ame̩ onugo li abu kʼomi dʼefojale-i ako̩la ñwu me̩.
Ame̩ ki nʼajifa che amo̩jo̩ manyu mi n, me̩ ki la nʼo̩jamalia che amo̩jo̩ ñw o̩la-me̩ n.
Uwe̩ ki bo̩ ubo̩ ike̩te̩ ñwu mi, tak uwe̩ akʼe̩wñ e̩gujo-we̩ kpai e̩wñ ure̩do̩-we̩, owñ chʼame̩wño̩re̩-we̩ egini kpai amo̩kokuno̩-we̩ wa kpa oji-wñ; ugbo du kʼu naje̩ ma rewa odu-mi, nawʼugbowe̩ oñ nade̩nyo̩ ñw e̩.
I la chʼubo̩ okuta oñ e̩ ne ñwu mi, mak e̩ ki nʼokuta ku ma ñwo̩che ne n; todu iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ du e̩wñ uko̩lo̩-we̩ ki ale̩ kadʼo mak e̩ fʼu daji me̩.
E̩ ki la te̩gu agube tʼugbo ubo̩ iche̩bo̩-mi n, tode̩gba ku ma li ago ofo-we̩.
O̩da e̩wñ ojoji ojoji
Abʼe-i chʼoj ajo̩ kʼuwe̩ ako jo̩ ñwu ma, kakini,
E̩gba kʼuwe̩ fʼe̩ne̩ Hibru la kʼi chʼadu-we̩ mak o̩do̩ me̩fa i arʼe̩; tak o̩do̩ e̩kebie-wñ i atʼane̩ ofo pioo.
Iche̩wñ kʼi chʼowñ kate wa mak owñ kate alo; iche̩wñ kʼi ne̩ o̩ya wa mak o̩ya-wñ adufu kpai owñ.
I la che̩wñ kʼodu-wñ dʼo̩ya ñw u kʼi lafʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ abe̩k onobule̩ bi ñw u, mak o̩ya le̩ kpai amo̩ma-wñ ache e-odu-wñ, oñ e̩ne̩ le̩ kate alo.
I muda che̩wñ kʼadu le̩ ka ej o̩ja pee kakini, Nafe̩do̩ odu-mi kpai o̩ya-mi kpai amo̩ma-mi; natʼane̩ n,
tak odu-wñ adʼowñ wʼugbo O̩jo̩, i la adʼu wʼalugbo̩na abe̩k ugbo oli alo̩na; oñ odu-wñ anʼebije gu eti-wñ du; tak i arʼo̩ ogbegbele̩.
E̩gba kʼone̩ mʼo̩ma-wñ onobule̩ du ta kʼi chʼadu, i atane̩ alu kʼamadu e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ atane̩ n.
Iche̩wñ kʼi bie̩ne̩ eju odu-wñ kʼi le kʼi dʼu chʼo̩ya, e̩gbale̩ i aje̩ ñwu ma fʼu la tane̩; i nʼo̩da kʼi adʼu ta ñw abononojo n, abu kʼi fʼu gwo̩gwo̩ le̩.
I muda che̩wñ kʼi mʼowñ du kpʼo̩ma-wñ, i ache ñw u alu kʼoji ajo̩ ka ugbo amo̩ma onobule̩.
Iche̩wñ kʼi fʼo̩ya omune̩ ne̩ manyʼu, i nʼugbo kʼi abʼukpe̩ uje̩wñ kpʼukpo kpai ukpe̩ o̩ya wane̩ ñw u n.
I ma la che e̩wñ me̩ta-i ñw u n, mak onobule̩ le̩ atane̩ ofofo, i anʼo̩me̩ era n.
E̩ne̩ ki fʼe̩wñ nʼone̩ kʼi leku, ekpa ma akpa e̩ne̩ le̩.
Iche̩wñ kʼi ma kpala anede-wñ n, chai O̩jo̩ je̩ ñw u gbajiko; e̩gbale̩ nafʼugbo kʼi ara nyi date̩ ñw e̩.
I muda che̩wñ kʼone̩ gwejugede gwo̩ko̩ rʼone̩ o̩la kʼi fʼu kpa lef ugbeju, e̩ ki mʼu du bʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩-mi te̩, todu kʼi ku.
E̩ne̩ kʼi fʼe̩wñ gwʼata-wñ abe̩k iye-wñ, ekpa ma akpa e̩ne̩ le̩.
E̩ne̩ kʼi mʼoji one̩ ji, dagba i mʼu du ta, dagba ma fʼu li o̩wo̩-wñ, ekpa ma akpa e̩ne̩ le̩.
E̩ne̩ kʼi fʼata-wñ abe̩k iye-wñ bina, ekpa ma akpa e̩ne̩ le̩.
I la che̩wñ kʼone̩ meji jʼajiñwa, kʼoka mʼokuta du nʼekeji abe̩k ero̩kpo̩ ñw u, kʼe̩ne̩ le̩ ma ku n, kʼi muda dachi oj ate̩,
iche̩wñ kʼi ño̩ kwane̩ anʼo̩kpa lule̩, e̩gbale̩ e̩ne̩ kʼi gwʼone̩ mufu tane̩; chai o̩me̩ uko̩lo̩-wñ ki chi i ara ñw u, kʼi año̩ fejutʼo̩ kʼo̩la-wñ ki takpa jali.
I la che̩wñ kʼone̩ nʼo̩kpa gwo adu-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ abe̩k onobule̩, kʼi leku nyʼo̩wo̩, ma abʼudu ñw u chuu.
I muda che̩wñ kʼi ma ku n o̩jo̩ʼka abe̩k o̩jo̩ meji, ma abʼudu ñw u n; todu o̩ko̩-wñ de̩.
I la che̩wñ kʼaboke̩le̩ ja kpʼo̩la-ma ku ma lewa anu onobule̩ kʼi defu, kʼi mʼo̩ma ko rinyo̩, kʼe̩wñ e̩bie̩ne̩ omune̩ ma chʼo n, ma abʼo̩ko̩ ñw e̩ne̩ kʼi wa nʼu alu kʼo̩ko̩ onobule̩ le̩ aka chuu; i aro̩me̩ alu kʼamakajo̩ ñwa te̩.
I muda che̩wñ kʼe̩wñ e̩bie̩ne̩ omune̩ ño̩ manyʼu, mak uwe̩ adu oji koji oji.
Eju koji eju, enyi koji enyi, o̩wo̩ koji o̩wo̩, e̩re̩ koji e̩re̩,
e̩gujo koji e̩gujo, agbe koji agbe, ame̩ koji ame̩.
I la che̩wñ kʼone̩ fʼe̩wñ gwo adu-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ abe̩k onobule̩ eju kʼi fʼu kpo̩fo̩, i atʼadu le̩ no̩ tane̩ koji eju-wñ.
I la che̩wñ kʼi fʼe̩wñ gwo adu-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ abe̩k onobule̩ alu kʼenyi-wñ muchi, i atʼadu le̩ no̩ tane̩ koji enyi-wñ.
I la che̩wñ kʼo̩kokuno̩ rʼigba nyʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ abe̩k onobule̩ kʼi leku, ma arʼokuta kpa o̩kokuno̩ le̩, ma muda aje̩ e̩la-wñ n; odu o̩kokuno̩ le̩ muda mufu tane̩.
Ama iche̩wñ kʼo̩kokuno̩ le̩ te̩tar igba akwoubi, ku ma rʼodu-wñ aino̩ kʼi ma la dʼu tʼuro n, tak i lewa fʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ abe̩k onobule̩ kpa, ma arʼokuta kpʼo̩kokuno̩ le̩, ma la ñʼadʼodu-wñ kpa ge̩.
Iche̩wñ ku ma fʼe̩wñ kʼi adu la oji o̩la-wñ tane̩ ka ñw u, e̩gbale̩ i akʼe̩wñ du ku ma ka ñw u wa kʼi du la oji o̩la-wñ tane̩.
Dagba i chʼo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ dagba i chʼo̩ma onobule̩ kʼi rʼigba nyʼu, ma achʼo alu kʼoji ajo̩-i ka.
Iche̩wñ kʼo̩kokuno̩ rʼigba nyʼadu e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ abe̩k onobule̩, odu-wñ akʼo̩ko̩ ajifa ogue̩gwa ñw odu adu le̩, ma lañʼarʼokuta kpʼo̩kokuno̩ le̩ ge̩.
I la che̩wñ kʼone̩ tʼalu ura no̩ te̩, abe̩k one̩ fʼura gwa kʼi ma la du e̩wñ boma n, tak o̩kokuno̩ abe̩k o̩ke̩ke̩te̩ ñwa tʼefu-wñ,
e̩ne̩ kʼi ne̩ ura le̩ adʼakoji ñw u; i adʼo̩ko̩ ñw odu-wñ, tak i mʼoku e̩la le̩ du.
I la che̩wñ kʼo̩kokuno̩ e̩ne̩ʼka fʼe-e̩ne̩ omune̩ chagbe kʼi leku, e̩gbale̩ taku ma adʼo̩kokuno̩ e-ki deju ta, ku ma fʼo̩ko̩-wñ kpe̩, taku ma akpe̩ e-ki ku.
I la che̩wñ ku ma ma ka kʼo̩kokuno̩ le̩ te̩tarʼigba akwoubi, kʼodu-wñ ma dʼu tʼuro n; mak i aro̩me̩ o̩kokuno̩ koji o̩kokuno̩ chuu, tak i mʼe-kʼi ku du.
O̩da e̩wñ ojoji ojoji
I la che̩wñ kʼone̩ mʼoji o̩kokuno̩ abe̩k e̩wño̩re̩ egini ji, kʼi la fʼu kpa, abe̩k i mʼu du ta, i aro̩me̩ okuno̩ me̩lu koji o̩kokuno̩ʼka, e̩wño̩re̩ egini me̩le̩ la akoji e̩wño̩re̩ʼka.
Iche̩wñ ku ma fʼajoji li abu kʼi agu o̩do̩ lo̩, ku ma la dʼe̩wñ nʼu kʼi leku, udu e̩bie̩-wñ dʼoji e̩ne̩ du n.
I muda che̩wñ kʼolu muta dufu ke̩re̩bʼo̩ taku ma li, e̩gba le̩ udu e̩bie̩-wñ ado̩mo̩; i ma dukpe̩ kʼi kʼe̩wñ akoji wa chuu; i ma ne̩ e̩wñ du n, ma ki mʼowñ onugo du ta koji oji kʼi ji.
Iche̩wñ ku ma li udeju e̩la kʼi ji o̩wo̩-wñ, dagba i chʼo̩kokuno̩, dagba i chʼo̩ke̩ke̩te̩, dagba i chʼe̩wño̩re̩ egini, i arʼo̩me̩-wñ onu meji.
Iche̩wñ kʼone̩ kʼame̩wño̩re̩ jo̩ ajije̩ oko, abe̩k ef uche̩ achiwebe̩te̩ma, abe̩k i tʼe̩la-wñ ki anʼadu no̩ tane̩ tak i nyʼajije̩ oko e̩ne̩ omune̩, mak i ako e̩wñ e-ki nyo̩ tule efu uche̩ e-wñ, kpai ef uche̩ achiwebe̩te̩ma-wñ ro̩me̩ koji.
Iche̩wñ kʼuna kwotane̩ kʼi la fʼe̩tutu mu gbogbo tak i fʼo̩bo o̩ka abe̩k e-ki dago jo̩, abe̩k i fʼuche̩ onugo gujo rinyo̩; e̩ne̩ ki gwʼuna le̩ aro̩me̩ alu ki cheju-wñ chuu.
Iche̩wñ kʼone̩ mʼo̩ko̩ abe̩k ane̩ ko nyʼekeji-wñ o̩wo̩ kʼi de, taku ma mʼu ji kwef unyi e̩ne̩ le̩, iche̩wñ ku ma fʼajoji le̩ li, i aro̩me̩-wñ onu meji.
Iche̩wñ ku ma ma li ajoji le̩ n, tak odu unyi le̩ ate̩wʼugbo O̩jo̩, ku ma li abe̩k i dʼo̩wo̩-wñ tunyu ane̩ ekeji-wñ abe̩k i che n.
Todu o̩la du ku ma daba, dagba i chʼutodu o̩kokuno̩ todu o̩ke̩ke̩te̩, todu e̩wño̩re̩ egini, todu ukpo o̩la, abe̩ku todu e̩wñ du ki lenyo̩, e-kʼe̩ne̩ʼka aka kakini, E̩wñ le̩ de̩, ama meji anʼalu-ma wa o̩gba O̩jo̩ aka; e̩ne̩ kʼO̩jo̩ akpʼo̩ abi aro̩me̩ ñw ekeji-wñ onu meji.
Iche̩wñ kʼone̩ dʼo̩ke̩ke̩te̩ abe̩k o̩kokuno̩ abe̩k e̩wño̩re̩ egini abe̩k e̩ta abe̩re̩me̩le̩ du nyʼekeji-wñ o̩wo̩ kʼi de, kʼe̩la le̩ leku abe̩k e̩wñʼka chʼo abe̩k e̩wñʼka fʼu ne bʼo̩mo̩ te̩, kʼe̩ne̩ du ma liʼu n,
maku Jihofa ego̩ adʼagbagba ama meji, ku ma li abe̩k i dʼo̩wo̩ kado e̩wñ ekeji-wñ n, tak e̩ne̩ ki nʼe̩ agba ego̩ kʼi go̩ le̩, oñ e̩ne̩ le̩ ma adʼakoji-wñ wa ge̩ n.
Ama iche̩wñ ki chʼeji ma ji kwugbo-wñ, i adʼakoji ñw e̩ne̩ kʼi ne̩.
Iche̩wñ kʼi chefana pe̩le̩ pe̩le̩, i ki mʼu ko wa kʼi chʼijali-wñ; i aro̩me̩ koji e̩wñ ku ma fana n.
I la che̩wñ kʼone̩ bi e̩wñʼka ugbo ekeji-wñ, kʼe̩wñʼka chʼo, abe̩k i leku, kʼodu-wñ ma dʼugbo e̩wñ le̩ n, e̩ne̩ ki bi adʼakoji-wñ ñw odu-wñ chuu.
Iche̩wñ kʼodu-wñ dʼugbo-wñ, i aro̩me̩ koji n; i la che̩wñ ki chʼe̩faya i faya, mak e-le̩ dʼef o̩me̩ ki ra le̩.
I la che̩wñ kʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ fʼo̩ma onobule̩ kʼi ma mʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ n ku ma ma du kpʼo̩ko̩ ta n gwo̩gwo̩, kʼi la bʼo̩ dachi, i achʼana-wñ kʼi mud o̩ya-wñ.
Iche̩wñ kʼata-wñ ko̩ edʼu ñw u pioo, mak i adʼo̩ko̩ ro̩me̩ alu ku ma chʼana onobule̩ kʼi ma ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ n.
E̩ ki je̩ ñw ajochu kʼi deju n.
Ekpa ma akpa e̩ne̩ du kʼi bʼe̩la abe̩re̩me̩le̩ dachi.
E̩ne̩ kʼi fʼe̩wñ kpa ñw o̩jo̩ omune̩ kʼi ma che Jihofa kate n, ma adu te̩ ñw O̩jo̩.
E̩ ki chʼilowa ihianyi n, e̩ ki la fʼu kpama n, todu ame̩ chʼamilowa ane̩ Ijipti le̩.
E̩ ki fʼo̩yaukuo̩ko̩ dema n, abe̩k o̩ma kʼi ma nʼata n.
Iche̩wñ kʼe̩ fʼuma dema re ku ma la raku do̩ mi, nagbo̩ aku-ma chuu;
uwe̩do̩-mi la akpuna nyo̩gba, oñ nadʼo̩kwo̩chageli kpa me̩; tak amo̩ya-me̩ amud amo̩yaukuo̩ko̩, amo̩ma-me̩ la anʼata n.
Iche̩wñ kʼe̩ne̩-miʼka kʼi chʼe̩no̩bata dʼugbo-we̩ kʼe̩ fʼo̩ko̩ me̩ ñw u, e̩ ki chʼo dab e̩ne̩ kʼe̩ dʼo̩ko̩ ta ñw u n; e̩ ki la bʼabune ñw u n.
Iche̩wñ kʼekeji-we̩ dʼukpo-wñ tʼofʼo̩ko̩ ñw e̩, uwe̩ ki mʼe̩wñ-wñ ko ñw u tak olu ki tunyʼane̩;
todu e̩wñ kate kʼi ne̩ bʼo̩la ma de̩, e̩wñ kʼi adu bʼaño̩la-wñ ma i che; e̩wñ i adʼu bʼo̩la ma adachi? Oñ i awatu e̩gba kʼi araku do̩ mi, nagbo̩, todu e̩ne̩ kʼi ali one̩ eju omi che.
E̩ ki bʼO̩jo̩ ina n, e̩ ki la nama ñw idachi amone̩-we̩ n.
E̩ ki che̩du eko e̩gbaru e̩wñ e̩yo̩ etito̩ kʼe̩ gwu kpai omi agwo̩ko̩lo̩-we̩ wa ñw O̩jo̩ n.
Amo̩mo̩gba-we̩ e-e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, e̩ ki ko ñwu mi.
Abe̩le̩ uwe̩ ache kpai amo̩kokuno̩-we̩, kpai ame̩wño̩re̩-we̩ egini: i adʼugbo iye-wñ o̩jo̩ mebie; tak o̩jo̩ e̩ke̩jo̩-wñ uwe̩ adʼu wa ñwu mi.
Oñ ame̩ achʼaboke̩le̩ kiafo̩ ñwu mi; todule̩ me̩ ki je̩ o̩re̩la du kʼe̩la fana oko n; ame̩ ki mʼe-le̩ ko rikpolo ñw amabia.
O̩da e̩wñ ojoji ojoji
E̩ ki gba o̩la o̩lemi kʼe̩ du ka n. E̩ ki du o̩wo̩-we̩ dama kpai e̩ne̩bibi kʼe̩ mud e̩nibenu o̩lachi n.
E̩ ki tʼo̩wo̩ one̩ ubi kʼe̩ che e̩wñ bie̩ne̩ n; e̩ ki la rida tʼo̩wo̩ one̩ ubi kʼe̩ gbibenu kʼe̩ rʼoji ajo̩ da n;
e̩ ki la lʼe̩nubie̩ eju tod ale-wñ ef o̩la n.
Iche̩wñ kʼe̩ de kpai o̩kokuno̩ abe̩k o̩ke̩ke̩te̩ e̩no̩la-we̩ kʼi achila rinyo̩, e̩ dʼu dabi wa ñw u.
Iche̩wñ kʼe̩ li o̩ke̩ke̩te̩ e̩ne̩ ki achulaka we̩ kʼadu fʼu ka mʼane̩, e̩ nago ehiʼu tinyo̩ o̩mo̩, ebo̩che e̩ bʼo̩ che.
E̩ ki rʼoji ajo̩ enale-we̩ da n.
E̩ nahimama o̩la olemi, e̩ ki kpa e̩ne̩ hiolo kpai e̩ne̩ o̩kpakpa n; todu omi adale ñw e̩ne̩bibi n.
E̩ ki la gbʼo̩ko̩ obi n; todu o̩ko̩ obi afʼeju abo ki gane̩ chubi, i ñʼarʼo̩la abo o̩kpakpa da ge̩.
E̩ ki kpʼilowa ma n; todu ame̩ chema alu kʼe̩do̩ ilowa de̩, abu kʼame̩ chʼamilowa ane̩ Ijipti le̩.
O̩do̩ me̩fa e̩ la agbe̩ e̩wñ ane̩-we̩ kʼe̩ la kʼe̩ro-wñ wʼunyi;
e̩ muda ato̩no̩ o̩do̩ e̩kebie-wñ ki ñmi, o̩wo̩-we̩ ki muta, kʼabo-we̩ ku ma chʼe̩nale ki je̩; e̩wñ kʼama le̩ to̩no̩, ame̩wñ iñmi oko ki je̩. Abe̩le̩ e̩ ñʼache kpai uche̩ achiwebe̩te̩ma-we̩ kpai uche̩ o̩lif-we̩ ge̩.
O̩jo̩ me̩fa e̩ chʼuko̩lo̩-we̩ kade, o̩jo̩ ekebie-wñ e̩ la ñmi; todu kʼo̩kokuno̩-we̩ kpai o̩ke̩ke̩te̩-we̩ ki li uña uñmi, kʼo̩la o̩ma adu-we̩ onobule̩ kpai ilowa ki ruko.
E̩ ki fejutʼe̩wñ du kʼomi ko̩la ñw e̩-i; e̩ ki dedʼodu amo̩jo̩ omune̩ n, e̩ ki la je̩ ñwu ma gbʼodu-wñ alu-we̩ n.
E̩ ki de uje̩wñ uyo̩ ñwu mi onu me̩ta o̩do̩ du.
Uwe̩ ki de uje̩wñ uyo̩ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma dʼo̩ n; e̩ ki je̩ uje̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma dʼefu-wñ n o̩jo̩ mebie, iko kʼu da ñwu me̩ ochu Abib, alu kʼu ñwa ñw e̩ le̩, todu ef ochu le̩ e̩ kwʼIjipti dufu. E̩ne̩ du la adufu wʼo̩gba-mi o̩wo̩ ofo n.
Uwe̩ ki de uje̩wñ uyo̩ e-e̩wñ oko eko wʼunyi, owñ chʼejo̩ga e̩wñ kwef akanya uko̩lo̩-we̩ kʼe̩ che, owñ chʼe-kʼe̩ gbe̩ oko. E̩ ki la de uje̩wñ uyo̩ e-e̩wñ akule̩ eko wʼunyi e̩gba kʼo̩do̩ da, owñ chʼe̩gba kʼe̩ fʼe̩wñ kʼe̩ chʼakanya-wñ oko le̩ ko wʼunyi.
Onu me̩ta o̩do̩ du aboke̩le̩-we̩ chaka akʼo̩la-ma wa jo̩ o̩gba Ondu Jihofa.
E̩ ki kʼe̩bie̩ e̩wñ ku me̩ kpa ñwu mi wa ñwu mi manyu e̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu dʼo̩ n; ula e̩la ef uje̩wñ uyo̩-mi abo̩ gbʼodudu n.
E̩wñ ejodudu pale ef ejo̩ga ane̩-oko-we̩, e̩ ki ko wʼef unyi Jihofa O̩jo̩-we̩.
Uwe̩ ki hi o̩mewo ef omi e̩nya iye-wñ n.
Go, omi akpʼonuche̩ʼka tʼo̩gba-we̩ kʼi fʼuwe̩ de ej o̩na le̩, kʼi laño̩ dʼuwe̩ wa uña e-kʼomi ñwo̩che te̩.
Me̩ fʼo̩la-me̩ de o̩gba-wñ, ku me̩ la gbʼomu-wñ gbo̩; me̩ ki la rʼe̩re̩ ubi ñw u n, todu i atʼada ku me̩ je̩ no̩ ñwu me̩ n; todu odu-mi dʼefu-wñ.
Iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ muda agbʼomu-wñ gbo̩ ochochi, kʼe̩ la che e̩wñ du kʼu naka, e̩gbale̩ nachʼe̩nebi abo ku ma chʼame̩nebi-we̩, oñ nakobʼabo ku ma kobʼuwe̩.
Todu onuche̩-mi atʼuwe̩ o̩gba, kʼi la mʼuwe̩ du nyʼugbo abo Amo̩r kpai abo He̩t kpai abo Pe̩re̩z kpai abo Kenan kpai abo Hifai kpai abo Je̩bius, oñ nakʼuma da rinyo̩.
E̩ ki dojikane̩ ñw amo̩jo̩ e-ma n, e̩ ki re̩ ma n, e̩ ki la che likpa uko̩lo̩-ma n, e̩ ki muda gu uma lo̩ hioko, kʼe̩ la kʼojibo-ma kpo̩fo̩ ye̩ge̩ye̩ge̩.
Uwe̩ ki re̩ Jihofa O̩jo̩-me̩, tak owñ ade̩nyo̩ ñw uje̩wñ-we̩ kpai omi-we̩: owñ la akʼo̩ga bʼalumeji-we̩ te̩.
E̩wñ du la akʼo̩ma rinyo̩ n, e̩wñ du la achʼagaji oj ane̩-we̩ n; naje̩ ñw aluka o̩jo̩-we̩ ki jo̩ kpa.
Naje̩ ñw ailo-mi ki tʼuwe̩ o̩gba, oñ nadʼamone̩ du kʼe̩ nyʼugbo ma le̩ utu, u la aje̩ ñw ame̩nebi-we̩ chaka mubidagbʼe̩.
Nakpʼamanukpe tʼuwe̩ o̩gba, ma la anʼabo Hifai kpai abo Kenan kpai abo He̩t bʼuwe̩ o̩gba te̩.
U la ane̩ ma kwo bʼe̩ o̩gba te̩ o̩do̩ okate n, tode̩gba kʼane̩ le̩ mud akpokpo te̩, kʼame̩wñ iñmi oko awewe nyʼuwe̩ o̩la.
O̩pe̩ pe̩ pe̩ nane̩ ma kwo bʼe̩ o̩gba te̩, gbogbo tak e̩ wewe kʼe̩ la mʼane̩ le̩ gba.
Omi la ahi o̩me̩-we̩ te̩ akwʼohimini Ekpikpa gbogbo wa kado ohimini abo Filistia, kpai akwo aje̩tachi le̩ gbogbo wʼohimini Yufretis; todu nakʼabo ane̩ le̩ nyʼef o̩wo̩-we̩, oñ uwe̩ ane̩ ma kwo bʼe̩ o̩gba te̩.
E̩ ki kpʼalo du kpai ama n, abe̩k amo̩jo̩-ma n.
Ama le̩ adodo oj ane̩-we̩ n, tode̩gba ku ma je̩ ñw e̩ du mi re; todu iche̩wñ kʼuwe̩ re̩ amo̩jo̩ e-ma, i achʼoku ñw e̩ chuu.
Mose̩s fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ne, tak i mute̩gu tʼoj uwo le̩
Tak i ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩ mute̩gu wʼugbo Jihofa-i, uwe̩ kpai Aro̩n kpai Nedab kpai Abaihiu, kpai abogijo Israe̩l e̩te̩gwa, ku me̩ dojikane̩ jo̩ o̩najiji.
Mose̩s kate ate̩ me̩ru ugbo Jihofa; abo kibo̩ muda ate̩ me̩rʼu n, abo kibo̩ ki la te̩gu wa kpai owñ n.
Taku Mose̩s lewa dʼo̩la Jihofa le̩ chaka ka ñw amone̩ le̩ kpai oji ajo̩-wñ kʼi kojo̩ chaka; tak amone̩ le̩ chaka dohi alukate, ma kakini, O̩la du ku Jihofa ka le̩ awa ache.
Taku Mose̩s fʼo̩la Jihofa du ko̩ nyʼe̩wñ. Oñ i takpa kwane̩ odudu, i la fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ne e̩re̩ uwo o̩mo̩, kpai e̩wñ eguanyane̩ dago me̩gweji, likpa alu kʼo̩lo̩pu o̩lo̩pu abo Israe̩l chʼe̩gwe̩ji.
Tak i fʼabokolobia amo̩ma Israe̩l kpuche̩, abo le̩ la kʼamo̩kokuno̩ wa chʼe̩wñ e̩gujo, ma laño̩ fʼe̩wñ ure̩do̩ kpa ñwu Jihofa.
Taku Mose̩s mʼukpe̩reji e̩bie̩ le̩ du, oñ imʼu du danyu ugba jo̩, i la mʼukpe̩re̩ji e̩bie̩ le̩ du tafio̩ ubo̩ iche̩bo̩;
tak i mʼo̩takada alo du, oñ i fʼo̩kalatu-wñ che nyʼamone̩ le̩ eti; taku ma kakini, E̩wñ du ki Jihofa ka le̩, awa ache, a la agbʼo̩la-wñ gbo̩.
Taku Mose̩s mʼe̩bie̩ le̩ du oñ i tafio̩ amone̩ le̩ o̩la, i kakini, Me̩ go, e̩bie̩ alo e-ki Jihofa kpe̩ kpai ame̩ ugbo o̩la-i du de̩.
Taku Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n kpai Nedab kpai Abaihiu kpai abogijo Israe̩l e̩te̩gwa le̩ mute̩gu le.
Oñ ma fʼO̩jo̩ e-Israe̩l li, uko̩lo̩ okuta safaya la dʼo̩gane̩ e̩re̩-wñ dab ajita, i de̩ gbaa dabe̩ne̩ kʼefojale onugo.
I la dʼo̩wo̩ kado amidachi ef amo̩ma Israe̩l le̩ n; ma fʼO̩jo̩ li, ma la je̩ e̩wñ, ma la ñmo̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Mute̩gu wʼoj uwo ugbo-mi-i, kʼe̩ dago omo̩; kʼu nakʼalo okuta le̩ ñw e̩, manyʼuko̩-o̩la kpai uko̩ kʼu te̩ ñw e̩ e-kʼomi kʼorubutu-wñ-i ku ma ko̩che̩.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s kpai Jo̩shua kʼi ache uko̩lo̩ ñw u kwane̩, oñ Mose̩s mute̩gu tʼoj uwo O̩jo̩.
Oñ i ka ñw abogijo le̩ kakini, Me̩ nede wa emi gbogbo kʼa dabiwa ugbo me̩; me̩ go, Aro̩n kpai He̩r la jʼugbo-me̩; e̩ne̩ du ki nʼo̩la, i ki nyʼugbo ma.
Taku Mose̩s mute̩gu tʼoj uwo, oñ akpa le̩ bʼoj uwo-wñ ma.
Tak ojima Jihofa lewa gugu oj uwo Sainai, akpa le̩ la bʼoji-wñ ma gbogbo o̩jo̩ me̩fa; tak o̩jo̩ e̩kebie-wñ, i dʼalumeji akpa le̩ ado̩ Mose̩s udo̩.
E̩ go ojima Jihofa la dab una ki afʼe̩wñ lie̩ oj uwo le̩ eju amo̩ma Israe̩l.
Taku Mose̩s mugudu tʼalumeji akpa, oñ i mute̩gu tʼoj uwo le̩. Mose̩s la dʼoj uwo le̩ o̩jo̩ o̩gbo̩ meji kpai odu o̩gbo̩ meji.
Unyabo kpai e̩wñ eku ki jʼefu-wñ
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
E̩ nako̩la ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l ka kʼama ki fʼe̩wñ ku ma ko ne jo̩ le̩ te̩re̩ wa ñwu mi; me̩ gba e̩wñ ku ma te̩re̩ wa ñwu mi le̩ o̩wo̩ e̩ne̩ du kʼe̩do̩-wñ du.
E̩wñ ku ma ko ne jo̩ ku me̩ agba o̩wo̩-ma le̩ de̩: o̩jamalia kpai ajifa kpai ebijeikpa
kpai e̩wñ odufa kpai ekpikpa odufa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju kpai edudu ewo
kpai año̩ okolo ku ma hi ekpikpa kpai año̩ e̩la omiʼka kpai oli akesia
kpai ekpo tod agege kpai e̩wñ kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ ku ma du chʼotulale tod ekpo ku ma du ba tʼone̩ oji kpai e-ki chʼutodu otulale ku ma gujo kʼi akpo le̩
kpai okuta one̩ks kpai okuta ojoji ku ma dʼo̩na nyʼu, tod e̩fo̩d kpai e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩.
E̩ ki la je̩ ñwu ma che uña kiafo̩ ñwu mi, kʼu gugu efu-ma.
Likpa e̩wñ du kʼu nadu ña uwe̩, uwo̩li uña ugugu le̩, kpai uwo̩li e̩wñ eku du ki jʼefu-wñ, abe̩le̩ ame̩ ki che.
Ma ki ne̩ oli akesia che akpati, ujiji-wñ ki chʼohibo̩wo̩ meji nyʼukpe̩reji, unabe̩-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpe̩re̩-ji, o̩gba-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpe̩reji.
E̩ ki la kʼo̩jamalia hiolo bʼo̩la-wñ ma, tʼejefu-wñ, tʼejo̩do̩da-wñ, e̩ ki laño̩ fʼo̩jamalia gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ kʼe̩ du lamʼeti-wñ daka.
E̩ ki la fʼo̩na o̩jamalia me̩le̩ da dab elika todu-wñ, kʼe̩ du tunyʼe̩re̩-wñ me̩le̩, elika meji ajʼo̩wo̩ʼka-wñ, elika meji la ajʼo̩wo̩ ekeji.
E̩ ki dʼoli akesia fa ugbo̩lo̩ oli kʼe̩ mʼo̩jamalia ko wenyʼu.
E̩ ki la mʼugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩ ko tunyʼelika o̩wo̩ mejeji akpati le̩, ku ma du oli le̩ ne̩ akpati.
Ugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩ atunyʼelika akpati: ma ki wʼo̩ bʼo̩ te̩ n.
Tak uwe̩ ako e̩wñ ibenu kʼomi ako ñw e̩ nyʼef akpati le̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki nʼo̩jamalia hiolo che uchi-wñ ki chʼugugu unye̩do̩; ujiji-wñ ki chʼohibo̩wo̩ meji nyʼukpe̩reji, unabe̩-wñ la achʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpe̩reji.
Uwe̩ ki la nʼo̩jamalia che amiche̩rub meji; eruru oñ e̩ gwu, ma ajo̩ iba ugugu unye̩do̩ le̩ mejeji.
Cherubʼka adʼiba-wñ o̩wo̩ʼka, che̩rub ekeji la adʼiba-wñ o̩wo̩ ekeji; me̩ ki che amiche̩rub le̩ ki chʼalu okate kpai ugugu unye̩do̩ iba-wñ mejeji.
Oñ amiche̩rub le̩ anʼika-ma dala ate̩, ika-ma ata ate̩ adebonʼoji ugugu unye̩do̩, ma akpejuru omune̩; eju amiche̩rub le̩ afe̩ru ugugu unye̩do̩ le̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki du ugugu unye̩do̩-i tʼoji akpati le̩; tak e̩ mʼe̩wñ ibenu kʼomi ako ñw e̩ ko nyʼef akpati le̩.
O̩mo̩ le̩ omi ade kpai uwe̩, oñ nadʼate̩ ugugu unye̩do̩, agbagba amiche̩rub ku ma jo̩ oj akpati e̩wñ ibenu le̩ achʼoluka kpai uwe̩, oluka e̩wñ du kʼu nañwa ñw e̩ ugbo amo̩ma Israe̩l nache kpai uwe̩ o̩mo̩.
Tak uwe̩ ane̩ oli akesia fa ite-bulu; ujiji-wñ ki chʼohibo̩wo̩ meji, unabe̩-wñ la achʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka, o̩gba-wñ la achʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpe̩reji.
E̩ ki du o̩jamalia hiolo bʼo̩la-wñ ma, kʼe̩ la fʼo̩jamalia gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ kʼe̩ du lamʼeti-wñ daka.
E̩ ki la fʼo̩gba bu nyʼoji-wñ daka kʼunabe̩ e-le̩ kʼi chʼe̩do̩wo̩ʼka, tak e̩ fʼo̩jamalia gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ kʼe̩ dʼu lamʼo̩gba-wñ daka.
Uwe̩ ki la ada elika o̩jamalia me̩le̩ todu-wñ, oñ e̩ mʼelika le̩ ko nyʼalo-wñ me̩le̩ ugbo e̩re̩-wñ me̩le̩.
Elika le̩ ame̩ru o̩gba ku ma bu nyʼu ki chʼugbo kʼoli ku ma adu ne̩ itebulu le̩ atunyu.
E̩ la anʼoli akesia che ugbo̩lo̩ oli kʼe̩ du o̩jamalia wenyu o̩la-wñ, todu ku ma dʼe-le̩ ne̩ itebulu le̩.
Uwe̩ ki che ugba-wñ kpai ucha-wñ kpai ago iche̩bo̩-wñ kpai ukpa ku ma ane̩ dʼomi iche̩bo̩ danyʼoji e̩wñ iche̩bo̩; e̩ ki nʼo̩jamalia ki de̩ hiolo che.
Uwe̩ ki la kʼakala eju O̩jo̩ jʼoji itebulu le̩ o̩gba-mi oko-ko̩lo̩.
Tak uwe̩ anʼo̩jamalia hiolo che akete agege. Eruru ma agwu akete le̩, e̩re̩-wñ kpʼoli-wñ kpʼe̩bu-wñ kpʼakpo-wñ kpai ododo-wñ achʼokate kpai owñ;
e̩to̩ me̩fa adufu akolo-wñ; e̩to̩ akete me̩ta adufu akolo-wñ oka, oñ e̩to̩ akete me̩ta adufu akolo-wñ ekeji;
e̩bu-wñ me̩ta ku ma che ki dabe̩ne̩ kʼalmo̩nd ajʼef e̩to̩ʼka, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ anʼakpo-wñ kpai ododo-wñ; e̩bu me̩ta ku ma che dabe̩ne̩ kʼalmo̩nd ñʼajʼef e̩to̩ ekeji, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ anʼakpo-wñ kpai ododo-wñ. Abe̩le̩ i ade̩ ñw e̩to̩ me̩fa ki dufu o̩la akete agege le̩;
tak e̩bu-wñ me̩le̩ ku ma che dabe̩ne̩ kʼalmo̩nd ajʼo̩la onugo akete le̩ manyʼakpo-wñ kpai ododo-wñ,
takakpo adʼofe e̩to̩ meji, oñ akpo adʼofe e̩to̩ meji, akpo adʼofe e̩to̩ meji. Abe̩le̩ i de̩ todu e̩to̩ me̩fa ki dufu o̩la akete agege le̩.
Akpo-wñ kpai e̩to̩-wñ achʼalu okate kpai owñ, o̩chaka-wñ chʼuko̩lo̩ okate ku ma nʼo̩jamalia hiolo gwu eruru.
Tak e̩ fʼagege-wñ mebie che; ma la akʼo jo̩ ki chʼugane̩ o̩gba-wñ o̩mo̩.
Ma anʼo̩jamalia hiolo che alapa-wñ ku ma ne̩ kpʼuna lu kpai ugba ku ma ko e̩wñ ku ma du kpʼuna lunyʼu.
O̩jamalia ki de̩ hiolo alu tale̩nt oka oñ e̩ du che, kpai e̩wñ eku-i du.
E̩ nago, kʼe̩ che wo̩li e̩wñ ku ma du ñʼuwe̩ oj uwo-i.
Unyabo
Tak uwe̩ ki kʼibali ukpo me̩gwa ta che uña ugugu; ukpo-wñ ki che line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ kʼi chʼodufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa; amiche̩rub kʼabo ku ma chʼo̩ka uko̩lo̩-wñ che ajʼo̩la-wñ.
Ujiji ibali ukpo ku ma ko̩ ta le̩ okoke la achʼohibo̩wo̩ ogu nyoke me̩jo̩, unabe̩-wñ okoke la achʼo̩hibo̩wo̩ me̩le̩; e̩ñwa o̩chaka ukpo ku ma ko ta le̩ achʼalukate.
Ibali ukpo me̩lu agamʼomune̩; ukpo me̩lu ki bo̩ la agamʼomune̩ ge̩.
E̩ ki la che ate odufa nyʼeti ibali ukpo ku ma ko ta le̩ e-ki dʼotitala e̩gwodama-wñ oka; abe̩le̩ uwe̩ ñʼache nyʼeti ibali ukpo ki dʼoditala e̩gwodama-wñ ekeji.
Uwe̩ ki che ate ooje nyʼe̩gwodama ibali ukpo ku ma ko ta le̩ oka, e̩ ki laño̩ che ate ooje nyʼeti e̩gwodama ibali ukpo ku ma ta le̩ ekeji; ate ukpo meji le̩ akpejurʼomune̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki nʼo̩jamalia che atanyi-wñ ooje, kʼe̩ ne̩ atanyi le̩ fʼukpo ku ma ko ta le̩ gamʼomune̩: abe̩le̩ oñ uña ugugu le̩ achʼokate.
Tak uwe̩ ki ño̩ nʼedudu ewo hi ibali ibali ukpo kʼi chʼunyabo kʼi abʼuña ugugu le̩ ma; uwe̩ ki che ibali-wñ me̩gwaka.
Ujiji ibali-wñ okoke achʼohibo̩wo̩ ogue̩gwa, unabe̩ ibali-wñ okoke achʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩le̩; e̩ñwa ibali ibali me̩gwaka le̩ achʼalukate.
Tak e̩ namʼibali ukpo ku ma ta le̩ me̩lu ko̩ gamʼomune̩, e̩ ki ño̩ kʼibali me̩fa gamʼomune̩ ojoji, ibali e̩ke̩fa ki bale nʼo̩gba unyabo le̩.
Uwe̩ ki la chʼate ooje nyʼeti ibali ukpo ku ma ko ta e-kʼi dʼotitala o̩wo̩ʼka ñw abʼe-ku ma gamʼomune̩ le̩; kpai ate ooje nyʼeti ibali ukpo otitala ef abo ekeji ku ma gamʼomune̩ le̩.
Tak e̩ ki fʼatanyi ebijeikpa ooje che, kʼe̩ kʼatanyi le̩ tunyʼate, kʼe̩ la fʼunyabo gamʼomune̩ kʼi mud okate.
Tak ukpo ku ma ko ta kibo̩ le̩ kʼi a bale unyabo, ukpe̩reji ibali ki bo̩ le̩, e-le̩ abale ejubi uña ugugu.
Tak ohibo̩wo̩ʼka o̩wo̩ʼka-wñ kpai ohibo̩wo̩ʼka o̩wo̩ ekeji-wñ, owñ chʼe-kʼukpo ku ma ko ta le̩ jiji tʼunyabo le̩, e-le̩ abale nʼiba uña ugugu ej emi-wñ kpai ejano̩mo̩-wñ, kʼi bʼo ma.
Tak uwe̩ ki kʼaño̩ okolo ku ma hi ekpikpa che e̩wñ ki abʼoji unyabo le̩ ma, kʼe̩ la nʼaño̩ e̩la omi le̩ che e̩wñ ki abʼoji e-le̩ ate̩ ma.
Tak uwe̩ ane̩ oli akesia che akatakpo uña ugugu le̩, edago i adago.
Ujiji akatakpoʼka ache ohibo̩wo̩ me̩gwa, unabe̩ akatakpoʼka oka la ache ohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpe̩re̩ji.
Akatakpo du ane̩ e̩re̩ meji e̩ji, ku ma jo̩ okujo̩; abe̩le̩ uwe̩ ki che nyʼakatakpo uña ugugu le̩ du.
Uwe̩ ki fʼakatakpo che todu uña ugugu le̩; akatakpo ogu achʼutodu o̩wo̩ o̩pata-wñ o̩gane̩;
uwe̩ ki la ane̩ ajifa che o̩ka o̩gbo̩ meji kʼoli akatakpo ogu le̩ ki dago jo̩ oji-wñ, o̩ka meji ajʼofe akatakpoʼka todu e̩re̩-wñ meji, o̩ka meji ki ño̩ jʼofe akatakpo omune̩ todu e̩re̩ e-wñ meji;
akatakpo ogu ñʼade̩ todu uña ugugu le̩ akolo-wñ ekeji, o̩wo̩ o̩pata-wñ ate̩,
kpai o̩ka-wñ o̩gbo̩ meji ku ma nʼajifa che le̩, o̩ka meji ajʼofe akatakpoʼka, o̩ka meji la ajʼofe akatakpo omune̩;
e̩ ki la fʼakatakpo me̩fa che todu ejubi uña ugugu o̩wo̩ o̩lane̩-wñ.
E̩ ki chʼakatakpo meji todu alo alo uña ugugu ej ubi-wñ;
ma a gamʼomune̩ e̩re̩-wñ o̩gane̩, tak i amanyʼomune̩ kʼoji-wñ ki tunyʼelikaʼka; abe̩le̩ i ade̩ ñw ejeji-wñ; ab e-le̩ achʼalo-wñ meji.
Akatakpo la ache e̩jo̩, kpai o̩ka-wñ e-ajifa le̩ achʼe̩gwe̩fa; o̩ka meji ajʼofe akatakpoʼka, Oka meji ñʼajʼofe akatakpo omune̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki fa ugbo̩lo̩ oli akesia; oli ugbo̩lo̩ me̩lu chʼutodu akatakpo uña ugugu le̩ akolo-wñ oka,
oli ugbo̩lo̩ me̩lu la chʼutodu akatakpo uña ugugu le̩ o̩wo̩ ekeji-wñ, oli ugbo̩lo̩ me̩lu la chʼutodu akatakpo ejubi uña ugugu, o̩wo̩ o̩lane̩-wñ.
Oñ ugbo̩lo̩ oli ki dʼalumeji akatakpo le̩ agudu akwo ejuʼka-wñ tʼeju ekeji.
Uwe̩ ki dʼo̩jamalia bʼo̩la akatakpo ma kʼe̩ la che elika o̩jamalia ñw u, todu ki gwo̩nyʼugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩; e̩ ki la dʼo̩jamalia wenyʼugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki ko uña ugugu le̩ dago alu ku ma dʼoji-wñ te̩ ku ma du ñʼe̩ oj uwo-i.
Uwe̩ ki la nʼukpo odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ che ukpo ugbeju unyi; abo ku ma chʼo̩ka uko̩lo̩-wñ ache kʼamiche̩rub ki jʼo̩la-wñ;
e̩ ki la dʼu ta tʼoli urane̩ akesia me̩le̩ kʼo̩jamalia wenyʼu kʼi jʼoji o̩ka me̩le̩ ku ma nʼajifa che; uko̩-wñ ache o̩jamalia.
Uwe̩ ki kʼukpo ugbeju le̩ ta nyʼatanyi-wñ. Tak e̩ du akpati ibenu wa ejefu ukpo ugbeju; oñ ukpo ugbeju unyi le̩ afʼuña kiafo̩ daru bʼuña efo̩ e-e̩fo̩ te̩ ñw e̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki dʼugugu unye̩do̩ nʼoj akpati ibenu efu uña efo̩ e-efo̩.
Tak uwe̩ adʼitebulu-wñ dago ejo̩do̩da ukpo ugbeju unyi, akete agege-wñ la adago ef uña ugugu o̩wo̩ o̩pata o̩gane̩-wñ, owñ kpʼitebulu akpejurʼomune̩; uwe̩ ki la du itebulu le̩ dago o̩wo̩ o̩pata ate̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki chʼukpo uro̩na todu alugbo̩na unyabo, ukpo odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ kʼuko̩lo̩ e̩ne̩ ki achiya nyʼo̩la ukpo adʼo̩la-wñ.
Uwe̩ ki la afa oli urane̩ akesia me̩lu todu ukpo uro̩na le̩, kʼe̩ la fʼo̩jamalia wenyʼo̩la-wñ me̩lu; uko̩-wñ achʼo̩jamalia ge̩; uwe̩ ki ne̩ ebijeikpa da o̩ka me̩lu todu-wñ.
Ubo̩ iche̩bo̩: ologbo-wñ
Oñ e̩ ne̩ oli akesia che ubo̩ iche̩bo̩; ujiji-wñ ki che ohibo̩wo̩ me̩lu, unabe̩-wñ la che ohibo̩wo̩ me̩lu; ago̩go̩ me̩le̩ ubo le̩ la achʼokujo̩, o̩gba-wñ la ache ohibo̩wo̩ me̩ta.
Tak uwe̩ ki chʼigba nyʼu oji uka-wñ me̩le̩; igba-wñ achʼo̩la okate kpai owñ, e̩ ki dʼebijeikpa bʼo̩la-wñ ma chaka.
Tak uwe̩ achʼucha-wñ ku ma ne̩ gba elulu-wñ, kpai uko̩che̩-wñ, kpai ugba-wñ, kpai uko̩-wñ ku ma du e̩la lo̩ko̩li, kpai aido wñ; e̩wñ eku-wñ chaka le̩, uwe̩ anʼebijeikpa che.
E̩ ki laño̩ nʼebijeikpa ta e̩wñ pataka kʼi chʼiga ebije kʼuna ki jʼoji-wñ; tak e̩ nʼebijeikpa che elika me̩le̩ tunyʼuka-wñ me̩le̩.
Tak uwe̩ adu e-le̩ tʼofe e̩bale ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ todu kʼiga ebije le̩ kʼi de̩ alumeji ef ubo̩ iche̩bo̩.
Tak uwe̩ afa ugbo̩lo̩ oli tod ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩, oli akesia i ache, e̩ ki la dʼebijeikpa wenyʼo̩la-wñ.
Ma la ako ugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩ tunyʼelika-wñ todu kʼugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩ ki jʼakolo ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ o̩wo̩ mejeji, e̩gba ku ma ne̩.
E̩ ki nʼakatakpo che kʼefu-wñ chʼo̩dagbolo, alu ku ma du ñʼuwe̩ oj uwo-i, abe̩le̩ ma ache.
Uwe̩ ki la che ologbo uña ugugu le̩. Ma anʼukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ kʼujiji-wñ che o̩hibo̩wo̩ ogu me̩lu ku ma du bʼologbo-wñ o̩wo̩ o̩pata o̩gane̩;
oli urane̩-wñ la achʼogu, o̩ka-wñ la chʼogu, ebijeikpa e-le̩ ache; ma muda anʼajifa chʼuko̩ oli urane̩ le̩ kpai ugbo̩lo̩-wñ.
Abe̩le̩ o̩wo̩ o̩pata-wñ ate̩ ge̩, ujiji ukpo ku ma du bʼolo̩gbo̩-wñ ache o̩hibo̩wo̩ ogume̩lu, oli urane̩-wñ achʼogu, o̩ka-wñ la achʼogu, ebijeikpa e-le̩ ache, uko̩ oli urane̩-wñ kpai ugbo̩lo̩-wñ ate̩ muda ache ajifa.
Ujiji ukpo ku ma du bʼologbo todu unabe̩ ologbo le̩ o̩wo̩ olane̩-wñ achʼo̩hibo̩wo̩ ooje, oli urane̩-wñ achʼe̩gwa, o̩ka-wñ la chʼe̩gwa.
Unabe̩ ologbo le̩ o̩wo̩ olodudu-wñ la achʼohibo̩wo̩ ooje.
Ujiji ukpo ku ma du bʼologbo o̩wo̩ʼka alaku-wñ achʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩gwe̩lu; oli urane̩-wñ achʼe̩ta, o̩ka-wñ la achʼe̩ta.
Ujiji ukpo ku ma du bʼologbo o̩wo̩ ekeji-wñ la achʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩gwe̩lu; oli urane̩-wñ achʼe̩ta, o̩ka-wñ la achʼe̩ta.
Ujiji ukpo uro̩na alaku ologbo le̩ achʼohibo̩wo̩ ogu, odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ e-le̩ ache, uko̩lo̩ e̩ne̩ ki chʼo̩ka iya ukpo eche e-le̩ ache; oli urane̩-wñ achʼe̩le̩, o̩ka-wñ la achʼe̩le̩.
Oli ugbo̩lo̩ ajifa anʼoji oli urane̩ ologbo le̩ ate̩ le daka; uko̩-wñ achʼajifa, o̩ka-wñ la achʼebijeikpa.
Ujiji ologbo le̩ achʼohibo̩wo̩ ogu me̩lu, unabe̩-wñ achʼo̩hibo̩wo̩ ooje, o̩gba-wñ la achʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩lu, ma kʼukpo line̩n ki chʼe̩hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ bʼologbo-wñ, o̩ka-wñ la chʼebijeikpa.
E̩wñ eku uña ugugu le̩ tod uko̩lo̩-wñ chaka, kpai ale-wñ chaka, kpai ale olo̩gbo-wñ chaka achʼebi-jeikpa.
Tak uwe̩ añwa ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l ku ma ko ekpo o̩lif ki de̩ hiolo ku ma fu de̩ wa tod e̩mu le̩, todu kʼuna ki dʼagege o̩mo̩ kʼi najo o̩ko̩ko̩lo̩.
Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ajʼef unyabo ujeju le̩ ejo̩do̩da ukpo ugbeju ki dʼo̩gba akpati ibenu afʼu te̩ru jo̩ o̩gba Jihofa kwʼolane̩ gbogbo tʼodudu. E-le̩ achʼo̩da ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l gbogbo tʼo̩hio̩gu-ma ogbegbele̩.
E̩wñ o̩la arama rod Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ
Tak e̩ mʼo̩maye-we̩, Aro̩n, kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ko kwef amo̩ma Israe̩l mʼo̩la, todu ku ma chʼamatama ku ma che e̩wñ ñwu mi—owñ che Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma Aro̩n, Nedab kpai Abaihiu kpai E̩leaza kpai Itamar.
Uwe̩ ki ga e̩wñ o̩la kiafo̩ todu Aro̩n o̩maye-we̩, todu ojima kpai alifia.
Uwe̩ ki ka ñw abo du ku ma nʼibe efu, e-kʼomi mʼafu e-ibe du tʼuma efu e̩ko̩, kʼama ki fʼe̩wñ o̩la Aro̩n ga, ku ma je̩ ñw u ki nafo̩, todu kʼi chʼatama kʼi ache e̩wñ ñwu mi.
E̩wñ o̩la-wñ ku ma la aga de̩: e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma kpai e̩fo̩d kpai otogbo kpai afe̩ ki chʼe̩kina kpai alawo̩ni kpai e̩wñ ujiñmi; ma la aga e̩wñ o̩la kiafo̩ ñw Aro̩n o̩maye-we̩, kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ todu ku ma chʼatama ku ma che e̩wñ ñwu mi.
Ma la agba o̩jamalia kpai odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju.
Ma la anʼo̩jamalia kpai odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ che e̩fo̩d le̩, abo ku ma chʼo̩ka uko̩lo̩-wñ ache.
I ane̩ e̩wñ ojika-wñ meji ki chʼe̩gamʼeti-wñ meji, ku ma ane̩ ga mʼomune̩.
Oñ igbe̩chi uje̩do̩ ku ma fu hi o̩ka, kʼi dʼo̩la-wñ ku ma du lʼago, uko̩lo̩-wñ adabu uko̩lo̩ e̩fo̩d onugo, i achʼalu okate kpai owñ; e-o̩jamalia e-odufa kpai ekpikpa odufa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki kʼokuta one̩ks meji kʼe̩ la fʼodu amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Israe̩l ko̩ nyʼo̩la-wñ,
odu-ma me̩fa ajʼo̩la okutaʼka, oñ odu ama me̩fa ki bo̩ ajʼo̩la okuta ekeji, alu ku ma bi ma aro̩ne aro̩ne.
Alu kʼe̩ne̩ ki agbe̩ okuta agbe̩ e̩wñ uhiuko̩, alu le̩ uwe̩ ki kʼodu amo̩ma Israe̩l nyʼokuta le̩ meji. E̩ ki fʼo̩jamalia da nyʼago̩go̩-wñ me̩le̩.
Tak e̩ ki mʼokuta meji le̩ ko nʼoji e̩wñ ojika e̩fo̩d le̩ kʼi chʼokuta urewa todu amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Israe̩l; Aro̩n la anʼodu-ma oj ika-wñ meji wa o̩gba Jihofa todu urewa.
Uwe̩ ki la fʼo̩jamalla da kʼe̩wñ le̩ ki gugu efu-wñ,
kpai iyagba o̩jamalia ki de̩ hiolo meji, uko̩lo̩-wñ adabe̩ne̩ kʼiku ku ma ba nyo̩nyo̩; tak e̩ ki fʼiyagba ku ma ba le̩ ji mʼe̩wñ ugugu ojika le̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki chʼe̩wñ ube̩do̩ma e-oji ajo̩ eka, uko̩lo̩ e̩ne̩ kʼi chʼo̩ka i ache; uwe̩ ache kʼi dab uko̩lo̩ e̩fo̩d le̩; e̩ ki la nʼo̩jamalia kpai odufa kpai ekpikpa odufa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ che.
E̩guche̩no-wñ ago̩go̩-wñ me̩le̩ achʼokujo̩; ujiji-wñ la chʼo̩chaliʼka, unabe̩-wñ la chʼo̩chaliʼka.
Uwe̩ ki la kʼokuta nyʼefu-wñ o̩gba o̩gba me̩le̩. O̩gba-wñ ejodudu che sardius kpai topaz kpai karbunke̩l;
o̩gba-wñ ekeji ache e̩me̩rald kpai safaya kpai daimo̩nd;
o̩gba e̩ke̩ta la che je̩sint kpai age̩t kpai ame̩tist;
o̩gba e̩ke̩le̩ la che be̩re̩l, kpai one̩ks, kpai jaspe̩r; ama kifʼo̩jamalia da nyʼu.
Okuta le̩ achʼe̩gweji kʼodu-wñ dʼalu kʼodu amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Israe̩l de̩; i la adab e̩wñ uhiuko̩, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ anʼodu-wñ todu abo o̩lo̩pu me̩gweji le̩.
Uwe̩ ki la nʼo̩jamalia ki de̩ hiolo chʼiyagba ki dab iku tod e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩;
uwe̩ ki la chʼelika o̩jamalia meji jʼo̩la e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩, kʼe̩ la fʼelika meji le̩ ro̩ tʼeti e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma meji.
Tak uwe̩ ki mʼiyagba o̩jamalia meji le̩ ko tunyʼelika meji ki jʼo̩la e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩ eti-wñ meji;
oji iyagba meji ku ma ba ki bo̩ tane̩ e̩ mʼu du ro nyʼo̩jamalia ku ma da nyʼokuta le̩ kʼe̩ ko jʼojika e̩fo̩d atama ej o̩gba-wñ.
Tak uwe̩ ki chʼelika o̩jamalia meji kʼe̩ ko e-le̩ jʼiba e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma mejeji, e̩ ko jʼeti-wñ ejefu kʼi kado e̩fo̩d le̩.
E̩ ki la fʼelika o̩jamalia meji che kʼe̩ du ro̩ tʼofe e̩wñ ojika e̩fo̩d le̩, kʼi jʼej o̩gba-wñ ame̩ru ugbo atanyi-wñ ate̩ e̩wñ ujiñmi ku ma hi o̩ka o̩la e̩fo̩d le̩.
Taku ma adʼo̩jaja odufa ki dab iku ki nabe̩ pe̩ tunyʼelika-wñ ku ma fʼe̩wñ ube̩do̩ma ji manyʼe̩fo̩d ki nʼo̩la e̩wñ ujiñmi ku ma hi o̩ka o̩la e̩fo̩d le̩, todu kʼe̩wñ ube̩do̩ma ki we etu bʼe̩fo̩d te̩.
Abe̩le̩ Aro̩n anʼodu amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Israe̩l ef e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma e-oji ajo̩ eka abʼe̩do̩-wñ ma, e̩gba kʼi alo tef uña kiafo̩ le̩, todu kʼi chʼe̩wñ urewa o̩gba Jihofa o̩ko̩ko̩lo̩.
Uwe̩ ki la ko̩ Urim kpai Tumim tunyʼe̩wñ ube̩do̩ma e-oji ajo̩ eka le̩, ku ma gamʼe̩do̩ Aro̩n e̩gba kʼi anyʼejefu o̩gba Jihofa; abe̩le̩ Aro̩n ane̩ ajo̩ amo̩ma Israe̩l nʼe̩do̩-wñ o̩gba Jihofa o̩ko̩ko̩lo̩.
Uwe̩ ki la nʼe̩wñ odufa chʼotogbo todu e̩fo̩d le̩.
O̩fa-wñ ugbo kʼoji atunyʼu adʼalumeji-wñ; ma ada o̩jaja gamʼo̩fa-wñ; o̩fa-wñ adab otogbo ebije ku ma du jogu ki we enʼugbo kiafana.
E̩ ki la nʼe̩wñ odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa fʼe̩ro po̩me̩grane̩t po̩me̩grane̩t ronyʼeti e̩re̩ otogbo le̩ daka, ilo e-o̩jamalia akpe̩gwa nyʼu daka,
ilo o̩jamalia kpai e̩ro po̩me̩grane̩t, ilo o̩jamalia kpai e̩ro po̩me̩grane̩t aronyʼeti otogbo le̩ o̩gane̩ daka.
E-le̩ adʼo̩la Aro̩n e̩gba kʼi ache e̩wñ ñw O̩jo̩, ma la agbo̩ uko̩la-wñ e̩gba kʼi anyi ef uña kiafo̩ o̩gba Jihofa, kpai e̩gba kʼi adufu kwʼo̩mo̩ wa, tode̩gba kʼi aku.
Tak uwe̩ ki fʼo̩jamalia ki de̩ hiolo gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ okokolo, kʼe̩ la fʼina ko̩ nyʼu alu ku ma kʼina nyʼe̩wñ uhiuko̩, kakini, Efo̩ ñwu Jihofa.
Tak uwe̩ anʼo̩jaja odufa dʼe-le̩ gamʼalawoni, o̩gba alawoni i ade̩.
I la ade̩ o̩gbo-ji Aro̩n, oñ Aro̩n anʼudu du ku ma fe̩ ugbo e̩wñ kiafo̩ ku ma ko wa, owñ chʼe-kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l achʼo kiafo̩ ef ele-ma kiafo̩ du; e-le̩ adʼo̩gboji-wñ o̩ko̩ko̩lo̩, ku ma gba ma o̩gba Jihofa.
Uwe̩ la anʼukpo line̩n ki chʼe̩hi reju gʼafe̩ e̩kina; e̩ ki laño̩ nʼukpo line̩n ki chʼe̩hi reju che alawoni; tak e̩ fʼe̩wñ ujiñmi ku ma chiya nyʼu ba.
E̩ ki laño̩ chʼafe̩ kpai e̩wñ ujiñmi kpai o̩tajiya ki gbo̩gba tod amo̩ma Aro̩n ge̩; kʼi chʼojima kpai alifia ñw u.
Uwe̩ ki ko e̩wñ le̩ nyʼo̩la Aro̩n, o̩maye-we̩, kpai o̩la amo̩ma-wñ aboke̩le̩ manyʼowñ, tak uwe̩ ki bʼekpo tʼuma oji, kʼe̩ la ko e̩wñ nyʼuma o̩wo̩ e̩ko̩, kʼe̩ fʼuma o̩la gwo rinyo̩ ku ma fo̩ ku ma chʼamatama ku ma che e̩wñ ñwu mi.
Uwe̩ ki la ga ichaka line̩n efufu ñwu ma kʼi bʼo̩re̩la ofo-ma ma; i ate̩ kwʼago kad uta;
e-le̩ adʼago Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩gba ku ma gudu tef unyabo e-ujeju le̩, abe̩k e̩gba ku ma te̩me̩rʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ku ma che e̩wñ ef uña kiafo̩; tode̩gba ku ma fʼudu fa bʼo̩la-ma ma ku ma ku. E-le̩ achʼuhio̩me̩ ogbegbele̩ tod owñ, kpai todu ugbe̩-wñ ubi-wñ aro̩ne aro̩ne ge̩.
Ma kʼe̩wñ nyʼamatama o̩wo̩ e̩ko̩
E̩wñ kʼuwe̩ la ache ñwu ma kʼe̩ je̩ ñwu ma fo̩ ku ma ki chʼamatama ku ma ki che e̩wñ ñwu mi de̩. E̩ mʼo̩mokuno̩ e-o̩ko̩ʼka kpai okolo meji ki mufu kpa,
kpai uje̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma do̩ n, kpai akala ki ma nʼo̩jo̩wu n kʼekpo kpe̩gwa nyʼu kpai okpukpulu ki ma ne̩ o̩jo̩wu n kʼekpo che̩ba tʼoji-wñ. Omu wit te̩ke̩te̩ke̩ oñ e̩ du che.
Tak e̩ kʼo jʼef agbaʼka kʼe̩ ne̩ ef agba le̩ wa jo̩ manyʼo̩kokuno̩ kpai okolo meji le̩.
E̩ ki la kʼAro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ wa alo̩na unyabo ujeju le̩, kʼe̩ la nʼomiofo fʼuma o̩la gwe̩.
Tak e̩ mʼe̩wñ o̩la le̩ ko kʼe̩ dʼafe̩-wñ tʼo̩la Aro̩n kpai otogbo e̩fo̩d kpai e̩fo̩d kpai e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma, kʼe̩ la nʼujiñmi e̩fo̩d jiʼi ago-wñ;
tak e̩ mʼalawo̩ni le̩ du dʼoji-wñ, kʼe̩ mʼike̩be̩ kiafo̩ le̩ du gamʼalawo̩ni le̩.
Tak e̩ mʼe̩kpo ku ma ba tʼone̩ oji le̩ du, oñ e̩ mʼu du danyʼoji-wñ, kʼe̩ dʼu kulʼu o̩la.
Tak e̩ kʼamo̩ma-wñ wa kʼe̩ kʼafe̩ nyʼuma o̩la,
oñ e̩ mʼe̩wñ ujago ko lʼuma ago de, owñ chʼAro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ, tak e̩ kʼo̩tajiya ki gbo̩gba le̩ do ma oji; abe̩le̩ o̩da atama ache e-ma lugbo uhio̩me̩ ogbegbele̩. Abe̩le̩ uwe̩ akʼe̩wñ nyʼAro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ o̩wo̩ e̩ko̩.
Tak uwe̩ anʼo̩kokuno̩ le̩ wa o̩gba unyabo ujeju. Oñ Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ ako o̩wo̩-ma nʼoji o̩kokuno̩ le̩,
tak uwe̩ akpa o̩kokuno̩ le̩ o̩gba Jihofa, ugbo alugbo̩na unyabo ujeju le̩.
Tak e̩ che kwef e̩bie̩ o̩kokuno̩ kʼe̩ nʼo̩ma o̩wo̩-we̩ du kulu igba ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩, tak e̩ kʼe̩bie̩-wñ kibo̩ dajane̩ e̩re̩ ubo̩ iche̩bo̩.
Tak e̩ mʼula du ki jʼo̩la ifi-wñ ko kpai udo̩nare-wñ, kpai ekpili-wñ meji manyʼula-wñ, kʼe̩ fʼe-le̩ gujo oj ubo̩ iche̩bo̩.
Ama e̩la o̩kokuno̩ le̩ kpai año̩-wñ kpai echu-wñ, uwe̩ anʼuna gu e-le̩ jo ej o̩do̩da uru; e̩wñ ku ma du wa tod adure i che.
Tak uwe̩ ki mʼokolo le̩ʼka du, oñ Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ akʼo̩wo̩-ma nʼoji okolo le̩,
tak uwe̩ ki fʼokolo le̩ kpa, kʼe̩ la mʼe̩bie̩-wñ du kʼe̩ du tafio̩ ugbo du o̩la ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩.
Tak uwe̩ ki fʼokolo le̩ kwu, kʼe̩ fʼifu-wñ kpai e̩re̩-wñ gwe̩, kʼe̩ ko jʼugbo e̩la-wñ ki bo̩ manyʼoji-wñ,
kʼe̩ fʼo̩gbo̩dudu okolo le̩ gujo oj ubo̩ iche̩bo̩; e̩wñ e̩gujo ku ma du wa ki ate̩gu tʼugbo Jihofa i che; e̩wñ ki akpo kʼi chʼe̩wñ ku ma du wa ñwu Jihofa lef una i che.
Tak e̩ mʼokolo ekeji le̩ du; oñ Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ akʼo̩wo̩-ma nʼoji okolo e-le̩,
tak uwe̩ akpa okolo le̩, kʼe̩ fʼe̩bie̩-wñ che pe̩ kʼe̩ du kad o̩fe̩fe̩ne̩ eti e-Aro̩n awo̩to̩ kpai o̩fe̩fe̩ne̩ eti amo̩ma-wñ awo̩to̩, kpai o̩monu o̩wo̩-ma awo̩to̩, kpai o̩monu e̩re̩-ma awo̩to̩, tak e̩ dʼe̩bie̩ kibo̩ tafio̩ ugbo du o̩la ubo̩ iche̩bo̩.
Tak e̩ che kwef e̩bie̩ ki dʼoj ubo̩ iche̩bo̩, kpai ekpo eba kʼe̩ du tafio̩ o̩la Aro̩n, kpai e̩wñ o̩la-wñ; kpai o̩la amo̩ma-wñ, kpai e̩wñ o̩la amo̩ma-wñ manyʼu; tak owñ kpai e̩wñ o̩la-wñ kpai amo̩ma-wñ, kpai e̩wñ o̩la amo̩ma-wñ manyʼu afo̩.
Uwe̩ ki ño̩ mʼula okolo le̩ du kpai otihi-wñ ki yoyo kpai ula ki dʼo̩la ifi-wñ kpai udo̩nare-wñ kpai ekpili-wñ meji manyʼula ki dʼo̩la-wñ kpai uta-wñ awo̩to̩ (todu okolo eko nyʼo̩wo̩ e̩ko̩ i che),
kpai odukulu uje̩wñʼka kpai akala kekeleʼka kʼekpo dʼoji-wñ kpai okpukpuluʼka kwef agba uje̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma do̩ n kʼi gugu o̩gba Jihofa le̩;
e̩ ki la mʼo̩gbo̩dudu e̩wñ-i ko nyʼAro̩n o̩wo̩, kpai amo̩ma-wñ, kʼe̩ kʼo nyʼate̩ amiejo, kʼi chʼe̩wñ eduwa emiejo o̩gba Jihofa.
Tak e̩ mʼu gba bʼo̩wo̩-ma te̩ kʼe̩ fʼu gujo oj ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ manyʼe̩wñ eduwa gujo le̩, kʼi chʼe̩wñ ki akpo o̩gba Jihofa; e̩wñ ku ma du wa ñwu Jihofa lef una i che.
Tak uwe̩ amʼache̩do̩ okolo Aro̩n ki chʼe-kʼi ko nyʼo̩wo̩ e̩ko̩ le̩ du, kʼe̩ miejo o̩gba Jihofa kʼi che e̩wñ eduwa miejo; e-le̩ la achʼukpe̩ e-we̩.
Tak uwe̩ ache kʼache̩do̩ e̩la eduwa miejo le̩ kpai o̩wo̩ e̩la ku ma du nyʼate̩ kʼi fo̩, owñ chʼe-ku ma miejo ku ma la du nyʼate̩ kwef okolo eko nyʼo̩wo̩ e̩ko̩ le̩, tʼe-Aro̩n, tʼe-amo̩ma-wñ.
E-le̩ ado̩mo̩ ñw Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ, kʼi chʼe̩wñ uhio̩me̩-ma ogbegbe̩le̩ kwugbo amo̩ma Israe̩l; todu e̩wñ edu nyʼate̩ i che; i achʼe̩wñ ku ma du nyʼate̩ kwef e̩la iche̩bo̩ kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l ako wa chʼe̩wñ ure̩do̩ kʼi chʼe̩wñ-ma ku ma du nyʼate̩ ñwu Jihofa.
Oñ e̩wñ o̩la Aro̩n kiafo̩ le̩ ado̩mo̩ ñw amo̩ma-wñ ubi-wñ ge̩, ku ma ko̩ nyʼo̩la ku ma bʼekpo̩ tʼuma oji kʼi ño̩ dʼo̩la-ma e̩gba ku ma kʼe̩wñ le̩ nyʼuma o̩wo̩ e̩ko̩.
O̩ma ki chʼatama koji-wñ akʼo nyʼo̩la o̩jo̩ mebie e̩gba kʼi awa ef unyabo ujeju kʼi ache e̩wñ ef uña kiafo̩ le̩.
Uwe̩ ki la dʼe̩la okolo ku ma ko nyʼo̩wo̩ e̩ko̩ le̩, kʼe̩ fʼe̩la-wñ hi ugbo kiafo̩;
tak Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ ajʼalugbo̩na unyabo ujeju aje̩ e̩la okolo le̩ kpai uje̩wñ ki jʼef agba-wñ.
Ma la aje̩ e̩wñ ku ma ne̩ chʼe̩wñ uboma le̩, ku ma ko nyʼuma o̩wo̩ e̩ko̩ ku ma laño̩ che ma ku ma fo̩. E̩ne̩ ejaduña muda aje̩ e-le̩ n, todu i afo̩.
I la che̩wñ kʼe̩la ku ma ko nyʼuma o̩wo̩ e̩ko̩ abe̩k uje̩wñ le̩ bo̩ nyʼodudu, e̩gba le̩ e̩ ki fʼabubo̩-wñ gujo ef una; ma ki je̩ e-le̩ n, todu i afo̩.
Abe̩le̩ uwe̩ ache ñw Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ, owñ chʼalu du kʼomi ñwa ñw e̩ le̩; o̩jo̩ mebie e̩ kʼe̩wñ nyʼuma o̩wo̩ e̩ko̩,
o̩jo̩ du e̩ ki du o̩kokuno̩ wa chʼiche̩bo̩ adure kʼi chʼe̩wñ eboma. Uwe̩ ki ño̩ gwʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩ rinyo̩ e̩gba kʼe̩ che e̩wñ uboma todu-wñ; kʼe̩ la fʼekpo ba tʼo̩la-wñ kʼe̩ che kʼi fo̩.
E̩ ki che e̩wñ uboma todu ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩ o̩jo̩ mebie kʼe̩ che kʼi fo̩, tak ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ afo̩ e-efo̩; e̩wñ du ki akadʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩ afo̩.
E̩wñ kʼuwe̩ la adu wa chʼiche̩bo̩ oj ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩ de̩: amo̩mala meji ku ma chʼo̩ma o̩do̩ʼka o̩do̩ʼka, e̩ ko wa che o̩jo̩ñwa o̩jo̩ñwa o̩ko̩ko̩lo̩.
E̩ ki du o̩malaʼka wa che odudu, e̩ la dʼo̩mala ekeji wa che e̩gba ane̩;
ukpe̩gwa e̩ñwa omu ku ma no̩ te̩ke̩te̩ke̩ kʼukpe̩ e̩ke̩le̩ ekpo ku ma de̩ amanyʼo̩malaʼka, kpai ukpe̩ke̩le̩ omi achiwebe̩te̩ma todu omi edarane̩.
Tak e̩ dʼo̩mala ekeji le̩ wa che e̩gba ane̩, kʼe̩ kʼe̩wñ ele kpai omi edarane̩-wñ wa manyʼu alu kʼe̩ che odudu le̩, kʼi kpo e̩rinyo̩, kʼi chʼe̩wñ eduwa ku ma che lugbo una ñwu Jihofa.
E-le̩ ache e̩wñ eduwa gujo o̩ko̩ko̩lo̩ gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-me̩ ugbo alugbo̩na unyabo ujeju o̩gba Jihofa, ugbo kʼomi kpai uwe̩ ade, kʼu nako̩la ñwe̩ o̩mo̩.
O̩mo̩ omi kpai amo̩ma Israe̩l ade, o̩mo̩ le̩ afo̩ lugbo ojima-mi;
nache kʼunyabo ujeju kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ki fo̩; naño̩ che kʼAro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ ku ma fo̩, ku ma chʼamatama ku ma che e̩wñ ñwu mi.
Tak u nagugu ef amo̩ma Israe̩l kʼu la achʼO̩jo̩-ma.
Tak ama ama ka kʼomi che Jihofa, O̩jo̩-ma kʼi ko ma kwʼane̩ Ijipti dufu, kʼu gugu efu-ma; omi che Jihofa, O̩jo̩-ma.
Ubo̩ otulale egujo kpai ukpachi ugwo̩wo̩ ku ma nʼebije ikpa che
Uwe̩ ki ño̩ fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ che ku ma gu e̩wñ ki akpo jo oji-wñ; oli akesia oñ uwe̩ ane̩ che.
Ujiji-wñ ki chʼo̩hibo̩wo̩ʼka, unabe̩-wñ ki la chʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka; ago̩go̩-wñ me̩le̩ ki chʼokujo̩; o̩gba-wñ ki la chʼohibo̩wo̩ meji; igba-wñ ki chʼalu okate kpai owñ.
E̩ ki la kʼo̩jamalia ki de̩ hiolo lamʼo̩la-wñ, tʼoji-wñ, tʼakolo-wñ daka, kpai igba-wñ; tak uwe̩ ki fʼo̩jamalia gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ kʼe̩ dʼu lamʼeti-wñ daka.
E̩ ki laño̩ che elika meji todu-wñ o̩gane̩ o̩jamalia pe̩te̩ke̩ kʼe̩ du lamʼo̩ le̩, akolo-wñ meji eji e̩ che jo̩; e-le̩ achʼugbo ku ma dʼugbo̩lo̩ oli tunyʼu ku ma ne̩.
E̩ ki la dʼoli akesia che ugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩, kʼe̩ dʼo̩jamalia wenyʼu.
Tak e̩ mʼu du dago o̩gba ukpo ugbeju e-kʼi dʼugbo akpati ibenu le̩, o̩gba ugugu unye̩-do̩ kʼi bʼoji e̩wñ ibenu le̩ ma, ugbo kʼomi ade kpai uwe̩.
Tak Aro̩n akʼe̩wñ kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ ki akpo wa gujo oji-wñ; odudu du e̩gba kʼAro̩n do̩mo̩ añwʼagege che, e̩gba le̩ i agu e̩wñ e̩kpo le̩ jo oji-wñ,
oñ ane̩ odu e̩gba kʼAro̩n adʼuna tʼagege le̩ i ñʼagujo kʼi mud e̩wñ ki akpo o̩gba Jihofa gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-me̩ o̩ko̩ko̩lo̩.
E̩ ki kʼe̩wñ ejaduña ki akpo kpai e̩wñ egujo n kpai e̩wñ ele wa che ki te̩gu kwʼoji-wñ n; e̩ ki la dʼe̩wñ wa danyʼoji-wñ n.
Aro̩n la achʼe̩wñ e̩boma oj igba-wñ onuʼka o̩do̩ʼka; i anʼe̩bie̩ e̩wñ ku ma duwa tod adure e-e̩wñ e̩boma le̩ che e̩wñ e̩boma todu-wñ onuʼka o̩do̩ʼka gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-me̩; e̩wñ efo̩ e-efo̩ todu Jihofa i che.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
E̩gba kʼe̩ kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l aluka, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ adʼe̩wn ulʼoji o̩la-wñ tane̩ ñwu Jihofa e̩gba kʼe̩ kʼuma aluka todu kʼe̩wñ bie̩ne̩ ki we ebʼuma ma e̩gba kʼe̩ kʼuma aluka.
E̩wñ kʼe̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ku ma kaluka adu wa de̩: ukpe̩reji she̩ke̩l alu ki she̩ke̩l e-uña kiafo̩ de̩ (she̩ke̩l le̩ che gera ogu), ukpe̩reji she̩ke̩l kʼi chʼe̩wñ edu nyʼate̩ ñwu Jihofa.
E̩ne̩ du kʼo̩do̩-wñ jo̩ ogu ef abo ku ma kaluka le̩, adu e̩wñ edu nyʼate̩ ñwu Jihofa le̩ wa.
Anana aduwa tule n, e̩nubie̩ aduwa ki anyaru ukpe̩reji she̩ke̩l le̩ e̩gba ku me̩ kʼe̩wñ ku me̩ du nyʼate̩ le̩ wa ñwu Jihofa le̩ ku me̩ chʼe̩wñ e̩boma tod amonugo-me̩ n.
Uwe̩ la agbʼo̩ko̩ e̩boma le̩ kwʼo̩wo̩ amo̩ma Israe̩l, kʼe̩ la kʼo̩ko̩ le̩ jo̩ todu uko̩lo̩ unyabo ujeju; todu ki chʼe̩wñ urewa amo̩ma Israe̩l o̩gba Jihofa, kʼame̩ ki che e̩wñ e̩boma todu onugo-me̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
Uwe̩ ki ño̩ dʼebijeikpa che ukpachi ugwʼo̩wo̩ kpai e̩wñ kʼi agugu oji-wñ, o̩mo̩ ma agwʼo̩wo̩. E̩ ki dʼe-le̩ gugu agbagba unyabo ujeju kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩, kʼe̩ la chʼomiofo nyʼu,
Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ agwe̩ o̩wo̩-ma kpai e̩re̩-ma o̩mo̩.
E̩gba kuma nyʼef unyabo ujeju kpai e̩gba ku ma te̩me̩rʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ku ma che e̩wñ egujo ñwu Jihofa ama anʼomiofo agwe̩ ku ma we eku.
Abe̩le̩ ma agwe̩ o̩wo̩-ma kpai e̩re̩-ma ku ma we eku: e-ie̩ achʼuhio̩me̩ o̩gbegbele̩, owñ chʼe-wñ kpai e-ugbe̩-wñ gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-ma.
Jihofa ño̩ ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
Uwe̩ ki mʼe̩wñ ido̩ro̩ e-o̩me̩me̩le̩ ko: e-mur kʼi chʼomi kʼi chʼalu she̩ke̩l oli me̩gwa, e-sinamo̩n ki akpo ki chʼukpe̩reji alu le̩, owñ chʼoli me̩lu, e-kalamus ki akpo ki chʼalu she̩ke̩l oli me̩lu,
e̩kasia la chʼalu oli me̩gwa, e̩ñwa-wñ chʼalu ku she̩ke̩l e-uña kiafo̩ de̩, kpai ekpo o̩lif e̩ñwa hin oka;
e̩ kʼe-le̩ che ekpo kiafo̩ ku ma du ba tʼo̩la e̩wñ, ma agwe̩gwa nyʼomune̩ alu kʼabo ku ma chʼo̩ka otulale ache; ekpo efo̩ ku ma ba tʼe̩wñ o̩la i che.
Uwe̩ ki dʼe-le̩ kulu o̩la unyabo ujeju kpai akpati ibenu le̩,
kpai itebulu kpai ane̩-wñ chaka, kpai akete manyʼane̩-wñ chaka, kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ugbo ku ma gu e̩wñ ki akpo jo le̩,
kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e-e̩wñ e̩gujo oji-wñ le̩ manyʼane̩-wñ du, kpai ukpachi ugwo̩-wo̩ kpai e̩wñ kʼi gugu oji-wñ le̩;
uwe̩ la ache e̩wñ le̩ du ki fo̩, kʼi mud, e̩wñ ki afo̩ e̩-efo̩; e̩wñ du ki kado abʼe-le̩ afo̩.
Uwe̩ ki la fʼekpo ba tʼo̩la Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, kʼe̩ che ma ku ma fo̩, ku ma chʼamatama kʼama ki che e̩wñ ñwu mi.
Tak uwe̩ ki ka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l kakini, E-kide̩ achʼekpo kiafo̩ todu mi ku ma ba tʼe̩wñ o̩la gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-me̩.
Ma adʼe-le̩ danyʼaño̩la one̩ n, me̩ ki la che e̩go̩-wñ n, owñ chʼugbo e̩wñ ki jʼefu-wñ; efo̩ i afo̩, e̩wñ ki afo̩ i ache ñwu me̩.
E̩ne̩ ki fʼe̩go̩-wñ che, abe̩k e̩ne̩ du kʼi mʼu du tʼo̩la e̩ne̩ ejaduña re, ma akʼe̩ne̩ le̩ da bʼamone̩-wñ te̩.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Mʼe̩wñ ido̩ro ki akpo ko, owñ che stakte̩ kpai onicha kpai gal-ba-num, e̩wñ ido̩ro̩ ki akpo le̩ manyu frankinse̩ns ki de̩ hiolo, (e̩ñwa e̩le̩ e̩le̩-wñ achʼokujo̩)
kʼe̩ mʼe-le̩ ko che e̩wñ ku ma gujo ki akpo ku ma che likpa alu kʼabo ku ma chʼo̩ka otulale ache, omu ki chʼe̩burʼu, i de̩ hiolo, i la fo̩;
e̩ bu kwefu-wñ kʼe̩ fʼu gwu ne̩ke̩ne̩ke̩ kʼe̩ dʼu kwefu-wñ tʼo̩gba e̩wñ ibenu ef unyabo ujeju ugbo kʼomi ade kpai uwe̩; e̩wñ ki afo̩ e-efo̩ ñwu me̩ i che.
Oñ e̩wñ ku me̩ che ku me̩ gujo kʼi akpo le̩, me̩ ki che e̩go̩-wñ alu ki gwe̩gwanyʼomune̩ ñw o̩la-me̩ n; e̩wñ kiafo̩ ñwu Jihofa ugbo me̩ i che̩.
E̩ne̩ du ki ache e̩go̩ e-le̩, kʼi gbo̩ e̩kpo-wñ, ma akʼe̩ne̩ le̩ da bʼamone̩-wñ te̩.
Ma chi Be̩zale̩l kpai Oholiab tod uko̩lo̩ unyabo
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
Go, omi fʼodu Be̩zale̩l o̩ma Uri, o̩ma He̩r kʼi chʼabo o̩lo̩pu Juda do̩.
Omi la je̩ ñw u kpe̩ko̩ ñw Afu O̩jo̩, kpai ibe kpai oji o̩la ema kpai e̩wñ ema kpai emeju uko̩lo̩ e̩wñ ojoji ojoji du eche,
kʼi ñwa uko̩lo̩ o̩ka, kʼi che uko̩lo̩ o̩jamalia kpai ajifa kpai ebijeikpa,
kpai okuta eda ku ma du tunyʼe̩wñ, kpai igbo oli efa, kʼi chʼuko̩lo̩ ojoji ojoji du.
E̩ la go, omi fʼOholiab, o̩ma Ahisamak, kʼi chʼabo o̩lo̩pu Dan, chi manyʼu, u laño̩ dʼibe tʼibe tef e̩do̩ amone̩ chaka ku ma nʼibe efu, ku ma ki che e̩wñ du kʼomi ñwa ñw e̩:
unyabo ujeju kpai akpati ibenu kpai ugugu unye̩do̩ kʼi dʼoji-wñ kpai ane̩ unyabo le̩ chaka
kpai itebulu le̩ kpai ane̩-wñ kpai akete hiolo le̩ manyʼane̩-wñ chaka kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ku ma gu e̩wñ kʼi akpo jo oji-wñ
kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e̩wñ egujo manyʼane̩-wñ chaka kpai ukpachi ugwo̩wo̩ kpai e̩wñ ki agugu oji-wñ
kpai otogbo ku ma hi reju kpai otogbo e-efo̩ todu Aro̩n, atama le̩, kpai otogbo amo̩ma-wñ, ku ma ne̩ che e̩wñ atama,
kpai ekpo ku ma ba tʼo̩la kpai otulale ki akpo todu uña kiafo̩. Likpa alu du kʼomi ñwa ñw e̩, ama ki che.
O̩jo̩ uñmi ede
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
Uwe̩ ki ño̩ ka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l kakini, Ame̩ ki fʼo̩jo̩ uñmi-mi de chuu, todu owñ chʼujiwe ki tʼagbagba omi kpai ame̩ gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-me̩, todu kʼame̩ ki ma ka kʼomi, Jihofa, ache me̩ ku me̩ fo̩.
Abe̩le̩ ame̩ ade o̩jo̩ uñmi, todu i afo̩ todu me̩; e̩ne̩ du ki fʼu daji, ekpa ma akpa; e̩ne̩ du kʼi fʼuko̩lo̩ʼka che o̩jo̩ le̩, ma akʼonugo e̩ne̩ le̩ da bʼamone̩-wñ te̩.
O̩jo̩ me̩fa oñ ma achʼuko̩lo̩ kade; o̩jo̩ e̩kebie-wñ muda chʼo̩jo̩ uñmi e-uñmi kiafo̩ todu Jihofa; e̩ne̩ du ki fʼuko̩lo̩ du che o̩jo̩ uñmi, ekpa ma akpa.
Todule̩ oñ amo̩ma Israe̩l ade o̩jo̩ uñmi, ku ma dejute̩ o̩jo̩ uñmi gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-ma, kʼi mud alo ekpe̩ ogbegbele̩.
Owñ chʼujiwe ki tʼagbagba omi kpai amo̩ma Israe̩l ogbegbele̩, todu o̩jo̩ me̩fa Jihofa che efojale kpai ane̩-ile̩, tak i ñmi o̩jo̩ e̩kebie, oñ i rʼiñmi.
E̩gba kʼi fʼoluka che kpai Mose̩s oj uwo Sainai kpa, i la mʼalo ibenu meji le̩ ko ñw u, alo okuta i che, o̩wo̩ O̩jo̩ ko̩.
Abo Israe̩l dojikane̩ ñw o̩mokuno̩ o̩jamalia
Tak e̩gba kʼamone̩ le̩ li ka ku Mose̩s kpo̩kpe̩ egwo̩ru kwʼoj uwo wʼane̩, amone̩ le̩ fʼo̩la-ma do̩ jeju wʼugbo Aro̩n, oñ ma ka ñw u kakini, Kwane̩, kʼe̩ fʼamo̩jo̩ che ñw a, kʼama ki tʼuwa o̩gba; i chʼe-Mose̩s kʼi ko wa kwʼane̩ Ijipti dufu wa-i, a mema abu kʼi le n.
Tak Aro̩n ka ñwu ma kakini, Fʼile̩li o̩jamalia ki dʼeti amo̩ya-me̩ kpai e-amo̩ma-me̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ kpai onobule̩ le̩ jada ku me̩ mʼu ko wa ñwu mi.
Abe̩le̩ amone̩ le̩ chaka fʼile̩li o̩jamalia ki dʼeti-ma jada, oñ ma mʼu ko wʼugbo Aro̩n.
Tak i mʼu gba kwʼo̩wo̩-ma oñ abu kʼi fʼu da o̩ma okuno̩, i la nʼadude̩ fʼina-wñ ko̩. Taku ma kakini, Abo Israe̩l, amo̩jo̩-me̩ ku ma ko me̩ kwʼane̩ Ijipti dufu wa de̩!
Oñ abu kʼAro̩n li, i fʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ne o̩gba-wñ; tak Aro̩n fʼakoya-wñ ta kakini, O̩na chʼuje̩wñ uyo̩ ñwu Jihofa.
Taku ma takpa kwane̩ o̩jo̩ñwa-wñ, oñ ma mʼe̩wñ e̩gujo kowa che, ma ño̩ kʼe̩wñ ure̩do̩ wa ge̩; oñ amone̩ le̩ gugu ane̩ ku ma je̩ e̩wñ ku ma ñmo̩, taku ma kwane̩ achiya.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Gwo̩ru tane̩ alo; todu amone̩-we̩, kʼuwe̩ ko kwʼane̩ Ijipti dufu wa le̩, fʼo̩la-ma kpabie̩ me̩;
ma hika muna bʼo̩na kʼomi ñwa ñwu ma te̩ piopio-i; ma fʼo̩ma okuno̩ da ñw o̩la-ma, oñ ma dojikane̩ ñw u, ma la fʼe̩wñ e̩bie̩ kpa ñw u; oñ ma kakini, Ame̩ abo Israe̩l, amo̩jo̩-me̩ ku ma ko me̩ kwo ane̩ Ijipti dufu wa jo̩-i!
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, U fʼamone̩-i li me̩, e̩ la go, amone̩ ku ma fʼo̩lo̩-ma lo dago, ma che;
todule̩ ifai, e̩ tʼumi no̩ kʼuwe̩do̩-mi ki tajo bʼuma ma una una, todu kʼu fʼuma lie̩. Tak u nadʼuwe̩ chʼuche̩ amone̩ ki wewe.
Mose̩s muda gbo̩ko̩bo̩ Jihofa, O̩jo̩-wñ, oñ i kakini, O Jihofa, e̩wñ chi kʼuwe̩do̩-we̩ mutajo bʼamone̩-we̩ e-kʼuwe̩ nʼukpahiu ki nana kpai o̩wo̩ ki gbiti ko ma kwʼane̩ Ijipti wa ma una una-i taa?
E̩wñ chi kʼabo Ijipti aka kakini, Todu ibe bie̩ne̩ ki dʼefu-wñ oñ i ko ma dufu, kʼi fʼuma kpa oj uwo oj uwo kʼi la fʼuma lie̩ bʼeju ane̩ ile̩ te̩? Murida bʼuwe̩do̩-we̩ ki kpuna-i te̩, kʼe̩bie̩ne̩-i eche amone̩-we̩ ki wʼe̩.
E̩ nalibekado Ebraham kpai Aise̩k kpai Israe̩l, amadu-we̩ le̩, e-kʼuwe̩ fʼo̩la-we̩ onugo go̩ ñwu ma, kʼe̩ la ka ñwu ma kakini, Naje̩ ñw ugbe̩-me̩ wewe nyo̩gba dab awo awo ojale, oñ ane̩ kʼomi ko̩la-wñ-i du nadu ñw ugbe̩-me̩, tak i achʼe̩wñ ogu-ma ogbegbele̩.
Tak i wo̩ Jihofa ugbo e̩bie̩ne̩ kʼi nʼibe ka kʼi ache amone̩-wñ le̩.
Taku Mose̩s murida gwo̩ru uwo le̩ tane̩, alo ibenu meji le̩ jʼo̩wo̩-wñ, alo ki chʼe̩ko̩ eju mejeji i che; o̩wo̩ʼka-wñ kpʼo̩wo̩ ekeji-wñ che̩ko̩.
Alo le̩ la chʼuko̩lo̩ kʼO̩jo̩ che, ina-wñ la chʼina kʼO̩jo̩ ko̩, ina-wñ chewane̩ o̩la alo le̩.
Taku Jo̩shua gbʼekuku amone̩ ku ma jʼakpogu le̩ oñ i ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Ekuku ogu dʼef uru-wa-i.
Oñ i kakini, I chʼo̩ga echi todu edu ku ma du n, i la chʼogu ekpa todu edu ku ma du ma n; chai ekuku abo ku ma jʼa-keli oñ nagbo̩-i.
Tak i lewatu, abu kʼi lewa me̩ru uru le̩ ababa, kʼi la fʼo̩mokuno̩ ku ma da le̩ li kpai ido ku ma jʼata, uwe̩do̩ Mose̩s mutajo, oñ i mʼa lo le̩ ko rikpolo bʼo̩wo̩-wñ te̩, i la fʼu kpo̩fo̩ e̩re̩ uwo o̩mo̩.
Tak i mʼo̩mokuno̩ ku ma da le̩ du, i la fʼu gujo ef una, tak i fʼu no̩ efulu, oñ i fʼu buru ej omi, tak i je̩ ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l ñmʼo̩.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw Aro̩n kakini, Ab amone̩-i chʼe̩ kʼe̩ fʼadure inaina-i fa bʼuma oji ma taa?
Tak Aro̩n kakini, Uwe̩do̩ odu-mi ki tajo n; uwe̩ chema amone̩-i, kʼe̩do̩-ma chʼe-kado e̩wñ e̩bie̩ne̩ eche.
Todu, ama ka ñwu mi kakini, Fʼamo̩jo̩ che ñw a, ku ma atʼuwa o̩gba; todu i chʼe-Mose̩s kʼi ko wa kwʼane̩ Ijipti dufu wa le̩, a mema abu kʼowñ le n.
Tak u ka ñwu ma kakini, E̩ne̩ du ki nʼo̩jamalia kʼi fʼu jada wa; taku ma mʼu ko wa ñwu mi, oñ u mʼu ko rikpolo nyʼuna, tak o̩mokuno̩-i kwʼo̩mo̩ dufu wa.
Tak e̩gba ku Mose̩s li kʼamone̩ le̩ mʼofe-ma du tʼo̩fe̩ (todu Aro̩n je̩ ñwu ma dʼofe-ma tʼo̩fe̩ ki mud ubio̩la ugbo ame̩nebi-ma),
taku Mose̩s kwodago alaku uru le̩, oñ i kakini, E̩ne̩ chʼabo Jihofa? i kʼi wʼugbo mi. Tak o̩chaka amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Lifai fʼo̩la-ma do̩ jeju jʼugbo-wñ.
Tak i ka ñwu ma kakini, Abu ku Jihofa O̩jo̩ e-Israe̩l aka de̩ kakini, E̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ki dʼo̩kwo̩chageli-wñ tʼachala kʼi tʼalaku alaku ale ugbo du ef uru-i kʼe̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ki kpʼo̩maye-wñ, kʼe̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ki la kpa e̩ne̩ uma-wñ, kʼe̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ ki kpa ekeji-wñ.
Tak amo̩ma Lifai che tʼeju o̩la Mose̩s; Oku one̩ ki wane̩ o̩jo̩ le̩ dabu e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ me̩ta.
Mose̩s la ka kakini, Me̩ kʼe̩wñ nyʼo̩wo̩-me̩ e̩ko̩ todu Jihofa eñini-i, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ kobʼo̩ma-wñ kpai o̩maye-wñ; todu kʼi de̩nyo̩ ñwu me̩ eñini-i.
Oñ i lewatu o̩jo̩ñwa-wñ, Mose̩s ka ñw amone̩ le̩ kakini, Me̩ fʼadure inaina ta me̩. Ifai tak u nate̩gu nyʼugbo Jihofa; ikani i nʼe̩wñ kʼu nache kʼi abʼadure-me̩ ma.
Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s mudabi nyʼugbo Jihofa, i kakini, Aaya, amone̩-i fʼadure inaina ta me̩; ma la fʼamo̩jo̩ o̩jamalia che ñw o̩la-ma.
I muda che̩wñ ki dʼuwe̩ e̩do̩, e̩ dʼadure-ma tinyo̩; i ma dʼabe̩le̩ n, oko nagbabʼe̩-i, kʼe̩ ki fumi kpalu bʼef ibuku-we̩ kʼe̩ ko̩ le̩ te̩.
Jihofa muda ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩ne̩ kʼi du mi re, e̩ne̩ le̩ oñ nakpalu kwef ibuku-mi.
Lo fai, kʼe̩ ne̩ amone̩ le̩ nyʼugbo kʼu ko̩la ñw e̩ le̩; go, onuche̩-mi atʼuwe̩ o̩gba; ama o̩jo̩ kʼu nawa fejudo ma, nawa kpai adure-ma edu nʼuma oji.
Oñ Jihofa fʼamone̩ le̩ gwoda todabu ku ma fʼo̩mokuno̩ le̩ da, owñ chʼe-kʼAro̩n che le̩.
Mose̩s nachologu tod abo Israe̩l alo waa
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Kwo bʼemi te̩ alo, uwe̩ kpai amone̩ kʼe̩ ko kwʼane̩ Ijipti dufu wa le̩, kʼe̩ nyʼane̩ kʼomi go̩ ñw Ebraham kpai Aise̩k kpai Jeko̩b kakini, Ugbe̩-we̩ oñ nadʼu ñw u.
Omi la akpʼonuche̩ tʼuwe̩ o̩gba, oñ u nane abo Kenan kpai abo Amo̩r kpai abo He̩t kpai abo Pe̩re̩z kpai abo Hifai kpai abo Je̩bius bʼo̩mo̩ te̩.
E̩ ki mute̩gu nyʼane̩ ugbo kʼomi e̩nya kpai iño̩ acha; omi muda atʼalumeji-we̩ te̩gu alo n, tode̩gba kʼu fʼe̩ lie̩ ej o̩na le̩, todu uwe̩ chʼamone̩ kʼo̩lo̩-we̩ lo dago.
Tak e̩gba kʼamone̩ le̩ gbo̩ inabali e̩bie̩ne̩ ki de̩, ma kwodaido̩; e̩ne̩ du la kʼe̩wñ ijaga nyʼo̩la n.
Todu Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩ ka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l kakini, Ame̩ chʼamone̩ kʼo̩lo̩-ma chʼe̩lo dago; iche̩wñ kʼomi ma tʼalumeji-we̩ alo iminitiʼkate, u ma fʼe̩ lie̩. Todule̩ fai e̩ namʼe̩wñ ijaga-we̩ ko jane̩ bʼo̩la-we̩ te̩, kʼu fʼe̩wñ kʼu nachʼuwe̩ ma.
Todule̩ amo̩ma Israe̩l mʼe̩wñ ijaga-ma gwo̩ bʼo̩la-ma te̩ hioko, akwo uwo Ho̩re̩b le̩ gbogbo alo.
Mose̩s la te̩tafʼunyabo le̩ ta ejo̩do̩da uru-ma, owe-wñ kpai uru le̩ chete̩ jiji, oñ i dʼodu-wñ ko̩ Unyabo Ujeju. Oñ e̩ne̩ du ki tene Jihofa adufu nyʼugbo unyabo ujeju kʼi dʼo̩do̩da uru le̩.
Tak i lewatu, e̩gba du ku Mose̩s dufu nyʼugbo unyabo le̩, amone̩ le̩ chaka kwane̩, oñ e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ dago alugbo̩na unyabo e-wñ, ma la fʼeju-ma bu Mose̩s le, gbogbo tak i mugudu tef unyabo.
Oñ e̩gba ku Mose̩s mugudu tef unyabo, akpa ki dago waala le̩ nagwo̩ru wane̩ kʼi dago alugbo̩na unyabo, taku Jihofa ako̩la ñwu Mose̩s.
Oñ e̩gba kʼamone̩ le̩ du li abu kʼakpa le̩ dago waala alugbo̩na unyabo, amone̩ le̩ chaka nakwane̩ adojikane̩, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ che alugbo̩na unyabo e-wñ.
Abe̩le̩ eju kparʼeju oñ Jihofa ko̩la ñwu Mose̩s, alu kʼone̩ ako̩la kpai onuku-wñ. Tak i mudabi tef uru. Ama Jo̩shua o̩ma Nun, okolobia kʼi ache e̩wñ ñw u le̩, muda kwo bʼunyabo le̩ te̩ n.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñwu Jihofa kakini, Go ta, uwe̩ ka ñwu mi kakini, Mʼamone̩-i ko te̩gu wa; e̩ la je̩ ñwu mi ma e̩ne̩ kʼuwe̩ akpuche̩ lebʼumi n. E̩ la ka ñwu mi kakini, U chema uwe̩, u chema odu kʼe̩ ko, uwe̩ ño̩ chʼe̩ne̩ kʼu nali eju.
Todule̩ narodubʼuwe̩ fai, iche̩wñ kʼe̩ li mi eju, mak e̩ kʼo̩nʼO̩na-we̩ ña mi kʼomi ki fʼuwe̩ ma, kʼu ma alu kʼu nale kʼe̩ li mi eju. E̩ ki ño̩ fʼejuwo̩ ka kʼuche̩ amone̩-i chʼamone̩-we̩.
Tak i kakini, Eju-mi ale bʼuwe̩, oñ nadʼuñmi ñw e̩.
Tak i kakini, Iche̩wñ kʼeju-we̩ ma le bʼumi n, e̩ ki ne̩ wa kwʼemi alo n.
Todu lugbo e̩wñ oñ ma ama ka kʼe̩ li mi eju, omi kpai amone̩-we̩-i? I chʼef elo kʼe̩ lo kpai wa n? kʼomi kpai amone̩-we̩ kʼa chʼojoji ñw amone̩ du ku ma jʼoj ane̩ ile̩-i n?
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Omi ñʼache e̩wñ kʼuwe̩ ka-i ge̩; todu uwe̩ chʼe̩ne̩ kʼu nali eju, u la chema uwe̩, tʼodu kʼe̩ ko̩.
Tak i kakini, Nagbo̩ko̩bʼe̩, kʼe̩ dʼojima-we̩ ña mi.
Tak i kakini, Naje̩ ñw e̩nyo̩-mi chaka ki lale o̩gba-we̩, oñ nafʼodu-mi, Jihofa, do̩ o̩gba-we̩; omi la achʼufe̩de̩nyo̩ ñw e̩ne̩ ki du mi e̩do̩ kʼu chʼufe̩de̩nyo̩ ñw u, u la ali ejumomi e̩ne̩ ki du mi e̩do̩ kʼu nali ejumomi-wñ.
Ama, i kakini, E̩ neke li eju-mi n; todu one̩ ali mi kʼi adeju n.
Taku Jihofa kakini, Go, uñaʼka do̩mo̩ me̩ru mi ugbo kʼuwe̩ adago oj okuta omo̩;
oñ i awatu, abu kʼojima-mi alale, nadʼuwe̩ tef e̩kpana okuta le̩, tak u nadʼo̩wo̩-mi bʼe̩ ma gbogbo tak u lale;
tak u namʼo̩wo̩-mi du, oñ uwe̩ ali ubi-mi; ma muda ali eju-mi n.
O̩jo̩ dabi dʼalo-wñ le̩ nyʼane̩
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, Fʼalo okuta meji dab e-ejodudu le̩ gbe̩ ñw o̩la-we̩; tak omi adʼo̩la ki dʼo̩la alo ejodudu kʼe̩ kpo̩fo̩ le̩, ko̩ nyʼalo e-le̩.
E̩ fʼo̩la-we̩ mu nyʼodudu, kʼe̩ te̩gu wa oj uwo Sainai odudu, kʼonugo-we̩ ki dago kpenyu mi oj uwo omo̩.
E̩ne̩ du ki te̩gu wa kpai uwe̩ n, e̩ ki je̩ ñwu ma li e̩ne̩ du o̩la uwo le̩ ugbo du n; e̩ ki la je̩ ñw ame̩wño̩re̩ egini kpai amokuno̩ jije̩ e̩re̩ uwo le̩ n.
Taku Mose̩s fʼalo okuta meji gbe̩ dab e-ejodudu le̩; oñ i takpa kwane̩ odudu-wñ, i la mute̩gu tʼoj uwo Sainai alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñw u, alo okuta meji la jʼef o̩wo̩-wñ.
Taku Jihofa gwo̩ru ef akpa le̩ wane̩, i kwodago kpai owñ o̩mo̩, oñ i fʼodu Jihofa do̩ taa.
Jihofa tale o̩gba-wñ, oñ i nadudo̩ kakini, Jihofa, Jihofa, kʼi chʼO̩jo̩ kʼi ali one̩ ejumomi kʼi ali one̩ eju, i hika we̩do̩ n, ufe̩de̩nyo̩-wñ kpai ochochi-wñ chʼololo.
I ade ufe̩de̩nyo̩-wñ todu abo icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩, abu kʼi akʼudu kpai ada kpai adure rinyo̩ bʼone̩ o̩la te̩, kʼi muda adale ofofo kilikili n, i akʼudu kʼamata fe̩ nʼamo̩ma kpai amaaju-ma oji, gbogbo tʼo̩gba e̩ke̩ta kpai e̩ke̩le̩.
Taku Mose̩s hika dʼoji lo̩, i la dojikane̩.
Oñ i kakini, O Ondu, iche̩wñ kʼe̩ li mi eju, nagbo̩ko̩bʼe̩, Ondu ki tʼalumeji-wa alo; todu amone̩ kʼo̩lo̩-ma chʼelo dago ma che; tʼudu-wa kpai adure-wa no̩, kʼe̩ la mʼuwa ko chʼe̩wñ ogu-we̩.
Tak i kakini, Go, alo nakpe̩-i. Eju amone̩-we̩ du nache e̩wñ aye ku ma ma che e̩go̩-wñ ugbo du ile̩-i abe̩k ef uche̩ichi amone̩ mama ta n; oñ amone̩ du kʼe̩ dʼefu-ma le̩ ali uko̩lo̩ Jihofa; todu e̩wñ kʼu nache kpai uwe̩ chʼe̩wñ ubailo.
E̩ nafejutʼe̩wñ kʼu nañwa ñw e̩ eñini-i. Go, nanʼabo Amo̩r kpai abo Kenan kpai abo He̩t kpai abo Pe̩re̩z kpai abo Hifai kpai abo Je̩bius rinyo̩ bʼuwe̩ o̩gba te̩.
E̩ nafʼo̩la-we̩ de, tode̩gba kʼe̩ kpʼalo kpai abo ku ma dodo ane̩ ugbo kʼe̩ lo, tode̩gba kʼi amud oku te̩ alumeji-we̩.
Me̩ ki kpʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩-ma fo̩, me̩ ki fʼojibo-ma kpo̩fo̩ rinyo̩, me̩ ki fʼoli Ashe̩rim-ma lo̩ wane̩ 14(todu uwe̩ ñʼadojikane̩ ñw o̩jo̩ omune̩ du n, todu Jihofa, kʼodu-wñ ko̩ Ajogu, owñ chʼO̩jo̩ ajogu),
tode̩gba kʼe̩ kpʼalo kpai abo ku ma dodo ane̩ o̩mo̩, ku ma la jo̩ko̩ bʼamo̩jo̩ e-ma ku ma chane̩ ekpa e̩wñ e̩bie̩ ñw amo̩jo̩-ma, kʼe̩ne̩ʼka fʼe̩ do̩ kʼe̩ fʼe̩wñ iche̩bo̩-wñ je̩,
kʼuwe̩ la fʼamo̩ma-ma onobule̩ ne̩ ñw amo̩ma-we̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩, kʼamo̩ma-ma onobule̩ le̩ chane̩ ejo̩ko̩ bʼamo̩jo̩-ma, ku ma la je̩ ñw amo̩ma-we̩ e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ jo̩ko̩ bʼamo̩jo̩ e-ma.
Uwe̩ ki la fʼamo̩jo̩ da ñw o̩la-we̩ n.
Uwe̩ ki de uje̩wñ uyo̩ e-ki ma nʼo̩jo̩wu n le̩. Uwe̩ ki je̩ uje̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu ma do̩ n kad o̩jo̩ mebie, iko-wñ ki che̩date̩ ochu Abib alu kʼu ñwa ñw e̩; todu ochu Abib oñ e̩ kwʼIjipti dufu wa le̩.
Omi ne̩ o̩chaka e̩wñ ki akpʼo̩gba iye-wñ na, kpai ame̩wñukpa-we̩ du ku ma bi oko, owñ chʼamo̩mojo̩do̩ okuno̩ kpai ame̩wño̩re̩ egini.
E̩ ki nʼe̩wño̩re̩ egini la oji o̩mo̩jo̩do̩ o̩ke̩ke̩te̩ tane̩, i la che̩wñ ki ma dʼuwe̩ e̩do̩ kʼe̩ latane̩ n, e̩gbale̩ e̩ fʼo̩lo̩-wñ guche̩. Amo̩mo̩gba-we̩ du kʼi chʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ e̩ ki fʼoji-ma latane̩. E̩ne̩ du ki la wa o̩gba-mi o̩wo̩ ofo n.
O̩jo̩ me̩fa oñ uwe̩ achʼuko̩lo̩, o̩jo̩ e̩kebie-wñ uwe̩ muda añini; iko e̩be̩ eko̩ kpai iko e̩wñ oko eko wʼunyi, uwe̩ añini.
Uwe̩ ki la fejutʼuje̩wñ uyo̩ e-o̩jo̩ mebie o̩jo̩ mebie le̩ kpai ejo̩ga o̩ka wit kʼe̩ ko wʼunyi kpai uje̩wñ uyo̩ e-e̩wñ eko wʼunyi oj o̩do̩ le̩.
Aboke̩le̩-we̩ chaka awa jʼo̩gba Ondu Jihofa, O̩jo̩ e-Israe̩l, onu me̩ta o̩do̩ du.
Todu nakʼuche̩uche̩ amone̩ rikpolo bʼe̩ o̩gba te̩, kʼu hi alo̩me̩-we̩ nyʼubi; ane̩-we̩ la anyʼe̩ne̩ du eju kʼi ne̩ ubi-we̩ e̩gba kʼe̩ te̩gu alo kʼe̩ dufu wa o̩gba Jihofa O̩jo̩-we̩ onu me̩ta o̩do̩ du le̩ n.
Uje̩wñ kʼo̩jo̩wu dʼo̩ amanyʼe̩wñ e̩bie̩ iche̩bo̩-mi kʼe̩ kpa n; e̩wñ iche̩bo̩ e-uje̩wñ uyo̩ e-Elaloji la abo̩ jʼane̩ nyʼodudu n.
Uwe̩ ki ko e̩wñ ejodudu ef ejo̩ga e̩wñ ane̩-we̩ wʼef unyi Jihofa O̩jo̩-we̩. E̩ ki la hi o̩mewo ef omi e̩nya iye-wñ n.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩ nafʼo̩la-i ko̩; todu likpa alu kʼo̩la-i ka, omi fʼalo kpe̩ kpai uwe̩ kpai abo Israe̩l ge̩.
I la dʼugbo Jihofa o̩mo̩ o̩ro̩ka o̩gbo̩ meji kpai odu o̩gbo̩ meji; i la jʼuje̩wñ n i la ñmʼomi n. Oñ i fʼo̩la alo kʼi kpe̩ ko̩ nyʼalo le̩, owñ chʼo̩la me̩gwa le̩.
Mose̩s gwo̩ru kwʼoj uwo le̩ tane̩
Oñ i lewatu e̩gba ku Mose̩s gwo̩ru kwʼoj uwo Sainai tane̩, alo ibenu meji le̩ jʼef o̩wo̩ Mose̩s e̩gba kʼi gwo̩ru uwo le̩ wane̩, Mose̩s la ma ka kʼaño̩ eju-wñ ade̩ ña ña ña noji eko̩la kʼi ko̩la kpai owñ n.
Oñ e̩gba kʼAro̩n kpai amo̩ma Israe̩l du fu Mose̩s li, go, año̩ eju-wñ ade̩ ña ña ña oñ ma railo ete̩me̩rʼu.
Mose̩s muda do̩ ma; tak Aro̩n kpai amidachi o̩gbadu le̩ du mudabi wʼugbo-wñ, oñ Mose̩s ko̩la ñwu ma.
Ubi le̩ tak amo̩ma Israe̩l chaka te̩me̩rʼu, tak i mʼo̩la du ki Jihofa ka ñw u oj uwo Sainai ko ñwu ma kʼi chʼe̩wñ kʼO̩jo̩ ñwa ñwu ma.
Tak e̩gba ku Mose̩s fʼo̩la ka ñwu ma kpa, i mʼukpo ko bʼeju ma.
Ama e̩gba ki Mose̩s nyʼejefu o̩gba Jihofa kʼi ko̩la ñw u, i mʼukpo ube-juma le̩ ko jane̩, gbe̩gba kʼi le dufu; tak i dufu, kʼi ka e̩wñ kʼO̩jo̩ ñwa ñw u le̩ ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l.
Oñ amo̩ma Israe̩l fʼeju Mose̩s li kʼaño̩ eju Mose̩s ade̩ ña ña ña; taku Mose̩s dabi akʼukpo bʼeju ma ge̩, gbe̩gba kʼi nyʼejefu kʼi ko̩la ñw u.
Ma kʼe̩wñ ele wa tod unyabo
Taku Mose̩s fʼo̩gbadu amo̩ma Israe̩l chaka do̩ jeju, oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, O̩la-i chʼo̩la ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu me̩ ku me̩ che.
O̩jo̩ me̩fa ma achʼuko̩lo̩ kade, o̩jo̩ e̩kebie-wñ muda chʼo̩jo̩ ki afo̩ ñwu me̩, o̩jo̩ uñmi e-uñmi ñwu Jihofa, i che; e̩ne̩ du ki achʼuko̩lo̩ o̩jo̩ le̩ ekpa ma akpa.
Me̩ ki kʼuna okate o̩jo̩ uñmi ugbo du ku me̩ dodo n.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw o̩gbadu amo̩ma Israe̩l du kakini, E̩wñ ki Jihofa ñwate̩ le̩ de̩, kakini,
Me̩ ki gba e̩wñ ku me̩ du nyʼate̩ le̩ kwʼo̩wo̩ o̩la-me̩ wa ñwu Jihofa; e̩ne̩ du kʼi chʼe̩numo̩la, e̩ne̩ le̩ ki dʼu wa, owñ chʼe̩wñ kʼi du nyʼate̩ ñwu Jihofa le̩: o̩jamalia kpai ajifa kpai ebijeikpa;
kpai odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ki che̩hi reju kpai edudu ewo
kpai año̩ okolo ku ma hi ekpikpa kpai año̩ e̩la omi le̩; kpai oli akesia
kpai ekpo todu agege kpai e̩wñ kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ ki akpo todu ekpo ku ma ba tʼo̩la kpai todu otulale ki akpo ku ma gujo le̩,
kpai okuta one̩ks kpai okuta ku ma da ebije nyʼu, todu e̩fo̩d kpai todu ebije ube̩do̩ma.
E̩ne̩ke̩le̩ du efu-me̩ ki nʼofili efu kʼi lewa, kʼi fʼe̩wñ du ki Jihofa ñwate̩ che:
owñ chʼuña ugugu kpai unyabo-wñ kpai e̩wñ ki abʼoji-wñ ma ate̩, atanyi-wñ kpai akatakpo-wñ, oli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ kpai oli urane̩-wñ kpai o̩ka-wñ:
kpai akpati le̩ kpai oli ku ma ko tunyʼu kpai ugugu unye̩do̩ le̩ kpai ukpo ugbeju;
itebulu le̩ kpai oli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ kpai ane̩-wñ chaka kpai akala e-eju le̩;
kpai akete todu ugane̩-wñ ge̩ kpai e̩wñ eku-wñ kpai agege-wñ kpai ekpo tod ugane̩ le̩;
kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e-otulale ku ma gujo kpai oli ku ma ko tunyʼu kpai ekpo ku ma du batʼo̩la kpai otulale ki akpo ku ma gujo kpai ukpo uro̩na alugbo̩na uña ugugu;
ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e-e̩wñ e̩gujo kpai ebijeikpa ku ma ta kʼuna ki jo oji-wñ, oli ku ma ko tunyʼu kpai ane̩-wñ chaka, ukpachi u gw o̩wo̩ kpai e̩wñ kʼi agugu oji-wñ;
ukpo ku ma ko bʼologbo, oli urane̩-wñ kpai o̩ka-wñ kpai ukpo uro̩na tod alaku ologbo le̩;
ale uña ugugu kpai ale ologbo-wñ kpai iku-wñ;
otogbo ku ma hi reju ku ma nyi ache e̩wñ ef uña kiafo, otogbo ki afo̩ todu Aro̩n, atama, kpai otogbo amo̩ma-wñ, ku ma nyi ache e̩wñ atama le̩.
Tak ujeju amo̩ma Israe̩l chaka kwo bʼeju Mose̩s te̩.
Oñ ma lewa, owñ chʼe̩ne̩ du kʼe̩do̩-wñ kwane̩, kpai e̩ne̩ du kʼafu-wñ du tef e̩do̩-wñ, oñ ma mʼe̩wñ ku ma ko nyʼate̩ ñwu Jihofa le̩ kowa todu uko̩lo̩ unyabo ujeju kpai todu e̩wñ ku ma che o̩mo̩ chaka kpai todu otogbo kiafo̩ le̩.
