Abe̩le̩ ma lewa, tʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ tʼonobule̩; aluka one̩ du kʼi chʼe̩numo̩la kʼelika iñmo̩ kpai ile̩li eti kpai elika kpai ude̩ o̩wo̩ wa, o̩chaka-wñ chʼe̩wñ ijaga o̩jamalia, e̩ne̩ du nʼe̩wñ wa amiejo ñwu Jihofa.
Oñ e̩ne̩ du ku ma li e̩wñ odufa kpai e̩wñ odufa ekpikpa kpai e̩wñ ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ki chʼe̩hi reju kpai edudu ewo kpai año̩ okolo ku ma hi ekpikpa kpai año̩ e̩la omi le̩ ugbo-wñ, e̩ne̩ le̩ mʼu ko wa.
E̩ne̩ du kʼi mʼe̩wñ ajifa abe̩k ebijeikpa du nyʼate̩, mʼe̩wñ kʼi ko nyʼate̩ ñwu Jihofa le̩ ko wa; e̩ne̩ du ku ma fʼoli ake̩sia todu uko̩lo̩ ojoji du tod e̩wñ eche le̩ li ugbo-wñ, e̩ne̩ le̩ mʼu ko wa.
Abobule̩ du ku ma nʼofili efu la nʼo̩wo̩-ma che owu, oñ ma mʼowu ku ma da le̩ kowa, owñ chʼe-odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju.
Abobule̩ du kʼe̩do̩-ma kwane̩ ku ma nʼibe fʼedudu ewo da.
Tak amidachi mʼokuta one̩ks kpai okuta ku ma tene ku ma fʼebije danyʼu todu e̩fo̩d kpai todu ebije ube̩do̩ma ko wa,
kpai e̩wñ idoro̩ kpai ekpo todu e̩mu kpai todu ekpo ebatʼo̩la kpai todu otulale ku ma gujo ki akpo le̩.
Amo̩ma Israe̩l chaka, tʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ tʼonobule̩ kʼe̩do̩-ma kʼuma e̩che̩ ku ma kʼe̩wñ wa todu uko̩lo̩ du ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu ma lʼo̩wo̩ Mose̩s ku ma che, gʼe̩dʼo̩la-ma ko wa ñwu Jihofa.
Taku Mose̩s ka ñw amo̩ma Israe̩l kakini, Me̩ go, Jihofa la dʼodu Be̩zale̩l, o̩ma Uri, ki chʼo̩ma He̩r kʼi chʼabo o̩lo̩pu Juda;
i la je̩ ñw u chʼe̩ko̩ ñw Afu O̩jo̩, ef ibe kpai oji e̩wñ ema kpai e̩wñ ema kpai uko̩lo̩ o̩wo̩ ojoji ojoji du eche,
kʼi fʼibe uko̩lo̩ e̩te̩le̩ ñwa, kʼi chʼuko̩lo̩ o̩jamalia kpai ajifa kpai ebijeikpa,
kpai okuta egbe̩ ku ma da ebije nyʼu, kpai oli egbe̩, kpai uko̩lo̩ o̩ka ojoji ojoji du kʼo̩wo̩ ache.
Oñ i du tef e̩do̩-wñ kʼi ko̩ one̩ uko̩lo̩, tʼowñ, tʼOholiab, o̩ma Ahisamak, kʼi chʼabo o̩lo̩pu Dan le̩.
I je̩ ñw ibe chʼe̩ko̩ ef e̩do̩-ma ku ma chʼuko̩lo̩ o̩wo̩ ojoji ojoji du, uko̩lo̩ alo̩ egwu kpai o̩ka uko̩lo̩ kpai e̩ne̩ ki achiya nyʼukpo odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai e-line̩n ku ma hi reju, kpai e̩ne̩ kʼi ahi ukpo—owñ chʼabo ku ma chʼuko̩lo̩ du, kpai abo ku ma ñw ibe ina e̩te̩le̩ eko̩ nyʼe̩wñ.
Ane̩ uko̩lo̩ unyabo le̩
Taku Be̩zale̩l kpai Oholiab kpai e̩ne̩ du ki nʼofili efu, owñ chʼe̩ne̩ ku Jihofa mʼibe kpai oji e̩wñ ema du tʼowñ efu kʼi meju uko̩lo̩ du tod e̩wñ ef uña kiafo̩ le̩ eche, achʼuko̩lo̩ likpa alu du ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu ma.
Taku Mose̩s fu Be̩zale̩l kpai Oholiab do̩, manyʼe̩ne̩ du ki nʼofili efu, e-ki Jihofa dʼibe tʼowñ efu; owñ chʼe̩ne̩ du kʼe̩do̩-wñ kwane̩ kʼi wa che uko̩lo̩ le̩;
taku ma mʼe̩wñ du ku ma ko̩ nyʼate̩ kʼamo̩ma Israe̩l ko wa ku ma ne̩ chʼuko̩lo̩ e̩wñ du ku ma ache ef uña kiafo̩, gba o̩wo̩ Mose̩s. Ma laño̩ gʼe̩do̩la-ma ako e̩wñ wʼugbo-wñ odudu o̩jo̩ duu.
Tak amanibe chaka ku ma che uko̩lo̩ uña kiafo̩ le̩ du, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ kwo bʼuko̩lo̩-wñ kʼi ache te̩ wa,
oñ ma ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini, E̩wñ kʼamone̩ ako wa-i tʼuko̩lo̩ ki Jihofa ñwa ñw a kʼa che le̩ gu e̩gu du.
Taku Mose̩s ñwa ñwu ma, oñ ma fʼakoya-wñ ta ugbo du ef uru le̩ kakini, Tʼe̩ne̩ke̩le̩ tʼonobule̩ ki ño̩ che uko̩lo̩ e̩wñ omune̩ ku ma ko̩ nyʼate̩ tod uña kiafo̩-i ge̩ n. Abe̩le̩ ma fʼamone̩ ba ku ma we ekʼe̩wñ wa.
Todu e̩wñ ku ma ne̩ bʼuko̩lo̩ le̩ jo̩ kwubo̩.
Oñ aboke̩le̩ du ku ma nʼofili ef e̩do̩ chaka ku ma jʼef abo ku ma che uko̩lo̩ le̩ kʼibali ukpo me̩gwa ta che uña ugugu le̩; ukpo-wñ che line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩, kʼi chʼodufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa; ma famiche̩rub chenyʼu e̩te̩le̩.
Ujiji ibali ukpo ku ma ko ta le̩ okoke chʼo̩hibo̩wo̩ ogu nyoke me̩jo̩, unabe̩ ibali-wñ okoke la chʼo̩hibo̩wo̩ me̩le̩; e̩ñwa ibali-wñ du la chʼalukate.
Oñ i fʼibali ukpo ku ma ta le̩ me̩lu gamʼomune̩, ibali ukpo me̩lu ki bo̩ i ño̩ fʼu gamʼomune̩.
I la che ate odufa nyʼeti ibali ukpo ki dʼotitala e̩gwodama-wñ ejodudu; i ño̩ fʼabele̩ che nyʼeti ibali ukpo ki dʼotitala e̩gwodama-wñ o̩wo̩ ekeji;
i fʼate ooje che nyʼeti e̩gwodama ukpo le̩ oka, i laño̩ fʼate ooje che nyʼeti ibali ukpo otitala ef e̩gwodama-wñ ekeji; ate-wñ la kpejurʼomune̩.
Tak i nʼo̩jamalia che atanyi ooje, oñ i nʼatanyi le̩ fʼe̩gwodama ukpo meji le̩ ta tʼomune̩; abe̩le̩ oñ uña ugugu le̩ mud alukate.
I ño̩ nʼedudu ewo hi ibali ibali ukpo ku ma ata kʼi chʼunyabo uña ugugu le̩; i fʼibali ukpo ku ma ta le̩ me̩gwaka che.
Ujiji ibali-wñ okoke la chʼohibo̩wo̩ ogue̩gwa, unabe̩ ibali-wñ okoke la chʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩le̩; e̩ñwa ibali ukpo ku ma ta me̩gwaka le̩ chʼalukate.
I fʼibali me̩lu gamʼomune̩; oñ i fʼibali me̩fa gamʼomune̩ ojoji.
Tak i fʼate ooje che nyʼeti ibali ukpo ki dʼotitala e̩gamʼomune̩-wñ oka; i laño̩ che ate ooje nyʼeti ibali ukpo ki dʼotitala e̩gamʼomune̩-wñ o̩wo̩ ekeji ge̩.
Tak i nʼebijeikpa che atanyi ooje kʼi ne̩ fʼunyabo le̩ ta tʼomune̩ kʼi chʼalukate.
I laño̩ nʼaño̩ amokolo ku ma hi ekpikpa ko che e̩wñ ki abʼoji unyabo le̩ ma, kpai año̩ e̩la omi le̩ kʼi bʼe-le̩ ma ate̩.
Tak i nʼoli akesia chʼakatakpo ki adago kpakpa todu uña ugugu le̩.
Ujiji akatakpoʼka chʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩gwa, unabe̩ akatakpoʼka la chʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpe̩reji.
Akatakpo du nʼe̩re̩ meji, efa ma fa tunyʼu; i fʼabe̩le̩ che todu akatakpo uña ugugu le̩ chaka.
Abu kʼi chʼakatakpo todu uña ugugu le̩ de̩: akatakpo todu o̩wo̩-wñ o̩pata awo̩to̩ chʼogu;
tak i nʼajifa che o̩ka o̩gbo̩ meji kʼi jʼofe akatakpo ogu le̩; o̩ka meji jʼofe akatakpoʼka tod e̩re̩-wñ meji le̩, o̩ka meji la jʼofo akatakpo omune̩ tod e̩re̩-wñ meji ge̩.
Taku todu o̩wo̩ ekeji uña ugugu le̩, owñ chʼakolo-wñ o̩wo̩ awohi i fʼakatakpo ogu che ge̩
kpai o̩ka ajifa o̩gbo̩ meji, o̩ka meji jʼofe akatakpoʼka, o̩ka meji la jʼofe akatakpo omune̩.
I la fʼakatakpo me̩fa che todu ejubi uña ugugu le̩, o̩wo̩ olane̩-wñ.
Oñ i fʼakatakpo meji che todu ejubi uña ugugu le̩ ugbo ku ma dʼalo-wñ meji.
Ma chʼegamʼomune̩ o̩gane̩; tak oji-wñ ate̩ tunyʼelikaʼka, abe̩le̩ i fʼeji che tod ugbo kʼalo-wñ meji ade.
Abe̩le̩ akatakpo-wñ chʼe̩jo̩, manyʼoka ajifa-wñ; o̩ka-wñ la chʼe̩gwe̩fa, oka meji jʼofe akatakpo okoke du.
Oñ i nʼoli akesia fʼoli ugbo̩lo, e̩lu-wñ chʼutodu akatakpo o̩woʼka uña ugugu le̩.
Oli ugbo̩lo̩ me̩lu la chʼutodu akatakpo o̩wo̩ ekeji uña ugugu le̩, oli ugbo̩lo̩ me̩lu la chʼutodu akatakpo ejubi uña ugugu, o̩wo̩ olane̩-wñ.
I la che oli ugbo̩lo̩ ki dʼalumeji ki tunyu alumeji akatakpo akatakpo akwʼo̩wo̩ʼka-wñ gbogbo tʼo̩wo̩ ekeji.
Tak i fʼo̩jamalia wenyʼakatakpo akatakpo le̩; i nʼo̩jamalia che elika-wñ todu kʼi chʼugbo kʼoli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ atunyu, i laño̩ fʼo̩jamalia wenyu oli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ ge̩.
Tak i nʼodufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ che ukpo ugbeju le̩. Amiche̩rub jʼo̩la-wñ, uko̩lo̩-wñ chʼuko̩lo̩ o̩ka.
Tak i fʼoli urane̩ akesia me̩le̩ fa todu-wñ, i la dʼo̩jamalia wenyʼu; uko̩-wñ chʼo̩jamalia; i laño̩ fʼo̩ka ajifa me̩le̩ da todu-wñ.
I ño̩ fʼukpo uro̩na che todu alugbo̩na unyabo le̩, i chʼodufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩; uko̩lo̩ e̩ne̩ kʼi achiya nyʼukpo jʼo̩la-wñ;
manyʼoli urane̩-wñ me̩lu kpai uko̩-wñ. I kʼo̩jamalia wenyʼoji-wñ, oli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ ate̩ chʼo̩jamalia, o̩ka-wñ me̩lu kʼi jʼofe-wñ muda chʼebijeikpa.
Akpati alo kpai ugugu unye̩do̩ le̩
Oñ Be̩zale̩l nʼoli akesia che akpati le̩; ujiji-wñ chʼohibo̩wo̩ meji nyʼukpe̩reji, unabe̩-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpereji, o̩gba-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpe̩reji.
I la kʼo̩jamalia ki de̩ hiolo bʼo̩la-wñ ma tʼejefu tʼejo̩do̩da, oñ i fʼo̩jamalia gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ kʼi dʼu lamʼeti-wñ daka.
Tak i fʼelika o̩jamalia me̩le̩ da todu e̩re̩-wñ me̩le̩, elika meji la jʼo̩wo̩ʼka-wñ, elika meji omune̩ la jʼo̩wo̩ ekeji-wñ.
Tak i nʼoli akesia fa oli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ, oñ i kʼo̩jamalia wenyʼu.
I la mʼoli ugbo̩lo̩ ko tunyʼelika akolo akpati le̩, ku ma gwo̩nyʼu anʼakpati le̩.
Oñ i nʼo̩jamalia hiolo che ugugu unye̩do̩; ujiji-wñ chʼohibo̩wo̩ meji nyʼukpe̩reji, unabe̩-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpe̩reji.
Tak i nʼo̩jamalia gwu amiche̩rub meji; i gwʼu jo̩ o̩wo̩ afida ugugu unye̩do̩ le̩ meji,
che̩rubʼka la dʼo̩wo̩ afida-wñ kekeleʼka, che̩rub ekeji la dʼo̩wo̩ afida-wñ kekele ekeji; i mʼiche̩rub du che alukate kpai ugugu unye̩do̩ le̩, o̩wo̩-wñ mejeji.
Amiche̩rub le̩ la fʼika-ma nadala ate̩, ika-ma la bʼoji ugugu unye̩do̩ ma ate̩, ma kpejuru o̩la-ma; eju amiche̩rub la che̩kparu ugugu unye̩do̩ le̩.
I ño̩ nʼoli ake̩sia che itebulu le̩; ujiji-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ meji, unabe̩-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka, o̩gba-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ʼka nyʼukpe̩re̩ji;
i la mʼo̩jamalia hiolo ko bʼo̩la-wñ ma, oñ i fʼo̩jamalia gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ kʼi dʼu lamʼeti-wñ daka.
I la nʼo̩jamalia fʼo̩gba bu nyʼeti-wñ daka, unabe̩ o̩gba-wñ chʼadaba o̩wo̩ʼka, tak i fʼo̩jamalia gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ kʼi dʼu lamʼeti-wñ daka.
Tak i fʼelika o̩jamalia me̩le̩ da todu-wñ, oñ i mʼelika le̩ ko tunyʼuka-wñ me̩le̩, ugbo e̩re̩-wñ me̩le̩.
Elika le̩ me̩ru o̩gba-wñ, ugbo ku ma dʼoli ugbo̩lo̩ tunyu ku ma ne̩ itebulu le̩ de̩.
I nʼoli akesia fa ugbo̩lo̩ oli ku ma du ne̩ itebulu le̩, oñ i fʼo̩jamalia wenyʼu.
Tak i nʼo̩jamalia hiolo chʼe̩wñ eku ki ajo̩ oji itebulu le̩, ugba-wñ kpai ucha todu otulale-wñ kpai ago iche̩bo̩-wñ kpai ukpa-wñ ku ma ane̩ dʼomi iche̩bo̩ danyʼoji e̩wñ iche̩bo̩.
I ño̩ ne̩ o̩jamalia hiolo chʼakete le̩. Egwu i gwu e̩re̩-wñ kpʼoli-wñ; akpo-wñ kpʼe̩bu-wñ kpai ododo-wñ chʼalukate kpai owñ.
E̩to̩-wñ ki ta dufu akolo-wñ mejeji chʼe̩fa, e̩to̩ akete le̩ me̩ta kado akolo-wñ o̩wo̩ʼka, e̩to̩ me̩ta omune̩ la kado akolo akete le̩ o̩wo̩ ekeji;
e̩bu-wñ me̩ta ku ma che dab ikoko almo̩nd manyʼakpo-wñ kpai ododo-wñ kado e̩to̩-wñ oka; e̩bu-wñ me̩ta kti ma che dabu ikoko almo̩nd manyʼakpo-wñ kpai o̩do̩do̩-wñ kado e̩to̩ ekeji—abe̩le̩ i che todu e̩to̩ me̩fa ki ta dufu kwef akete le̩.
Oñ ago me̩le̩ ku ma che dab ikoko almo̩nd jʼo̩la oli akete le̩ onugo, manyʼakpo-wñ kpai ododo-wñ,
akpo laño̩ dʼofe ugbo kʼe̩to̩ meji e̩ji ta kwo, abe̩le̩ i de̩ tod e̩to̩-wñ me̩fa.
Akpo-wñ kpai e̩to̩-wñ chʼalukate kpai owñ; o̩chaka-wñ chʼuko̩lo̩ ku ma nʼo̩jamalia hiolo gwu alukate.
I nʼo̩jamalia hiolo che agege-wñ mebie kpai alapa-wñ kpai e̩wñ kʼalapa le̩ ajo̩ efu-wñ.
O̩jamalia hiolo alu ta-le̩ntʼka, i du che, owñ kpai ane̩-wñ chaka.
I la nʼoli akesia che ubo̩ ku ma gu e̩wñ ki akpo le̩ jo̩ oji-wñ; ujiji-wñ chʼo̩hibo̩wo̩ʼka, unabe̩-wñ ño̩ chʼo̩hi-bo̩wo̩ʼka; akolo-wñ me̩le̩ chʼokujo̩; o̩gba-wñ la chʼo̩hibo̩wo̩ meji; igba-wñ la chʼalukate kpai owñ.
Oñ i mʼo̩jamalia hiolo ko bʼo̩la-wñ ma, tʼoji-wñ, tʼakolo-wñ daka, kpai igba-wñ; oñ i fʼo̩jamalia gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ lamʼeti-wñ daka.
I ño̩ fʼe̩lika o̩jamalia meji che todu-wñ o̩gane̩ o̩jamalia ku ma gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ lamʼeti-wñ le̩, ugbo uka-wñ meji, akolo-wñ meji, kʼi chʼugbo kʼugbo̩lo̩ oli atunyu ku ma ne̩.
I la nʼoli ake̩sia fa ugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩, oñ i fʼo̩jamalia wenyu.
I laño̩ fʼekpo ki afo̩ ku ma du bato̩la le̩ che ge̩, kpai otulale hiolo ku ma gujo kʼi nʼe̩wñ kwe̩ kwe̩ kwe̩ ki akpo che, i che alu kʼe̩ne̩ ki chʼo̩ka otulale ache.
Ane̩ ef unyabo le̩
I ño̩ nʼoli akesia che ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e̩gujo ge̩; ujiji-wñ chʼo̩hibo̩wo̩ me̩lu, unabe̩-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩lu, akolo-wñ me̩le̩ chʼokujo̩, o̩gba-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩ta.
I la fʼigba che oji uka-wñ me̩le̩; igba-wñ la chʼalukate kpai owñ, i la nʼebijeikpa wenyʼo̩la-wñ.
Oñ i fʼe̩wñ eku ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩ che chaka, ucha-wñ kpai uko̩che̩-wñ kpai ugba-wñ kpai uko̩-wñ ku ma du tatʼe̩la kpai e̩wñ kʼelulu awane̩ jʼoji-wñ: o̩chaka e̩wñ e̩ku-wñ le̩ i nʼebijeikpa che.
I la fʼebijeikpa gwu kpataka kʼi chʼe̩gudu e̩gudu dab iga tod ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩, i chʼe̩hiwane̩ bʼalu-wñ te̩ tʼalumeji-wñ.
I nʼebijeikpa fʼelika me̩le̩ da todu uka me̩le̩ ebijeikpa kpataka le̩, kʼi chʼugbo ku ma ko ugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩ tunyʼu;
i la nʼoli akesia gbe̩ ugbo̩lo̩ oli-wñ, oñ i fʼebijeikpa wenyʼu.
Tak i ko ugbo̩lo̩ oli le̩ tunyʼelika ki jo̩ akolo ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩, ku ma ne̩. I nʼakatakpo che kʼefu-wñ ki te̩ ofo.
Oñ i nʼebijeikpa che ukpachi ugwo̩wo̩-wñ, e̩wñ ugugu-wñ laño̩ chʼebijeikpa ge̩; ogigo abobule̩ ku ma jeju jʼalugbo̩na unyabo ujeju le̩ oñ i ne̩ che.
Tak i fʼologbo-wñ bu; ukpo ku ma du bʼologbo o̩pata o̩wo̩ awo̩to̩-wñ chʼukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩, i chʼohibo̩wo̩ ogu me̩lu;
oli urane̩-wñ chʼogu, o̩ka-wñ chʼogu, ebijeikpa i che; uko̩ oli urane̩-wñ kpai ugbo̩lo̩-wñ ate̩ muda chʼajifa.
O̩pata-wñ o̩wo̩ awohi ño̩ chʼohibo̩wo̩ ogu me̩lu; oli urane̩-wñ chʼogu o̩ka-wñ chʼogu, ebijeikpa i che; uko̩ oli urane̩-wñ kpai ugbo̩lo̩-wñ ate̩ muda chʼajifa.
Ukpo ku ma la ta jʼo̩wo̩ olane̩ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ ooje, oli urane̩-wñ chʼe̩gwa, o̩ka-wñ la chʼe̩gwa; uko̩ oli urane̩ le̩ kpai ugbo̩lo̩-wñ ate̩ muda chʼajifa.
Todu o̩gba-wñ eju olodudu-wñ, i chʼohibo̩wo̩ ooje.
Ukpo-wñ o̩wo̩ʼka chʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩gwe̩lu, oli urane̩-wñ chʼe̩ta, oka-wñ la chʼe̩ta.
Abe̩le̩ i ño̩ de̩ o̩wo̩ ekeji-wñ; o̩wo̩ emi kpai o̩wo̩ ej ano̩mo̩ alu ologbo le̩, ukpo ku ma du bu chʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩gwe̩lu, oli urane̩-wñ chʼe̩ta, o̩ka-wñ la chʼe̩ta.
Ukpo du ku ma ko bʼologbo le̩ daka chʼukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju.
O̩ka kʼoli urane̩ le̩ atunyʼu la chʼebijeikpa; uko̩ oli urane̩ le̩ kpai ugbo̩lo̩-wñ ate̩ muda chʼajifa; ebije ku ma gwu tunyʼoji-wñ ño̩ chʼajifa, oli urane̩ ologbo le̩ du nʼugbo̩lo̩ ajifa ate̩ ta tʼomune̩.
Ukpo uro̩na alaku ologbo le̩ chʼuko̩lo̩ e̩ne̩ ki chʼo̩ka iya eche nyʼukpo odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai line̩n ku ma hi reju; ujiji-wñ la chʼohibo̩wo̩ ogu, o̩gba-wñ, owñ chʼo̩wo̩ unabe̩-wñ, chʼohibo̩wo̩ me̩lu, owñ chʼalu kʼukpo ku ma du bʼologbo le̩ de̩.
Oli urane̩-wñ la chʼe̩le̩; o̩ka-wñ me̩le̩ chʼebijeikpa, uko̩-wñ la chʼajifa, e̩wñ ki che̩gwu tʼoji-wñ kpai ugbo̩lo̩-wñ ku ma du nʼo̩ lale ño̩ chʼajifa ge̩.
Ale uña ugugu le̩ chaka kpai e-ologbo-wñ ki lʼo daka chʼebijeikpa.
Aluka e̩wñ todu uña ugugu le̩ de̩, owñ chʼuña ugugu e-ibenu le̩, ku ma kaluka-wñ alu ku Mose̩s dʼalu ñwu ma le̩, owñ chʼuko̩lo̩ kʼabo Lifai ku ma jʼef o̩wo̩ Itamar o̩ma Aro̩n atama che.
Oñ Be̩zale̩l, o̩ma Uri kʼi chʼo̩ma He̩r abo o̩lo̩pu Juda, fʼe̩wñ du ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s chekpa.
E̩ne̩ ki la manyʼowñ chʼOholiab, o̩ma Ahisamak, kʼi chʼabo o̩lo̩pu Dan, owñ chʼe̩ne̩ ki akina nyʼo̩la e̩wñ, o̩ka uko̩lo̩ ehi kpai echiya nyʼo̩la ukpo odufa, kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n ku ma hi reju i che.
O̩jamalia du ku ma ne̩ chʼuko̩lo̩ le̩, owñ chʼuko̩lo̩ uña kiafo̩ le̩ chaka, owñ chʼo̩jamalia ku ma ko wa miejo le̩, o̩chaka-wñ che tale̩nt ogu nyoke me̩la kpai she̩ke̩l e̩te̩gwa chi icham, owñ chʼishe̩ke̩l e-uña kiafo̩ le̩.
Ajifa abo ku ma kaluka ef abo o̩gbadu le̩ la che tale̩nt ogu me̩lu kpai she̩ke̩l icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ nyʼogume̩lu mebie nyʼe̩te̩gwa nyoke me̩lu alu ki she̩ke̩l e-uña kiafo̩ de̩:
e̩ne̩ʼka ne̩ be̩kaʼka tod oji-wñ, (owñ chʼukpe̩reji she̩ke̩l, alu ki she̩ke̩l e-uña kiafo̩ le̩ de̩), i chʼutodu e̩ne̩ du ki lale tef abo ku ma kaluka, e̩ne̩ du kʼo̩do̩-wñ jo̩ ogu, owñ chʼaboke̩le̩ icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ ugbo ulo̩gwa nyoke meta, one̩ oli me̩gwaka nʼoji-wñ.
Ajifa alu tale̩nt ogu me̩lu le̩ la chʼutodu ku ma ne̩ da o̩ka ki jʼofe uña kiafo̩ le̩, kpai o̩ka kʼi jʼofe ukpo ugbeju-wñ; o̩ka ogu me̩lu che tale̩nt ogu me̩lu; tale̩nt oka chʼo̩kaʼka.
Taku she̩ke̩l icham nyʼo̩gwo̩ko̩ nyʼogume̩lu mebie nyʼe̩te̩gwa nyoke me̩lu le̩ i muko chʼuko̩ todu oli urane̩-wñ, oñ i mʼu du gwu tunyʼoji-wñ, tak i mʼugbo̩lo̩-wñ ate̩ ko ta tʼo̩.
Ebijeikpa ku ma kowa miejo le̩ chʼalu tale̩nt e̩te̩gwa, manyu she̩ke̩l icham me̩ta.
E-le̩ i muko che o̩ka o̩ka todu alu o̩na unyabo ujeju le̩, kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ebijeikpa le̩ kpai ebijeikpa kpataka ki chʼe̩gudu e̩gudu ki de̩ efu-wñ kpai e̩wñ eku e-ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩ chaka
kpai o̩ka o̩ka ki la jʼe̩re̩ ologbo le̩ daka, kpai o̩ka o̩ka alu o̩na ologbo le̩ kpai ale uña ugugu le̩ chaka kpai ale ologbo ki ledaka.
E̩wñ o̩la amatama
Oñ ma mʼodufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa le̩ ko ga e̩wñ o̩la ku ma nyi ache e̩wñ ef uña kiafo̩; ma fʼe̩wñ o̩la kiafo̩ ga todu Aro̩n; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Tak i nʼo̩jamalia kpai odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ che e̩fo̩d le̩.
Ma la fʼo̩jamalia gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ oñ ma fʼu kpana mie̩le̩ mie̩le̩ ku ma du chiya o̩ka o̩ka nyʼodufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai line̩n ku ma hi reju le̩.
Ma fʼe̩wñ ojika-wñ che ku ma du gamʼo̩; eti-wñ meji chegamʼo̩.
Ma nʼo̩jamalia kpai odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ che e̩wñ ujiñmi e̩fo̩d ki dʼo̩la-wñ ku ma ne̩ damu mʼo̩, kʼi chʼalukate kpai owñ, uko̩lo̩-wñ chʼokate; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Taku ma fʼuko̩lo̩ okuta one̩ks le̩ che, ma fʼo̩jamalia da nyʼu, oñ ma fʼina ko̩ nyʼu alu ku ma kʼma nyʼe̩wñ uhiuko̩, alu kʼodu amo̩ma e̩ne̩ke̩le̩ Israe̩l de̩.
Tak i fʼu gamo̩ ukpo o̩j ika e-e̩fo̩d le̩, ki che okuta urewa todu amo̩ma Israe̩l; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Tak i fʼe̩wñ ube̩do̩ma che, uko̩lo̩-wñ chʼuko̩lo̩ o̩ka alu kʼuko̩lo̩ e̩fo̩d le̩ de̩; i chʼo̩jamalia kpai odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩.
Ago̩go̩-wñ me̩le̩ chʼokujo̩; ma fʼe̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩ che kʼi chʼeji nʼe̩do̩ o̩la-wñ, ujiji-wñ chʼo̩chali o̩wo̩ʼka, unabe̩-wñ la chʼo̩chali o̩wo̩ʼka, e̩ji nʼe̩do̩ omune̩.
Oñ ma fʼokuta ganyʼu o̩gba o̩gba ugbo me̩le̩. O̩gbaʼka-wñ che sardius kpai topaz kpai karbunke̩l e-le̩ chʼo̩gba ejodudu;
o̩gba ekeji la che e̩me̩rald kpai safaya kpai daimo̩nd;
o̩gba e̩ke̩ta la che jesint kpai age̩t kpai ame̩tist;
o̩gba e̩ke̩le̩ la che be̩re̩l kpai one̩ks kpai jaspe̩r; ma fʼo̩jamalia danyʼokuta ugbo ki jo̩ le̩.
Okuta le̩ la jo̩ alu kʼodu odu amo̩ma Israe̩l de̩, e̩gwe̩ji i che, alu kʼodu-ma de̩; i chʼe̩ko̩ nyʼu dab e̩wñ uhiuko̩, e̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ne̩ dʼalu kʼodu-wñ de̩, todu o̩lo̩pu me̩gweji le̩.
Taku ma fʼiyagba che tʼo̩la e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩ dabe̩ne̩ kʼiku, uko̩lo̩-wñ chʼo̩jamalia hiolo ku ma fuba;
oñ ma nʼo̩jamalia chʼagbamune̩-wñ meji kpai elika o̩jamalia meji, taku ma fʼelika meji le̩ gamo̩ akolo e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩ meji.
Taku ma mʼiyagba o̩jamalia meji ku ma ba le̩ ko tunyʼelika meji ki jʼeti e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩.
Ma la kʼoji iyagba ku ma ba meji ki bo̩ jane̩ tunyʼagbamune̩ meji le̩; abe̩le̩ ma fʼu gamo̩ ukpo oj ika e̩fo̩d le̩, e̩j o̩gba-wñ.
Taku ma fʼelika o̩jamalia meji da, oñ ma fʼu gamo̩ iba e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩ mejeji, eli-wñ kʼi me̩ru e̩fo̩d ejefu oñ ma du ne.
Ma la fʼelika o̩jamalia meji da, oñ ma fʼu gamo̩ o̩wo̩ o̩gane̩ ukpo ojika e̩fo̩d le̩ ejefu-wñ, e̩jo̩gba-wñ me̩ru ugbo ku ma ko gbako omune̩ ate̩ ñw e̩wñ ujiñmi e-e̩fo̩d le̩.
Taku ma mʼo̩jaja odufa ko tunyʼelika e̩wñ ube̩do̩ma kpai elika e-e̩fo̩d ku ma fuji mʼomune̩, todu ki nʼoji e̩wñ ujiñmi e-e̩fo̩d le̩ kʼe̩wñ ube̩do̩ma le̩ ki we etachi bʼe̩fo̩d te̩; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
I laño̩ fʼotogbo e̩fo̩d le̩ hi, o̩chaka-wñ chʼodufa;
e̩gudu alumeji otogbo le̩ dʼalu ku ma dʼo̩fa adika ogu; ma fʼe̩gba du nʼalu e̩gudu-wñ daka, kʼi we efana.
Taku ma ne̩ odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa kpai ukpo line̩n kʼowu-wñ chʼe̩da bie̩ ga mʼeti otogbo le̩ dab e̩ro oli ku ma do̩ ko̩ po̩me̩grane̩t.
Ma laño̩ ne̩ o̩jamalia hiolo da ilo ilo, oñ ma mʼilo le̩ ko tunyʼagbagba po̩me̩grane̩t le̩ lʼe̩re̩ otogbo le̩ daka kʼi kpe̩gwa nyu po̩me̩grane̩t le̩;
ilo kpai po̩me̩grane̩t, ilo kpai po̩me̩grane̩t nʼeti e̩re̩ otogbo le̩ daka, ku ma nyi ache e̩wñ-ma; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Oñ ma nʼukpo line̩n ki chʼe̩hi reju gʼafe̩ todu Aro̩n, kpai amo̩ma-wñ,
alawoni-wñ laño̩ che ukpo line̩n ki chʼe̩hi reju, o̩tajia ki fe̩rʼeju ño̩ che ukpo line̩n ki chʼe̩hi reju, ichaka-wñ che line̩n efufu ku ma hi reju ku ma dʼowu-wñ bie̩.
E̩wñ ujiñmi-wñ la che line̩n ku ma hi reju kʼowu-wñ chʼeda bie̩ kpai odufa kpai odufa ekpikpa kpai ekpikpa, uko̩lo̩ e̩ne̩ kʼi achiya nyʼukpo jʼo̩la-wñ; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Oñ ma fʼo̩jamalia hiolo gwu pe̩te̩ke̩ todu ike̩be̩ kiafo̩ le̩, ma la fʼolubutu ko̩ nyʼu alu ku ma kina nyʼe̩wñ uhiuko̩ kakini, EFO̩ ÑWU JIHOFA.
Taku ma fʼowu odufa daku nyʼu ku ma dʼu ji manyʼala-woni ate̩-wñ; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Abe̩le̩ ma fʼuko̩lo̩ uña ugugu e-unyabo ujeju le̩ che kpa; amo̩ma Israe̩l la fʼu che teju alu du ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s; abe̩le̩ ma che.
Taku ma mʼuña ugugu le̩ ko wʼugbo Mose̩s, unyabo kpai ane̩-wñ du kpai atanyi-wñ kpai akatakpo-wñ kpai oli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ kpai oli urane̩-wñ kpai o̩ka-wñ;
kpai año̩ okolo ku ma hi ekpikpa ku ma ko bʼoji-wñ ate̩ ma, kpai año̩ e̩la omi ku ma ko bʼoji e-le̩ ma, kpai ukpo ugbeju;
kpai akpati ibenu le̩ manyʼoli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ, kpai ugugu unye̩do̩;
itebulu-wñ kpai e̩wñ eku-wñ chaka kpai akala e-eju le̩,
akete ku ma nʼo̩jamalia hiolo che kpai agege-wñ, kʼagege-wñ tala jʼoji-wñ aro̩ne aro̩ne kpai e̩wñ eku-wñ chaka, kpai ekpo todu ugane̩;
kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e-o̩jamalia kpai ekpo ku ma du batʼo̩la kpai otulale ku ma gujo ki akpo kpai ukpo uro̩na tod alo̩na unyabo le̩;
ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e-ebijeikpa kpai ebijeikpa kpataka ki che̩gudu e̩gudu kʼi dʼefu-wñ, oli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ kpai e̩wñ eku-wñ chaka; ukpachi ugwo̩-wo̩ kpai e̩wñ ugugu-wñ;
ukpo ku ma du bʼologbo oli urane̩-wñ kpai o̩ka-wñ kpai ukpo uro̩na alu ologbo le̩, iku-wñ kpai ale-wñ; kpai e̩wñ eku chaka ku ma ne̩ che e̩wñ ef uña ugugu, owñ chʼutod unyabo ujeju le̩:
e̩wñ o̩la ku ma hi ku ma nyi ache e̩wñ ef uña kiafo̩, kpai afe̩ kiafo̩ todu Aro̩n atama le̩, kpai afe̩ todu amo̩ma-wñ, ku ma ne̩ che e̩wñ amatama.
Likpa alu du ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s, alu le̩ amo̩ma Israe̩l fʼuko̩lo̩-wñ che chaka.
Taku Mose̩s fʼuko̩lo̩ le̩ li chaka, me̩ la go, ma fʼu che me̩; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu ma abe̩le̩ ma fu che. Taku Mose̩s kadua ñwu ma.
Ma fʼunyabo le̩ fa
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Mose̩s kakini,
O̩jo̩ ejodudu ochu ejodudu oñ e̩ du uña ugugu e-unyabo ujeju-i dago.
Uwe̩ ki dʼakpati ibenu tʼefu-wñ, kʼe̩ la dʼukpo ugbeju le̩ ta gba akpati le̩ eju.
Tak e̩ mʼitebulu du wʼejefu, kʼe̩ la fʼe̩wñ ki ajo̩ oji-wñ te̩ru; tak e̩ dʼakete le̩ wa ejefu, kʼe̩ fʼuna tʼagege-wñ jo̩.
E̩ ki la du ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ o̩jamalia ku ma gu otulale jo oji-wñ le̩ dago o̩gba akpati ibenu, kʼe̩ fʼukpo uro̩na ta alu o̩na uña ugugu le̩.
Tak e̩ du ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e̩gujo dago o̩fe̩ o̩gba alo̩na uña ugugu e-unyabo ujeju le̩,
kʼe̩ mʼukpachi ugwo̩wo̩ du gugu agbagba unyabo ujeju kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩, kʼe̩ la fʼomiofo che nyʼu.
Tak e̩ fʼologbo le̩ bu daka, kʼe̩ fʼukpo uro̩na alu ologbo le̩ ta.
Tak e̩ mʼekpo ku ma ne̩ ba tʼo̩la le̩ du kʼe̩ fʼu ba tʼuña ugugu le̩ manyʼe̩wñ du ki jʼefu-wñ; e̩ che kʼi fo̩, kpai ane̩-wñ chaka; abe̩le̩ i amud e̩wñ ki afo̩.
E̩ ki ño̩ fʼekpo batʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e̩gujo kpai e̩wñ eku-wñ chaka, kʼe̩ che kʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩ ki fo̩: abe̩le̩ ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩ afo̩ e-efo̩.
E̩ ki laño̩ fʼekpo batʼukpachi ugwo̩-wo̩ kpai e̩wñ ugugu-wñ, kʼe̩ che kʼi fo̩.
Tak e̩ nʼAro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ wa alu o̩na unyabo ujeju, kʼe̩ nʼomiofo fʼuma o̩la gwe̩.
Tak e̩ mʼe̩wñ o̩la ki afo̩ le̩ ko nyʼAro̩n o̩la; kʼe̩ fʼekpo le̩ batʼowñ o̩la, kʼe̩ che kʼi fo̩, todu kʼi chʼatama kʼi ache e̩wñ ñwu mi.
E̩ ki ño̩ kʼamo̩ma-wñ wa ge̩, kʼe̩ kʼafe̩ nyʼuma o̩la,
kʼe̩ fʼekpo ba tʼuma o̩la, alu kʼe̩ batʼata-ma o̩la le̩, kʼama ki chʼamatama ku ma che e̩wñ ñwu mi. Ekpo ki chebatʼuma o̩la le̩ chʼutodu ugugu atama ku ma je̩ ogbegbele̩, gbogbo nyʼo̩hio̩gu-ma.
Mose̩s fʼabe̩le̩ che; alu du ki Jihofa ñwa ñw u, abe̩le̩ i che.
Oñ i lewatu ochu ejodudu ef o̩do̩ ekeji, o̩jo̩ ejodudu ochu le̩, ma mʼuña ugugu le̩ ko dago.
Mose̩s la mʼuña ugugu le̩ ko dago, i mʼo̩ka-wñ ko nyʼane̩ jo̩, tak i mʼakatakpo-wñ ko dago, i la mʼoli ugbo̩lo̩-wñ ko tunyʼu, oñ i mʼoli urane̩-wñ ko dago jo̩;
tak i fʼunyabo ta bʼuña ugugu le̩ ma, oñ i mʼe̩wñ e̩boma ko bʼoji-wñ ma ate̩, alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Tak i mʼe̩wñ ibenu le̩ du tʼef akpati, i la mʼugbo̩lo̩ oli ko tunyʼo̩la akpati, tak i dʼugugu unye̩do̩ nyʼate̩ kʼi nʼoji akpati le̩;
tak i dʼakpati le̩ wa ef uña ugugu, oñ i mʼukpo ugbeju ko ta, i la mʼu du gbʼakpati ibenu le̩ eju; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Tak i mʼitebulu le̩ du tef unyabo ujeju, o̩wo̩ o̩pata-wñ ate̩ uña ugugu ejo̩do̩da ñw ukpo ugbeju le̩,
oñ i mʼakala-wñ ko te̩ jo̩ oji-wñ o̩gba Jihofa; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Tak i mʼakete le̩ du tef unyabo ujeju o̩wo̩ o̩pata o̩gane̩ uña ugugu kʼi kpejuru itebulu le̩.
Tak i fʼuna tʼagege o̩gba Jihofa jo̩; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Oñ i mʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e-o̩jamalia du tef unyabo ujeju o̩gba ukpo ugbeju le̩,
oñ i fʼotulale ki akpo gujo oji-wñ; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Tak i mʼukpo uro̩na alugbo̩na uña ugugu ko ta e̩gu-wñ.
Tak i mʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ e̩gujo du dago alu o̩na uña ugugu e-unyabo ujeju le̩, oñ i fʼe̩wñ e̩gujo che oji-wñ kpai e̩wñ ele ku ma kowa; alu ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Tak i mʼukpachi ugwo̩wo̩ du gugu agbagba unyabo ujeju kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩, i la che omiofo nyʼu ku ma nagwʼo̩la.
Oñ Mose̩s kpai Aro̩n kpai amo̩ma-wñ nʼe-le̩ gwʼo̩wo̩-ma kpai e̩re̩-ma;
e̩gba ku ma nyʼef unyabo ujeju le̩ kpai e̩gba ku ma te̩me̩rʼubo̩ iche̩bo̩ ma fʼu gwe̩; aluki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Mose̩s.
Tak i fʼologbo le̩ bu nyʼuña ugugu kpai ubo̩ iche̩bo̩ le̩ daka, oñ i mʼukpo uro̩na alu olo̩gbo le̩ ko ta. Abe̩le̩ Mose̩s fʼuko̩lo̩ le̩ chekpa.
Tak akpa le̩ lewa bʼoji unyabo ujeju le̩ ma, oñ ojima Jihofa che̩ko̩ uña ugugu le̩.
Mose̩s la neke gudu tef unyabo ujeju le̩ n, todabu kʼakpa le̩ gugu oji-wñ, kʼojima Jihofa la che̩ko̩ uña ugugu le̩.
Ule̩ du ku ma le, e̩gba du ku ma mʼakpa le̩ du bʼoji uña ugugu te̩, amo̩ma Israe̩l kʼe̩re̩ nyʼule̩ alo̩;
i muda che̩wñ ku ma ma du akpa le̩ bʼo̩ te̩ n, maku ma chʼe̩re̩ ule̩ n gbogbo tʼo̩jo̩ ku ma mʼu du bʼo̩ te̩.
Todu akpa Jihofa le̩ bʼoji uña ugugu ma o̩ro̩ka, una la dʼefu-wñ odu, eju abo unyi Israe̩l chaka ugbo du ku ma le kade.
Jọshua
Ọjọ jẹ ñwu Jọshua koji Mosẹs
Oñ i lewatu abu ku Mosẹs, adu Jihofa lẹ, leku, Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua, ọma Nun kʼi ache ẹwñ ñwu Mosẹs lẹ, kakini,
Mosẹs adu-mi la leku mẹ; todulẹ uwẹ ki kwanẹ kʼẹ daba Jọrdan-i, uwẹ kpai amonẹ-i chaka, mẹ nyʼoj anẹ kʼu nadu ñwu ma, owñ chʼamọma Israẹl-i.
Ugbo du kʼadaba ẹrẹ-wẹ mʼanẹ, uwẹ omi du ñwu, alu kʼu ka ñwu Mosẹs lẹ.
Akwo ajẹtachi kpai anẹ Lẹbanọn kidẹ, gbogbo wʼohimini elile, owñ chʼohimini Yufretis, kpai anẹ abo Hẹt chaka gbogbo wʼOhimini Elile ọwọ olanẹ, e-lẹ chʼalọmẹ-wẹ.
I nʼẹnẹ du kʼi aneke gbʼọna nyʼuwẹ ọjọ du kʼudeju-wẹ kade n; alu kʼu dʼugbo Mosẹs, alu lẹ nadʼugbo wẹ gẹ; nawe ehi iñmi kʼẹ n, nahi uwẹ tinyọ n.
Fʼeju gbiti kʼẹ fʼẹdọ nẹ; todu uwẹ ajẹ ñw amonẹ-i jẹ anẹ kʼu gọ ñw amata-ma ka kʼu nadu ñwu ma-i ẹwñ ogu.
Fʼeju gbiti kate, kʼẹ fʼẹdọ nẹ nana, kʼẹ fejutẹ kʼẹ che teju alu du kʼukọọla ki Mosẹs, adu-mi, ñwa ñw ẹ lẹ ka; ẹ ki rida bʼọ tẹ tʼọwọ awọtọ abẹk awohi n, todu ki ra ñw ẹ ugbo du kʼuwẹ anyi.
Ọla ọtakada ukọọla-i akwo bʼuwẹ alu tẹ n, ama ẹ nayaye-wñ tʼọrọka tʼodu, todu kʼuwẹ ki dejutẹ kʼẹ che teju alu du ku ma kʼọrubutu efu-wñ; todu ẹgbalẹ ẹwñ-wẹ kʼẹ che anawo ñw ẹ, ẹgbalẹ tak i ara ñw ẹ.
I chʼomi ñwa ñw ẹ n? Ẹ fʼeju gbiti kʼẹ la fʼẹdọ nẹ; ẹ ki chokpo n, ẹdọ-wẹ ki da kpu n; todu Jihofa Ọjọ-wẹ dʼugbo wẹ ugbo du kʼuwẹ anyi.
Ma mʼọla ku ma daba Jọrdan
Taku Jọshua ñwa ñw amakọtakada amonẹ lẹ kakini,
Mẹ na le alumeji uru-i ku mẹ ka ñw amonẹ kakini, Mẹ fʼọna ujẹwñ che ñw ọla-mẹ; todu i ajọ ọjọ mẹta tak amẹ adaba Jọrdan-i kʼumẹ nyʼọmọ abʼuma gbʼanẹ ki Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ du ñwu mẹ ku mẹ nẹ-i n.
Taku Jọshua ka ñw abo Rubẹn, kpai abo Gad, kpai ukpẹreji ọlọpu abo Manasa kakini,
Mẹ nadibetʼọla e-ki Mosẹs adu Jihofa lẹ ñwa ñwu mẹ, kakini, Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ mʼuñmi du ñwu mẹ mẹ, i lañọ mʼanẹ-i du ñwu mẹ gẹ.
Amọya-mẹ kpai abo-mẹ egini, kpai amẹwñukpa-mẹ, ajọ oj anẹ e-ki Mosẹs du ñwu mẹ ejudaba Jọrdan-i; ama amẹnugbiti ku ma nʼuwohi ku ma jʼefu-mẹ chaka amʼọla ogu ku mẹ daba ọgba amọmaye-mẹ, ku mẹ bʼuma che;
gbogbo taku Jihofa du uñmi ñw amọmaye-mẹ alu kʼi du ñwu mẹ, kʼama ki ñọ mʼanẹ ki Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ adu ñwu ma gba gẹ; ẹgbalẹ tak amẹ adabi tʼoj anẹ kʼamẹ nẹ-i, ku mẹ mʼu gba, owñ chʼe-ki Mosẹs adu Jihofa du ñwu mẹ ejudaba Jọrdan ọwọ olodudu-wñ.
Taku ma dohi ñwu Jọshua kakini, Ẹwñ du kʼẹ ñwa ñw a ache, ugbo du kʼẹ kpʼuwa nyi a ale.
Alu kʼa netirʼọla Mosẹs ef ẹwñ du, alu lẹ a anetirʼọla-wẹ; Jihofa Ọjọ-wẹ kʼi dʼugbo wẹ alu kʼi dʼugbo Mosẹs lẹ dee.
Ẹnẹ du kʼi alañu rʼẹwñ kʼẹ ñwa ñw a tẹ, kʼi ma la netirʼọla-wẹ ẹwñ du kʼẹ ñwa ñw u n, ekpa ma akpʼẹnẹ lẹ kʼi ku. Uwẹ ki fʼeju gbiti kʼẹ la fʼẹdọ nẹ dee.
Amatu anẹ meji lewa Jẹriko
Taku Jọshua, ọma Nun lẹ, fʼonẹ meji kpẹ maja maja akwo Shitim atu anẹʼka, i kakini, Mẹ nyʼafʼanẹ lẹ go, owñ che Jẹriko. Taku ma le, ma lewa unyi ajọkọʼka kʼodu-wñ kọ Rehab, oñ ma ru ọmọ.
Taku ma mudu ka ñw onu Jẹriko kakini. Go, abokẹlẹ abo Israẹl mugudu wʼemi odu-i ku ma tu anẹ-wa.
Tak onu Jẹriko kpuchẹ nyʼugbo Rehab, kakini, Mʼabokẹlẹ ku ma wʼugbo wẹ lẹ ko dufu wa, owñ chʼabo ku ma gudu wʼef unyi-wẹ lẹ; todu ama wa ku ma tu anẹ-i.
Onobulẹ lẹ la mʼabokẹlẹ meji lẹ ko maja ẹgba lẹ mẹ; oñ i kakini, Ochochi abokẹlẹ lẹ wʼugbo mi, u muda ma ugbo ku ma kwo wa n;
oñ i lewatu amẹru iko ku ma rʼọna alaku lẹ, ẹgba kʼanẹ chubi, abokẹlẹ lẹ ledufu; u la mʼugbo kʼabokẹlẹ lẹ le n; rano ma piopio, todu mẹ amu ma.
Ẹgbalẹ i la mʼuma ko le tʼojokunyi, i ko ma maja ef oli flaks e-kʼi ko tẹjọ ojokunyi lẹ.
Tak abo lẹ rano ma tʼej ọna kʼuma nyi Jọrdan ugbo ki dẹ hiẹhiẹlẹ lẹ; abu kʼabo ku ma rano ma ledufu ababalẹ ma fʼalaku re.
Oñ ọgba taku ma dachi onobulẹ lẹ mutẹgu wʼugbo ma ojokunyi lẹ,
oñ i ka ñw abokẹlẹ lẹ kakini, U chema ka ki Jihofa mʼanẹ-i du ñwu mẹ, kʼokpo-mẹ fʼuwa mu mẹ, kʼabo ku ma dodo anẹ-i ayọ dab ekpo ru mẹ ọgba.
Todu a gbọ alu ki Jihofa jẹ ñw omi Ohimini Ekpikpa gbẹ bʼumẹ ọgba tẹ, ẹgba ku mẹ kwʼIjipti dufu wa lẹ, kpai ẹwñ ku ma che amonu Amọr meji ku ma jʼudaba Jọrdan lẹ, owñ chʼe-ku mẹ che Sihọn kpai Ọg, ku mẹ mʼuma kojọ ñw Ọjọ jali.
Oñ abu kʼa gbọ, ababalẹ ẹdọ-wa muyọ efu-wa, unẹdọ ñọ bọ efu ẹnẹ du gẹ n, todu mẹ; todu Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ chʼỌjọ efojale atẹ, kpai ilẹ ọganẹ-i.
Todulẹ narodubʼumẹ fai, kakini, Amẹ ki fi Jihofa gọ ñwu mi, ka kʼalu kʼu fʼẹnyọ che ñwu mẹ, abẹlẹ amẹ ñʼache ẹnyọ ñw abo unyi ata-mi, mẹ ki ñọ dʼẹwñ uhiọwọ ochochi ñwu mi gẹ;
kʼamẹ ajadu ata-mi, kpai iye-mi kpai amọmaye-mi, ẹnẹkẹlẹ kpai onobulẹ, kpai ẹwñ du ku ma nẹ, kʼamẹ ki la gba oji-wa tẹ kʼa we eku.
Tak abokẹlẹ lẹ ka ñw u kakini, Oji-wa ki koji e-mẹ, ichẹwñ kʼamẹ ma du ọla-wa-i ka dufu n; mak ẹgba ki Jihofa mʼanẹ-i du ñw a a ache ẹnyọ kpai ochochi kpʼuwẹ.
Tak i jẹ ñwu ma le bʼiku lʼowe windo tanẹ, todu unyi-wñ lamọla aku, unyi-wñ ugbo kʼi dẹ dʼoj aku lẹ.
Oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, Mẹ nyʼugbo uwo lẹ, todẹgba kʼabo ku ma rano mẹ wa kẹrẹbʼumẹ; mẹ maja ọmọ ọjọ mẹta, gbogbo tak abo ku ma rano mẹ lẹ mudabi; ubilẹ taku mẹ neke lo mẹ.
Tak abokẹlẹ lẹ ka ñw u kakini. Egọ kʼẹ jẹ ñw a gọ lẹ afu wa oji.
Go, ẹgba kʼa lewa oj anẹ-i, uwẹ ki mʼowu ekpikpa-i du nʼowe ugbo kʼẹ ko wa le tʼanẹ lẹ; tak uwẹ ki mʼata-wẹ kpai iye-wẹ, kpai amọmaye-wẹ, kpai abo unyi ata-wẹ chaka kowa jʼugbo wẹ ef unyi-wẹ-i.
I la chẹwñ kʼẹnẹ du lʼalugbọna unyi-wẹ dufu tʼej ọna, ẹbiẹ-wñ adʼoji e-wñ, i la anʼudu ñw a n; i muda chẹwñ kʼọwọ kado ẹnẹ du kʼi dʼef unyi kpai uwẹ mak ẹbiẹ-wñ adʼoji e-wa.
Ama ichẹwñ kʼuwẹ mʼọla-wa-i duka mak ẹgbalẹ egọ kʼẹ jẹ ñw a gọ ñw ẹ lẹ afʼuwa oji.
Tak i kakini, I ki dʼalu ku mẹ ka lẹ. Oñ i jẹ ñwu ma kwʼọmọ, oñ ma le ma; tak i mʼowu ekpikpa lẹ du ji mʼowe lẹ.
Tak abo lẹ le, oñ ma lewa anẹ uwo lẹ, ma la gugu ọmọ ọjọ mẹta, gbogbo tak abo ku ma rano ma lẹ mudabi; todu abo ku ma rano ma lẹ tejanẹ ma ugbo du ọna ọmọ, ma la li ma n.
Tak abokẹlẹ meji lẹ mudabi gwọru oji uwo tanẹ, oñ ma mudaba wʼugbo Jọshua ọma Nun; oñ ma mʼẹwñ du ki kẹrẹbʼuma du ka ñw u.
Oñ ma ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Ochochi, Jihofa mʼanẹ lẹ chaka ko nyʼuwa ọwọ mẹ; ẹdọ abo anẹ ọmọ chaka la muyọ rʼọgba-wa.
Ma mu Jọrdan daba
Taku Jọshua takpa kwanẹ odudu-wñ, owñ kpai abo Israẹl chaka muñọ bu Shitim tẹ lewa ọla Jọrdan; oñ ma ru ọmọ ọgba taku ma daba.
Abu kʼọjọ mẹta jọ amakọtakada lale alumeji uru lẹ;
oñ ma ñwa ñw amonẹ lẹ kakini, Ẹgba ku mẹ fʼakpati alo e-Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ li, abu kʼamatama ku ma chʼabo Lifai lẹ anẹ, ẹgbalẹ mẹ muñọ bʼuña-mẹ-i tẹ ku mẹ tʼọ ubi,
kʼamẹ ki ma ọna ki chʼukpẹ kʼamẹ ale; todu amẹ le ọna-i mama ta n. Owe muda atẹ agbagba amẹ kpai owñ, ujiji-wñ adab ohibọwọ icham nyʼọgwọkọ meji; amẹ ki tẹmẹrʼu n.
Taki Jọshua ka ñw amonẹ lẹ kakini, Mẹ che kʼọla-mẹ ki fọ; todu Jihofa ache ẹwñ awuwu efu-mẹ ọna.
Taki Jọshua ka ñw amatama lẹ kakini, Mʼakpati alo lẹ du ku mẹ dʼọgba amonẹ-i daba. Taku ma mʼakpati alo lẹ du, oñ ma tʼamonẹ lẹ ọgba.
Taki Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Eñini-i nachanẹ ejẹ ñw ẹ nana eju abo Israẹl chaka, kʼama ki ma ka kʼalu kʼu dʼugbo Mosẹs, alu lẹ nadʼugbo wẹ gẹ.
Uwẹ ki la ñwa ñw amatama ku ma nẹ akpati alo lẹ, kakini, Ẹgba ku mẹ lewa eti omi Jọrdan, mẹ ki dago choo efu omi Jọrdan.
Taki Jọshua ka ñw abo Israẹl chaka kakini, Mẹ lewa ku mẹ gbʼọla Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ.
Taki Jọshua kakini, Alu ku mẹ ale ku mẹ ama ka kʼỌjọ ki deju dʼefu-mẹ lẹ dẹ, ka ki nʼugbo du ki achi n, owñ lẹ afʼabo Kenan kpai abo Hẹt kpai abo Hifai kpai abo Pẹrẹz kpai abo Girgash kpai abo Amọr kpai abo Jẹbius ne dufu bʼumẹ ọgba tẹ.
Go, akpati alo Ondu e-abo ilẹ du alale ọgba-mẹ tefu Jọrdan.
Todulẹ nachʼonẹ mẹgwẹji kwef ọlọpu ọlọpu Israẹl fai, ọlọpu du nẹ ẹnẹʼka ẹnẹʼka.
Taki awatu, ẹgba kʼadaba ẹrẹ amatama ku ma nʼakpati Jihofa kʼi chʼOndu ilẹ du, tunyʼomi Jọrdan, mak omi Jọrdan lẹ amukọda meji, owñ chʼomi ki acha kwʼatẹ wa, i la agba dago ugbo okate logoo.
Abẹlẹ ẹgba kʼamonẹ lẹ kwo bʼunyabo-ma tẹ ku ma daba Jọrdan, kʼamatama ku ma nẹ akpati alo lẹ jʼọgba amonẹ lẹ,
tak ẹgba kʼabo ku ma nʼakpati lẹ lewa Jọrdan, kʼẹrẹ amatama ku ma nʼakpati lẹ kwo tunyʼeti omi (todu Jọrdan awobi bʼoji otete-wñ chaka ma iko ku ma ko ẹwñ oko wʼunyi lẹ),
omi ki kwʼọwọ atẹ awa kwodago, oñ i kwanẹ dago logoo ugbo okate, ọnajiji, ugbo Adam, ewo ki mẹru Zaretan, tak e-kʼi acha nyʼọganẹ rʼọwọ ohimini Araba, owñ chʼOhimini Omu lẹ, e-lẹ mukọda bʼe-atẹ tẹ hioko; tak amonẹ lẹ mudaba mẹru Jẹriko ananẹ.
Oñ amatama ku ma nẹ akpati alo e-Jihofa lẹ kwodago kpaka anẹ ẹgbẹ alumeji Jọrdan lẹ gbogbo tak abo ichi lẹ mudaba Jọrdan hioko.
Ma mʼokuta urewa ko dago jọ
Tak i lewatu, ẹgba kʼabo ichi lẹ chaka mudaba Jọrdan hioko, Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua kakini,
Fʼonẹ mẹgweji chi ñw ọla-wẹ kwef amonẹ-i, ọlọpu du nʼẹnẹʼka ẹnẹʼka,
tak ẹ ñwa ñwu ma kakini, Mẹ mʼokuta mẹgweji ko kwʼalumeji Jọrdan-i, kwʼugbo kʼẹrẹ amatama dago kpaka, ku mẹ mʼu ko daba kpai amẹ, oñ mẹ akʼo janẹ ef unyi uru lẹ odu eñini.
Taku Jọshua fʼabokẹlẹ mẹgweji ku ma chʼabo Israẹl e-kʼi ñwʼuma ọla che jọ dọ wa, ọlọpu ọlọpu du nʼẹnẹʼka ẹnẹʼka;
oñ Jọshua ka ñwu ma kakini, Mẹ ki dʼọgba akpati Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ lẹ lale rʼalumeji Jọrdan kʼẹnẹnẹnẹnẹ-mẹ kʼi mʼokuta du nʼika-wñ, likpa alu kʼuwewe ọlọpu ọlọpu abo Israẹl dẹ,
todu kʼi chʼujiwe efu-mẹ, todu ẹgba kʼamọma-mẹ atene ej ọgba kakini, Ẹwñ chʼofe okuta ku mẹ ko jọ-i ta?
Ẹgbalẹ amẹ aka ñwu ma kakini, Omi Jọrdan-i mukọda meji rʼọgba akpati alo Jihofa; ẹgba kʼakpati lẹ mudaba Jọrdan, omi Jọrdan lẹ mukọda. Oñ okuta-i achʼurewa ñw abo Israẹl ogbegbelẹ.
Tak abo Israẹl che alu ki Jọshua ñwa ñwu ma, oñ ma mʼokuta mẹgweji ko kwef alumeji Jọrdan, alu ki Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua, uwewe-wñ dʼalu kʼuwewe ọlọpu ọlọpu abo Israẹl dẹ; taku ma mʼu ko lebʼuma tʼugbo ku ma ru, oñ ma mʼu ko jʼanẹ ọmọ.
Taku Jọshua mʼokuta mẹgweji ko dago alumeji Jọrdan ugbo kʼẹrẹ amatama ku ma nʼakpati alo lẹ manẹ; i la jʼọmọ gbogbo tʼeñini.
Todu amatama ku ma nʼakpati lẹ dago alumeji Jọrdan, gbogbo tak ẹwñ du ki Jihofa ñwa ñwu Jọshua kʼi ka ñw amonẹ lẹ che kpa, teju alu du ki Mosẹs ñwa ñwu Jọshua. Tak amonẹ lẹ hiọwọ wanẹ daba;
oñ i lewatu, abu kʼamonẹ lẹ chaka mudaba hioko, tak akpati Jihofa kpai amatama lẹ ñọ daba eju amonẹ lẹ.
Oñ abo Rubẹn, kpai abo Gad, kpai ukpẹreji ọlọpu abo Manasa, fʼọlʼogu mu daba rʼọgba abo Israẹl, alu ki Mosẹs ka ñwu ma;
abo kʼọla-ma chʼẹmu ogu ku ma daba ọgba Jihofa nyʼegbili Jẹriko ku ma nyʼoko ogu, dab onẹ icham nyʼọgwọkọ ọgbọ meji.
Ọjọ lẹ Jihofa jẹ ñwu Jọshua mud ẹnẹ lile eju abo Israẹl chaka; taku ma railo owñ, alu ku ma railo Mosẹs, gbogbo mʼọjọ uku-wñ.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua kakini,
Ẹ nañwa ñw amatama ku ma nʼakpati ibenu lẹ kʼama ki tẹgu kwefu Jọrdan dufu wa.
Todulẹ Jọshua ñwa ñw amatama lẹ kakini, Mẹ mutẹgu kwefu Jọrdan wa.
Tak i lewatu, ẹgba kʼamatama ku ma nẹ akpati alo Jihofa lẹ mutẹgu kwʼalumeji Jọrdan dufu wa, kʼadabẹrẹ amatama lẹ kwo tʼanẹ ẹgbẹ, tak omi Jọrdan mudabi tʼẹgu-wñ, oñ i wobi lʼoji otete alu ki che akwoubi lẹ.
Amonẹ lẹ la mutẹgu kwefu Jọrdan dufu ọjọ ẹkẹgwa ochu ejodudu, oñ ma ru Gilgal kʼi dẹ alọmẹ Jẹriko ọwọ olodudu-wñ.
Tak okuta mẹgweji ku ma ko kwefu Jọrdan lẹ, e-lẹ Jọshua muko dago jọ Gilgal.
Tak i ka ñw abo Israẹl kakini, Ẹgba kʼamọma-mẹ atʼamata-ma ene ejọgba-i kakini, Ẹwñ chʼofe okuta-i ta?
Ẹgbalẹ amẹ ajẹ ñw amọma-mẹ ma kakini, Israẹl daba Jọrdan-i oj anẹ ẹgbẹ.
Todu Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ jẹ ñw omi Jọrdan-i gbẹ bʼumẹ ọgba tẹ, gbogbo taku mẹ daba kpa, dabalu ki Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ che Ohimini Ekpikpa kʼi jẹ ñw u gbẹ bʼuwa ọgba tẹ, gbogbo tak a mudaba,
todu kʼabo ilẹ-i du ki ma ka kʼọwọ Jihofa gbiti; kʼamẹ ki railo Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ ọjọ du ki ñwa.
Oñ i lewatu, ẹgba kʼamonu abo Amọr ku ma jʼudaba Jọrdan ọwọ olanẹ lẹ chaka kpai amonu abo Kenan ku ma jʼọlʼohimini chaka, gbọ abu ki Jihofa jẹ ñw omi Jọrdan gbẹ bʼabo Israẹl ọgba tẹ, gbogbo taku ma mudaba kpa, ẹdọ-ma muyọ efu-ma, afu lañọ bọ efu-ma gẹ n, tod abo Israẹl lẹ.
Ma dabi kʼẹpi da
Adiko lẹ Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Mẹ du okuta ọmu che abẹ ñw ọla-mẹ, ku mẹ dabi kʼẹpi abo Israẹl da onukeji.
Abẹlẹ Jọshua fʼabẹ okuta ọmu che ñw ọla-wñ, oñ i kʼẹpi abo Israẹl da Gibeat-haaralọt.
Ẹwñ ki chi ku Jọshua la dʼuma ẹpi lẹ dẹ: Abokẹlẹ du ku ma jʼef abo ku ma kwʼ Ijipti dufu wa lẹ, owñ chʼabokẹlẹ ku ma jogu chaka leku ej ọna ef ajẹtachi, abu ku ma kwʼIjipti dufu wa.
Todu amonẹ du ku ma kwʼọmọ dufu wa fʼẹpi da, ama amonẹ du ku ma bi ej ọna ef ajẹtachi abu ku ma kwʼIjipti dufu wa lẹ, la dʼẹpi ta n.
Todu abo Israẹl tale ef ajẹtachi lẹ ọdọ ọgbọ meji, gbogbo taku ma fʼabo ichi lẹ du, owñ chʼabokẹlẹ ku ma jogu ku ma kwʼ Ijipti dufu wa lẹ, liẹ kpa, todabu ku ma ma netirʼomu Jihofa n; owñ chʼabo ki Jihofa fugọ ñwu ma ka kʼi ajẹ ñwu ma fʼeju-ma do anẹ e-ki Jihofa gọ ñw amata-ma ka kʼi adu ñw ma, anẹ kʼomi ẹnya kpai iñọ acha efu-wñ.
Taku Jọshua fʼamọma-ma kʼi ko kwanẹ koji ma ẹpi da; todu ẹpi-ma chʼodukulu ta, abu ku ma ma dʼuma ẹpi ej ọna lẹ n.
Oñ i lewatu, ẹgba ku ma fʼabo ichi lẹ ẹpi da kpa, kʼama kwojọ ẹgu-ma ef uru lẹ gbogbo tak i biẹ.
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Omi fʼina Ijipti li bʼumẹ ọla tẹ eñini-i mẹ. Todulẹ ma dʼodu ugbo ki dẹ kọ Gilgal, gbogbo tʼeñini.
Ma fʼElaloji jẹ
Oñ abo Israẹl kworu Gilgal lẹ; ma la fʼElaloji jẹ anẹ ọjọ ẹkẹgwẹlẹ ochu lẹ ef egbili Jẹriko.
Tak ama fʼọka e-echi anẹ lẹ jẹ ọjọñwa Elaloji gbagẹdẹ, owñ chʼakala kʼọjọwu ma dọ n, kpai akakpa ẹrọ.
Taku mana lẹ we ọjọñwa-wñ, owñ chʼabu ku ma fʼẹwñ oko anẹ lẹ jẹ; oñ abo Israẹl ñọ nẹ mana lẹ gẹ n, chai ẹro anẹ Kenan ma jẹ ọdọ lẹ.
Oñ i lewatu, ẹgba ki Jọshua mẹru Jẹriko lẹ, kʼi la chi eju-wñ nyʼatẹ ago, ẹ la go, ẹnẹkẹlẹʼka dago kpenyʼu, ọbẹchageli-wñ chʼẹwọ nʼọwọ; taki Jọshua nyʼugbo-wñ aka ñw u kakini, Ẹnẹ-wa ẹ che? abẹk ẹ dʼef abo ku ma fʼuwa kpama?
Oñ i kakini, Ọda; ama todu kʼu chʼagboji abogu Jihofa oñ u wa-i. Taku Jọshua lewa fʼeju bʼanẹ ma, oñ i dojikanẹ, i la ka ñw u kakini, Ab odu-mi aka ñw adu-wñ-i?
Tak agboji abogu Jihofa lẹ ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Mʼẹda-wẹ gwọ bʼẹrẹ-wẹ tẹ, todu ugbo kʼẹ dago lẹ afọ. Taku Jọshua fʼabẹlẹ che.
Ma fu Jẹriko kpọfọ
Alaku Jẹriko chaka la chere, ma mʼukodo-wñ ko tunyu todu abo Israẹl; ẹnẹ du adufu n, ẹnẹ du la agudu wʼejefu n.
Oñ Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua kakini. Go, u mʼiJẹriko du tʼuwẹ ọwọ mẹ, kpai onu-wñ, kpai amẹnugbiti-wñ ku ma nʼuwohi,
oñ anẹ ale ewo lẹ daka, abokẹlẹ ku ma jogu chaka ale ewo lẹ daka onuʼka. Abẹlẹ uwẹ ache gbogbo nyʼọjọ mẹfa.
Oñ amatama mebie anẹ ọkakachi ọga echi mebie ale rʼọgba akpati lẹ; tak ọjọ ẹkebie-wñ ama ale ewo lẹ daka onu mebie, oñ amatama anʼọkakachi-ma afa.
Tak i awatu, ẹgba ku ma fa igba ọga echi lẹ taa, kʼamẹ la gbọ omu ọkakachi lẹ, amonẹ du anʼukwa akwa nana; tak ọdọ aku ewo lẹ agulọ bʼanẹ ma, oñ ẹnẹnẹnẹnẹ efu amonẹ lẹ afʼẹdọ kʼẹdọ-wñ atẹgu tʼọgba-wñ alo.
Abẹlẹ Jọshua, ọma Nun lẹ, fʼamatama dọ wa oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, Mẹ mʼakpati alo lẹ du, tak amatama mebie ki nʼọkakachi ọga echi mebie rʼọgba akpati Jihofa lẹ.
Tak i ka ñw amonẹ lẹ kakini, Mẹ kanyi alo ku mẹ le ewo lẹ daka, ku mẹ jẹ ñw abokẹlẹ kʼọla-ma chẹmu ogu ku ma lale rʼọgba akpati Jihofa.
Oñ alu ki Jọshua ka ñw amonẹ lẹ, amatama mebie ku ma nʼọkakachi ọga echi mebie ọgba Jihofa lẹ le rʼọgba, oñ ma nʼọkakachi-ma afa, akpati alo Jihofa la tʼuma ubi.
Oñ abokẹlẹ ku ma mʼọla ogu le rʼọgba amatama ku ma fa ọkakachi lẹ, oñ abo ki dʼubi tʼakpati ubi, ma nʼọkakachi afa abu ku ma alo.
Jọshua la ñwa ñw amonẹ lẹ kakini, Amẹ ki kpogu n, ẹnẹ du ki gbʼomu-mẹ n, ọla du ki kwef alu-mẹ dufu n, gbogbo nyʼọjọ kʼu naka ñwu mẹ ku mẹ kpogu; ẹgbalẹ taku mẹ akpogu.
Abẹlẹ i jẹ ñw akpati Jihofa ki le ewo lẹ daka, i le onuʼka; taku ma lewa uru lẹ, oñ ma kworu.
Taki Jọshua takpa kwanẹ odudu, oñ amatama mʼakpati Jihofa du.
dufu gẹ; oñ ma mʼuma ko jʼej ọdọda uru abo Israẹl lẹ.
Taku ma fʼewo gujo rinyọ kpai ẹwñ du ki jʼefu-wñ; chai ajifa-wñ kpai ọjamalia-wñ kpai ẹwñ eku ebijeikpa kpai ebije, ma mʼe-lẹ ko nyʼef akpulu ef unyi Jihofa.
Ama Jọshua fu Rehab ajọkọ lẹ kpai abo unyi ata-wñ kpai ẹwñ du kʼi nẹ jadu ku ma deju; oñ onobulẹ lẹ gugu alumeji abo Israẹl gbogbo tʼojolu eñini, todabu kʼi kʼamonuchẹ ki Jọshua kpẹ atʼanẹ Jẹriko lẹ maja.
Taku Jọshua jẹ ñwu ma gọ iko lẹ kakini, Ama ki fʼẹnẹ du kʼi kwanẹ anʼọdọ Jẹriko-i mu eju Jihofa. Ẹrẹ-wñ kʼi adudanẹ chʼọmọgba-wñ elenyọ, alaku-wñ edudago chʼudabi-wñ elenyọ.
Abẹlẹ Jihofa dʼugbo Jọshua; oñ uwohi-wñ dʼugbo du anẹ lẹ.
Ọwọ-ma bʼAi jọ n, tod adure Ekan lẹ
Ama amọma Israẹl fʼada jẹ efu ẹwñ ku ma kojọ ñw Ọjọ lẹ; todu Ekan, ọma Karmi, ọma Zabdi, ọma Zara, ef ọlọpu Juda, mʼẹwñ ko kwef ẹwñ ku ma kojọ ñw Ọjọ lẹ; tak uwẹdọ Jihofa mutajo abʼabo Israẹl ma.
Jọshua la fʼonẹ kpẹ kwo Jẹriko nyi Ai kʼi dʼọwọʼka Bẹt-afẹn, ọwọ olodudu Bẹtẹl, oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, Mẹ tẹgu nyʼọmọ atʼanẹ lẹ. Tak abokẹlẹ lẹ le natʼanẹ Ai.
Oñ ma mudabi wʼugbo Jọshua, oñ ma ka ñw u kakini, Uwẹ ki jẹ ñw ọchaka amonẹ-i le n, chai abokẹlẹ icham nyʼọgwọkọ meji abẹk ẹta ki le ku ma fʼAi kpọfọ; ẹ ki jẹ ñw amonẹ-i chaka ki chʼọbata anyʼọmọ n, todu abo lẹ wewe n.
Abẹlẹ uwewe abokẹlẹ ku ma dab onẹ icham nyʼọgwọkọ mẹta nyʼọmọ; oñ ma ra rʼọgba abokẹlẹ Ai.
Abokẹlẹ Ai lẹ la fʼabokẹlẹ-ma kpa dab onẹ oguẹgwa nyoke mẹfa; oñ ma fʼuma ne bʼalaku lẹ tẹ gbogbo nyi Shebarim, oñ ma fʼuma kpa ugbo agwọru lẹ. Tak ẹdọ amonẹ lẹ muyọ, oñ i mud omi efu-ma.
Taku Jọshua fʼẹwñ ọla-wñ fana, oñ i lewa fʼeju rọ bʼanẹ ma ọgba akpati Jihofa gbogbo tʼolanẹ, owñ kpai abogijo Israẹl; taku ma fʼebutu gba nyʼọla-ma oji.
Taku Jọshua kakini, Atogwo, Ondu Jihofa, ẹwñ chi kʼẹ kʼeko amonẹ-i du wʼudaba Jọrdan-i kʼẹ mʼuwa ko nyʼef ọwọ abo Amọr, kʼẹ jẹ ñw a lenyọ? Ẹdọ-wa du kʼa gugu ejudaba Jọrdan lẹ, i ma nyọ.
O, Ondu, abʼu naka, abu kʼabo Israẹl murida rʼamẹnebi-ma ọgba.
Todu abo Kenan, kpai abo ku ma dodo anẹ-i chaka agbʼinabali-wñ, taku ma ado nyʼuwa daka, taku ma akʼodu-wa da bʼanẹ-ilẹ tẹ; oñ abʼuwẹ ache todu odu-wẹ inaina-i ta?
Taki Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Kwanẹ dago, ẹwñ chi kʼẹ fʼeju-wẹ rọ bʼanẹ ma-i ta?
Abo Israẹl fʼadure ta; ma lañọ fʼalo-mi kʼu ñwa ñwu ma daba gẹ; ma la mʼẹwñ ko kwef ẹwñ ku ma kojọ ñw Ọjọ lẹ; ma la fʼoji ji, ma ñọ dʼọwọ ye eju gẹ; ma lañọ mʼẹwñ lẹ ko jʼef anẹ e-ma gẹ.
Todulẹ oñ amọma Israẹl ma neke dago ọgba amẹnebi-ma n; oñ ma murida rʼọgba amẹnebi-ma, todabu kʼama mʼọla-ma kojọ ñw Ọjọ mẹ. U ñʼadʼugbo mẹ gẹ n, chai ẹgba ku mẹ fʼẹwñ ku ma kojọ ñw Ọjọ lẹ chilẹchẹ bʼalumeji-mẹ tẹ.
Kwanẹ, fʼamonẹ-i che ku ma fọ, kʼẹ la kakini, Mẹ fʼọla-mẹ gwo rinyọ nyʼọna; todu abu ki Jihofa Ọjọ abo Israẹl ka dẹ kakini, O Israẹl, ẹwñ ku ma kojọ ñw Ọjọ oka dʼalumeji-mẹ; amẹ neke dago ọgba amẹnebi-mẹ n, gbogbo taku mẹ dʼẹwñ ku ma dutẹ ñw Ọjọ lẹ tinyọ bʼalumeji-mẹ tẹ.
Todulẹ ama ako mẹ wa, ọlọpu ọlọpu, odudu ọna; tak abu i adẹ dẹ, ọlọpu ki Jihofa mu adufu wa ikpunyi ikpunyi; tak ikpunyi ki Jihofa mu adufu wa akwọra unyi akwọra unyi, tak abo akwọra unyi ki Jihofa mu adufu wa okʼoka.
Taku ma afʼẹnẹku Jihofa mu kʼẹwñ ku ma dutẹ ñw Ọjọ lẹ dʼef ọwọ-wñ gujo, tʼowñ tʼẹwñ du kʼi nẹ: todabu kʼi mʼalo Jihofa daba kpai todabu kʼi fʼẹwñ tuñu che efu Israẹl.
Abẹlẹ Jọshua takpa kwanẹ odudu, oñ i kʼabo Israẹl wa ọlọpu ọlọpu, oñ ọla lẹ fʼabo ọlọpu Juda mu;
tak i mʼabo Juda ko wa; oñ i fʼabo ikpunyi Zera mu: tak i mʼabo ikpunyi Zẹra kowa okʼoka; oñ i fu Zabdi mu;
tak i mʼabo akwọra unyi-wñ duwa okʼoke; oñ i fu Ekan, ọma Karmi, ọma Zabdi, ọma Zẹra, ef ọlọpu Juda mu.
Tak i Jọshua ka ñw Ekan kakini, Ọma-mi, agba, ẹ ki dojima ñwu Jihofa, kʼi chʼỌjọ abo Israẹl, kʼẹ gbalu ñw u; ka ñwu mi ẹwñ kʼẹ che fai; ẹ ki du maja ñwu mi n.
Tak Ekan dohi ñwu Jọshua kakini, Ochochi, u fu Jihofa, Ọjọ abo Israẹl dure mẹ, ẹwñ kʼu che la dẹ;
ẹgba kʼu fʼotogbo Babilọn ọmẹmẹlẹ li ef anẹ kʼa ko lẹ, kpai ajifa alu shẹkẹl ulọkọ kpai odukulu ọjamaliaʼka kʼuwoji-wñ che shẹkẹl ooje, ẹgbalẹ u chʼejufufu-wñ oñ u mʼu ko; ẹ la go, i gwaji anẹpẹtẹ ef unyabo-mi lẹ, ajifa la jʼofe-wñ.
Abẹlẹ Jọshua fʼamonuchẹ kpẹ nyʼọmọ, oñ ma fule nyʼef unyabo lẹ; ẹ la go, i maja ef unyabo-wñ lẹ, oñ ajifa jʼofe-wñ ọganẹ.
Taku ma mʼu ko kwef unyabo lẹ, oñ ma mʼu ko wʼugbo Jọshua, kpai abo Israẹl chaka; taku ma mʼu ko jʼanẹ ọgba Jihofa.
Taku Jọshua, kpai abo Israẹl chaka, gwọnyu Ekan ọma Zẹra, kpai ajifa lẹ, kpai otogbo, kpai odukulu ọjamalia lẹ, kpai amọma-wñ ẹnẹkẹlẹ kpai onobulẹ kpai amọkokunọ-wñ kpai amọkẹkẹtẹ-wñ kpai amẹwñọrẹ-wñ egini kpai unyabo-wñ kpai ẹwñ du kʼi nẹ; oñ ma mʼu ko wa jʼef ọgọ Ekọr.
Taku Jọshua kakini, Ab ẹ le kʼẹ ma chʼuwa uñmi n? Jihofa achʼuwẹ uñmi eñini-i n. Tak abo Israẹl chaka kʼokuta rọ dʼo; ma la nʼuna fʼuma gujo, oñ ma kʼokuta rọ do ma.
Oñ ma mʼokuta re bʼọ oji ma dago dab ugbudu lile kʼi dʼọmọ gbogbo tʼeñini; taku Jihofa rida bʼẹkpuna uwẹdọ-wñ tẹ. Todulẹ oñ ma dʼodu ugbo kidẹ kọ Ọgọ Ekọr, gbogbo tʼeñini.
Ma fʼAi kpọfọ
Taku Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Ẹ ki railo n, ẹdọ-wẹ ki muda kpu n; mʼabo ku ma jogu chaka ko lebʼuwẹ, kʼẹ kwanẹ, kʼẹ nyi Ai; go, u mʼonu Ai, kpai abo-wñ, kpai ewo-wñ, kpai anẹ-wñ ko nyʼuwẹ ọwọ mẹ;
uwẹ ki la che Ai kpai onu-wñ alu kʼẹ che Jẹriko kpai onu-wñ lẹ; ẹ muda mʼanẹ-wñ kʼogu jẹ kpai amẹla abẹrẹmẹlẹ-wñ ko chʼẹwñ alujẹ ñw ọla-wẹ: ẹ ki kpala nyʼewo lẹ, ejubi-wñ.
Abẹlẹ Jọshua kwanẹ, kpai abo ku ma jogu chaka, ku ma nyi Ai; taku Jọshua fʼonẹ icham nyʼọgwọkọ oguẹgwa chi, amẹnugbiti ku ma nʼuwohi lẹ, oñ i jẹ ñwu ma le odu.
Tak i ñwa ñw ma kakini, Go, amẹ ki kpala nyʼewo lẹ ejubi-wñ; mẹ ki le jiji bʼewo lẹ tẹ n, ama ọla-mẹ ki chʼẹmu chaka;
tak omi, kpai amonẹ ku ma jʼugbo mi, atẹmẹrʼewo lẹ. Oñ i awatu, ẹgba ku ma dufu wa kʼuma kobʼuwa alu ku ma wa che ẹgba ejodudu lẹ, a ara rʼọgba-ma;
tak ama dufu wa atʼuwa ubi gbogbo tak a fʼuma fa bʼewo lẹ tẹ; todu ama akakini, Ma ra rʼọgba-wa alu ku ma che ejodudu lẹ. Abẹlẹ a ara rʼọgba-ma;
tak amẹ ki kwanẹ kwugbo ku mẹ kpala jọ lẹ, ku mẹ mʼewo lẹ gba; todu Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ amʼu du tʼumẹ ọwọ.
Tak i awatu, ẹgba ku mẹ mʼewo lẹ gba nyʼọwọ, tak amẹ adʼuna tʼewo lẹ, ku mẹ che alu ki Jihofa ka lẹ, mẹ go, omi ñwa ñwu mẹ mẹ.
Taku Jọshua fʼuma kpẹ lo; oñ ma nyʼakpala nyʼu lẹ, ma la jọ agbagba Bẹtẹl kpai Ai, ọwọ olanẹ Ai; Jọshua muda lẹ ef amonẹ lẹ odu ọjọ lẹ.
Oñ Jọshua takpa kwanẹ odudu-wñ, oñ i mʼamonẹ lẹ ko talajọ, tak owñ kpai abogijo Israẹl tʼamonẹ lẹ ọgba nyi Ai.
Tak abo ku ma jogu ku ma jʼugbo-wñ lẹ chaka mutẹgu alo, oñ ma tẹmẹru ejọgba ewo lẹ, oñ ma ru ọwọ ọpata atẹ Ai, ọgọ la dʼagbagba ama kpai Ai.
Tak i mʼonẹ dabu icham nyʼọgwọkọ mẹlu ko, oñ i jẹ ñwu ma kpala jọ agbagba Bẹtẹl kpai Ai, ọwọ olanẹ ewo lẹ.
Abẹlẹ Jọshua fʼAi gujo, oñ i mʼu du kọ ugbudu tʼogbegbelẹ, alachẹ i che gbogbo tʼeñini.
I la mʼonu Ai lẹ du lọkọli oj oli gbogbo dʼọjọ: tak abu kʼolu atunyanẹ Jọshua ñwa ñwu ma, taku ma mʼoku-wñ du tanẹ bʼoj oli tẹ, oñ ma mʼu du rikpolo tʼalaku ewo lẹ, ma la fʼokuta re bʼoji-wñ ma ki gba dab ugbudu lile, kʼi dago ọmọ gbogbo tʼeñini.
Jọshua fʼọla mẹgwa lẹ kọ nyʼokuta oj uwo Ebal
Taku Jọshua fʼubọ ichẹbọ kpa ñwu Jihofa, Ọjọ e-Israẹl, oj uwo Ebal,
alu ku Mosẹs, adu Jihofa lẹ ñwa ñw abo Israẹl, owñ chʼalu kʼi chẹkọ tanẹ ef ubuku ukọọla Mosẹs, ubọ-wñ chʼokuta okuta odukulu, e-kʼonẹ ma dʼebije kado kʼi gbẹ n; oñ ma kʼẹwñ ichẹbọ ẹgujo wa che ñwu Jihofa oji-wñ, kpai ẹwñ ichẹbọ urẹdọ.
Tak i fʼuwọli ọlubutu ukọọla Mosẹs kʼi du wa eju abo Israẹl lẹ kọ nyʼọla okuta ọmọ.
Tak abo Israẹl, tʼọmanẹ, tʼilowa, kpai amakọtakada-ma, kpai amakajọ-ma chaka, kwodago ejemi kpai ejanọmọ akpati lẹ ọgba amatama ku ma chʼabo Lifai ku ma nʼakpati alo Jihofa, ukpẹreji-ma jʼọgba uwo Gerizim, ukpẹreji-ma la jʼọgba uwo Ebal; alu ki Mosẹs adu Jihofa ñwa ñwu ma ẹgba ejodudu lẹ, kʼama ki kadua ñw abo Israẹl.
Oñ anubilẹ, i fʼọla ọtakada ukọọla duu kalata, tʼẹnyọ-wñ kʼi adu ñw onẹ, tʼama-wñ kʼi ana ñw onẹ, teju ẹwñ duu ku ma kọ nyʼọtakada ukọọla lẹ.
I nʼọla duu ku Mosẹs ñwa tẹ, ku Jọshua ma dago ọgba ujeju Israẹl lẹ akalata n, tʼabobulẹ, tʼabo egini, tʼamilowa ku ma jʼale efu ma.
Ma kpʼalo kpai abo Gibeọn
Oñ i lewatu, ẹgba kʼamonu du ku ma jʼudaba Jọrdan anẹ uwo-wñ kpai anẹ ọgọ-wñ ọla Ohimini Elile ọgba Lẹbanọn lẹ gbʼinabali-wñ, owñ chʼabo Hẹt kpai abo Amọr kpai abo Kenan kpai abo Pẹrẹz kpai abo Hifai kpai abo Jẹbius lẹ;
ma kʼọla-ma wa jeju jọ, alu-ma chʼokate, ku ma kʼogu bọ Jọshua kpai abo Israẹl.
Ama ẹgba kʼabo ku ma dodo Gibeọn gbʼinabali ẹwñ ki Jọshua che Jẹriko kpai e-kʼi che Ai,
ma la fʼugbeju che, ma fʼọla-ma che dabẹnẹ kʼama chʼamonuchẹ onuʼka, ma mʼẹgbo akpulu ko nʼubi amọkẹkẹtẹ-ma wa, kpai aiko omi achiwebẹtẹma e-igbele ki chʼẹkpana taku ma ga,
kpai ẹda ki gbo taku ma bʼẹwñ mọ jʼẹrẹ-ma, ẹwñ ọla ẹgbo jʼọla-ma; ujẹwñ du ku ma nẹ nyʼọna ajẹ la chʼẹgbẹ, i chʼẹkpebu.
Taku ma nyʼuru Gilgal ugbo Jọshua, oñ ma ka ñw u kpai abokẹlẹ Israẹl kakini, A kwʼanẹ ọnajiji wa; todulẹ mẹ kpʼalo kpai awa ke.
Tak abokẹlẹ Israẹl ka ñw abo Hifai lẹ kakini, Ikani i chʼefu-wa oñ mẹ dodo; ab a le kʼa kpʼalo kpai amẹ?
Taku ma ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Amadu-wẹ a che. Taki Jọshua ka ñwu ma kakini, Abo ugbo mẹ che ta? Ugbo mẹ kwo wa?
Ma ka ñw u kakini, Anẹ ki dʼọnajiji oñ amadu-wẹ kwo wa-i, todu odu Jihofa Ọjọ-wẹ; todu a gbọ uwohi-wñ, kpai ẹwñ du kʼi che Ijipti,
kpai ẹwñ du kʼi che amonu abo Amọr meji ku ma jʼudaba Jọrdan lẹ, owñ che Sihọn onu Hẹshbọn, kpai Ọg onu Beshan, e-kʼi dẹ Ashtarọt.
Oñ abogijo-wa kpai abo anẹ-wa chaka ka ñw a kakini, Mẹ mʼujẹwñ ku mẹ jẹ ej ọna ko nyʼọwọ, ku mẹ ledo ma, ku mẹ la ka ñwu ma kakini, Amadu-mẹ a che; todulẹ fai mẹ kpʼalo kpai awa ke.
Ujẹwñ ulẹ-wa-i chebọ una ẹgba kʼa ko kwef unyi-wa dufu kʼa wʼugbo mẹ-i, fai, ẹ la go, i gbẹ, i la kpebu;
aiko omi achiwebẹtẹma-i chʼetitọ ẹgba kʼa chʼomi nyʼu ẹkọ kʼa kwanẹ unyi; ẹ la go, i kpana mẹ; ẹwñ ọla-wa-i, kpai ẹda-wa gbo noj ujiji ulẹ-wñ ki tabale.
Tak abokẹlẹ lẹ bʼuma jʼujẹwñ ulẹ-ma, ma la ti Jihofa ene n.
Taku Jọshua fʼurẹdọ che kpai ama, oñ i fʼalo kpẹ kpai ama, kʼi jẹ ñwu ma deju; amidachi abo ọgbadu lẹ gọ ñwu ma.
Oñ i lewatu ẹgba kʼọjọ ẹkẹta ku ma kpʼalo kpai ama lẹ jọ, ma gbʼinabali ka ku ma chʼabo ki dodo mẹru ma ananẹ, ma lañọ dodo efu-ma gẹ.
Tak amọma Israẹl kʼẹrẹ nyʼulẹ oñ ma lewa ewo-ma ọjọ ẹkẹta. Alu kʼodu ewo-ma kọ dẹ; Gibeọn kpai Chefira kpai Birot kpai Kiriat-jearim.
Abo Israẹl muda kpa ma n, todabu kʼamidachi abo ọgbadu lẹ fu Jihofa, Ọjọ Israẹl, gọ ñwu ma. Tak abo ọgbadu lẹ chaka chanẹ ekʼeñmini nyʼamidachi ọla.
Ama amidachi lẹ du ka ñw abo ọgbadu chaka kakini, A fi Jihofa, Ọjọ e-Israẹl gọ ñwu ma mẹ, todulẹ a neke ñọ dọwọkado ma fai gẹ n.
Ẹwñ kʼa ache ñwu ma dẹ, a jẹ ñwu ma deju; todẹgba kʼuwẹdọ lewa bʼuwa ma todu egọ kʼa gọ ñwu ma lẹ.
Tak amidachi lẹ ka ñwu ma kakini, Jẹ ñwu ma deju. Abẹlẹ ma mud abo ku ma kpʼiji na kpai abo ku ma kpʼomiofo ñw abo ọgbadu lẹ chaka, alu kʼamidachi lẹ ka ñwu ma.
Taki Jọshua fʼuma dọ wa, oñ i ka ñwu ma kakini, Ẹwñ chi ku mẹ gwʼuwa ọgwọ, kʼamẹ kakini, Awa chʼabo ọnajiji? mẹ la dodo efu-wa.
Todulẹ ama fʼumẹ mu mẹ, adu eche ada efu-mẹ ogbegbelẹ n, owñ chʼabo ku ma kpʼiji na kpai abo ku ma kpʼomiofo todu unyi Ọjọ-mi.
Ma dohi ñwu Jọshua kakini, Todabu ku ma ka ñw amadu-wẹ-i kpaka, alu ki Jihofa Ọjọ-wẹ ñwa ñw adu-wñ Mosẹs, kʼi adʼanẹ-i chaka ñwu mẹ, kʼi la fʼabo ku ma dodo anẹ-i kparinyọ bʼumẹ ọgba tẹ; todabẹlẹ a chokpo oji ọla
Ma fʼamonu du oñ ma fʼuma kpa Bẹtʼhọrọn
Oñ i lewatu, ẹgba kʼAdoni-Zedẹk onu Jẹrusalẹm gbọ alu ki Jọshua fu Ai du kʼi la mʼu dutẹ ñw Ọjọ hioko, (kʼi la che Ai kpai onu-wñ alu kʼi che Jẹriko kpai onu-wñ gẹ), kpai alu kʼabo ku ma dodo anẹ Gibeọn fʼurẹdọ che kpai abo Israẹl, ku ma la jọ efu-ma,
ma chanẹ erailo tabale, todabu ku Gibeọn chʼewo ki nana, dabẹnẹ kʼewo onu, todabu kʼi lañọ nana tʼAi le, abokẹlẹ-wñ chaka la chʼamagbiti.
Todulẹ Adoni-Zedẹk, onu Jẹrusalẹm lẹ fʼonẹ kpẹru Hohma onu Hẹbrọn, kpai Piram onu Jarmut, kpai Jafia onu Lakish, kpai Dẹbir onu Eglọn, kakini,
Mẹ tẹgu wa ku mẹ tẹko mi, kʼa ki fu Gibeọn kpọfọ; todu owñ fʼurẹdọ che kpai Jọshua kpai abo Israẹl.
Tak amonu abo Amọr mẹlu lẹ, owñ chʼonu Jẹrusalẹm kpai onu Hẹbrọn kpai onu Jarmut kpai onu Lakish kpai onu Eglọn, kʼọla-ma jeju jọ, tak ama kpai abogu-ma chaka mutẹgu ku ma ru le Gibeọn daka, oñ ma kʼogu bʼọ.
Tak abo Gibeọn kpʼonẹ nyʼugbo Jọshua uru Gilgal lẹ, ma kakini, Ẹ ki bọwọlọ ugbo atẹko amadu-wẹ-i n; mutẹgu wʼugbo wa piopio, kʼẹ mʼuwa gba; todu amonu Amọr du ku ma dodo anẹ uwo lẹ kʼọla-ma jeju nyʼuwa.
Abẹlẹ Jọshua kwo Gilgal mutẹgu le, owñ, kpai abogu du ku ma jʼugbo-wñ kpai amagbiti ku ma nʼuwohi chaka.
Taki Jihofa ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Ẹ ki railo ma n, todu omi mʼuma ko nyʼuwẹ ọwọ; ẹnẹkate efu-ma adago ọgba-wẹ n.
Abẹlẹ Jọshua lewa bʼuma ma achigili, abu kʼi kwo Gilgal tẹgu alo gbogbo ñw ọjọ.
Oñ Jihofa fʼuma biya ọgba abo Israẹl, oñ i nʼuku elile akpa ma Gibeọn, tak i fʼuma ne lʼọna atẹgu Bẹt-họrọn, i la gwo ma da gbogbo wa Azika gbogbo wa Makeda.
Oñ i lewatu abu ku ma jʼara rʼọgba abo Israẹl, abu ku ma agwọru Bẹt-họrọn lẹ, Jihofa ko okuta elile rọ kwo ojale wa abʼuma oji ma gbogbo wa Azika, oñ ma leku; abo ku ma ku noj okuta ọmọjọcha la wewe tʼabo kʼabo Israẹl nʼugbada kpa le.
Taki Jọshua kọla ñwu Jihofa ọjọ ki Jihofa mʼabo Amọr ko nyʼabo Israẹl ọwọ lẹ, oñ i ka eju abo Israẹl kakini, Olu, uwẹ ki we dago atẹ Gibeọn; kpai uwẹ, ochu, ef ọgọ Aijalọn.
Tak olu kwodago, ochu la kwʼẹgu-wñ n, gbogbo tak abo ichi lẹ fʼachẹ ọla-ma na ugbo amẹnebi-ma. I chʼinabali-wñ oñ ma kọ rʼef ubuku Jashar lẹ n? Oñ olu dago ẹgu-wñ alumeji ojale, i la hika tunyʼanẹ n, dabẹnẹ kʼọjọʼka odukulu.
Ọjọʼka ki Jihofa netirʼomu onẹ abẹlẹ la dʼọgba-wñ n, i la dʼubi-wñ n; todu Jihofa fʼogu ja todu abo Israẹl.
Taku Jọshua mudabi, oñ abo Israẹl chaka la lebʼowñ nyʼuru Gilgal lẹ.
Oñ amonu mẹlu lẹ ra nyʼakʼọla-ma maja ef owo Makeda.
Taku ma mudu ka ñwu Jọshua kakini, Ma fʼamonu mẹlu lẹ li abu ku ma maja ef owo Makeda.
Taki Jọshua kakini, Mẹ mʼokuta elile li bʼalu owo lẹ ma, ku mẹ kʼonẹ jʼọmọ ku ma fʼuma de;
mẹ ki muda kpọkpẹ ọmọ n, mẹ ki rano amẹnebi-mẹ lẹ, mẹ gbʼuma ubi, mẹ jẹ ñwu ma gudu wʼef ewo-ma n; todu Jihofa Ọjọ-mẹ mʼuma ko nyʼumẹ ọwọ mẹ.
Oñ i lewatu, ẹgba ki Jọshua kpai abo Israẹl gwo ma dajanẹ ẹkutẹ gbogbo taku ma liẹ rinyọ, kʼẹbọbọ-ma ki bọ mugudu nyʼef ewo ewo ki nʼaku,
tak amonẹ lẹ chaka mudabi wʼuru-ma ugbo Jọshua Makeda kpai urẹdọ; ẹnẹ du gbẹdọ hi alu kado abo Israẹl ọla n.
Taku Jọshua kakini, Mʼalu owo bi ku mẹ kʼamonu mẹlu lẹ kwef owo lẹ dufu ñwu mi.
Taku ma fʼabẹlẹ che, ma la kʼamonu mẹlu lẹ kwef owo dufu ñw u, owñ che onu Jẹrusalẹm kpai onu Hẹbrọn kpai onu Jarmut kpai onu Lakish kpai onu Eglọn.
Oñ i lewatu, ẹgba ku ma kʼamonu dufu wʼugbo Jọshua, Jọshua fʼabokẹlẹ Israẹl chaka dọ wa, oñ i ka ñw amẹnutọgba ef abogu ku ma le bʼowñ lẹ kakini, Mutẹwa, ku mẹ mʼẹrẹ ko dʼamonu-i ọlọ. Oñ ma mutẹwa, taku ma mʼẹrẹ-ma ko dʼuma ọlọ.
Taki Jọshua ka ñwu ma kakini, Mẹ ki chokpo n, ẹdọ-mẹ ki muda kpu n; mẹ fʼeju gbiti, mẹ fʼugbẹdọ nẹ; todu abẹlẹ oñ Jihofa ache amẹnebi-mẹ kʼamẹ
Ubilẹ taku Jọshua fʼuma gwo utili utili, oñ i ko ma kpa, tak i ko ma lọkọli ọla oli mẹlu. Oñ ma lọkọli ọla oli lẹ gbogbo dʼọjọ.
Oñ i lewatu adiko kʼolu atunyʼanẹ Jọshua ñwa ñwu ma, oñ ma mʼuma ko kwʼoji oli wʼanẹ, taku ma ko ma rikpolo jʼef owo ugbo ku ma kʼọla-ma maja lẹ, oñ ma kʼokuta elile-lile bʼalu owo lẹ ma, gbogbo tʼeñini.
Ma f ʼabo Kenan ọwọ ọpata ọganẹ du
Jọshua la fu Makeda du ọjọ lẹ, oñ i nʼalu ugbada gwo ma, kpai onu-wñ da gẹ; i mʼuma ko jọ ñw Ọjọ hioko tʼowñ tʼonugo onẹ du ku ma jʼefu-wñ, i tʼẹnẹ kate nọ kʼi bọ n; i la che onu Makeda alu kʼi che onu Jẹriko.
Taku Jọshua kwo Makeda lale tu Libna, abo Israẹl du la jʼugbo-wñ, oñ i kʼogu bọ Libna lẹ;
taki Jihofa ñọ mʼọmọ kpai onu-wñ ko nyʼabo Israẹl ọwọ gẹ; oñ i nʼalu ugbada gwʼo da, kpai amonugo onẹ du ku ma jʼefu-wñ; i tʼẹnẹ kate nọ kʼi bọ efu-wñ n. I la che onu-wñ alu kʼi che onu Jẹriko lẹ gẹ.
Taki Jọshua kpai abo Israẹl chaka manyʼowñ, kwo Libna lale tu Lakish, oñ ma ru nyʼu jọ, ma la kʼogu bʼọ;
Jihofa lañọ mu Lakish lẹ du tʼabo Israẹl ọwọ gẹ, oñ i fʼu du ọjọ ekeji-wñ, i la nʼalu ugbada gwʼo da, kpai amonugo onẹ du ku ma jʼefu-wñ, alu du kʼi che Libna lẹ.
Taku Horam onu Gezẹr lewa kʼi gbutu ñwu Lakish lẹ; oñ Jọshua fʼowñ kpai amonẹ-wñ gwoda gboogbo, i la tʼẹnẹ du nọ kʼi bọ ọmọ n.
Taki Jọshua kpai abo Israẹl du manyʼu kwo Lakish lale nyi Eglọn, ma la ru nyʼu, oñ ma kʼogu bʼọ; ma la fʼu du ọjọ lẹ;
taku ma nʼalu ugbada gwo da; oñ i mʼamonugo onẹ du ku ma jʼefu-wñ kojọ ñw Ọjọ ọjọ lẹ hioko, alu du kʼi che Lakish lẹ.
Taki Jọshua kpai abo Israẹl du kwo Eglọn lale tu Hẹbrọn; oñ ma kogu bʼọ.
Ma la fʼu du oñ ma nʼalu ugbada gwʼo da tʼonu tʼadogbe-wñ chaka tʼamonugo onẹ du ku ma jʼefu-wñ; i tʼẹnẹ du nọ kʼi bọ n, alu du kʼi che Eglon; i la mʼu dutẹ ñw Ọjọ hioko manyʼamonugo onẹ du ku ma jʼefu-wñ.
Taku Jọshua kpai abo Israẹl du mudabi nyi Debir, oñ ma kogu bʼọ,
i la fʼu du manyʼonu-wñ kpai adogbe-wñ chaka; oñ ma nʼalu ugbada gwo ma da, ma la mʼamonugo onẹ chaka ku ma jʼefu-wñ kojọ ñw Ọjọ; i tʼẹnẹ kate nọ kʼi bọ n. Alu kʼi che Hẹbrọn, kpai alu kʼi che Libna, abẹlẹ i ñọ che Debir, kpai onu-wñ gẹ.
Abẹlẹ Jọshua fʼanẹ lẹ chaka gwoda, tʼanẹ uwo-wñ, tʼọwọ ọpata ọganẹ, tʼanẹ ọgọ, tʼatẹgu-wñ, tʼamonu-ma chaka; i tʼẹnẹ kate nọ kʼi bọ n, i mʼẹwñ du ki añmiñmi kojọ ñw Ọjọ, alu ki Jihofa Ọjọ e-Israẹl ñwatẹ.
Oñ Jọshua gwo ma da akwo Kedẹsh-barnea gbogbo wa Gaza, kpai anẹ Goshẹn chaka gbogbo wa Gibeọn.
Oñ Jọshua mʼamonu-i chaka kpai anẹ-ma gba ẹgba kate, todabu ki Jihofa, Ọjọ e-Israẹl, jogu tod abo Israẹl.
Taki Jọshua kpai abo Israẹl chaka mudabi wʼuru Gilgal lẹ
